### [1] [Reservoir computing by thin film embedded with magnetic impurities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01360)
*Shuto Kamakura,Tomi Ohtsuki,Jun-ichiro Ohe*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文数值研究了基于嵌入磁性杂质的薄膜并考虑长程偶极-偶极相互作用的储层计算（reservoir computing），发现即使仅使用空间平均输出，该系统在手写数字识别任务中仍能达到高分类精度，表明长程相互作用能有效将复杂空间输入模式编码到时域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索薄膜中长程偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interaction）对储层计算性能的影响，尤其是当仅能获取空间平均输出时，系统是否仍能有效处理复杂空间输入模式。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，通过考虑偶极-偶极相互作用模拟磁化动力学（magnetization dynamics），并执行手写数字识别任务（handwritten-digit recognition task），训练数据通过对样本进行空间平均（spatial average）来准备。

Result: 尽管训练数据仅包含空间平均信息，该系统仍实现了高分类准确率（high classification accuracy）。长程相互作用能够将复杂的空间输入模式有效编码到时域，即便只有空间平均输出可用。

Conclusion: 该研究证明长程相互作用在储层计算中具有时序编码能力，为易于实现的磁性储层计算（magnetic reservoir computing）系统铺平了道路。

Abstract: The reservoir computing based on the thin film embedded with magnetic impurities in the presence of the long-range (the dipole-dipole) interaction is numerically investigated. We simulated the magnetization dynamics by taking into account the dipole-dipole interaction and performed the handwritten-digit recognition task. Although the training data is prepared by taking spatial average in the sample, the high classification accuracy is achieved. Our result demonstrates that the long range interaction effectively encodes the complex spatial input pattern into the time domain, even when only a spatially averaged output is accessible. The proposed system paves the way for easily realizable magnetic reservoir computing.

</details>


### [2] [The free energy limit of the SYK model at high temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02768)
*David Gamarnik,Francisco Pernice,Alexander Schmidhuber,Alexander Zlokapa*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文针对Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型，在足够高但恒定的温度下，严格计算了其退火与淬火自由能极限。证明方法新颖，依赖稀疏随机图的成分结构理论和空穴法（cavity method）的变体，与物理方法不同但在数值上一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SYK模型在凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）和黑洞全息理论（holographic theory）中具有重要地位，但其严格的数学分析极为困难，甚至连退火自由能（annealed free energy）这样的基本问题都难以处理。本文旨在为这一核心难题提供严格的数学证明。

Method: 作者采用了一种全新的数学证明路径，区别于物理学的启发式方法。该方法基于两个支柱：(a) 稀疏随机图（sparse random graphs）的成分结构理论；(b) 空穴法（cavity method）的一个变体——该方法此前已广泛应用于经典自旋玻璃（spin glasses）的严格和启发式处理中。

Result: 在足够高但恒定的温度下，严格计算了SYK模型的退火自由能极限和淬火自由能（quenched free energy）极限。所得结果与物理方法推导的数值结果吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作为SYK模型的自由能计算提供了严格的数学基础，并展示了一条不同于传统物理方法的新证明路径。数值上的一致性验证了物理结果的正确性，而方法的独立性为后续相关模型的严格分析开辟了可能性。

Abstract: The Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model is a disordered quantum mean-field model studied in condensed matter physics and the holographic theory of black holes. Its structural properties can be derived heuristically using a combination of the replica method and path integration techniques. Analyzing it mathematically rigorously, however, turned out to be notoriously difficult, even for basic questions such as computing the annealed free energy.
  In this paper we rigorously compute the free energy limit (annealed and quenched) for this model at high enough but constant temperature. Our results are in numerical agreement with the results derived by physics methods. Remarkably, though, our method of proof is novel and is different from the physics approach. It is based on (a) the theory of the component structure of sparse random graphs and (b) a variant of the cavity method, used widely in prior rigorous and heuristic treatments of classical spin glasses.

</details>


### [3] [Computational Methods towards Ultrastable Glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02679)
*Fabio Leoni,Misaki Ozawa,John Russo,Taiki Yanagishima,Andrea Ninarello*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文综述了超稳定玻璃（ultrastable glasses）的计算实现方法，系统梳理了该领域最有效算法的关键步骤、效率、局限性及物理解释，并对不同方法所达成的稳定性进行了比较分析，旨在为相关研究者提供对该领域现状与机遇的直观理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超稳定玻璃因其极低的能量态以及增强的动力学、热力学和力学稳定性，长期以来一直是实验研究的热点。然而，传统冷却协议无法触及深度过冷（deeply supercooled）和非平衡（nonequilibrium）玻璃态，数值方法利用非物理（unphysical）移动成为突破这一瓶颈的关键途径。

Method: 本文以综述形式梳理了凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）领域中实现超稳定玻璃的最有效算法，逐一讨论了每种方法的效率、局限性和物理解释，并进行了跨方法的稳定性比较分析。

Result: 本文给出了对该领域现有算法及其所达成稳定性的系统性比较，为理解玻璃转变（glass transition）与非晶态（amorphous states）的本质提供了关键见解，并为设计力学性能稳健的玻璃材料提供了指导。

Conclusion: 该综述为新手和专家提供了对超稳定玻璃计算实现领域当前状态与未来机遇的直观且全面的理解。

Abstract: Ultrastable glasses, amorphous solids with exceptionally low-energy states and enhanced kinetic, thermodynamic and mechanical stability, have long been a subject of intense experimental interest. Over the past decade, their computational realization has emerged as a major goal in condensed matter physics, as numerical methods can exploit unphysical moves to access deeply supercooled and nonequilibrium glassy states far beyond the reach of conventional cooling protocols, thereby providing key insights into the nature of the glass transition and amorphous states and enabling the design of mechanically robust glassy materials. In this review, we outline the key steps underlying the most effective algorithms developed across the field. For each approach, we discuss its efficiency, limitations, and physical interpretation. We finally present a comparative analysis of the stability achieved across these methods, with the aim of equipping both newcomers and experts with an intuitive and comprehensive understanding of the field's current state and the opportunities it presents.

</details>

### [4] [Loop expansion in polymer field theory: application to phase separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01261)
*Kiyoharu Kawana,Kyosuke Adachi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过将聚合物密度的倒数类比为量子场论中的普朗克常数，发展了一套场论圈图展开（loop expansion）方法，对均聚物体系的随机相位近似（RPA）自由能进行逐级修正（RPA+和RPA++），并借助分子动力学模拟验证了RPA+对双节线（binodal）的改进效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机相位近似（random phase approximation, RPA）虽广泛用于预测聚合物溶液的液-液相分离行为，但其在高密度区域之外的定量准确性（尤其是对双节线）尚未得到充分表征，因此需要发展系统性的修正方法。

Method: 通过将逆聚合物密度ρ⁻¹识别为量子场论中的普朗克常数ħ，在均聚物体系中构建场论圈图展开；计算了RPA自由能的领头阶（leading-order）和次领头阶（next-to-leading-order）修正，分别记为RPA+和RPA++；采用具有高斯对相互作用的珠-弹簧链（bead-spring chains）进行分子动力学模拟，以验证RPA+预测的双节线。

Result: 与分子动力学模拟对比发现，RPA+在定性上改善了稀相共存密度（dilute-phase coexistence density）的预测，优于原始RPA；但临界点（critical point）误差与RPA相当，未见显著改进。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了圈图展开作为一种系统性途径，可用于优化基于RPA的聚合物相分离双节线预测。

Abstract: Liquid-liquid phase separation underlies phenomena ranging from protein condensate formation to the phase coexistence of synthetic polymers. Although the random phase approximation (RPA) is widely used to predict such phase behavior, its quantitative accuracy for binodals of polymer solutions, particularly outside the high-density regime, remains incompletely characterized. Here, we develop a field theoretic loop expansion in homopolymer systems by identifying the inverse polymer density $ρ^{-1}$ as the Planck constant $\hbar$ in quantum field theory. We calculate the leading-order and next-to-leading-order corrections to the RPA free energy, denoted as RPA+ and RPA++, respectively. Testing the binodal predicted by the RPA+ against molecular dynamics simulations of bead-spring chains with Gaussian pair interactions, we find that the RPA+ qualitatively improves the dilute-phase coexistence density over the RPA, while the critical point error remains comparable to that of the RPA. Our results establish the loop expansion as a systematic route for refining the RPA-based binodal predictions for polymer phase separation.

</details>


### [5] [Colloidal layer deposition with a controllable number of layers and compositional order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01470)
*Akshaya Kumar Jena,Aashima Aashima,Pritam Kumar Jana,Bortolo Matteo Mognetti*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文设计了一种二元胶体（binary suspension of colloids）悬浮系统，通过将胶体与表面装饰多种具有特异性相互作用的DNA寡聚体（DNA oligomers），实现了有限厚度微晶（crystallites）的可控自组装。表面触发DNA寡聚体间的链式反应驱动局部组装，聚集体的厚度由平衡原理（equilibrium principles）控制，而组分有序性（compositional order）则通过调控反应动力学（reaction kinetics）实现。理论分析与反应-扩散模拟（reaction-diffusion simulation）验证了该设计，表明动力学工程为DNA组装聚集体的形态控制提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自组装方法难以同时精确控制聚集体的厚度和两种不同类型颗粒的层内排布。为解决这一问题，本文提出一种利用DNA寡聚体特异性相互作用的二元胶体-表面系统，以实现厚度可控且组分有序的有限厚度微晶组装。

Method: 在胶体颗粒和表面修饰多种DNA寡聚体，赋予其特异性相互作用；表面触发DNA寡聚体间的链式反应以驱动局部自组装；通过平衡原理控制聚集体厚度，通过调控反应动力学限制同类型胶体间的相互作用以实现组分有序性；采用理论和反应-扩散模拟算法验证设计。

Result: 所设计系统成功实现了有限厚度微晶的自组装，聚集体的层数可受控，两类颗粒被约束在不同平面内。反应-扩散模拟捕捉到相互作用的多体性（multibody nature），验证了设计的可行性。

Conclusion: 动力学工程为控制DNA组装聚集体的形态提供了新途径，拓展了利用非平衡过程（non-equilibrium processes）调控自组装结构的可能性。

Abstract: We design a system with a binary suspension of colloids and a surface that triggers the self-assembly of crystallites with a finite thickness. The proposed design allows controlling the number of layers forming the aggregate and constrains the two types of particles to lie on different planes. These functionalities are achieved by decorating the colloids and the surface with multiple DNA oligomers featuring specific interactions. The surface triggers a chain of reactions between DNA oligomers, leading to localized self-assembly. Equilibrium principles control the thickness of the aggregates. Instead, compositional order is achieved by engineering the reaction kinetics between DNA oligomers in a way that limits interactions between colloids of the same type. We validate our design using theory and reaction-diffusion simulation algorithms, which capture the multibody nature of the interactions. This work demonstrates how engineering the kinetics provides a new avenue for controlling the morphology of aggregates assembled by DNA.

</details>


### [6] [Dimple-Encoded Reprogrammable Origami](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01531)
*Qun Zhang,Weicheng Huang,Amir Hajiyavand,Hyunyoung Kim,Claire Dancer,Karl Dearn,Mingchao Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于凹陷编码（dimple-encoded）的折纸平台，通过双稳态凹陷的快速翻转（snapping）在连续弹性薄板中生成空间可寻址的铰链，实现可编程折叠与可重复编程的形状变换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可编程弹性薄板折叠方法依赖预定义折痕或活性材料铰链，缺乏内在双稳态（intrinsic bistability），且单个结构中可重编程性（reprogrammability）受限。

Method: 通过设计双稳态凹陷的排布与选择性反转（selective inversion），将凹陷的快速翻转行为转化为具有指定折叠角度的空间可寻址铰链；建立折叠角度设计图表（folding-angle design charts），形成无需改变基本单元几何的铰链库（hinge library）。

Result: 单个凹陷薄板可被重编程实现三角形、正方形、五边形等多种构型；方法可扩展至平面到三维的多面体折纸（polyhedral origami）变形，并通过实验与有限元模拟验证；实现了自支撑立方壳结构（增强抗冲击性）和部分可展开立方体构型。

Conclusion: 该策略提供了一条制造友好（fabrication-friendly）的路径，用于构建可重编程的形状变形（reprogrammable shape-morphing）与自适应力学系统（adaptive mechanical systems）。

Abstract: Programmable folding of elastic sheets typically relies on predefined flexible creases or active materials-enabled hinges, which lack intrinsic bistability and limit reprogrammability within a single structure. Here, we present a dimple-encoded origami platform that converts bistable dimple snapping into spatially addressable hinges with prescribed folding angles in a continuous sheet. This interaction-enabled mechanism enables the design of distributed hinge networks through the arrangement and selective inversion of dimples. We establish folding-angle design charts that can be directly used to select local dimple arrangements for target fold angle, forming a practical hinge library without altering the underlying unit geometry. Using this approach, a single dimpled sheet can be reprogrammed to realize multiple distinct configurations, such as triangle, square, and pentagon shapes. We further extend the method to flat-to-3D morphing of polyhedral origami and validate the results through experiments and finite element simulations. As demonstrations, we realize self-supporting cubic shells with enhanced impact resistance and partially deployable cube configurations that remain stable upon opening, highlighting their potential for protective enclosures and deployable architectural structures. The proposed strategy provides a fabrication-friendly route to reprogrammable shape-morphing and adaptive mechanical systems.

</details>


### [7] [Hindered transport of spherical particles in cylindrical pores: The role of structural heterogeneity in rejection-permeability trade-offs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01820)
*Debanik Bhattacharjee,Yaniv Edery,Guy Z. Ramon*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对圆柱孔中球形颗粒的位阻受限输运（steric hindered-transport）框架，明确解析了孔径与粒径的单重及耦合双重异质性（dual heterogeneity），并系统分析了异质性对膜分离中截留率（rejection）与渗透性（permeability）权衡关系的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有膜分离研究主要关注理想或弱异质性体系，但在强异质性（strongly heterogeneous）介质中，孔径与粒径的耦合分布如何影响对流-扩散局部平衡以及截留-渗透权衡尚不清楚。

Method: 构建了一个位阻受限输运框架，针对圆柱孔中球形颗粒，显式解析单重与耦合双重粒径和孔径分布异质性，并计算系综平均截留率及有效Péclet数（effective Péclet number）的分布。

Result: 系综平均截留率随颗粒-孔径纵横比$λ$和Péclet数$Pe$增加而上升；对流在中等的$λ$下可将位阻排斥（steric exclusion）增强约20%。双重异质性拓宽了有效$Pe$的分布，增加了反常截留趋势的变异性和发生率，并在固定截留率下系统地将截留-渗透权衡向更高渗透率方向偏移。

Conclusion: 受控异质性可作为设计杠杆（design lever），用于扩展同时实现高选择性（high selectivity）与高通量（high throughput）的可达操作空间。

Abstract: Membrane separations rely on balancing rejection and permeability. Extensive work has clarified how pore structure and operating conditions control each quantity in idealized or weakly heterogeneous systems. However, it remains unclear how this trade-off emerges in strongly heterogeneous media, where coupled distributions of pore and particle sizes shape the local balance between advection and diffusion and generate substantial variability in performance among distribution realizations. Here we present a steric hindered-transport framework for spherical particles in cylindrical pores that explicitly resolves both single and coupled dual heterogeneity in size distributions. We show that the ensemble-averaged rejection increases with the particle-pore aspect ratio $λ$ and with the Péclet number $Pe$, while advection enhances steric exclusion by up to $\sim$20\% at intermediate $λ$. Dual heterogeneity broadens the distribution of effective $Pe$, increases the variability and incidence of anomalous rejection trends, while systematically shifting the rejection-permeability trade-off toward higher permeability at fixed rejection. These results suggest that controlled heterogeneity can serve as a design lever to expand the attainable operating space for simultaneous high selectivity and high throughput.

</details>


### [8] [Unraveling and controlling the self-assembly pathways of cubic colloids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01859)
*Dillip Kumar Mohapatra,Teun W. J. Verouden,Janne-Mieke Meijer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本实验通过调控立方体胶体(cubic colloids)形状诱导的方向性键(directional bonds)强度，揭示了三种自组装(self-assembly)机制：成核生长(nucleation and growth)、动态重排(dynamic)与动力学停滞(static)，并证明这些机制间的可逆转变可用于路径工程(pathway engineering)以控制结构有序度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 各向异性构筑单元(anisotropic building blocks)的自组装是材料科学中的重要设计策略，但各向异性相互作用如何影响无序（非）平衡结构的早期生长与形成机制尚不明确。

Method: 通过追踪不同吸引力强度下小团簇(clusters)的生长动力学与内部重排，实验表征了立方体胶体的自组装路径。

Result: 识别出三种自组装机制：(i) 以缓慢重排为主导的结晶团簇成核生长区，(ii) 扩散受限生长伴随动态重排导致无序结晶团簇的动态区，(iii) 因方向性键约束而无法重排的动力学停滞团簇的静态区；且各区间的转变是可逆的。

Conclusion: 方向性键主导路径选择(pathway selection)，为可重构胶体、纳米与生物材料的理性设计(rational design)提供了重要见解。

Abstract: The self-assembly of anisotropic building blocks into complex spatial architectures is an important design strategy in material science but the mechanisms by which the anisotropic interactions influence the early-stage growth and formation of disordered (non-)equilibrium structures remain poorly understood. Here, we experimentally demonstrate that tuning the strength of shape-induced directional bonds changes the self-assembly pathways of cubic colloids. By tracking the growth kinetics and internal reorganizations of small clusters at increasing attraction strength, we identify three self-assembly regimes: (i) nucleation and growth regime: slow reorganization-dominated growth of crystalline clusters, (ii) dynamic regime: diffusion-limited growth with dynamic cube reorganizations leading to disordered crystalline clusters and (iii) static regime: diffusion-limited growth of kinetically arrested clusters unable to reorganize due to directional bonding constraints. We further show that transitions between these regimes are reversible and allow pathway engineering to control the structure and disorder. Our results reveal how directional bonding governs pathway selection, providing important insights for the rational design of reconfigurable colloidal, nano-, and biomaterials.

</details>


### [9] [Diffusio-osmotic transport in nanochannels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02419)
*Lydéric Bocquet*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本章聚焦纳米通道中扩散渗流（diffusio-osmosis）这一熵驱动输运现象，论证其源于固体边界扩散层内的熵驱动力，指出扩散渗流可在无需半透性（semi-permeability）的条件下产生渗透驱动，从而扩展了熵驱动输运的适用范围。文章通过Onsager框架（Onsager framework）和全局/局域力平衡将渗透与扩散渗流统一表述，并展示了其在增强扩散、机械敏感性、整流渗透流以及渗透能量转换等方面的概念性应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示扩散渗流作为熵驱动输运（entropically-driven transport）的一种微妙表面输运机制，阐明其在纳米通道（nanochannels）中无需半透膜即可产生渗透驱动，从而拓展熵驱动输运的存在范围。

Method: 采用Onsager框架（Onsager framework）对扩散渗流与经典渗透进行统一形式化描述，并通过局域和全局力平衡（local and global force balances）进行定量分析；同时选取一系列具有概念重要性的示例进行阐释。

Result: 证明扩散渗流可在无半透性条件下产生渗透驱动，从而将熵驱动输运的适用范围从经典半透膜体系扩展到纳米通道；揭示扩散渗流表现为增强扩散（enhanced diffusion）、机械敏感性（mechano-sensitivity）、整流渗透流（rectified osmotic flows）以及渗透能量转换（osmotic energy conversion）等多种形式。

Conclusion: 扩散渗流与经典渗透是同一现象的两面，纳米通道是扩散渗流及其衍生效应得以充分展现的特权场所；该机制可支撑从单纳米孔到膜模块级别的渗透能量转换，具有接近工业应用的潜力。

Abstract: In this chapter, I will enter into the roots of entropically-driven transport with a focus on diffusio-osmotic transport in nanochannels. Diffusio-osmosis is a subtle surface transport, originating in entropic driving forces occuring within the diffuse layers at solid boundaries. Specifying diffusio-osmosis to nanochannels may first look like a marginal refinement, yet it reveals that osmotic drivings can arise in channels and membranes without the prerequisite of semi-permeability, so that diffusio-osmosis extends the domain of existence of entropically driven transport. Osmosis and diffusio-osmosis are two faces of the same phenomenon, naturally embedded in an Onsager framework and quantified by local and global force balances. This perspective clarifies why nanochannels are privileged arenas where diffusio-osmosis and its consequence do flourish. Throughout the chapter, I discuss a set of conceptually relevant examples to show how diffusio-osmosis "pops up" in various situations: as enhanced diffusion, mechano-sensitivity, rectified osmotic flows and, ultimately, as a lever for osmotic energy conversion from single nanopores to membrane modules approaching industrial reality.

</details>


### [10] [Nonlinear isotropic odd elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02476)
*Shiheng Zhao,Pierre A. Haas*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文建立了二维各向同性柯西弹性固体在有限变形下的非线性理论框架，并将其应用于Rivlin问题。研究发现“奇弹”效应抑制了二维Rivlin正方形的分岔行为，但三维Rivlin立方体的分岔在奇弹性存在下仍然保留，尽管三维空间中不存在各向同性的线性奇弹性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性固体（active solids）中非保守弹性响应的研究热潮集中于二维“奇”弹性（odd elasticity）的小线性变形行为，但大非线性变形下的理论描述尚属空白。本文旨在建立二维各向同性柯西弹性固体在有限变形下的非线性框架，并以此为基础探索奇弹性在经典非线性问题（如Rivlin问题）中所产生的意外行为。

Method: 采用非线性弹性理论，建立二维各向同性柯西弹性固体（Cauchy elastic solids）在有限变形下的描述框架，并将其应用于Rivlin问题——在死载荷牵引（dead load tractions）下正方形弹性体的变形问题。

Result: 奇弹性抑制了二维Rivlin正方形的分岔（bifurcations）行为；然而，三维Rivlin立方体的分岔在奇弹性存在下仍然保留，尽管三维空间中不存在各向同性的线性奇弹性。

Conclusion: 该结果为描述活性生物固体的大变形行为奠定了理论基础，并揭示了即使在最简单的弹性问题中也会出现的意外非线性行为。

Abstract: The nonconservative elastic responses of active solids have driven a recent explosion of interest in two-dimensional "odd" elasticity: small, linear deformations of these Cauchy elastic solids enable new behaviour absent from classical, passive elasticity. Here, we establish the description of large, nonlinear deformations of isotropic two-dimensional Cauchy elastic solids. We apply our framework to the Rivlin problem, perhaps the simplest problem of elasticity lacking a linear analogue: a square deforms under dead load tractions. Surprisingly, we find that oddness suppresses the bifurcations of a passive Rivlin square. By contrast, we discover that the bifurcations of a three-dimensional Rivlin cube survive oddness even though there is no isotropic, odd linear elasticity in three dimensions. Our results thus form the basis for describing large deformations of active, biological solids while revealing their unexpected nonlinear behaviour that arises even in minimal problems.

</details>


### [11] [Shape anisotropy governs organization of active rods: Swarming, turbulence, flocking, and jamming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02590)
*Yogesh Shelke,Anpuj Nair S,Hanumantha Rao Vutukuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验与模拟相结合的方法，探究光驱动自推进杆状粒子的长径比与面积分数如何通过形状诱导的排列、空间排斥以及水动力学相互作用，驱动系统从主动布朗运动向蜂拥、主动湍流、集群、大团簇及堵塞等多种自组织状态转变，并建立了相应的状态图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解单个构建块（building block）的形状各向异性如何在非平衡系统中调控自组织行为，并区分物理相互作用与生物机制在杆状微游泳体（rodlike microswimmers）集体运动中的贡献。

Method: 采用光驱动自推进杆（light-driven self-propelled rods）开展实验与模拟相结合的联合研究，通过改变杆的长径比（aspect ratio）和面积分数（area fraction），系统观察其对自组织行为的影响。

Result: 发现系统随参数变化依次表现出主动布朗运动（active Brownian motion）、蜂拥（swarming）、主动湍流（active turbulence）、集群（flocking）、大团簇（large clusters）和堵塞（jamming）等多种涌现行为；建立了一个完整的状态图（state diagram），并通过时空分析揭示了不同状态下的巨数涨落（giant-number fluctuations）特征。

Conclusion: 该最小模型有助于解耦物理与生物机制，为理解杆状微生物游泳体的自组织提供了新视角；同时为可编程合成活性材料（programmable synthetic active materials）提供了设计规则，并揭示了与细菌菌群及其他生物组装体的相似性。

Abstract: Shape anisotropy of individual building blocks plays a crucial role in creating exotic structures and controlling phase behavior in equilibrium systems. We present a combined experimental and simulation study in which we used light-driven self-propelled rods to investigate when and how shape-induced alignment and steric and hydrodynamic interactions govern self-organization. Varying rod aspect ratio and area fraction causes the system to evolve from active Brownian motion to swarming, active turbulence, flocking, large clusters, and jamming. A state diagram summarizes emergent behaviors, and spatiotemporal analyses reveal distinct giant-number fluctuations across states. This minimal model offers insight into the self-organization of biological rodlike microswimmers, enabling the decoupling of physical from biological mechanisms. Our results provide design rules for programmable synthetic active materials and highlight parallels with bacterial swarms and other biological assemblies.

</details>


### [12] [Polymer Knots in Thin Films: Thickness Dependence, Local Effects, and Stiffness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02644)
*Maurice P. Schmitt,Hendrik Meyer,Peter Virnau*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文研究了受限聚合物薄膜厚度 h 对拓扑结构和构象的影响，发现结概率在中间厚度（接近本体回转半径 R_g,bulk）处出现峰值，而在小厚度时趋于零，大厚度时恢复本体值。靠近壁面时，缠结长度单调增加，构象趋于扁平。通过层分辨分析重构了厚度依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究受限（confinement）如何影响聚合物薄膜中的拓扑（topology）性质和构象（conformation），特别是薄膜厚度 h 对结概率（knotting probability）和缠结长度（entanglement length）的调控机制。

Method: 采用层分辨分析（layer-resolved analysis）方法，对聚合物薄膜的结构和拓扑性质进行逐层解析，并通过积分厚膜的层分辨性质来重构显式的厚度依赖关系。

Result: 结概率在中间厚度接近本体回转半径（bulk radius of gyration）R_g,bulk 时出现最大值；小厚度时结概率趋于零，大厚度时趋近本体值。靠近壁面处，缠结长度单调增加，构象变得扁平。

Conclusion: 聚合物薄膜厚度通过改变链的受限程度和壁面附近的局部环境，对拓扑结构和构象产生非单调且空间不均匀的影响；层分辨分析可有效建立局部性质与整体厚度依赖关系之间的联系。

Abstract: We study how confinement affects topology and conformations in polymer films of varying thickness $h$. The knotting probability exhibits a maximum at intermediate thicknesses near the bulk radius of gyration $h \approx R_\mathrm{g,bulk}$, vanishes at small $h$ and approaches bulk values for large $h$. Close to walls, the entanglement length increases monotonically and conformations become flatter. A layer-resolved analysis of structural and topological properties allows us to reconstruct the explicit thickness dependencies by integrating layer-resolved properties of a thick film.

</details>


### [13] [Equilibrium Adsorption of Hard Disks on Patterned Adhesive Surfaces: A Monte Carlo Simulation Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02671)
*Nazar Kukarkin,Taras Patsahan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）研究了盘状颗粒在图案化粘附表面上的平衡吸附行为，发现吸附效率不仅取决于粘附区域总面积，还受表面图案几何结构（特别是域尺寸）的显著影响，当颗粒与粘附域尺寸相同时吸附效果最强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解盘状颗粒在图案化粘附表面上的平衡吸附机制，探究表面图案几何结构（而非仅粘附区域总面积）对吸附行为的控制作用，为功能性表面设计提供理论依据。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟方法，将表面建模为含有规则或随机排列的圆形粘附域（adhesive domains）的二维平面，颗粒视为硬圆盘（hard disks），粒子与表面之间的相互作用能由颗粒与粘附域的接触面积（contact area）定义。

Result: 吸附行为由粘附区域总面积与表面图案几何结构共同控制；域尺寸对吸附效率有显著影响，当颗粒与域尺寸相等时吸附增强最为明显；在高化学势（chemical potential）下，颗粒表面覆盖度增加，位阻效应（steric effects）变得重要，削弱了表面图案几何结构的影响。

Conclusion: 通过选择粘附域的尺寸、覆盖度和空间排列，可以调控吸附效率与颗粒表面组织。该研究对功能性表面、选择性吸附平台、生物传感器（biosensors）及基于亲和力的细胞分选系统（affinity-based cell sorting systems）的设计具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Equilibrium adsorption of disk-like particles on patterned adhesive surfaces is studied using Monte Carlo simulations. The surface is represented as a two-dimensional plane with circular adhesive domains arranged either regularly or randomly, while the particles are modelled as hard disks. The interaction energy between a particle and the surface is defined by the contact area between the particle and the adhesive domains. It is shown that the adsorption behaviour is controlled not only by the total area of the adhesive regions, but also by the geometry of the surface pattern. In particular, the domain size is found to have a significant effect on the adsorption efficiency. The most pronounced effect is observed when the particle and domain sizes are equal, which leads to enhanced adsorption at intermediate values of the chemical potential. At high values of the chemical potential, however, when the particle surface coverage increases, steric effects become important, which weakens the influence of the surface pattern geometry. The obtained results demonstrate that the adsorption efficiency and surface organization of particles can be tuned by choosing the size, coverage, and spatial arrangement of adhesive domains. This study may be useful in the design of functional surfaces, selective adsorption platforms, biosensors, and affinity-based cell sorting systems.

</details>


### [14] [Emergent flocking dynamics in chemorepulsive active colloids: interplay of disorder and noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02854)
*Sagarika Adhikary,Rajesh Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过构建相图，系统研究了具有化学排斥相互作用的活性胶体（active colloids）在淬火无序（quenched disorder）和噪声（noise）共同作用下的集体行为，发现噪声驱动的相变具有显著的密度依赖性，而钉扎分数驱动的相变则无此依赖；此外，有效相互作用范围决定了密度带状结构等集体现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明化学排斥相互作用可在无显式对齐机制的情况下产生全局极性有序。本文旨在进一步探究此类化学相互作用活性胶体系统在淬火无序（部分粒子随机钉扎）和旋转噪声共同影响下的相变行为与集体动力学。

Method: 将部分粒子作为随机钉扎中心限制其平动但保留转动，并引入角噪声描述随机效应；基于极性序参量（polar order parameter）及其涨落构建相图（phase diagram），系统分析无序和噪声驱动的相变及有限尺寸效应。

Result: 噪声驱动的相变显著依赖于粒子密度，而钉扎分数驱动的相变则无此密度依赖性；当有效相互作用范围远小于系统尺寸时，系统形成密度带状结构，且相变点附近序参量分布呈双峰特征；长程相互作用条件下则无此现象。

Conclusion: 淬火无序与噪声在化学排斥活性胶体系统中引发出不同的相变行为，有效相互作用范围是决定集体动力学模式（如密度带状结构）的关键因素。

Abstract: Recent studies of active colloidal matter have revealed that a global polar order can arise from chemorepulsive interactions among particles without any explicit alignment interaction between them. In this work, we investigate such chemically interacting active colloids in the presence of quenched disorder, where a fraction of particles are randomly pinned in space. These pinned particles are restricted to rotational motion while remaining chemically coupled to the mobile population. In addition, angular noise is incorporated into the rotational dynamics to capture stochastic effects. To elucidate the interplay of quenched disorder and noise, we construct phase diagrams based on polar order and its fluctuations, and systematically analyze the associated disorder- and noise-driven phase transitions. Surprisingly, we find that the phase transition driven by the noise is significantly dependent on the density of the particles, whereas such a density-dependence is not present when the control parameter is the pinning fraction. The finite-size effects on these transitions are also examined. An effective interaction range, governed by the coefficient related to screening of the chemorepulsive interaction, plays a crucial role in collective behavior. When the effective interaction range is much smaller than the system size, the system exhibits density band formation, a feature absent in the long-range interaction regime. Moreover, near the transition point, the order parameter distribution becomes bimodal for the case of short-range interaction.

</details>

### [15] [The atomic nucleus as a bound system of $3A$ quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01573)
*B. Kosyakov,E. Popov,M. Vronsky*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文基于低能量子色动力学（low-energy quantum chromodynamics）的有效理论，综述了近期发展的核模型。费米气体模型解释了轻稳定核中 d 夸克与 u 夸克数量近似相等的原因；修正的袋模型（modified bag model）通过引入规范/引力对偶（gauge/gravity duality）描述重核的偏离，并预测了最轻胶球的主要衰变通道、稳定元素有限数目以及稳定重核的最大电荷数 Z_max ≈ 82（对应铅-208）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子核本质上应作为束缚夸克系统，由低能量子色动力学（low-energy quantum chromodynamics）的有效理论来描述；本文旨在综述近期发展的、体现该有效理论核心特征的核模型。

Method: 采用费米气体模型（Fermi gas model）解释轻核中 d 夸克与 u 夸克数量近似相等的现象；引入修正的袋模型（modified bag model）处理重核中对该规则的偏离；进一步借助规范/引力对偶（gauge/gravity duality）来充分发挥修正袋模型的预测能力。

Result: 修正的袋模型能够以合理精度描述多种稳定原子核的静态性质；基于规范/引力对偶的一个精炼版本，可以预测最轻胶球（glueball）的主要衰变通道，并解释元素周期表中稳定元素数目有限的原因，计算出稳定重核的最大容许电荷数 Z_max ≈ 82，即铅-208（^{208}_{82}Pb）的电荷量。

Conclusion: 所综述的模型（费米气体模型与修正的袋模型结合规范/引力对偶）为低能量子色动力学框架下的核结构提供了有效的理论描述，并对稳定核的极限性质给出了明确的理论预言。

Abstract: The atomic nucleus, viewed as a system of bound quarks, should, in principle, be described within an effective theory of low-energy quantum chromodynamics. This paper provides an overview of recently developed models that embody essential features of the desired effective theory. The Fermi gas model helps explain why the number of $d$ quarks is approximately equal to that of $u$ quarks in stable light nuclei up to ${\rm {}^{40}_{20}Ca}$. A modified bag model accounts for the deviation from this rule in heavier nuclei. With this model, the static properties of a wide range of stable nuclei can be described with reasonable accuracy. To make the most of the modified bag model, it is useful to invoke gauge/gravity duality. A refined version of duality states: ``The dynamics inside an extremal black hole in ${\rm AdS}_5$ is mapped onto the corresponding dynamics of a stable subnuclear system in ${\mathbb R}_{1,3}$''. This version of duality allows one to predict the primary decay channel of the lightest glueball. Another implication is that this framework explains why the periodic table contains a finite number of stable elements. Duality makes it possible to calculate the maximum allowed charge $Z_{\rm max}$ of stable heavy nuclei: $Z_{\rm max}\approx 82$, which is the charge of the ${\rm {}^{208}_{82}Pb}$ nucleus.

</details>

### [16] [Black Hole Supernovae Outcomes Across a Wide Progenitor Range](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01405)
*Oliver Eggenberger Andersen,Evan O'Connor,Liubov Kovalenko,Haakon Andresen,Sean M. Couch*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过23组长轴对称核心坍缩模拟，发现黑洞超新星（BHSNe）并非仅限于最致密、质量最大的前身星，而是在较广的前身星结构范围内系统性地出现。研究覆盖19.51-60 M☉的前身星质量范围，发现了18个BHSN结果，并分析了爆炸能量、黑洞质量等关键物理量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞超新星（black hole supernovae，BHSNe）是多维模拟延伸至反弹后数秒时自然出现的计算结果，但仍是核心坍缩（core collapse）中研究最少的结局之一。本文旨在检验BHSNe是否仅局限于最致密且大质量（从而诞生率低）的前身星，还是会在更广泛的前身星结构中系统性地出现。

Method: 对19.51-60 M☉、致密度（compactness）ξ₂.₅介于约0.31至0.63的23个前身星模型，执行长时程轴对称（2D axisymmetric）核心坍缩模拟。在黑洞形成（BH formation）后采用切除（excision）处理方法，将演化至少延续至5000秒。另外还将一个二维轴对称模型与一个三维（3D）模型进行了比较。

Result: 在几乎全部零龄主序（ZAMS）质量范围内发现了18个BHSN结果，对应致密度ξ₂.₅约0.40-0.63的前身星。黑洞形成发生在反弹后约0.7秒至4.4秒之间。最终爆炸能量（explosion energy）约2×10⁴⁹-3×10⁵¹ erg，最终黑洞引力质量（gravitational mass）约3-26 M☉。发现剩余质量与CO核心质量之间存在明显趋势，但CO核心本身不足以作为最终黑洞质量的恰当代理变量，尤其在CO核心分布的低质量端和高质量端。

Conclusion: BHSNe在较宽的前身星参数范围内系统性地出现，而非仅限于最致密大质量的罕见前身星。CO核心质量不能充分预测最终黑洞质量。除最高CO核心质量的模型外，没有任何单一的球形质量坐标能干净地分离抛射物（ejecta）与剩余物质。二维与三维几何之间的差异值得进一步研究。

Abstract: Black hole supernovae (BHSNe), the term we use for core-collapse events in which black hole (BH) formation occurs after shock revival but before the explosion is complete, have emerged as a natural outcome of multidimensional simulations as these calculations have been extended to seconds after bounce. Yet they remain one of the least studied outcomes of core collapse. Here, we assess whether they are confined to the most compact and massive progenitors, whose birth rates are low, or whether they arise systematically across a wider range of progenitor structures. We perform 23 long-term axisymmetric core-collapse simulations of progenitors spanning 19.51-60$\,M_\odot$ and compactnesses $0.31 \lesssim ξ_{2.5} \lesssim 0.63$. We find 18 BHSN outcomes across nearly the full ZAMS mass range considered, corresponding to progenitors with $0.40 \lesssim ξ_{2.5} \lesssim 0.63$. BH formation occurs between $\sim0.7$ s and $\sim4.4$ s after bounce. After BH formation, we continue the evolution with an excision treatment to at least 5000 s. The final explosion energies span $\sim2\times10^{49}$-$3\times10^{51}$ erg, while the final BH gravitational masses span $\sim3$-$26\,M_\odot$. We find a clear remnant-mass trend with CO-core mass, but show that the CO core alone is not an adequate proxy for the final BH mass, especially for progenitors at the low- and high-mass ends of the CO-core distribution. Except for the highest CO-core mass models, no single spherical mass coordinate cleanly separates ejecta from remnant material. Finally, a 2D axisymmetric and a 3D model are compared as we discuss differences between the two geometries.

</details>

### [17] [First-principles simulation of shocked H-He mixture along the principal Hugoniot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01593)
*Ammar A. Ellaboudy,Valentin V. Karasiev,S. X. Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理分子动力学模拟，结合先进交换关联泛函计算H-He混合物的光学反射率，发现反射率在高温下无明显不连续性，且与实验测量在推断为分相的温度范围内一致，表明仅凭反射率不足以作为低氦浓度下H-He分相的可靠诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期激光冲击实验通过光学反射率的不连续性推断木星内部H-He混合物存在不混溶区（immiscibility region），但该诊断方法的唯一性和敏感性尚需理论验证。

Method: 采用第一性原理分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics）模拟冲击压缩的H-He混合物，状态方程和离子构型由热Tr²SCANL meta-GGA交换关联泛函（exchange-correlation functional）获得，光学性质则通过Kubo-Greenwood形式论（Kubo-Greenwood formalism）及高精度的RS-KDT0 range-separated thermal hybrid XC泛函计算。

Result: 计算反射率与实验测量总体吻合，但在高温下未观察到反射率的不连续性；且在混合物被推断为已分相的温度范围内，反射率预测值与实验测量一致。

Conclusion: 反射率本身可能无法作为低氦浓度（11%原子分数）H-He体系在这种条件下分相的唯一或灵敏诊断指标。

Abstract: Recent laser-shock experiments on an H--He mixture containing 11~$\%$ helium (atomic fraction) have suggested the presence of an immiscibility region inside Jupiter. Reflectivity measurements were used as the primary diagnostic of H--He demixing, with discontinuities in the optical reflectivity proposed as a signature of phase separation under conditions relevant to Jupiter's interior. Here, we investigate shock-compressed H--He using \textit{ab initio} molecular dynamics simulations with optical properties evaluated within the Kubo--Greenwood formalism. The equation of state and ionic configurations were obtained using the thermal Tr$^2$SCANL meta-GGA exchange--correlation (XC) functional, while optical properties were computed using the recently developed RS-KDT0 range-separated thermal hybrid XC, which provides state-of-the-art accuracy for band-gap predictions in the warm dense matter regime. The calculated reflectivity shows overall good agreement with experimental measurements; however, no discontinuity is observed at elevated temperatures. Moreover, the reflectivity predictions for the mixed system are consistent with the experimental measurements in the temperature range where the mixture is inferred to be demixed. These results suggest that reflectivity alone may not provide a unique or sensitive diagnostic of H-He demixing at low helium concentrations under these conditions.

### [20] [On Quantum Indeterminacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01103)
*Maurice de Gosson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于凸几何（convex geometry）与辛拓扑（symplectic topology）的量子不确定性几何形式化框架，将标准不确定性不等式（uncertainty inequalities）重新解释为相空间（phase space）中凸体几何关系的必然推论，从而揭示量子不确定性（quantum indeterminacy）本质上是相空间的辛协变（symplectic covariance）结构性质，而非统计现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子不确定性原理通常依赖于方差、协方差等统计描述符，缺乏内在的几何与拓扑基础。本文旨在建立一种不借助统计量、而是基于相空间凸体几何与辛拓扑方法的不确定性形式体系，从而为不确定性原理提供更为统一和概念清晰的基础。

Method: 采用相空间中的凸几何（convex geometry）与辛拓扑（symplectic topology）方法，将经验位置和动量数据关联为凸体（convex bodies），利用h-极对偶（h-polar duality）和辛容量（symplectic capacities）作为核心工具，提供内蕴的、坐标无关的相空间可容许构型界限。

Result: 在该几何框架下，罗伯逊-薛定谔不等式（Robertson-Schrödinger inequalities）自然地作为更深层的几何与拓扑原理的体现而出现，而非来自统计推导。

Conclusion: 量子不确定性本质上不是统计现象，而是在辛协变性（symplectic covariance）支配下相空间的结构性质。该几何形式体系为不确定性原理提供了统一且概念透明的基础。

Abstract: We introduce a geometric formulation of quantum indeterminacy from which the standard uncertainty inequalities emerge as necessary consequences. Our approach is based on convex geometry in phase space and on methods from symplectic topology, and does not rely on statistical descriptors such as variances or covariances. Instead, we associate to empirical position and momentum data with convex bodies whose mutual relations encode the fundamental constraints of quantum mechanics. The central tools are h-polar duality and symplectic capacities, which provide intrinsic, coordinate-free bounds on admissible phase-space configurations. Within this framework, the Robertson-Schrodinger inequalities arise naturally as manifestations of deeper geometric and topological principles. This perspective suggests that quantum indeterminacy is not primarily a statistical phenomenon, but rather a structural property of phase space governed by symplectic covariance. The results thus provide a unified and conceptually transparent foundation for the uncertainty principle.

</details>


### [21] [Quantum jump trajectories, hybrid systems, non-Hermitian evolutions, quantum/classical walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01411)
*Alberto Barchielli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文以一般性方式构建了跳跃型量子随机主方程（quantum stochastic master equations of jump type），引入“典型轨迹”（typical trajectory）和“独占概率密度”（exclusive probability densities）概念，实现了对非线性随机主方程解的递归构造及跳跃相关概率的完整描述，并通过与量子/经典混合系统（quantum/classical hybrid systems）和量子滤波理论（quantum filtering theory）的联系，统一并推广了非厄米哈密顿量演化、随机时间量子信道、量子更新过程等多个领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 摘要未明确说明研究动机，但整体目标是为跳跃型量子随机主方程建立一般性框架，并藉此统一和推广若干看似不同的量子动力学领域。

Method: 论文采用一般性公式化方法（general formulation），引入“典型轨迹”概念以递归构造非线性随机主方程的解（即条件态，conditional state），同时引入“独占概率密度”概念描述跳跃的等待时间及其概率分布，并讨论该框架与量子/经典混合系统及量子滤波理论的联系。

Result: 通过所提出的一般性框架和混合系统（hybrid system）思想，成功统一并推广了非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonians）下的演化、随机时间量子信道（unitary dynamics interspersed by quantum channels at random times）插入的幺正动力学、量子更新过程（quantum renewal processes）、连续时间开放量子游走（continuous time open quantum walks）以及林德布拉德速率方程（Lindblad rate equation）等多个领域。

Conclusion: 该一般性公式化为跳跃型量子随机主方程提供了统一的数学结构，并通过典型轨迹和独占概率密度等新概念，为描述条件态和跳跃统计提供了系统性工具，具有广泛的跨领域推广能力。

Abstract: Quantum stochastic master equations of jump type are formulated in a general way and connections with quantum/classical hybrid systems and quantum filtering theory are discussed. By introducing the notion of ``typical trajectory", we show how to recursively construct the solution of the non-linear stochastic master equation (the conditional state). Moreover, by the notion of ``exclusive probability densities" we can describe all the probabilities related to the jumps, in particular, the waiting times of the jumps and their probability distributions. This general formulation and the idea of hybrid system allow to unify and generalize different fields: evolutions under non-Hermitian Hamiltonians, unitary dynamics interspersed by quantum channels at random times, quantum renewal processes, continuous time open quantum walks, Lindblad rate equation, ...

### [22] [Separability from Multipartite Measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02097)
*Chen-Te Ma,Ma-Ke Yuan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了三阶负性（third-order negativity）是三体纯态（tripartite pure states）完全可分性的充要判据，并将其推广至混合态以及多体qudit系统，同时讨论了在共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的可分性判据（如负性，negativity）主要局限于二体诊断，缺乏针对三体及更高体纯态与混合态完全可分性的系统判据。

Method: 从三阶负性出发，将其构建为三体纯态完全可分性的充要判据；通过四量子比特（four-qubit）纯态的实例，展示其约化密度矩阵的完整刻画需要六个体二体、八个体三体和四个四体测度，并推广至多体qudit系统。

Result: 三阶负性可作为三体纯态完全可分性的充要条件；四量子比特纯态的完整表征需要多种多体可分性测度，且三阶负性在其中扮演关键判据角色。

Conclusion: 该工作为多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）的可分性提供了统一框架，并指出其可应用于共形场论等物理系统。

Abstract: We show that the third-order negativity provides a necessary and sufficient criterion for full separability of tripartite pure states, and extend this to mixed states beyond bipartite diagnostics such as negativity. As a minimal nontrivial example, a four-qubit pure state has three-qubit mixed reductions; its complete characterization requires six bipartite, eight tripartite, and four quadripartite measures, with the third-order negativity serving as a key separability criterion. We further generalize these separability criteria to multipartite qudit systems and discuss an application to conformal field theory.

</details>


### [23] [Permutation Routing on Ramanujan Hypergraphs with Applications to Neutral Atom Quantum Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02498)
*Joshua M. Courtney*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从超图变换（hypergraph transformation）的角度研究了可重构晶格上中性原子的路由问题，证明了Ramanujan (d,r)-正则超图的路由数为Θ(log N)，并建立了包括SFM覆盖、虚拟覆盖定理、Abelian Alon–Boppana屏障、纠缠辅助路由、贪心自适应路由及分层多尺度路由在内的一系列理论结果与协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对可重构晶格上中性原子路由的效率与可扩展性问题，本文通过超图形式化（hypergraph formalization）替代传统谱图假设，以更弱的一侧条件分析路由深度（routing depth），并探索多种路由协议的深度-容量权衡。

Method: 采用超图变换框架，通过团扩张图（clique expansion graph）中的匹配（matching）实现路由；引入SFM覆盖（Song–Fan–Miao covering）分析均匀性缩放；提出虚拟覆盖定理（virtual overlay theorem）刻画3D声光透镜架构的容量-深度权衡；利用阿贝尔群上的Alon–Boppana下限（Abelian Alon–Boppana barrier）分析Cayley图的拉马努金性（Ramanujan property）及仿射去随机化（affine derandomization）；构建k重拉马努金覆盖塔实现递归路由提升（recursive routing lift）；引入纠缠辅助路由（entanglement-assisted routing）与预分发贝尔对（pre-distributed Bell pairs）；采用位移能量分析（displacement energy analysis）研究贪心自适应路由与混合贪心-Valiant协议；以及分层多尺度路由（hierarchical multi-scale routing）的边界仅传输（boundary-only transfers）策略。

Result: Ramanujan (d,r)-正则超图的路由数为Θ(log N)；SFM覆盖对任意均匀性的Ramanujan族均成立；3D AOL架构中多层堆叠（multi-layer stacking）在L=O(log N)个独立覆盖层下实现Θ(log N)路由；固定度Cayley图在Z_n²上不能是Ramanujan的，仿射去随机化实现15–30%拥塞减少；k重拉马努金覆盖塔递归路由提升实现O(log N)路由；纠缠辅助路由在约4轮路由时出现稳定交叉，实现O(log N)的隐形传态深度（teleportation depth）；混合贪心-Valiant协议在实际规模下实现约3倍加速；分层多尺度路由在k=O(√N log N)容量下实现O(log² N / log b)深度，最优块大小b=Θ(√n)时实现O(log N)深度。

Conclusion: 超图框架为可重构晶格上的中性原子路由提供了统一的理论基础，多种协议在深度和容量之间实现了不同程度的权衡，验证了O(log N)和O(log² N)深度路由的可行性。

Abstract: We consider the routing of neutral atoms on a reconfigurable lattice in terms of hypergraph transformations. We prove the routing number of a Ramanujan $(d,r)$-regular hypergraph on $N$ vertices satisfies $\mathrm{rt}(H) = Θ(\log N)$, where routing is via matchings in the clique expansion graph $G_{\mathrm{cl}}(H)$. Hypergraphs reframe the qubit routing problem by replacing Nenadov's two-sided spectral gap hypothesis with a one-sided condition based on eigenvalue centering. Song--Fan--Miao (SFM) coverings scale for Ramanujan families of every uniformity. A virtual overlay theorem establishes a capacity--depth tradeoff for 3D acousto-optic lens (AOL) architectures, with multi-layer stacking achieving $Θ(\log N)$ routing with $L = O(\log N)$ independent overlay layers. An abelian Alon--Boppana barrier shows that fixed-degree Cayley graphs on $\mathbb{Z}_n^2$ cannot be Ramanujan and affine derandomization on such graphs achieves 15--30% congestion reduction. Towers of $k$-fold Ramanujan coverings yield $\mathrm(H_L) = O(\log N)$ by recursive routing lift. Entanglement-assisted routing by pre-distributed Bell pairs achieves $O(\log N)$ teleportation depth with a stable crossover at $\sim\!4$ routing rounds. Displacement energy analyzes greedy adaptive routing, identifying stalling and a hybrid greedy--Valiant protocol achieving $\sim\!3\times$ speedup at practical scales. Hierarchical multi-scale routing achieves $O(\log^2 N / \log b)$ depth with boundary-only transfers at capacity $k = O(\sqrt{N} \log N)$, and $O(\log N)$ depth with optimal block size $b = Θ(\sqrt{n})$.

</details>


### [24] [Which Coherence Decoheres? Basis-Dependent Decoherence Rates in Symmetry-Broken Collective Spin Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00952)
*Stavros Mouslopoulos*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现，在 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 对称集体自旋系统的有序相中，局域化指针态与能量本征态对应两种不同的林德布拉德退相率（Lindblad dephasing rates），两者相差可达约 2.42 倍，其代数根源在于宇称（parity）约束使能量本征态的对角元 $\langle E_i|\hat{J}_z|E_i\rangle$ 严格为零，从而消除了指针态中存在的交叉项。研究给出了两种保护因子，并在利普金-梅什科夫-格利克（Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick, LMG）模型中通过精确对角化验证了三个标度区域的演化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 对称集体自旋系统中，量子退相（quantum dephasing）的速率可能依赖于所选取的基矢，但该差异的代数根源与物理机制尚不明确。本文旨在揭示局域化指针态与能量本征态下退相速率差异的起源，并量化其保护效应。

Method: 采用林德布拉德主方程（Lindblad master equation）框架，定义局域化指针态 $\{|P\rangle,|R\rangle\}$ 与能量本征态 $\{|E_0\rangle,|E_1\rangle\}$ 下的退相速率。利用 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 宇称对称性分析林德布拉德跳跃算符（Lindblad jump operator）的矩阵元结构，导出代数约束条件。在利普金-梅什科夫-格利克（LMG）模型中通过精确对角化（exact diagonalisation）进行数值验证。

Result: 局域化指针态与能量本征态的退相速率在热力学极限（$N\to\infty$）下收敛，在量子临界交叉区附近差异可达 2.42 倍。识别出两种保护因子：经典平均场估计的保护因子 $η_{\rm MF}=(Nm_*)^2/(2G_{01})\approx2.42$ 和精确物理比 $η_{\rm exact}=(G_{01}+J_{01}^2)/G_{01}\approx1.86$。在热力学极限下，世俗近似（secular approximation）失效，二重态简并，两种速率趋于一致。

Conclusion: 退相速率差异的唯一代数根源是 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 宇称迫使能量本征态中 $\hat{J}_z$ 的对角元为零，从而消除了局域化指针态中存在的交叉项。该发现揭示了基矢选择对量子退相动力学的重要影响，并给出了定量化的保护因子。

Abstract: In the ordered phase of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric collective spin system, two natural bases -- localised pointer states $\{|P\rangle,|R\rangle\}$ and energy eigenstates $\{|E_0\rangle,|E_1\rangle\}$ -- yield Lindblad dephasing rates that differ by a factor approaching $2$ as $N\to\infty$ and reaching $2.42$ near the quantum-critical crossover. The discrepancy has a single algebraic origin: parity forces $\langle E_i|\hat{J}_z|E_i\rangle=0$ exactly, eliminating the cross-term that doubles the localised-state rate. Two distinct protection factors are identified: $η_{\rm MF}=(Nm_*)^2/(2G_{01})\approx2.42$, where $m_*$ is the order parameter and $G_{01}=\frac{1}{2}(\langle E_0|\hat{J}_z^2|E_0\rangle+\langle E_1|\hat{J}_z^2|E_1\rangle)$ (advantage over the classical mean-field estimate), and $η_{\rm exact}=(G_{01}+J_{01}^2)/G_{01}\approx1.86$, where $J_{01}=\langle E_0|\hat{J}_z|E_1\rangle$ (exact physical ratio of pointer-state to eigenstate decay rate). In the thermodynamic limit the secular approximation fails, the doublet degenerates, and both rates converge. The three-regime structure is demonstrated in the Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick model via exact diagonalisation, and the algebraic origin of the discrepancy is established via the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ parity of the Lindblad jump operator.

</details>


### [25] [Comment on `On computing quantum waves exactly from classical action'](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02621)
*Gabor Vattay*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出 Lohmiller & Slotine 声称可以仅用经典最小作用量和经典流体密度精确求解薛定谔方程的推导存在根本性错误——他们忽略了概率密度振幅的空间导数，从而无意中省略了量子势（quantum potential），因此其提出的等价性并非精确解，而是标准的半经典近似（semiclassical approximation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠正 Lohmiller & Slotine 最近发表论文中的数学错误，该论文声称薛定谔方程可以仅通过经典最小作用量（classical least action）和经典流体密度（classical fluid density）精确求解，无需半经典近似。

Method: 通过检查原始推导中概率密度振幅（probability density amplitude）的空间导数项，揭示量子势被无意省略的错误；随后逐一分析论文中的示例以验证该错误的普遍性。

Result: 推导中的错误在于忽略了量子势——这一项最初由 Madelung 识别，后由 Bohm 强调。论文中的每个示例要么属于量子势因问题几何而恒为零的类别，要么通过初始条件导入量子本征函数（eigenfunctions）来恢复正确的量子结果，从而掩盖了根本性错误。

Conclusion: Lohmiller & Slotine 提出的方案并非对薛定谔方程的精确求解，而只是恢复了标准的半经典近似；其数学推导存在根本性缺陷，示例未能揭示这一错误。

Abstract: A recent article by Lohmiller \& Slotine (Proc.\ R.\ Soc.\ A \textbf{482}: 20250413) claims that the Schrödinger equation can be solved exactly using only classical least action and classical fluid density, asserting that this formulation avoids semiclassical approximations. We show that their mathematical derivation contains a foundational error. By neglecting the spatial derivatives of the probability density amplitude, the authors inadvertently omit the quantum potential -- the term originally identified by Madelung and later emphasised by Bohm. Consequently, their proposed equivalence is not exact but rather constitutes the standard semiclassical approximation. We further demonstrate that each of the paper's illustrative examples either belongs to a class where the quantum potential vanishes identically due to the geometry of the problem, or recovers the correct quantum result by importing quantum eigenfunctions through the initial conditions, thereby concealing the error.

### [26] [Universality of Quantum Gates in Particle and Symmetry Constrained Subspaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00979)
*Andreas Stergiou,Nicolas PD Sawaya*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用李代数（Lie algebra）技巧证明，在近期的量子计算机上，硬件高效门（hardware-efficient gates）能够在约束子空间（如固定粒子数或自旋的子空间）中实现态制备的普适性。关键机制是泡利Z修饰（Pauli Z dressing），通过交换子产生共享量子比特上的泡利Z算符，将多平面旋转分解为单平面生成元，张成整个𝔰𝔬(w) 或 𝔰𝔲(w) 代数，从而实现任意实态或复态制备。论文还提供了高效雅可比判据（Jacobian criterion），并应用于Fermi-Hubbard模型、Bose-Hubbard模型、分子电子结构及三维伊辛共形场论（CFT）的模糊球体正则化等物理场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模拟近期的量子计算机上的物理系统，通常需要在受约束的子空间（如固定粒子数或固定自旋的子空间）中制备量子态。然而，验证硬件高效门（hardware-efficient gates）能够普适地制备这些约束子空间中的任意态，仍然是一个关键的理论空白。

Method: 采用李代数（Lie algebra）方法进行分析，核心机制是泡利Z修饰（Pauli Z dressing）：重叠门之间的交换子（commutator）会在共享量子比特上产生泡利Z算符，作为旁观投影子（spectator projector）将多平面旋转（multi-plane rotations）分解为单平面生成元（single-plane generators），从而张成整个𝔰𝔬(w) 代数，实现实态制备普适性；进一步引入独立复相位（independent complex phases）可扩展至𝔰𝔲(w) 代数，实现任意复态制备。还提出了一个计算高效的雅可比判据（Jacobian criterion），用于验证电路能否从几乎任意参数配置出发沿目标流形（manifold）的所有方向探索。

Result: 证明了硬件高效门在约束子空间内态制备的普适性，并提供了雅可比判据（Jacobian criterion）作为实用性验证工具。具体应用包括：证明了二进制编码多能级粒子（binary encoded multi-level particles）拟设在粒子数守恒子空间中的完备性；为三维伊辛共形场论（CFT）的模糊球体正则化构建了对称性保持电路（symmetry-preserving circuits），并变分制备了基态和激发态，提取了CFT标度维度（scaling dimensions）。

Conclusion: 该李代数框架从理论上统一了硬件高效门在约束子空间态制备中的普适性，适用范围涵盖Fermi-Hubbard模型、Bose-Hubbard模型、分子电子结构及共形场论（CFT）模拟等多种物理问题领域，为近期量子计算机上的约束子空间模拟提供了理论保障和实用判据。

Abstract: Simulating physical systems on near-term quantum computers often requires preparing states within constrained subspaces, like those with fixed particle number or spin. We use Lie algebraic techniques to prove that hardware-efficient gates are universal for state preparation in these subspaces. The key mechanism is Pauli $Z$ dressing: commutators of overlapping gates produce Pauli $Z$ operators on shared qubits, acting as spectator projectors that decompose multi-plane rotations into single-plane generators spanning the full $\mathfrak{so}(w)$ algebra, where $w$ is the dimension of the constrained subspace, thereby guaranteeing universality for real state preparation. Adding independent complex phases extends this to $\mathfrak{su}(w)$, enabling arbitrary complex state preparation. We provide a computationally efficient Jacobian criterion for verifying that a circuit can explore any direction on the target manifold from almost any parameter configuration. Our findings are applicable to many problem areas, including Fermi-Hubbard models, Bose-Hubbard models, and molecular electronic structure. We apply our framework to two physical settings: we prove the completeness of the binary encoded multi-level particles ansatz on the conserved-particle-number subspace, and we construct symmetry-preserving circuits for the fuzzy sphere regularisation of the 3D Ising conformal field theory (CFT). For the latter, we variationally prepare the ground and excited states to extract CFT scaling dimensions.

### [27] [Phase-space measurements and decoherence for angular momentum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02696)
*Dorje C. Brody,Eva-Maria Graefe,Rishindra Melanathuru*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子角动量（angular momentum）系统在环境中退相干（decoherence）的两种建模方式：基于Lindblad方程的连续动力学模型与基于SU(2)相干态（coherent states）的迭代测量模型，发现两者虽在平坦相空间中等价，但在球面相空间（phase-space）上存在本质差异——超算符（super-operator）对易但本征值不同，且经典性的两种判据（密度矩阵衰减率与准概率分布的正定性）在此系统中不等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子角动量系统在无偏好取向的环境监测下，两种不同退相干模型（连续Lindblad动力学与迭代测量）的等价性与差异性，并澄清球面相空间中经典性（classicality）表征的不一致性。

Method: 第一种模型采用三个独立角动量算符生成的Lindblad方程描述连续动力学；第二种模型利用SU(2)相干态构造的正算子值测度（positive operator-valued measure, POVM）在球面上进行迭代“相空间”点测量。通过比较两种模型对应的超算符（super-operator）的代数结构（对易性）与本征值谱，以及分析密度矩阵元衰减速率与准概率分布正定性两种经典性判据。

Result: 两种模型的超算符互相对易，但本征值不同，表明动力学行为不等价；在角动量系统中，基于密度矩阵元衰减速率的退相干经典性判据与基于准概率分布正定性的经典性判据不等价。

Conclusion: 对于角动量系统，平坦相空间中两种退相干模型的等价性在球面相空间中不再成立；经典性的不同判据在此类系统中也不等价，揭示了角动量系统退相干理论的独特结构。

Abstract: The monitoring of the three independent components of the angular momentum (or spin) of a quantum system by its environment that does not isolate any preferred orientation is modelled in two different ways. One describes the dynamics by the Lindblad equation generated by three independent angular momentum operators. The other uses iterated measurements of the ``phase-space'' point on the sphere in terms of the positive operator-valued measure generated by SU(2) coherent states. In contrast to the equivalent scenario on a flat phase space, these two models give rise to subtle differences. Specifically, it is shown that the two super-operators corresponding to the two decoherence models for angular momentum systems are commutative, but their eigenvalues are different. Hence although both models give rise to phase-space decoherence, their dynamical behaviours are not equivalent. In either model, we find that the characterisation of classicality as represented by the decay rates of the elements of the density matrix (i.e. decoherence) and that as represented by the positivity of the quasiprobability distribution are not equivalent for angular momentum systems.

Abstract: We consider the one-dimensional Dirac equation with the most general relativistic contact interaction supported on two points symmetrically located with respect to the origin. ### [29] [Note on Strong Quantum Markov Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02877)
*Chi-Fang Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本笔记刻画了量子多体系统近似稳态的强马尔可夫性质（strong Markov property），证明其等价于特定可观测量对满足关联衰减（correlation decay），并推导了该性质在测量-恢复协议、态空间几何以及态混合唯一性方面的若干结构与操作后果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期工作将量子吉布斯态（Gibbs states）的局部马尔可夫性质（local Markov property）推广至主方程（master equation）近似稳态（metastable states），并提出了更强的后选择恢复性质。本文旨在精确刻画这一“强马尔可夫性质”成立的条件，并揭示其操作与结构上的推论。

Method: 基于条件互信息（conditional mutual information）和准局部恢复映射（quasi-local recovery map）的框架，通过等价性证明建立强马尔可夫性质与关联衰减之间的联系，并进一步利用主方程背景分析其操作后果。

Result: 强马尔可夫性质成立当且仅当状态满足特定可观测量对的关联衰减。该性质在操作上允许仅用单份拷贝（single copy）通过重复测量-恢复协议估计多个可观测量；在结构上，任意两个强马尔可夫态的局部边缘（local marginals）要么非常接近、要么充分分离；若一个强马尔可夫态可表示为两个强马尔可夫态的混合，则二者的局部边缘几乎不可区分。

Conclusion: 强马尔可夫性质系统性地刻画了满足局部恢复与关联衰减的量子稳态，为单次实验多观测量的估计、稳态空间几何以及混合—唯一性关系提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Quantum many-body Gibbs states satisfy an approximate local Markov property~\cite{chen2025GibbsMarkov}: local noise can be approximately recovered by a quasi-local recovery map, and the conditional mutual information decays for the corresponding tripartition. Recent work~\cite{bergamaschi2025structural} extends this property to approximate stationary states (metastable states) of certain master equations modeling system--bath dynamics, and proposes a strengthened post-selected recovery property requiring recovery to hold for each measurement outcome. In this note, we characterize this \textit{strong Markov property}: it holds if and only if the state additionally satisfies correlation decay for suitable pairs of observables.
  We further prove several structural and operational consequences of the strong Markov property in the presence of an underlying master equation. First, one can estimate multiple observables from a \textit{single copy} of the state via a repeated measurement--recovery protocol. Second, any two strongly Markov states must have local marginals that are either very close or well separated. Third, if a strongly Markov state can be expressed as a mixture of two strongly Markov states, then their local marginals must be nearly indistinguishable.

### [30] [Expectation Pauli-Lubanski vector and intrinsic angular momentum of relativistic wavepackets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01932)
*Konstantin Y. Bliokh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个统一形式论，结合非相对论角动量分解与相对论量子力学自旋描述，基于“期望Pauli-Lubanski向量”定义相对论波包的内禀角动量（包括自旋与轨道贡献），避免了零质量奇异性，允许质量为零的粒子也具有任意取向的内禀角动量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非相对论力学中总轨道角动量可分解为内禀（intrinsic）与外在（extrinsic）部分，而相对论量子力学中内禀角动量通常与自旋（spin）关联并通过Pauli-Lubanski四维向量描述。两类框架尚未统一，现有Pauli-Lubanski形式论在零质量情形下存在奇异性，无法完整描述波包的内禀角动量。

Method: 提出“期望Pauli-Lubanski向量”（expectation Pauli-Lubanski vector），基于波包动量与角动量的期望值构造，等价于相对于波包能量质心（energy centroid）定义的内禀角动量。

Result: 期望Pauli-Lubanski向量避免了传统Pauli-Lubanski形式论中的零质量奇异性（zero-mass singularity）；因此，即使对于质量为零的粒子，波包的内禀角动量也可具有相对于其动量的任意取向（arbitrary orientation）。

Conclusion: 该统一形式论通过多个携带自旋与轨道角动量的相对论波束（wave beams）及波包实例得到验证，为描述相对论波包的内禀角动量提供了更普适的框架。

Abstract: In non-relativistic mechanics, the total (orbital) angular momentum (AM) of a spatially-distributed system can be decomposed into intrinsic and extrinsic contributions. In relativistic quantum mechanics, intrinsic AM is typically associated with spin, which can be described using the Pauli-Lubanski four-vector. Here, we develop a unified formalism that combines the main features of both approaches and describes the intrinsic AM of a relativistic wavepacket, including both spin and orbital contributions. Our approach is based on the "expectation Pauli-Lubanski vector" constructed from the expectation values of the wavepacket's momentum and AM. Equivalently, it defines the intrinsic AM relative to the wavepacket's energy centroid. In contrast to the conventional Pauli-Lubanski formalism, the zero-mass singularity does not occur for the expectation Pauli-Lubanski vector. Consequently, the intrinsic AM of a wavepacket may have an arbitrary orientation with respect to its momentum, even for massless particles. We illustrate the general theory with a number of examples of relativistic wave beams and packets carrying spin and orbital AM.

Method: 将集体分子间电子关联映射到可解析求解的球形Sherrington-Kirkpatrick（SK）模型，从而对腔耦合分子系综中的多体问题建立可控的理论描述。

Abstract: Collective strong coupling of molecular ensembles to optical cavities opens a route to modifying matter through genuinely collective electronic correlations. Yet even in the absence of a cavity, Coulomb correlations are notoriously difficult to describe, and cavity coupling adds transverse correlation channels extending over the entire molecular ensemble. Here we show that this seemingly intractable problem admits a controlled description by mapping the collective intermolecular electronic correlations to the analytically solvable spherical Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model. The resulting theory predicts two collective correlation phases, a paracorrelated phase and a spin-glass correlation phase, beyond the conventional uncorrelated molecular regime. These phases reveal an entropy-driven localization-delocalization mechanism that transfers molecular electronic states into collectively correlated cavity-dressed states. Our work establishes cavity-mediated electron correlations as a microscopic mechanism for emergent phases in strongly coupled molecular ensembles.

### [32] [Quantum-enhanced sensing from the interplay of long-range interactions and non-Hermiticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01912)
*Keshav Das Agarwal,Tanoy Kanti Konar,Leela Ganesh Chandra Lakkaraju,Aditi Sen De*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究长程（long-range）量子自旋系统中的参数估计问题，发现长程相互作用与非厄米效应（non-Hermitian effects）的协同作用能够增强动力学量子Fisher信息（QFI）在时间和系统尺寸上的标度行为，但在临界磁场下，当探针处于最低能量本征态时，厄米与非厄米模型的QFI标度相同，存在一个否证性结果（no-go result）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程（long-range）量子自旋系统在量子信息处理和传感方面具有潜在优势，论文旨在探究长程相互作用与非厄米效应（non-Hermitian effects）对量子参数估计精度的协同影响。

Method: 研究基于一个与储层耦合的长程XX自旋模型，该模型可导出有效长程RT对称（RT-symmetric）非厄米iXY哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）。相互作用具有可调协调范围且随距离代数衰减，支持长程与短程（short-range）直接对比。系统初始化为全极化态，通过分析动力学量子Fisher信息（QFI）评估横向磁场和各向异性参数的估计性能。

Result: 在适当调节系统参数时，长程（LR）区域中QFI的时间和系统尺寸标度均优于短程（SR）区域；非厄米长程模型的动力学QFI可超越对应的厄米模型，展现出长程相互作用与非厄米效应协同诱导的度量学优势（metrological advantage）；然而，在临界磁场处，当探针制备于最低能量本征态时，厄米与非厄米模型的QFI标度一致，构成一个否证性结果（no-go result）。

Conclusion: 长程相互作用与非厄米效应的结合可显著提升量子参数估计的性能，但这一优势在临界磁场和特定初态条件下受到限制，揭示了长程非厄米量子度量学（quantum metrology）中优势存在的边界条件。

Abstract: Long-range (LR) quantum spin systems offer promising advantages for quantum information processing and sensing. Here, we investigate parameter estimation in an long-range XX spin model coupled to a reservoir, which gives rise to an effective long-range RT-symmetric non-Hermitian iXY Hamiltonian. The interactions extend up to a tunable coordination range and decay algebraically with distance, enabling a direct comparison between long-range and short-range (SR) regimes. Focusing on the estimation of the transverse magnetic field and anisotropy parameter, we initialize the system in a fully polarized state and analyze the resulting dynamical quantum Fisher information (QFI). We show that, with suitable tuning of the system parameters, both the time and system-size scaling of the QFI are enhanced in the LR regime relative to their SR counterparts. Moreover, the non-Hermitian LR model can exhibit superior dynamical QFI compared with the corresponding Hermitian model, demonstrating a genuine metrological advantage induced by the interplay of long-range interactions and non-Hermitian effects. In contrast, we establish a no-go result at the critical magnetic field: when the probe is prepared in the lowest-energy eigenstate, the QFI scaling remains identical for the Hermitian and non-Hermitian cases.

</details>


### [33] [Accelerating Noisy Variational Quantum Algorithms with Physics-Informed Denoising Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02066)
*Jie Liu,Xin Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出物理信息去噪网络（Physics-Informed Denoising Network, PIDN），学习零噪声外推（ZNE）的优化动力学替代模型，在保持ZNE性能的同时将电路执行次数减少约4–6倍，实现可扩展、资源高效的噪声鲁棒变分量子优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分量子算法（variational quantum algorithms）在近期量子计算中前景广阔，但严重受制于硬件噪声以及零噪声外推（Zero-Noise Extrapolation, ZNE）等误差缓解方法所需的大量电路开销，亟需一种能降低电路执行成本的替代方案。

Method: 将变分更新视为参数空间中的轨迹，训练PIDN学习ZNE缓解后的期望值（expectation values）与梯度方向（gradient directions），通过物理信息损失函数（physics-informed loss）保持梯度下降动力学（gradient descent dynamics）。训练后，PIDN直接从当前噪声观测值与历史轨迹中估计去噪期望和梯度，替代重复的多噪声级别电路评估。

Result: 在3-正则图、Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型、横场Ising模型上的量子近似优化算法（QAOA），以及LiH、BeH2、H2O的变分量子本征求解器（VQE）任务中，PIDN达到与ZNE相当的性能，电路执行次数减少约4–6倍；梯度余弦相似度（cosine similarity）保持在0.95以上；仅在ZNE本身不可靠时PIDN才失效；消融实验证实物理信息损失对维持方向一致性的必要性；有效损失景观保持强低频结构时PIDN跟踪优化动力学最为准确。

Conclusion: PIDN为含噪中等规模量子（noisy intermediate-scale quantum, NISQ）体制下的变分优化提供了一种可扩展、资源高效的策略，在显著降低电路执行开销的同时有效保持了噪声鲁棒性。

Abstract: Variational quantum algorithms are promising for near-term quantum computing, but are severely limited by hardware noise and the substantial circuit overhead required for error mitigation methods such as Zero-Noise Extrapolation (ZNE). We propose a Physics-Informed Denoising Network (PIDN) that reduces the cost of ZNE by learning a surrogate model of its optimization dynamics. By viewing the variational update as a trajectory in the parameter space, PIDN is trained to reproduce ZNE-mitigated expectation values and gradient directions while incorporating a physics-informed loss that preserves the gradient descent dynamics. Once trained, PIDN replaces repeated multi-noise evaluations with denoised expectation and gradient estimation directly from the current noisy observation and the historical trajectory, significantly reducing circuit executions. We benchmark the approach on the quantum approximate optimization algorithm for 3-regular graphs, Sherrington-Kirkpatrick, and transverse-field Ising models, as well as the variational quantum eigensolver for LiH, BeH$_2$ and H$_2$O. Across all tasks, PIDN attains performance comparable to ZNE, while reducing the number of circuit executions by a factor of approximately 4 to 6. Gradient cosine similarity with ZNE remains above 0.95 throughout training. Robustness analysis shows that PIDN fails only when ZNE itself becomes unreliable, and ablation studies confirm the necessity of the physics-informed loss for maintaining directional consistency. We further find that PIDN tracks optimization dynamics most accurately when the effective loss landscape retains strong low-frequency structure. These results establish PIDN as a scalable, resource-efficient strategy for noise-resilient variational optimization in the noisy intermediate-scale quantum regime.

### [34] [Thermodynamic completeness in quantum and classical Markovian dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02650)
*Yang Tian*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种路径空间作用量（path-space action）形式体系，用于研究量子与经典马尔可夫热力学（Markovian thermodynamics）中的一个重构问题（reconstruction problem）：哪些热力学可观测量可以从状态轨迹（state trajectory）中推断，哪些需要额外的电流（current）或测量记录（measurement record）。主要结果是一个热力学完备性检验（thermodynamic completeness test），揭示状态生成器无法唯一确定热力学电流统计量，其根源在于电流空间的几何与拓扑结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典与量子马尔可夫热力学中存在一个基本的不完备性问题：仅凭状态轨迹（state trajectory）的观测是否足以推断所有热力学可观测量？摘要试图明确区分哪些可观测量依赖于状态轨迹，哪些必须依赖于额外的电流（current）或测量记录（measurement record），从而解决这一重构问题（reconstruction problem）。

Method: 论文发展了一个路径空间作用量（path-space action）形式体系，将状态轨迹与热力学记录（thermodynamic record）视为马尔可夫路径（Markovian path）的不同组成部分。在量子系统中，记录由量子仪器（quantum instrument）定义；在经典表示中，记录由连续性方程（continuity equation）约束的密度流（density current）定义。基于此，作者提出了热力学完备性检验（thermodynamic completeness test），识别那些不改变状态轨迹的电流或测量记录扰动。

Result: 热力学完备性检验表明，任何被不改变状态轨迹的扰动所改变的可观测量，无法仅从状态数据重建。因此，两个马尔可夫模型可以具有相同的状态生成器（state generator）、稳态（stationary state）、线性响应（linear response）和局部状态几何（local state geometry），但热力学电流均值（current means）或电流噪声（current noise）不同。对于量子马尔可夫动力学，无条件的密度矩阵生成器（density-matrix generator）不能确定热流、粒子转移、光子计数、自旋转移或连续测量统计量，必须同时指定量子仪器和每个记录结果对应的热力学增量（thermodynamic increment）。对于经典密度-电流动力学，同一检验识别出投影到状态轨迹时被消除的隐藏交换、反应、输运和动力学电流记录。

Conclusion: 这种不完备性具有几何与拓扑起源：电流空间的海森矩阵（Hessian）投影到一个商状态几何（quotient state geometry），而图环（graph cycles）、无散电流（divergence-free currents）和谐波电流（harmonic currents）张成状态观测不可见的方向。该工作系统揭示了马尔可夫热力学中状态信息与电流信息之间的根本性信息鸿沟。

Abstract: We develop a path-space action formulation for quantum and classical Markovian thermodynamics that addresses a reconstruction problem: which thermodynamic observables can be inferred from state trajectories alone, and which require additional current or measurement record? The formulation treats the state trajectory and the thermodynamic record as distinct components of a Markovian path. In quantum systems, the record is specified by a quantum instrument; in the commutative classical representation, it is a density current constrained by a continuity equation. The main result is a thermodynamic completeness test. It identifies current or measurement-record perturbations that do not change the state trajectory and shows that any observable changed by such a perturbation cannot be reconstructed from state data alone. Hence two Markovian models can have the same state generator, stationary state, linear response, and local state geometry, but different thermodynamic current means or current noise. For quantum Markovian dynamics, an unconditioned density-matrix generator therefore does not determine heat-current, particle-transfer, photon-counting, spin-transfer, or continuous-measurement statistics; the quantum instrument and the thermodynamic increment assigned to each record outcome must also be specified. For classical density-current dynamics, the same test identifies hidden exchange, reaction, transport, and kinetic current records that are eliminated by the projection to the state trajectory. We further show that this incompleteness has geometric and topological origins: the current-space Hessian projects to a quotient state geometry, while graph cycles, divergence-free currents, and harmonic currents span directions invisible to state observations.

</details>

*J. Lisenfeld,A. K. Händel,A. Bilmes,A. V. Ustinov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文研究了超导transmon量子比特隧道势垒中一个强耦合的两能级系统（two-level system, TLS），发现该TLS与量子比特的读取谐振器之间存在强的有效共振耦合，导致谐振器态发生修饰（dressed）并产生共振频移，从而破坏读取信号，揭示了材料缺陷干扰固态量子处理器运行的新途径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用多光子光谱学（multi-photon spectroscopy）和TLS应变调谐（TLS strain tuning）技术，研究由TLS、量子比特及其读取谐振器组成的三体相互作用系统（three-partite system）的丰富光谱。

Result: 发现TLS与量子比特的读取谐振器之间存在强的有效共振耦合（strong effective resonant coupling），该耦合修饰了谐振器态（dresses the resonator states），并导致共振频率偏移（resonance frequency shift），从而破坏读取（readout）信号。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了材料缺陷干扰量子比特运行的一种新方式，这进一步阻碍了固态量子处理器的实现。

Abstract: Material defects give rise to parasitic two-level systems (TLS) which present a major source of decoherence in superconducting qubits. Here, we study a strongly coupled TLS that resides in the tunnel barrier of transmon qubit. We use multi-photon spectroscopy and TLS strain tuning to explore the rich spectrum of the interacting three-partite system consisting of TLS, qubit, and its readout resonator. This reveals a strong effective resonant coupling between the TLS and the qubit's readout resonator which dresses the resonator states and results in a resonance frequency shift that spoils the readout signal. Our finding presents yet another way how material defects can interfere with qubit operation and hinder the realization of solid-state quantum processors.

In this paper we focus on a practical computation method that leverages our formalism of many-body combinatorics, in order to perform an efficient numerical computation of the many-body density of states. In addition, this method provides further computational improvements by allowing most of the results to be cached in persistent storage and computed incrementally, making way for efficient use of parallelization and dynamic programming techniques. This precision enhancement can be employed in gravitational acceleration measurements with a finite number of particles trapped in optical lattices.

### [38] [Convolution-to-sum identities for Mittag-Leffler type functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01079)
*William Cvetko,Elena Cherkaev*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文从三角函数的积化和差（product-to-sum）恒等式出发，为Mittag-Leffler型函数建立了卷积到和（convolution-to-sum）的恒等式。通过分数阶算子的拉普拉斯域分析，识别出一族Mittag-Leffler型函数（$R_{α,v}$和$P_{α,w}$），证明了同阶函数的卷积可化简为两个$P/R$函数的和，且在阶数由有理数关联时，卷积结果可表示为$n+m$项之和。这些结果被应用于受迫次扩散（forced subdiffusion）和分数阶衰减波动方程（Caputo-Wismer-Kelvin模型）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三角函数的积化和差恒等式在函数理论和众多应用中具有基础性作用。受此启发，本文旨在为Mittag-Leffler型分数阶函数建立类似的卷积到和恒等式，以揭示该类函数在分数阶微积分中的代数结构。

Method: 采用拉普拉斯域（Laplace domain）分析分数阶算子，识别出$R_{α,v}$和$P_{α,w}$两类密切相关的Mittag-Leffler型函数参数化形式。通过拉普拉斯域的部分分式分解（partial-fraction decomposition），推导同阶函数的卷积简化；并利用欧拉恒等式（Euler's identity）的推广形式处理阶数为有理数倍时的卷积情形。

Result: 两个同阶Mittag-Leffler型函数的卷积可化简为两个$P/R$函数的和；当阶数之比为有理数$\frac{α_1}{α_2} = \frac{n}{m}$时，卷积结果可表示为$n+m$项之和。$R$和$P$函数满足推广的欧拉恒等式。

Conclusion: 本文建立的卷积到和恒等式为Mittag-Leffler型函数提供了类似于三角函数积化和差的代数工具，并通过受迫次扩散和分数阶Kelvin-Voigt模型等应用展示了其有效性。

Abstract: Product-to-sum identities for trigonometric functions play a fundamental role in function theory and numerous applications. In this spirit, we present convolution-to-sum identities for Mittag-Leffler type functions. Using a Laplace domain analysis of fractional operators, we identify a family of Mittag-Leffler type functions that encapsulates the eigenfunctions of Riemann-Liouville and Caputo fractional derivatives. We work with two closely-related parameterizations of this class, $R_{α,v}$ and $P_{α,w}$. The convolution of two such functions can be expressed as a series of them. Moreover, if the functions share the same order $α$, the convolution can be reduced to a sum of two $P/R$ functions through a partial-fraction decomposition in the Laplace domain. Furthermore, $R$ and $P$ functions satisfy a generalization of Euler's identity, which expands the scope of the previous result to convolutions of $P/R$ functions whose orders $α_1,α_2$ are related by a rational factor. For $\frac{α_1}{α_2} = \frac{n}{m}$, the resulting sum has $n+m$ terms. The foundational results and methods developed here are illustrated by their application to forced subdiffusion and to a fractionally attenuated wave equation (the Caputo-Wismer-Kelvin, or the fractional Kelvin-Voigt model).

</details>


### [39] [On the onset of correlations in Wave Turbulence close to singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02540)
*M. Escobedo,J. J. L. Velázquez*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文形式化地描述了在波湍流（wave turbulence）运动学方程自相似爆破（self similar blow up）时刻附近，薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）的湍流波动方程推导如何失效。研究表明，爆破时刻附近运动学方程必须被一个等价于随机场（random field）的方程层级所替代，该随机场定义在全体时间上并满足非线性非自治薛定谔方程（nonlinear non autonomous Schrödinger equation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过研究累积量层级（cumulants hierarchy）在爆破时刻附近能否用波湍流运动学方程的解来近似，形式化地分析推导失效的数学机制。

Result: 发现爆破时刻附近，运动学方程必须被一个等价的随机场所取代，该随机场定义在 $t\in (-\infty, \infty)$ 上并满足非线性非自治薛定谔方程。

Conclusion: 波湍流运动学方程在自相似爆破时刻附近不再适用，需代之以一个更一般的随机场方程层级来描述系统行为。

To this end, we study how the derivation of the cumulants hierarchy can not be approximated using solutions of the wave turbulence kinetic equation near the blow up time. It tuns out that near the blow up time the kinetic equation has to be replaced by a hierarchy of equations which is equivalent to a random field, defined for times $t\in (-\infty, \infty)$ and satisfying a nonlinear non autonomous Schrödinger equation.

### [40] [Generic Irreducibility of Bloch Varieties for Periodic Graph Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01212)
*Matthew Faust,Wencai Liu*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 该研究给出了周期图算子（periodic graph operators）的色散多项式（dispersion polynomial）和布洛赫簇（Bloch variety）在一般不可约性（generic irreducibility）方面的完整刻画：对于非平凡周期图，当且仅当商图（quotient graph）连通时，其色散多项式/布洛赫簇在边权与势能的一般选取下是不可约的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用参数化洛朗多项式（parameterized Laurent polynomials）的强二分性（strong dichotomy）：可约性要么对所有参数成立，要么在非空扎里斯基开集（Zariski-open set）上不成立；在此基础上将问题约化到极小连通周期图（minimally connected periodic graphs）。

Result: 证明了对于非平凡周期图，边权与势能的一般选取下色散多项式/布洛赫簇不可约当且仅当商图连通。

Conclusion: 该结果完整刻画了周期图算子色散多项式与布洛赫簇的一般不可约性，将充要条件归结为商图的连通性这一简单拓扑性质。

Abstract: We give a complete characterization of generic irreducibility for dispersion polynomials and Bloch varieties of periodic graph operators. More precisely, we prove that for a generic choice of edge weights and potentials, the dispersion polynomial/Bloch variety of a nontrivial periodic graph is irreducible if and only if the quotient graph is connected.
  Our proof uses a strong dichotomy for parameterized Laurent polynomials: reducibility either occurs for every parameter or fails on a nonempty Zariski-open set. After establishing this dichotomy, we reduce the problem to minimally connected periodic graphs.
