### [41] [On the role of crack electrolyte wetting in the degradation and performance of battery active particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01806)
*S. Luza-Vega,Y. Zhao,E. Martínez-Pañeda*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文通过对比全耦合电化-力学模型与常规均匀通量假设的单粒子模型，揭示了锂离子电池阴极颗粒裂纹中电解液浸润可导致界面反应速率在裂纹尖端产生约8倍的通量放大，均匀通量模型会系统性低估容量（1C倍率下25%）和拉伸应力（10%），说明忽略裂纹-电解液耦合会严重低估电池利用极限和疲劳相关应力历史。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阴极颗粒裂纹被广泛认为是锂离子电池（lithium-ion batteries）的主要退化机制，但裂纹也使电解液浸润新暴露的内表面，从而改变界面反应路径。然而，电解液浸润在裂纹颗粒内重新分配反应的机制性作用尚不清楚。

Method: 通过受控对比两套模型进行研究：(i) 全耦合电化-力学模型（fully coupled electro-chemo-mechanical model），同时解析活性材料及裂纹内外电解液中的锂浓度、静电势和应力场；(ii) 采用常规均匀通量假设（uniform flux assumption）的单粒子化学-力学模型（single-particle chemo-mechanical model）。

Result: 耦合模型预测界面反应速率存在强烈的空间异质性，裂纹尖端通量放大倍数约为施加均匀通量的8倍。反应再分布主要由局部固态锂浓度和应力变化主导，裂纹内部电解液电势梯度在所考虑条件下为次要因素。均匀通量模型在1C倍率下低估容量达25%，高倍率时偏差进一步增大；同时在脱锂全过程中低估拉伸应力约10%。

Conclusion: 忽略裂纹-电解液耦合会导致系统性低估电池的容量利用极限以及疲劳相关的应力历史，直接影响裂纹驱动力条件（crack driving conditions）的准确评估。

Abstract: Cathode particle fracture is widely recognised as a major degradation mechanism in lithium-ion batteries, yet cracking also permits electrolyte wetting of newly exposed internal surfaces, modifying interfacial reaction pathways. The mechanistic role of electrolyte wetting in redistributing reactions within cracked particles remains unclear. Here, we isolate this effect through a controlled comparison between (i) a fully coupled electro-chemo-mechanical model resolving lithium concentration, electrostatic potential, and stress fields in both the active material and the electrolyte inside and outside cracks, and (ii) a single-particle chemo-mechanical model employing the conventional uniform flux assumption. The coupled model predicts strong spatial heterogeneity in interfacial reaction rates, with flux amplification approximately 8x relative to the imposed uniform flux at the crack tip. Reaction redistribution, and thus lithium flux, is governed predominantly by local solid-state lithium concentration and stress variations, while electrolyte potential gradients inside cracks remain secondary under the conditions considered. Uniform flux models can underpredict delivered capacity by 25% at 1C-rate; this discrepancy increases at higher rates. They also underestimate tensile stresses throughout the delithiation process by 10%, directly affecting crack driving conditions. These results demonstrate that neglecting crack-electrolyte coupling leads to systematic underestimation of both utilisation limits and fatigue-relevant stress histories.

</details>


<div id='gr-qc'></div>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [42] [Full spacetime inversion generated by electromagnetic Abelian gauge transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00867)
*Alcides Garat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨在电磁规范变换（electromagnetic gauge transformation）下，于类光曲面（null surface）内部时空区域中实现时间反演（time reversal）或完全反转（full inversion）的可能性。研究表明，通过构造依赖于电磁规范的新标架场（tetrad），可以改变时空的物理运动学性质，从而将未来指向的类时矢量（future directed timelike vector）转化为过去指向的类时矢量（past directed timelike vector），实现时间流向的逆转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作中已证明电磁规范变换可在类光曲面内部产生反射效应，本研究进一步探索在该框架下实现完全时空反转的可能性，旨在通过物理手段逆转时间流向。

Method: 基于依赖于电磁规范构造的新标架场（tetrad），通过设定特定的场配置（field configuration）来实现时间反演。研究采用理论证明的方式，论证未来指向类时矢量可被物理地转化为过去指向类时矢量。

Result: 证明可以通过物理手段（如特定电磁场配置）将未来指向类时矢量转变为过去指向类时矢量，从而实现时间流向的逆转。此前从未有实验讨论过实现时间反演或完全反转的相关方案。

Conclusion: 在电磁规范变换框架下，通过适当设计场配置，在类光曲面内部区域实现时空完全反转在理论上是可能的，这为时间反演的物理实现提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: In a previous manuscript we addressed the possibility of generating a reflection in a region of spacetime inside a null surface under electromagnetic gauge transformations. In this manuscript we will deal with the possibility of full inversions in a region of spacetime inside a null surface under electromagnetic gauge transformations. Since new tetrads whose construction depends on electromagnetic gauge were introduced it has been proved that the physical kinematic nature of spacetime can be altered as proved previously. In this case we will see how to create a field configuration that will reverse the flow of time. We will prove that we can turn a future directed timelike vector into a past directed timelike vector by physical means. Experiments devised in order to achieve time reversal or full inversion have been never discussed before.

</details>


### [43] [Oscillon Formation in Palatini Modified Gravity Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00945)
*Shreyas Upadhye,Sukanta Panda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Palatini形式主义（Palatini Formalism）下，通过修改爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert Action），研究宇宙暴胀（Inflation）结束后再加热（preheating）阶段形成的准稳定非拓扑孤子状能量结构——振荡子（Oscillons），并利用CosmoLattice进行数值模拟，分析了其动力学、功率谱及产生的原初引力波（Primordial Gravitational Wave）频谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要在广义相对论（General Relativity）的度规形式主义（Metric Formalism）下分析振荡子，本文旨在探索在Palatini形式主义下，通过引入标量场与里奇标量（Ricci Scalar, R）的非最小耦合（non minimal coupling）来修改引力部分，进而研究振荡子的形成及其物理后果。

Method: 采用多项式形式（polynomial form）的势能，利用数值格点模拟工具CosmoLattice，在Palatini形式主义框架下求解暴胀子（Inflaton）标量场的动力学方程，并对k模扰动的增长进行功率谱分析；同时计算由振荡子非对称分布产生的原初引力波谱。

Result: 数值结果显示，标量场动力学方程确实给出振荡且衰减的解，符合振荡子的预期行为；状态方程（equation of state）表明早期宇宙中存在一个振荡子主导的延长时期；此外，振荡子的非对称分布产生了超高频（Ultra-High Frequency）范围内的原初引力波，该频段落在未来规划的探测器与实验的探测范围内。

Conclusion: 本文在Palatini形式主义下成功模拟了振荡子的形成与演化，证实该框架下存在振荡子主导的早期宇宙阶段，并预言了可被未来实验探测的超高频引力波信号。

Abstract: We investigate the formation of spatially localized, oscillatory in time and non topological solitonic, quasi-stable energy configurations, Oscillons, which are formed at the end of Inflationary epoch, during the preheating phase and decay over long periods of time. Oscillons have been previously studied in literature in the regime of General Relativity using Metric Formalism. In this paper we look for formation of these energy lumps by modifying the gravity part of the Einstein Hilbert Action, considering a non minimal coupling of the scalar field with Ricci Scalar,$R$, and working in an alternative formulation of General Relativity known as Palatini Formalism. The potential we consider is of polynomial form. We demonstrate numerically, using CosmoLattice, that the equation governing the dynamics of the Inflaton scalar field give oscillatory and decaying solutions as it is expected in the case of Oscillons, with power spectrum governing the growth of perturbations of $k$ modes. The equation of state reveals an extended period of Oscillon domination in the early universe. Along with this, the Primordial Gravitational Wave spectrum due to asymmetric distribution of these energy configurations have also been studied. We observe that these generate Ultra-High Frequency regime Gravitational Waves, which lie in the range of the planned future detectors and experiments.

</details>


### [44] [Nonperturbative Danielson-Satishchandran-Wald Decoherence with Unruh-DeWitt detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00956)
*Levy B. N. Batista,André G. S. Landulfo,Robert B. Mann,George E. A. Matsas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过一个非微扰（nonperturbative）的有限时间探测器模型，分析了DSW机制——一种由软光子（soft photons）和软引力子（soft gravitons）导致的、在包含分叉Killing视界（bifurcating Killing horizon）的时空中均匀加速叠加态的退相干（decoherence）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DSW机制揭示了在包含分叉Killing视界的时空中，均匀加速的电荷或物质空间叠加态会因软光子和软引力子的发射与吸收而发生退相干。研究该机制有助于理解量子引力与量子信息理论交叉领域中的基本退相干源。

Method: 采用一个无隙（gapless）有限时间探测器，制备在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中沿均匀加速路径的空间叠加态，并与有质量标量场（massive scalar field）相互作用，进行非微扰计算。

Result: 该非微扰模型能够在更可控的条件下分析退相干过程，突出了导致DSW机制的主要因素。

Conclusion: DSW机制导致的退相干可在有限固有时间（finite proper time）内发生，本文模型为更精确地研究该退相干过程的物理根源提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Recently, Danielson, Satishchandran, and Wald (DSW) have proposed a novel source of decoherence for uniformly accelerated charges and masses in spatial superposition in spacetimes containing a bifurcating Killing horizon. Such an effect can be traced back to the emission and absorption of soft photons and gravitons, which effectively act as "which-path'' information probes. This results in the decoherence of any such superposition in a finite proper time. With this in mind, we study the DSW mechanism using a gapless finite-time detector prepared in a spatial superposition of uniformly accelerated paths in Minkowski spacetime that interacts with a massive scalar field. The calculation is nonperturbative. Such a model will enable us to analyze the decoherence process in a more controlled manner, highlighting the main factors that give rise to this interesting mechanism.

</details>


### [45] [Series solutions to the TOV equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00986)
*Paulo Luz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了致密星体Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程的通用级数解，建立了由物态方程及其热力学导数计算幂级数系数的算法，并利用Padé近似理论得到包含孤立极点的亚纯函数级数表示，进而推导出星体半径与质量的闭合近似表达式。该形式化方法被应用于仿射物态方程与多方流体模型，并扩展至分段物态方程情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密星体的结构由Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV)方程描述，但该方程的解析求解困难，现有方法多依赖数值积分。本文旨在建立TOV方程的通用级数解法，以获得星体半径与质量的闭合形式近似表达式，并系统分析解析解性质与物态方程正则性之间的关联。

Method: 首先，基于物态方程（equation of state）及其关于热力学变量的导数，发展了一种计算幂级数系数的算法。然后，运用Padé近似（Padé approximants）理论，得到了收敛域可包含孤立极点的亚纯函数（meromorphic functions）的级数表示。最后，将该形式化方法拓展到分段物态方程（piecewise equations of state），并推导了可在过渡超曲面（transition hypersurfaces）上匹配的级数解。

Result: 得到了致密星体TOV方程的通用级数解，推导出星体半径与质量的闭合形式近似表达式。将该方法应用于仿射物态方程（affine equations of state）与多方流体（polytropic fluids）等具体模型，计算结果与数值积分结果吻合良好。此外，成功将方法推广至分段物态方程情形。

Conclusion: 提出的级数解法为致密星体结构分析提供了一种通用解析框架，能够有效逼近星体半径与质量，且适用于多种物态方程（包括分段情形）。该方法与数值积分结果一致，验证了其可靠性与实用性。

Abstract: We present general series solutions to the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations for compact stellar objects. We develop an algorithm to compute the coefficients of the power series in terms of the equation of state and its derivatives with respect to the thermodynamic variables. Using these results, we establish general properties of analytic solutions and their relation to the regularity of the equation of state. Applying the theory of Padé approximants, we derive series representations for meromorphic functions whose domains of convergence may include isolated poles. These analytic solutions are then used to obtain closed-form expressions to approximate the radius and mass of stellar objects. We apply the formalism to specific models, namely fluids with affine equations of state and polytropic fluids, and compare the results with those obtained from numerical integration. Lastly, we extend the formalism to piecewise equations of state, deriving series solutions that can be matched across transition hypersurfaces.

</details>


### [46] [Gravitational Waves from a Black Hole Falling Radially into a Thin-Shell Traversable Wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01216)
*Mohammad Nosherwan Malik,James B. Dent,William E. Gabella,Thomas W. Kephart*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文计算了恒星质量黑洞径向落入薄壳史瓦西可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）所产生的引力波信号，推导了包含质量四极矩和高阶多极矩贡献的解析波形，发现信号具有与反复穿越喉道相关联的特征脉冲-间隙结构。振幅谱密度分析表明，对于最优取向的源，该信号在约500 Mpc距离内可被地面探测器探测到，从而为引力波数据中识别可穿越虫洞提供了潜在观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索可穿越虫洞这一理论天体在引力波观测中可能留下的独特信号特征，为区分虫洞与黑洞等致密天体提供可检验的观测预言。

Method: 将恒星质量黑洞视为试验粒子（test particle），推导其径向落入薄壳史瓦西可穿越虫洞时产生的引力波形，分析包含质量四极矩及高阶多极矩的解析表达式，并计算振幅谱密度（amplitude spectral density）。

Result: 得到的引力波信号呈现由反复穿越喉道导致的特征脉冲-间隙结构（pulse-gap structure）。振幅谱密度与地面探测器灵敏度比较表明，对于最优取向的源，该信号在约500 Mpc距离内可落入探测器的灵敏度范围。

Conclusion: 该结果为从引力波数据中寻找可穿越虫洞提供了潜在的可观测特征，有望用于未来引力波探测实验中对虫洞候选体的识别与区分。

Abstract: We compute the gravitational-wave signal generated by the radial infall of a stellar-mass black hole into a thin-shell Schwarzschild traversable wormhole. Modeling the black hole as a test particle, we derive analytic expressions for the emitted waveform, including contributions from the mass quadrupole and higher-order multipoles. The resulting signal exhibits a characteristic pulse-gap structure associated with repeated throat crossings. We further compute the amplitude spectral density and compare it with representative ground-based detector sensitivities, finding that such signals could lie within the sensitivity range for optimally oriented sources at distances of order ~500 Mpc. These results provide a potential observational signature of traversable wormholes in gravitational-wave data.

</details>


### [47] [Photon Spheres and shadow of modified black-hole entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01303)
*Fang Liu,Yu-Bo Ma,Yun-Zhi Du,Huai-Fan Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了黑洞熵修正与度规函数之间的显式对应关系，利用修正度规计算了光子球半径和黑洞阴影尺寸，发现不同熵修正导致特征性光学偏移，并结合事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）对Sgr A*的观测数据，约束了修正熵中引入的参数范围，为检验广义熵框架及Bekenstein-Hawking面积律的偏离提供了可行途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞熵修正对时空几何和光学观测的影响，并利用实际天文观测数据约束修正熵中的自由参数，从而检验广义熵框架（generalized entropy frameworks）以及Bekenstein-Hawking面积律（Bekenstein-Hawking area law）的偏离。

Method: 从黑洞热力学第一定律（first law of black hole thermodynamics）出发，在固定黑洞能量和视界位置条件下建立修正熵与度规函数之间的显式对应关系；利用修正度规进一步计算光子球半径（photon sphere radius）和阴影尺寸（shadow size）。

Result: 不同形式的熵修正会导致特征性的光学偏移（optical shifts）；通过与事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）对Sgr A*的观测结果比较，成功约束了修正熵中引入的参数范围。

Conclusion: 该研究为检验广义熵框架和探测Bekenstein-Hawking面积律的偏离提供了一种可行的理论-观测联合检验方法。

Abstract: Starting from the first law of black hole thermodynamics, we establish an explicit correspondence between the corrected entropy and the metric function under the condition of fixed black hole energy and horizon position. Using the corrected metric, we further compute the photon sphere radius and shadow size, demonstrating that different entropy corrections lead to characteristic optical shifts. By comparing with the Event Horizon Telescope observations of Sgr A*, we constrain the parameter range introduced in the corrected entropy. This provides a feasible approach for testing generalized entropy frameworks and probing deviations from the Bekenstein-Hawking area law.

</details>


### [48] [Feasible Stellar Interiors Beyond Einstein Gravity: Insights from Non-Metricity-Matter Coupled Gravitational Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01343)
*M. Sharif,M. Zeeshan Gul,Adeeba Arooj*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 $f(Q,L_m)$ 引力框架下（其中 $Q$ 为非度规（non-metricity），$L_m$ 为物质拉格朗日量（matter Lagrangian）），通过选取特定函数形式推导场方程，利用两种新型非奇异解分析静态球对称各向异性致密天体的存在性和稳定性，并结合光滑匹配（smooth matching）条件确定度量系数中的未知常数。图形分析与声速方法（sound speed method）均表明所研究的致密天体满足所有必要条件，是可行且稳定的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验各向异性（anisotropic）致密天体在 $f(Q,L_m)$ 修改引力理论中的存在性和稳定性，拓展对致密星体在非黎曼几何框架下行为的理解。

Method: 假定该理论的具体函数形式以显式写出场方程；采用两种新型非奇异解（non-singular solutions）构造静态球对称（static spherically symmetric）构型；通过光滑匹配条件确定度量系数中的未知常数；运用图形分析评估物理特性的可行性，并借助声速方法检验稳定性。

Result: 图形分析表明所考虑的致密星体在物理上是可行的；声速方法证实这些恒星对象满足所有必要的稳定性条件。

Conclusion: 在所研究的 $f(Q,L_m)$ 引力模型下，各向异性致密天体是可行且稳定的。

Abstract: This manuscript examines viability and stability of anisotropic compact objects in the framework of $f(Q,L_m)$ gravity ($Q$ is the non-metricity and $L_m$ is the matter Lagrangian). We assume a particular functional form of this theory to get explicit expressions for the field equations which govern the behavior of matter and geometry in this context. The configuration of static spherically symmetric structures is evaluated using the two innovative non-singular solutions. We use smooth matching conditions to evaluate the values of unknown constants in the metric coefficients. The viability of considered compact stars is assessed using a graphic analysis of various important physical characteristics. We also investigate stability of the considered stellar objects through sound speed method. It is found that these stellar objects are viable and stable, as all the required conditions are satisfied.

</details>


### [49] [Acausal exact vacuum solutions in nonlocal gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01413)
*Zhe Zhao,Leonardo Modesto,Cosimo Bambi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究非局域引力（nonlocal gravity）中一类允许闭合类时曲线（closed time-like curves）的Gödel型宇宙解，指出重整化要求（renormalizability requirement）本身不足以避免因果性破坏（causality violation），且非微扰量子效应使从平坦宇宙到Gödel宇宙的跃迁概率极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验非局域引力作为超可重整（super-renormalizable）或有限量子引力理论（finite quantum gravity theory）在经典层面是否允许违反因果性的Gödel型宇宙解，并评估重整化要求作为避免因果性破坏的充分性。

Method: 分析非局域引力在真空中的经典运动方程（classical equations of motion），显式验证一类特殊的Gödel型宇宙是否为其精确解（exact solution），并考察非局域形状因子（nonlocal form factors）的选择对解存在性的影响。

Result: 特定子类的Gödel型宇宙是非局域引力在真空中的精确解，但仅对特定（尽管广泛）的非局域形状因子类成立；重整化要求本身不足以作为真空中避免因果性破坏的指导原则；因果性破坏从非局域基本尺度（non locality fundamental scale）延伸到宏观尺度（macroscopic scales）；物质的出现可以打破闵可夫斯基宇宙（Minkowski Universe）与Gödel宇宙之间的经典简并性（classical degeneracy）；非微扰量子水平下，从平坦宇宙到Gödel宇宙的跃迁概率极小。

Conclusion: 非局域引力在经典层面允许Gödel型宇宙解，但该解的存在受非局域形状因子制约；仅凭可重整性（renormalizability）不足以在真空中排除因果性破坏；物质场和量子效应在恢复因果性方面起关键作用。

Abstract: Nonlocal gravity is a promising super-renormalizable or finite quantum gravity theory consistent with unitarity. In this paper, we focus on the classical equations of motion and explicitly show that a particular subclass of Gödel-type Universes, where closed time-like curves are allowed, is an exact solution of nonlocal gravity in vacuum. The result is consistent with a well defined theory at quantum level, but it is realized only with a special, although large, class of nonlocal form factors. Therefore, by itself the renormalizability requirement is not a sufficient guiding principle in vacuum whether we want to avoid the causality violation. From the physical point of view, the causality violation takes place from the non locality fundamental scale to macroscopic scales. Therefore, it is the presence of matter to break the classical degeneracy between the Minkowski and the Gödel Universe. Finally, we have shown that at the non-perturbative quantum level the transition from a flat to a Gödel Universe is ridiculously small.

</details>


### [50] [A note on methods for computing the critical curve of Kerr-like black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01426)
*Siddharth Kumar Sahoo,Indrani Banerjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了三种定义克尔型黑洞临界曲线（即“阴影”）的天体坐标方案——Bardeen、de Vries 以及 Grenzebach 等人的定义，发现它们在大距离真空中或非均匀等离子体环境下一致，但在有限距离观测者或均匀等离子体场景下存在显著分歧，并探讨了 tetrad 变换的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有多种方法定义黑洞阴影的临界曲线，但这些定义之间是否等价尚不清楚，尤其是在存在等离子体或观测者位于有限距离时，不同定义可能导致显著差异，需系统比较以澄清分歧的来源。

Method: 本文以 Kerr 型黑洞为背景，系统比较了 Bardeen、de Vries 以及 Grenzebach 等人三种临界曲线定义；针对真空、非均匀等离子体、均匀等离子体以及不同观测距离的条件进行对比；还推导了 de Vries 定义的假设基础，并考察了 Bardeen tetrad 与 Carter tetrad 对临界曲线的影响。

Result: 三种定义在大距离真空或非均匀等离子体环境中一致；在有限距离下，Bardeen 定义给出的临界曲线最小，de Vries 定义最大；在均匀等离子体下，Bardeen 定义的曲线甚至在大距离处也与另两种偏离，且随等离子体密度增大而收缩，与另两种定义及经典引力透镜研究的预期矛盾；tetrad 变换仅导致临界曲线的水平平移。

Conclusion: 不同临界曲线定义在有限距离和均匀等离子体条件下存在本质分歧，其中 Bardeen 定义在均匀等离子体中的行为与引力透镜理论预期不一致，需谨慎选择定义；tetrad 变换对临界曲线形状影响较小。

Abstract: This study systematically compares Bardeen's, de Vries's, and Grenzebach et al.'s celestial coordinate definitions of the critical curve ("shadow") of Kerr-like black holes. We find that all three definitions agree for black holes in vacuum or surrounded by inhomogeneous plasma observed from large distances. However, they diverge for observers located at a finite distance: Bardeen's definition yields the smallest critical curve, while de Vries's yields the largest. When homogeneous plasma is considered, critical curve computed using Bardeen's definition deviates from the other two even at large distances and contracts compared to the vacuum case with increasing plasma density. This is in clear contradiction with the behaviour predicted by de Vries's, Grenzebach et al.'s definitions, and previous gravitational lensing studies. We derive de Vries's definition assuming a critical curve on the observer's sky plane and explain its discrepancy with Grenzebach et al.'s definition. We further explore the effect of the change of tetrad on the critical curve. Using Bardeen and Carter tetrads, we plot the critical curve for Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes in the presence of plasma, highlighting that tetrad changes introduce only a horizontal shift in the critical curve.

</details>


### [51] [Constraints on Einstein-aether gravity from the precision timing of PSR J1738+0333](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01436)
*Massimo Vaglio,Amodio Carleo,Abhimanyu Susobhanan,Enrico Barausse,Bilel Ben Salem,Alessandro Corongiu,Paulo C. C. Freire,Delphine Perrodin*

TL;DR: 该论文利用PSR J1738+0333脉冲星的多个高精度计时数据集（EPTA第二版、NANOGrav九年等），通过贝叶斯方法约束爱因斯坦-以太引力（Einstein-aether gravity）中的理论参数，获得了迄今单个双脉冲星系统对爱因斯坦-以太耦合常数的最强强场限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦-以太引力是广义相对论（General Relativity）的一种洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz-violating）扩展，其中引入了一个动力学单位类时矢量场来选出一个优先参考系。利用脉冲星计时的高精度观测来约束这一理论中的洛伦兹破缺效应，以检验其偏离广义相对论的程度。

Method: 方法同时考虑了由洛伦兹破缺引起的一阶后牛顿（first post-Newtonian）保守项和耗散项修正。采用贝叶斯计时管道Vela处理全部到达时间（ToA）数据集，对双星成分质量、后开普勒（post-Keplerian）参数和质心速度分量进行联合后验采样，然后通过重采样方案将后验分布传播为基本理论参数的鲁棒约束。

Result: 获得迄今单个双脉冲星系统对爱因斯坦-以太耦合常数的最强强场限制（the most stringent strong-field bounds on the Einstein-aether coupling constants from a single binary pulsar system to date）。

Conclusion: 基于PSR J1738+0333多个高精度计时数据集的联合分析，有效约束了爱因斯坦-以太引力中的洛伦兹破缺参数，为检验引力理论提供了更强、更可靠的观测限制。

Abstract: We constrain Einstein-aether gravity -- a Lorentz-violating extension of General Relativity in which a dynamical, unit timelike vector field selects a preferred frame -- using updated high-precision pulsar timing observations of PSR J1738+0333 from EPTA second Data Release and the NANOGrav 9-year release, in combination with ToAs from Arecibo, Green Bank, Nancay, Parkes, and Westerbork. Our method accounts for both conservative and dissipative first post-Newtonian corrections arising from Lorentz violation; here we apply it to PSR J1738+0333 using the Bayesian timing pipeline Vela to process the full ToA dataset. We sample the joint posterior over binary component masses, post-Keplerian parameters and center-of-mass velocity components, and then apply a resampling scheme to propagate posteriors into robust constraints on the fundamental theory parameters, obtaining the most stringent strong-field bounds on the Einstein-aether coupling constants from a single binary pulsar system to date.

### [52] [On the formulations of the Fermat principle in general relativity and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01532)
*Erasmo Caponio,Miguel Angel Javaloyes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了广义相对论框架下的费马原理（Fermat principle），从经典光学到洛伦兹几何（Lorentzian geometry）中现代变分表述的演化过程。论文提供了光滑类光曲线（smooth lightlike curves）情形下的证明，分析了类光曲线空间的数学困难（Sobolev拓扑下不构成光滑流形），讨论了以二次到达时间泛函（quadratic arrival time functional）为核心的替代框架，并介绍了该原理在扩展光源、芬斯勒时空（Finsler spacetimes）及非连续界面斯涅尔定律（Snell law）等多个方向上的重要推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论（general relativity）中，光线的传播由类光测地线（lightlike geodesics）描述，经典的费马原理需要被重新表述为洛伦兹几何中的变分原理（variational principle）。本文旨在系统梳理这一原理的数学演化过程，并着重分析其在相对论框架下面临的独特数学困难——例如类光曲线空间缺乏光滑流形结构，从而阻碍了标准变分方法的直接应用。

Method: 论文采用综述与数学分析相结合的方法。首先在光滑类光曲线框架下给出费马原理的证明；然后通过分析Sobolev拓扑下类光曲线空间的结构，指出其因零锥条件（null condition）的锥面性质而不具备光滑流形结构；为规避这一变分障碍，讨论引入二次到达时间泛函（quadratic arrival time functional）的替代框架，用以建立光线的多重性结果（multiplicity results）。

Result: 结果表明，在Sobolev拓扑下，满足零锥条件的类光曲线空间不具备光滑流形结构，这是相对论费马原理变分表述的核心数学困难。二次到达时间泛函的引入为克服这一障碍提供了可行途径，并可用于证明光线的多重存在性。此外，原理的诸多推广——包括扩展到延长光源与接收器、任意到达曲线、指定固有时的时间型测地线（timelike geodesics）、芬斯勒时空以及非连续界面产生的斯涅尔定律——均被有效纳入统一框架。

Conclusion: 该综述不仅厘清了广义相对论中费马原理从经典到现代变分表述的完整脉络，而且明确指出了类光曲线空间的流形结构缺失这一关键数学障碍，并展示了通过二次到达时间泛函进行替代建模的有效性。这些结果为相对论性光线传播的变分理论奠定了更严格的数学基础，并为未来在更复杂时空几何（如芬斯勒时空）中的应用提供了系统参考。

Abstract: This paper presents a survey of the Fermat principle within the framework of general relativity, tracing its evolution from classical optics to its modern variational formulation in Lorentzian geometry. In particular, we provide its proof in the framework of smooth lightlike curves. We also analyze the mathematical difficulties inherent in the relativistic setting, specifically demonstrating that the space of lightlike curves in the Sobolev topology does not admit a smooth manifold structure due to the cone nature of the null condition. To address these variational obstacles, we discuss alternative frameworks highlighting the role of the quadratic arrival time functional in establishing multiplicity results for light rays. Furthermore, we explore significant extensions of the principle, such as its application to extended sources and receivers, arbitrary arrival curves, timelike geodesics with prescribed proper time, Finsler spacetimes, or settings with a non-continuous interface giving rise to a Snell law.

</details>


### [53] [Relational quantum dynamics of the black hole interior: singularity resolution and quantum bounce](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01576)
*Paolo Fragolino,Saeed Rastgoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于完全关系性且规范不变的量子化框架，研究了与Kantowski-Sachs宇宙学模型等距的Schwarzschild黑洞内部。通过精细代数量子化构建物理希尔伯特空间，并利用Page-Wotters形式论恢复量子动力学，发现Kretschmann标量和膨胀标量在黑洞内部保持有限，而二维球面面积存在正比于系统变量不确定度的下界。膨胀标量在量子反弹处为零并改变符号，建立了黑到白洞的转变。奇点消解直接源于关系性、海森堡不确定原理和物理希尔伯特空间结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统广义相对论中Schwarzschild黑洞内部存在经典奇点，而量子引力理论旨在解决该奇点问题。此前研究虽尝试从不同量子化方案处理，但缺乏完全关系性且规范不变的统一框架来清晰论证奇点消解的根源。

Method: 采用精细代数量子化（refined algebraic quantization）构建物理希尔伯特空间，通过Page-Wotters形式论（Page-Wootters formalism）结合协变POVM时钟恢复量子动力学。利用群平均（G-twirl）构造规范不变的关系性可观测量（relational observables），包括二维球面面积、Kretschmann标量和零测地线膨胀标量。

Result: Kretschmann标量和膨胀标量在黑洞内部始终保持有限；二维球面面积存在一个与系统变量（非时钟变量的另一个构型变量）不确定度成正比的极小下界；膨胀标量在量子反弹（quantum bounce）处为零并改变符号，表明黑洞到白洞的转变。

Conclusion: 奇点消解直接源于关系性（relationality）、海森堡不确定原理（Heisenberg uncertainty principle）和物理希尔伯特空间结构，不依赖于特定的量子化方案，仅需薛定谔表象（Schrödinger representation）。

Abstract: We study the interior of the Schwarzschild black hole which is isometric to the Kantowski-Sachs cosmological model, using a fully relational and gauge-invariant quantization framework. The physical Hilbert space is constructed via refined algebraic quantization, and quantum dynamics is recovered through the Page-Wootters formalism with a covariant POVM clock built from one of the two configuration variables, whose Hamiltonian is proportional to the momentum of the said variable. Gauge-invariant relational observables for the area of 2-spheres, the Kretschmann scalar, and the expansion scalar of null geodesic are constructed via group averaging (G-twirl) and evaluated on physical states. We find that the Kretschmann and expansion scalars remain finite throughout the black hole, while the area of 2-spheres is bounded below by a minimum value proportional to the uncertainty in the system variable, which is the other configuration variable distinct from the clock variable. In particular, the expansion scalar vanishes and changes sign at the quantum bounce, establishing a black-hole-to-white-hole transition. These results hold for any general clock whose operator forms a canonical pair with the clock Hamiltonian, and require no specific quantization scheme other than the Schrodinger representation. The singularity resolution emerges directly from relationality, the Heisenberg uncertainty principle, and the structure of the physical Hilbert space.

Conclusion: 正则、渐近平坦的可穿越四维虫洞可以从高维标量-张量理论中自然地产生，从而建立了高维理论与四维可穿越虫洞解之间的明确联系。

Abstract: We investigate traversable wormhole solutions within a four-dimensional effective theory derived from a five-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell-Chern-Simons action with a non-minimally coupled scalar field. A warped Kaluza-Klein compactification yields an Einstein-frame theory containing a phantom dilaton, a canonical axion, a Maxwell field, and a Kaluza-Klein vector, with the couplings fixed by the higher-dimensional origin. Focusing on the Ellis-Bronnikov geometry, we construct solutions that incorporate both dyonic Maxwell and Kaluza-Klein fields. For exponential gauge couplings, the Einstein equations determine the scalar kinetic term and the combined potentials, while the remaining field equations reduce to algebraic relations fixing the individual potentials and the radial behaviour of the electric charges. We obtain a systematic classification of configurations, ranging from the pure phantom-supported wormhole to fully coupled dilaton-axion-gauge configurations. The Kaluza-Klein sector enriches the solution space with additional structure while preserving analytic tractability. These results show that regular, asymptotically flat traversable four-dimensional wormholes arise naturally from higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories.

Abstract: Based on the conventional metric tensor and driven by a nearly constant energy density, cosmic inflation, characterized by a remarkably accelerated expansion, was proposed as an early epoch in the Universe. This mechanism addresses horizon, flatness, and relic problems, while also generating quantum fluctuations that are stretched to cosmological scales, leading to emergence of primordial curvatures and tensor perturbations. Despite its empirical success, significant questions remain regarding identity of the inflaton, origin of the potential, and role of quantum gravity. We have established a closed and internally consistent set of analytical formulas for scalar and tensor power spectra, including their spectral tilts, runnings, and the tensor-to-scalar ratio, among other parameters. The quantum corrections appear to provide a clear physical interpretation related to measure scaling and momentum-induced kinetic deformation, which facilitates modifications to the inflationary observables in a controlled and predictive manner. While maintaining the classical limits, these corrections provide a well-defined phenomenological perspective on potential quantum-gravitational structures in the early Universe.

### [56] [Shirokov and Shapiro Effects in the Hartle-Thorne Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01639)
*Anuar Idrissov,Kuantay Boshkayev,Serzhan Momynov,Hernando Quevedo,Daniya Utepova,Ainur Urazalina,Bagila Baitimbetova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Hartle-Thorne时空中研究了自转与四极变形对Shirokov效应和Shapiro时间延迟的影响，通过测地偏离方程和数值分析揭示了角动量与四极矩如何耦合影响这些相对论性可观测量，并与Lense-Thirring和Zipoy-Voorhees度规的结果进行了比较。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨天体物理致密天体的旋转（rotation）和四极变形（quadrupole deformation）如何影响Shirokov效应与Shapiro时间延迟（Shapiro time delay），从而理解致密天体的形变与自转对周围时空相对论性可观测量的作用机制。

Method: 采用Hartle-Thorne度规（描述缓慢旋转、轻微形变天体的外部引力场），利用测地偏离方程（geodesic deviation equations）分析邻近试验粒子轨迹的振荡运动，并对Shapiro时间延迟的两种极限构型进行全数值分析，未使用弱场近似。

Result: 角动量J与四极矩Q的联合作用影响Shirokov效应，径向与方位角振荡之间的耦合趋势与Lense-Thirring及Zipoy-Voorhees度规的结果一致；在Lense-Thirring框架拖拽情形下，Shapiro效应在J正负值时均存在；在静态四极情形下，更扁平的源在更远距离处产生更强的引力时间延迟；四极变形与角动量可产生模拟效应（mimicking effects）。

Conclusion: 致密天体的形变与自转会显著影响周围时空中的相对论性可观测量，四极变形与角动量之间存在可相互模拟的效应，这些发现有助于更精确地描述天体物理致密天体的引力场特征。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of rotation and quadrupole deformations of astrophysical compact objects on the Shirokov and Shapiro effects within the Hartle-Thorne spacetime, which describes the exterior gravitational field of slowly rotating, slightly deformed celestial objects. Using geodesic deviation equations, we analyze the oscillatory motion of neighboring test particle trajectories and show how the combined impact of angular momentum $J$ and quadrupole moment $Q$ affects the Shirokov effect. The results are compared with our previous analysis for the Lense-Thirring and Zipoy-Voorhees metrics, revealing consistent trends in the coupling between radial and azimuthal oscillations. For the Shapiro time delay, we examine two limiting configurations: (i) the Lense-Thirring frame-dragging case with $J^2=0$, $Q=0$ and $J\neq0$, where the effect persists for both positive and negative values of the angular momentum; and (ii) the static quadrupolar case with $J=0$ and $Q\neq0$, where more oblate sources produce a stronger gravitational time delay with increasing distance. We also study these effects in the Hartle-Thorne spacetime without employing the weak-field approximation, performing a full numerical analysis. In particular, we examine the mimicking effects produced by the quadrupole deformation and the angular momentum of the compact object. These results illustrate how the deformation and rotation of compact objects influence the relativistic observables in the surrounding spacetime.

</details>


### [57] [Axial $w$-modes of anisotropic neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01737)
*Sushovan Mondal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了各向异性中子星的轴向w-模振荡，通过两种状态方程（BSk21和SLy4）和两种各向异性模型（Horvat ansatz和Bowers-Liang ansatz）构建星体构型，计算了轴向w-模频率和阻尼时间，揭示了它们与星体质量、紧凑度及各向异性强度的依赖关系，并给出了经验拟合公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星内部可能存在压力各向异性（pressure anisotropy），即径向压力与切向压力不等，这会影响星体的振荡模式。本文旨在系统研究各向异性对中子星轴向w-模（axial w-mode）引力波特征的影响，填补相关理论空白。

Method: 采用两种真实状态方程（equation of state）BSk21和SLy4构建各向异性中子星构型，分别使用Horvat ansatz和Bowers-Liang ansatz两种方案描述压力各向异性。通过连续分数法（continued-fraction method）求解线性化扰动方程，计算轴向w-模频率和阻尼时间。

Result: 轴向w-模频率沿稳定分支随星体质量增加单调递减，其大小依赖于状态方程和各向异性性质。在低质量端，径向主导压力（$p_r>p_t$）构型频率更高；在高质量端，切向主导压力（$p_t>p_r$）构型频率更高。频率与紧凑度（compactness）近似呈线性关系，各向异性同时改变斜率和截距。Bowers-Liang ansatz产生的频率散布更宽。阻尼时间随质量增加而增大，在稳定分支上端快速上升；固定质量下，增强切向压力会缩短阻尼时间，而径向主导压力使阻尼时间更长；各向异性对阻尼时间的影响在更致密星体中更显著，Bowers-Liang ansatz产生系统性更大的阻尼时间。

Conclusion: 各向异性显著影响中子星轴向w-模的振荡频率和阻尼时间，其效应依赖于具体的各向异性模型和状态方程。提供的经验公式可望用于未来引力波观测中对中子星内部各向异性的约束。

Abstract: We investigate the axial $w$-mode oscillations of anisotropic neutron stars. Stellar configurations are constructed using two realistic equations of state, BSk21 and SLy4, with two prescriptions for pressure anisotropy, the Horvat ansatz and the Bowers-Liang ansatz. The axial $w$-mode frequencies are computed by solving the linearized perturbation equations using a continued-fraction method. For each fixed anisotropy strength, the axial $w$-mode frequency decreases monotonically with increasing stellar mass along the stable branch, with its magnitude depending on both the equation of state and the nature of the anisotropy. At low stellar masses, configurations with dominant radial pressure ($p_r>p_t$) exhibit higher frequencies than those with dominant tangential pressure, whereas toward the upper end of the stable branch this ordering is reversed, and configurations with $p_t>p_r$ attain higher frequencies at the same mass. The axial $w$-mode frequency displays an approximately linear dependence on compactness, with anisotropy modifying both the slope and the intercept. The Bowers-Liang ansatz produces a wider spread in the frequency values compared to the Horvat ansatz. We also analyze the damping times associated with the axial $w$-modes and find that they increase with stellar mass, with a rapid rise toward the upper end of the stable branch. At a fixed mass, increasing the tangential pressure relative to the radial pressure leads to shorter damping times, while configurations with dominant radial pressure exhibit longer damping times. The sensitivity of the damping time to anisotropy is more pronounced for more compact stars, and the Bowers-Liang ansatz yields systematically larger damping times than the Horvat ansatz. Finally, we provide empirical expressions for the axial $w$-mode frequency and damping time as functions of stellar compactness and anisotropy strength.

</details>


### [58] [Polarization structure of gravitational waves in extended relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01802)
*Yaakov Friedman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在扩展相对论（Extended Relativity, ER）框架下，利用偏离张量（deviation tensor）作为基本可观测量，分析了引力波（gravitational waves）的极化结构。通过将时空依赖完全归入延迟相位（retarded phase），而张量系数仅依赖于源倾角，实现了探测响应的统一处理。关键结果：极化分量非独立，张量、矢量和标量贡献的相对幅度由源几何固定，从而产生约束的极化态族和相应的脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays, PTAs）关联模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波极化分析多针对广义相对论（General Relativity），缺乏对扩展相对论框架下极化结构的系统性研究。本文旨在建立该理论中极化分量间的关系，并导出可直接检验的观测特征。

Method: 从点源解出发，推导致密双星（compact binary）在波区（wave zone）的辐射场，将偏离张量表示为延迟相位承载时空依赖、张量系数仅依赖源倾角的形式。针对干涉仪探测器（interferometric detectors），信号由潮汐矩阵（tidal matrix）控制；针对脉冲星计时阵列，响应通过零测地线传播（null geodesic propagation）简化为边界项，可观测量由发射点和接收点处的投影 $k^\mu k^\nu h_{\mu\nu}$ 决定。

Result: 极化分量并非独立：张量（tensor）、矢量（vector）和标量（scalar）贡献的相对幅度由源几何唯一确定，形成一个受约束的极化态家族及其对应的脉冲星计时阵列关联模式。

Conclusion: 该公式体系建立了扩展相对论的理论结构与可观测特征之间的直接联系，为区分不同引力理论提供了可行的观测检验途径。

Abstract: We analyze the polarization structure of gravitational waves in the framework of Extended Relativity (ER), using the deviation tensor as the fundamental observable quantity. Starting from the point-source solution, we derive the radiation field of a compact binary in the wave zone and express the deviation tensor in a form in which the spacetime dependence is carried entirely by the retarded phase, while the tensorial coefficients depend only on the inclination angle of the source.
  This representation allows for a unified treatment of detector responses. For interferometric detectors, the signal is governed by the tidal matrix, which depends on second derivatives of the deviation tensor. For pulsar timing arrays (PTAs), the response follows from null geodesic propagation and reduces to boundary terms, so that the observable is determined by the projection $k^μk^νh_{μν}$ evaluated at the emission and reception points.
  A key result is that the polarization components are not independent: the relative amplitudes of tensor, vector, and scalar contributions are fixed by the source geometry. This leads to a constrained family of polarization states and corresponding PTA correlation patterns. The formulation provides a direct connection between the theoretical structure of ER and observable signatures.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文通过半经典近似和Madelung近似，研究了施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）在引力坍缩晚期出现的“闵可夫斯基破缺”（Minkowski breaking）现象，并指出量子势（quantum potential）在该阶段开始强烈抵抗坍缩向施瓦西奇点（Schwarzschild singularity）推进。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用半经典近似（semiclassical approximation）描述能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor），并结合Madelung近似（Madelung approximation）处理坍缩物质。通过在Raychaudhuri方程（Raychaudhuri equation）中引入量子势，分析坍落过程的动力学变化。

Result: 在“闵可夫斯基破缺”发生之后，Raychaudhuri方程中的量子势开始显著地抑制坍缩向施瓦西奇点方向进行。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，量子效应在引力坍缩的最终阶段扮演了关键抵抗角色，为理解黑洞奇点问题的半经典图像提供了新的支持。

Abstract: Schwarzschild black holes are expected to emerge as the end states of the classical gravitational collapse from non-singular configurations. After integrable curvature singularities appear, the interior geometry can be modelled to exhibit a transition, called ``Minkowski breaking'', when the inner horizon disappears, before all matter collapses into the central singularity. This picture implies a quantum framework to describe the final stages of the gravitational collapse, and here we will provide more insights from the semiclassical approximation for the energy-momentum tensor and the Madelung approximation for collapsing matter. In particular, we will show that the quantum potential in the Raychaudhuri equation starts to strongly oppose the collapse towards the Schwarzschild singularity precisely after the Minkowski breaking.

Method: 采用综述性（review-style）叙述方式，梳理 Choquet-Bruhat 从 1952 年关于真空爱因斯坦场方程（vacuum Einstein field equations）局部解存在性的奠基性成果，到后续在爱因斯坦演化方程（Einstein evolution equations）、约束方程（Einstein constraint equations）以及超引力方程（equations of supergravity）方面的一系列研究。

Result: Choquet-Bruhat 的研究成果对数值相对论（numerical relativity）产生了重要方法论影响；她还撰写了多部教科书和一部回忆录。本文的删节版已提交给《美国数学会通告》（AMS Notices）。

Conclusion: Yvonne Choquet-Bruhat 被公认为数学广义相对论和偏微分方程领域的伟大先驱之一，其研究工作具有持久的学术价值。

Abstract: This is a memorial article for Yvonne Choquet-Bruhat, who was one of the great pioneers of mathematical general relativity and of partial differential equations. Starting with her 1952 result on local existence of solutions of the vacuum Einstein field equations, she obtained many results on the Einstein evolution equations, the Einstein constraint equations, and the equations of supergravity. Her methods have also been important for numerical relativity. She also wrote several textbooks and a memoir. An abridged version of this article has been submitted to AMS Notices.

### [61] [Bertotti-Robinson and Bonnor-Melvin universes in nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01811)
*David Kubiznak,Otakar Svitek,Tayebeh Tahamtan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文综述了非线性电动力学（NLE）中Birkhoff定理的适用性，并将其推广至非渐近平坦情形。由此导出Bertotti-Robinson型直积几何，其AdS₂与S₂因子具有一般不相等的半径，该半径由NLE模型决定。这种几何亦可从相应极值NLE带电黑洞的近 horizon 极限得到。研究表明，与Maxwell-Λ情形不同，特定NLE模型下的极值黑洞是线性稳定的。通过替换黑洞内部为Bertotti-Robinson型几何，构造了正则粒子状模型。此外，还重新审视了Bonnor-Melvin宇宙的NLE推广，描述了引力-磁场平衡中的正则轴对称磁力线构型，并以Maxwell、Born-Infeld、RegMax和Frolov-Hayward理论给出了显式示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展Birkhoff定理在非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics, NLE）框架下的适用性分析，尤其是非渐近平坦情形；并澄清与Maxwell-Λ情形在近 horizon 几何与稳定性方面的差异。

Method: 将Birkhoff定理推广至NLE情形，推导Bertotti-Robinson型直积几何（direct product geometry）条件；通过近 horizon 极限（near-horizon limit）从极值NLE带电黑洞恢复该几何；采用线性稳定性分析方法检验特定NLE模型；通过内部几何替换构造正则粒子状模型；并重新审视Bonnor-Melvin宇宙的NLE推广。

Result: 发现Bertotti-Robinson型几何的AdS₂与S₂因子半径一般不相等，由具体NLE模型决定；特定NLE模型下极值黑洞是线性稳定的，这与Maxwell-Λ情形不同；成功构造了正则粒子状模型，并在Maxwell、Born-Infeld、RegMax、Frolov-Hayward等理论中给出了显式示例。

Conclusion: 非线性电动力学（NLE）中Birkhoff定理的推广揭示了更丰富的近 horizon 几何结构，极值黑洞的线性稳定性依赖于具体NLE模型，且正则粒子状模型与Bonnor-Melvin型构型均可通过NLE框架统一描述。

Abstract: We review the status of Birkhoff's theorem in the presence of nonlinear electrodynamics (NLE) - extending the analysis to the case without asymptotic flatness. This leads to the Bertotti-Robinson-type (direct product) geometry with generally unequal radii for its $AdS_{2}$ and $S_{2}$ factors, determined by a given NLE model. As can be expected, such a geometry can also be recovered from a near-horizon limit of the corresponding extremal NLE charged black hole (if it exists). These extremal black holes are shown to be linearly stable for specific NLE models, unlike in the Maxwell-$Λ$ case where unequal radii also arise in near-horizon geometry. Regular particle-like models are constructed by replacing the interior of these black holes with corresponding Bertotti-Robinson-type geometry. We also revisit the NLE generalization of the Bonnor-Melvin universe, describing a regular axisymmetric configuration of magnetic field lines in gravito-magnetic equilibrium. Explicit examples are derived for the Maxwell, Born-Infeld, RegMax, and Frolov-Hayward theories of electrodynamics.

### [62] [Ergosphere Geometry and Thermodynamic Properties of Boosted Kerr-Taub-NUT Solutions in Kaluza-Klein Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02000)
*Hasan Oguz,Goksel Daylan Esmer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过对Kerr-Taub-NUT时空施加Kaluza-Klein boost，研究了降维后得到的旋转黑洞的四维几何与热力学性质，发现静界面的坐标位置在变换下保持不变，但物理能层体积因诱导度规的修正而显著增大。同时，包含电和磁Kaluza-Klein功项的黑洞热力学第一定律得到验证，表明高维动量在不改变视界半径、熵或温度的情况下增强了ZAMO测量的有效惯性系旋转和能层体积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Kaluza-Klein boost（一种沿紧致方向施加的Lorentz变换）对旋转黑洞几何与热力学的影响，特别是高维动量如何在不引入独立物质源的情况下表现为四维Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton黑洞中的电荷，并进一步揭示能层（ergoregion）的物理体积与视界热力学之间的分离行为。

Method: 对Kerr-Taub-NUT时空施加Kaluza-Klein boost得到五维解，随后通过维度约化（dimensional reduction）获得四维Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton黑洞。在Einstein标架中分析静界面（stationary limit surface，$g_{tt}=0$）的坐标位置，并计算常时超曲面上的固有空间体积以衡量物理能层。通过包含电与磁Kaluza-Klein功项验证第一定律，区分种子质量参数、渐近ADM质量与视界Komar质量。

Result: 静界面的坐标位置在Kaluza-Klein boost下保持不变，但物理能层的固有空间体积因诱导空间度规的修正而显著增大。包含电和磁Kaluza-Klein功项的黑洞热力学第一定律得到验证，其中磁项是NUT电荷与boost相互作用的独特双荷（dyonic）特征。视界热力学量（半径、熵、温度）在boost下保持不变，而全局几何性质（能层体积、ZAMO测量的惯性系旋转）则与boost参数相关。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了boost不变的视界热力学与boost依赖的全局几何性质之间的清晰分离。高维动量在不改变视界基本热力学量的情况下显著增强了能层体积和ZAMO参考系中的有效旋转，这为在旋转黑洞时空中探测额外维度提供了干净的几何特征。

Abstract: We investigate rotating black holes obtained by applying a Kaluza-Klein boost to the Kerr-Taub-NUT spacetime and study the resulting four-dimensional geometry and thermodynamics after dimensional reduction. The boost along the compact direction generates an Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton black hole in which the electric charge originates purely from higher-dimensional momentum rather than from an independent matter source.
  We demonstrate that the coordinate location of the stationary limit surface, defined by the condition $g_{tt}=0$ in the Einstein frame, is invariant under the Kaluza-Klein boost. Nevertheless, the boost induces a substantial enlargement of the \emph{physical} ergoregion, as measured by the proper spatial volume on constant-time hypersurfaces, through its modification of the induced spatial metric. We further verify the first law of black-hole thermodynamics with both the electric and magnetic Kaluza-Klein work terms included -- the latter being a genuinely dyonic feature generated by the interplay of the boost with the NUT charge -- and carefully distinguish the seed mass parameter from the asymptotic ADM mass and from the horizon Komar mass.
  Our results establish a clear separation between boost-invariant horizon thermodynamics and boost-dependent global geometric properties. In particular, higher-dimensional momentum enhances the effective inertial-frame rotation measured by ZAMOs and ergoregion volume without altering the horizon radius, entropy, or temperature, providing a clean geometric signature of extra dimensions in rotating black hole spacetimes.

### [63] [Scalar-Electromagnetic Couplings as Source of Deformed Black Hole: From Shadows to Thermodynamic Topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01934)
*Ednaldo L. B. Junior,José Tarciso S. S. Junior,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Jorde A. A. Ramos,Manuel E. Rodrigues,Diego Rubiera-Garcia,Luís F. Dias da Silva,Henrique A. Vieira*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过逆向构造方法，从磁荷非线性电动力学（NED）场与标量场非最小耦合的作用量出发，重构了一个静态球对称黑洞几何。研究发现该解在光子球拓扑荷Q_tot=-1和热力学拓扑荷W=0方面与Reissner-Nordström黑洞同属一个拓扑类，且满足扩展相空间热力学第一定律和Smarr关系，呈现Hawking-Page相变但无van der Waals型临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为先前提出的有效度规黑洞几何寻找一致的物质源，通过确定来自基本作用量的物质源来赋予该几何以理论自洽性。

Method: 采用逆向构造形式（inverse construction formalism），从磁荷非线性电动力学场非最小耦合标量场的作用量出发，通过量纲一致性将参数空间约化至单一磁荷，得到一族电磁拉格朗日量L(F)=F^{n+1}/(n+1)，涵盖线性和非线性电动力学。

Result: 确定了临界磁荷以区分黑洞解与无视界解；计算了光子球（photon sphere）及其阴影半径（shadow radius），并利用Event Horizon Telescope对Sgr A*的观测约束限定了磁荷范围。热力学方面，解满足第一定律和Smarr关系，出现Hawking-Page相变，呈现单一稳定性变化但无van der Waals型临界行为。光子球拓扑荷Q_tot=-1，热力学矢量场的全局缠绕数W=0，与Reissner-Nordström黑洞同属一个拓扑类。

Conclusion: 该非最小耦合框架具有多功能性，既能为先前引入的解提供理论支持，也能在强场引力场景中将其与观测联系起来。

Abstract: We reconstruct a static and spherically symmetric black hole geometry originally proposed as an effective metric by identifying a consistent matter source derived from a fundamental action. The space-time is supported by a magnetically charged nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) field non-minimally coupled to a scalar field. Dimensional consistency reduces the parameter space to a single magnetic charge, and the inverse construction formalism yields a one-parameter family of electromagnetic Lagrangians $\mathcal{L}(F)=F^{n+1}/(n+1)$, encompassing both linear and nonlinear electrodynamics. We analyze the horizon structure and determine the critical magnetic charge separating black hole and horizonless configurations. The photon sphere and the corresponding shadow radius are computed, and observational bounds from the Event Horizon Telescope for Sagittarius A* constrain the allowed range of the magnetic charge. In the extended phase space thermodynamics, the solution satisfies the first law and the Smarr relation, exhibits a Hawking-Page phase transition, and presents a single change in stability without van der Waals-type critical behavior. We also investigate the topological properties of both the photon sphere and the thermodynamic parameter space. The photon sphere carries a total topological charge $Q_{\text{tot}}=-1$, while the thermodynamic vector field yields a global winding number $W=0$, placing the solution in the same topological class as the one of the Reissner-Nordström black hole. We finally discuss the versatility of this non-minimal coupling framework in both providing theoretical support to previously introduced solution and also to connect them to observational settings within strong-field gravity.

</details>


### [64] [The radiation zone in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01951)
*David Garfinkle*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用电动力学（electrodynamics）中辐射区（radiation zone）的概念，解释了广义相对论（general relativity）中两个令人困惑的问题：一是根据等效原理（equivalence principle）认为静态电荷在引力场中会辐射的悖论，二是为何存在天体引力波源但缺乏人造引力波源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决广义相对论中两个长期存在的难题：基于等效原理的静态电荷引力辐射悖论，以及天体引力辐射源与人造引力辐射源之间的存在性差异。

Method: 借助电动力学中辐射区的概念——即远离电荷的区域，$1/r$项场占主导而$1/r^2$项可忽略——来类比分析广义相对论。

Result: 利用辐射区概念澄清了静态电荷在引力场中是否辐射的悖论，并解释了为何天体尺度能产生可观测的引力辐射而人造设备尚无法实现。

Conclusion: 电动力学辐射区的概念为理解广义相对论中的上述两个疑难问题提供了有效的物理类比和解释框架。

Abstract: The radiation zone in electrodynamics is the region far enough away from the charges that the $1/r$ part of the field dominates over the $1/{r^2}$ piece. This concept is key in explaining two puzzling aspects of general relativity: The first is an old paradox that invokes the equivalence principle to argue that a static charge in a gravitational field will radiate. The second is the fact that while there are astrophysical sources of gravitational radiation, we do not have any man-made sources.

### [65] [Pole Structure of Kerr Green's Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01964)
*Hayato Motohashi,Yuto Suichi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了频域中Kerr黑洞扰动的极点结构，明确建立了Teukolsky形式体系中的Matsubara极点结构，并揭示了分解的Green函数贡献中的零频奇异性及其在总径向Green函数中的集体消除机制，为理解时域ringdown波形的瞬态响应提供了频域基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Kerr黑洞扰动Green函数的极点结构对于分析时域ringdown波形的瞬态响应（prompt response）至关重要，但此前在非渐进AdS的渐近平直亚极端Kerr黑洞中，Teukolsky形式体系下的Matsubara极点结构尚未被明确建立。

Method: 通过频域分析Kerr黑洞扰动的径向Teukolsky方程（radial Teukolsky equation），系统考察齐次径向解（homogeneous radial solutions）、连接系数（connection coefficients）以及Green函数自身的极点行为，特别关注Matsubara频率和零频奇异性。

Result: 齐次解和局域连接系数在Matsubara频率处出现简单极点（simple poles）；在局域固定扇区连接公式（local fixed-sector connection formula）中，连接系数比值中的Matsubara极点因子相互抵消；分解的Green函数贡献中存在按ω^{-2l-1}标度的高阶零频奇异性（higher-order zero-frequency singularities），这些奇异性在总径向Green函数中集体消除。

Conclusion: 该结果阐明了Matsubara极点和扇区化零频奇异性如何在Teukolsky形式体系中产生，并为理解Kerr时空中时域ringdown波形的瞬态响应提供了频域基础。

Abstract: We investigate the pole structure of Kerr black-hole perturbations in the frequency domain, focusing on the building blocks of the Green's function for the radial Teukolsky equation: the homogeneous radial solutions, the connection coefficients, and the Green's function itself. We show that the homogeneous solutions and the local connection coefficients develop simple poles at the Matsubara frequencies, thereby establishing the Matsubara pole structure explicitly within the Teukolsky formalism for asymptotically flat subextremal Kerr black holes. At the level of the local fixed-sector connection formula, the explicit Matsubara-pole factors cancel in the ratio of connection coefficients entering a decomposed Green-function contribution. We also identify higher-order zero-frequency singularities in the decomposed Green-function contributions, which scale as $ω^{-2l-1}$ and cancel collectively in the total radial Green's function. These results clarify how Matsubara poles and sectoral zero-frequency singularities arise in the Teukolsky formalism and provide a frequency-domain foundation for understanding prompt response in time-domain ringdown waveforms in Kerr spacetime.

### [66] [Reviving Motivated Inflationary Potentials with $K$-inflation in the light of ACT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01992)
*Milad Solbi,Daris Samart,Peera Simakachorn*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种带有场依赖非标准动能项（non-canonical kinetic term）的K-inflation框架，通过引入额外摩擦效应，使α吸引子T模型（α-attractor T-models）和自然暴胀（natural Inflation）与最新的Planck-ACT-LB-BK18宇宙学观测数据相符合。研究还分析了再加热（reheating）状态方程、暴胀的Swampland一致性条件，并预测了两种模型在引力波背景上的不同特征——后者可能被下一代引力波探测器观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近的ACT（Atacama Cosmology Telescope）数据倾向于更高的标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）$n_s$，使得α吸引子T模型和自然暴胀模型与当前观测产生张力。有必要提出新的理论框架来调和这些模型与最新宇宙学约束之间的矛盾。

Method: 采用K-inflation框架，引入与暴胀子场相关的非标准动能项（field-dependent non-canonical kinetic term）$G(φ)$，通过非最小动能耦合产生的额外摩擦效应（additional friction）来调整模型的观测预测。对再加热状态方程参数$w_{\rm re}$进行精细计算，避免标准幂律近似，并检验暴胀模型与Swampland距离猜想（Swampland Distance Conjecture）和de Sitter猜想（de Sitter Conjecture）的一致性。

Result: 对于α吸引子T模型（$n=2$），可行解出现在$\beta\sim \mathcal{O}(10)$，Swampland一致性要求$\alpha\gtrsim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$，预测物质样再加热（matter-like reheating）和红移倾斜（red-tilted）的引力波背景，短期内难以被探测。对于自然暴胀（$n=4,5$），$\alpha\lesssim 7,8$和$\beta\lesssim -1$时与CMB约束兼容，导致刚性再加热（stiff reheating）和蓝移倾斜（blue-tilted）的引力波背景，可能被LISA、Cosmic Explorer、Einstein Telescope、DECIGO和BBO等下一代探测器观测到，同时满足大爆炸核合成（BBN）和$ΔN_{\rm eff}$界限。

Conclusion: 将引力波探测（gravitational-wave probes）与Swampland判据相结合，有助于区分暴胀的不同紫外完备化（UV completion）方案。两种模型在引力波背景谱上截然不同的倾斜特征提供了可观测的区分判据。

Abstract: Recent ACT data favor a higher scalar spectral index $n_s$, placing models such as $α$-attractor T-models and natural Inflation in tension with current observations. We propose a K-inflation framework with a field-dependent non-canonical kinetic term $G(φ)$ that reconciles these models with the latest Planck-ACT-LB-BK18 constraints. Our analysis includes a refined calculation of the reheating equation-of-state parameter $w_{\rm re}$, avoids standard power-law approximations, and tests consistency with the Swampland Distance and de Sitter Conjectures. We find that the additional friction from the non-minimal kinetic coupling shifts both models into the favored observational regions. For the $α$-attractor T-model with $n=2$, viable solutions occur for $β\sim \mathcal{O}(10)$, with Swampland consistency favoring $α\gtrsim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$. This case predicts matter-like reheating and a red-tilted gravitational-wave background that is unlikely to be detected soon. In contrast, natural Inflation with $n=4,5$ is compatible with CMB constraints for $α\lesssim 7,8$ and $β\lesssim -1$, respectively, leading to stiff reheating and a blue-tilted gravitational-wave background potentially observable by LISA, Cosmic Explorer, Einstein Telescope, DECIGO, and BBO while satisfying BBN and $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ bounds. Combining gravitational-wave probes with Swampland criteria may therefore help distinguish possible UV completions of inflation.

### [67] [Gravitational baryogenesis in scalar-nonmetricity $f(Q,φ)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02008)
*F. Mavoa,M. C. Sow,M. G. Ganiou,C. S. Touré,C. R. Tefo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在标量-非度量性（scalar-nonmetricity）引力理论框架下研究引力重子生成（gravitational baryogenesis），通过两种修正引力模型 $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$ 和 $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$ 分析重子-熵比（baryon-to-entropy ratio）的演化，发现观测到的重子不对称性（约 $10^{-11}$ 至 $10^{-10}$）可在合理的参数范围内成功再现，表明标量-非度量性引力为解释宇宙重子不对称性起源提供了可行的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索标量-非度量性引力框架下的引力重子生成机制，旨在解释宇宙重子不对称性（baryon asymmetry of the Universe）的起源，并检验修正引力理论在早期宇宙学中的适用性。

Method: 考虑两类修正引力模型 $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$ 和 $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$，通过引入标量场与非度量性标量（nonmetricity scalar）之间的非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling）扩展标准 $f(Q)$ 引力；假设尺度因子（scale factor）呈幂律行为，分析重子-熵比随宇宙膨胀参数 $γ$ 的演化。

Result: 对于第一个模型，重子-熵比随 $γ$ 增大单调递减，在 $γ≈0.2$–$0.3$ 范围内无需精细调谐即可复现 $10^{-11}$ 至 $10^{-10}$ 量级的观测重子不对称性；对于第二个模型，在 $α∼10^{-3}$ 至 $10^{-2}$ 且 $β∼10^{-2}$ 至 $10^{-1}$ 的物理合理参数范围内，重子-熵比符合观测约束。

Conclusion: 标量-非度量性引力为重子不对称性起源提供了可行且稳健的理论框架，非线性几何项与标量场耦合之间的相互作用（interplay）在调控重子生成机制中发挥关键作用，为修正引力和早期宇宙学研究开辟了新视角。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate gravitational baryogenesis in the framework of scalar-nonmetricity theories by considering two classes of modified gravity models, namely $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$ and $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$. These models extend standard $f(Q)$ gravity through the inclusion of nonminimal couplings between the scalar field and the nonmetricity scalar, leading to nontrivial modifications of the cosmological dynamics. We analyze the evolution of the baryon-to-entropy ratio in terms of the cosmic expansion parameter $γ$, assuming a power-law behavior of the scale factor. For the first model, we show that the baryon-to-entropy ratio decreases monotonically with increasing $γ$, reflecting the impact of the expansion rate on the efficiency of baryogenesis. The observed baryon asymmetry, of order $10^{-11}$ to $10^{-10}$, is successfully reproduced for $γ\approx 0.2$--$0.3$ without requiring fine-tuning of the model parameters. For the second model, we explore the parameter space of $α$ and $β$, and demonstrate that the correct order of magnitude of the baryon asymmetry can be achieved for physically reasonable values of the parameters. In particular, we find that the baryon-to-entropy ratio lies within observational bounds for $α\sim 10^{-3}$ to $10^{-2}$ and $β\sim 10^{-2}$ to $10^{-1}$, with specific combinations yielding excellent agreement with observations. Overall, our results show that scalar-nonmetricity gravity provides a viable and robust framework for explaining the origin of the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. The interplay between nonlinear geometric terms and scalar field couplings plays a crucial role in controlling the baryogenesis mechanism, opening new perspectives in the study of modified gravity and early Universe cosmology.

### [68] [Non-variational scalar field cosmology: Exact Bianchi I solutions for near-minimal scalar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02078)
*Joshua Ritchie*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦方程与一种非变分“近最小耦合”标量场耦合的空间均匀且平坦的宇宙学解，推导出四个精确的Bianchi I解，发现这些解可产生大爆炸、大挤压、大撕裂以及振荡（循环）行为等多种宇宙学现象，并对解进行了数值稳定性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨爱因斯坦方程与非变分（non-variational）“近最小耦合”（near-minimal）标量场耦合下的空间均匀且平坦的宇宙学解，以研究标准理论的微小偏离——即标量场自相互作用项与其势能导数解耦——所导致的宇宙学后果。

Method: 假设二次势（quadratic potential）以及正比于势能的自相互作用项，推导出四个精确的Bianchi I解；并对这些解进行关于平均曲率（mean curvature）的空间非均匀扰动（spatially inhomogeneous perturbations）的数值稳定性分析。

Result: 得到了四个精确的Bianchi I解，它们可产生大爆炸（Big Bang）、大挤压（Big Crunch）、大撕裂（Big Rip）奇点以及振荡（循环，“cyclic”）行为；且这些奇点在无穷本征时（infinite proper time）发生，因此观测者永远无法真正到达。振荡解和具有挤压奇点的解对空间非均匀扰动不稳定，而具有大撕裂奇点的解（在无穷远处）则是稳定的。

Conclusion: 近最小耦合标量场模型可产生丰富的宇宙学行为，但不同奇点类型的解在稳定性上存在显著差异：具有大撕裂奇点的解表现出稳定性，而振荡和挤压型奇点解则不稳定。

Abstract: The purpose of this work is to investigate spatially homogeneous and flat cosmological solutions of the Einstein equations coupled to a non-variational ``near-minimal'' scalar field. This coupling model represents a minimal departure from standard theory by decoupling the scalar field's self-interaction term from the derivative of its potential. By assuming a quadratic potential and a self-interaction term that is proportional to the potential, we derive four new exact Bianchi I solutions. We demonstrate that these solutions produce a diverse range of cosmological phenomena, including Big Bang, Big Crunch, and Big Rip singularities, as well as oscillatory (``cyclic'') behaviour. For our exact solutions, these singularities occur in infinite proper time and hence are never truly reachable by an observer. To assess the stability of these cosmologies, we perform a numerical stability analysis against spatially inhomogeneous perturbations of the mean curvature. We find that the oscillatory solution is unstable to perturbations of this type, as are solutions in possession of a crushing singularity. Conversely, solutions with a Big Rip singularity (at infinity) are stable to spatially inhomogeneous perturbations of the mean curvature.

### [69] [Spinning charged test particle dynamics around a Schwarzschild black hole embedded in a homogeneous magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02084)
*Misbah Shahzadi,Martin Kolos,Ondrej Zelenka,Georgios Lukes-Gerakopoulos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在浸入均匀磁场的史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）附近，自旋带电测试粒子的动力学行为。通过数值模拟赤道面和赤道面外的运动，分析了自旋-曲率耦合与电磁相互作用对粒子轨道的影响，并在赤道面外发现了由非可积性导致的混沌（chaos）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在磁化天体物理环境（如黑洞吸积盘附近），粒子运动可能同时受到自旋-曲率耦合（spin-curvature coupling）和电磁相互作用（electromagnetic interaction）的影响。该工作旨在建立一个简单但物理相关的框架，以统一理解这两类效应对带电自旋粒子轨道动力学的贡献。

Method: 采用数值方法求解赤道面和赤道面外两种构型下的粒子轨道；在赤道面上推导了守恒能量、角动量以及径向和轨道频率的解析表达式，并构造有效势（effective potential）；针对非可积的赤道面外运动，使用四维庞加莱截面（Poincaré surface of sections, PS）和递归分析（recurrence analysis）研究相空间中的混沌行为。

Result: 在赤道面内，由于时空对称性和磁场对齐，动力学保持可积；在赤道面外，系统仅能降阶至三个自由度，呈现非可积性，并在特定参数和初始条件下出现混沌运动。通过与自旋中性粒子和非自旋带电粒子两种极限子情况的对比，区分了自旋-曲率耦合与电磁相互作用的各自贡献。

Conclusion: 自旋与电荷的共同存在可导致粒子运动从可积过渡到混沌，表明在磁化紧凑天体附近模拟粒子动力学时，必须同时考虑自旋-曲率耦合和电磁相互作用，而不能仅依靠其中一种极限近似。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of spinning charged test particles orbiting a Schwarzschild black hole immersed in a test uniform magnetic field. This setup provides a simple but physically relevant framework for modeling particle motion in magnetized astrophysical environments near compact objects, where both spin-curvature coupling and electromagnetic interactions can play a significant role. The particle trajectories are obtained numerically in both equatorial and off-equatorial configurations, allowing us to examine the influence of spin-curvature and Lorentz forces on the motion. In the equatorial plane, assuming the particle's spin vector is orthogonal to the orbital plane, we derive analytical expressions for the conserved energy and angular momentum, as well as for the radial and orbital frequencies as functions of spin parameter and magnetic parameter. We also construct the corresponding effective potential to determine the allowed regions of particle motion. The equatorial dynamics remain integrable due to the existence of conserved quantities associated with the spacetime symmetries and the alignment of the magnetic field. In contrast, the off-equatorial motion constitutes a non-integrable dynamical system. While limiting subcases of the system, i.e., the spinning neutral and non-spinning charged cases, can be analyzed using two-dimensional Poincaré surface of sections (PSs), the combined system can be reduced only up to three degrees of freedom. Hence, to investigate the resulting complexity, we analyze the phase space using four-dimensional PS along with recurrence analysis, revealing the presence of chaotic behavior for particular choices of parameters and initial conditions. Finally, we compare the dynamics of spinning charged test particles with the limiting cases, thereby distinguishing the respective contributions of spin-curvature and electromagnetic interactions.

### [70] [Helicity-dependent corrections to black-hole shadows from the gravitational spin Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02136)
*C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，黑洞阴影在次领头阶几何光学近似下不再纯粹是几何可观测量：光的自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）会使得不同螺旋度的偏振光在光子球半径附近产生螺旋度依赖的临界碰撞参数偏移，从而导致极化辐射的阴影边界发生分裂。该修正具有解析形式且普适，在极端赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦（Reissner-Nordström）黑洞中可增强至2.5倍；在缓慢旋转的克尔（Kerr）时空中，参考系拖拽效应会引入方位角调制，自旋χ≳0.21时阴影分裂符号可在图像一侧反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在领头阶几何光学近似下，黑洞阴影被视为纯几何量，其边界由零测地线（null geodesics）决定，且不携带探测辐射的偏振信息。本文旨在突破这一传统认知，考察次领头阶修正下引力自旋霍尔效应对黑洞阴影边界的影响，揭示偏振信息如何进入阴影结构。

Method: 从自旋霍尔运动方程（spin Hall equations of motion）出发，推导出临界碰撞参数的螺旋度依赖修正；通过数值射线追踪（ray-tracing）计算进行验证；将分析推广至带荷的赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦黑洞；对缓慢旋转的克尔时空发展微扰处理方法。

Result: 螺旋度依赖的阴影边界分裂效应是解析且普适的，修正量正比于1/ω，仅依赖于光子球半径处的一个几何函数。在极端赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦黑洞中，效应可放大至2.5倍。在克尔时空中，参考系拖拽引入cosφ调制，自旋χ≳0.21时阴影分裂在图像一侧发生符号反转。

Conclusion: 尽管效应幅值较小，但其概念性含义明确：黑洞阴影并非纯粹的几何可观测量，次领头阶的偏振效应从根本上改变了阴影的几何光学图像。

Abstract: Black-hole shadows are purely geometric in the leading-order geometric-optics approximation: their boundary is set by null geodesics and carries no information about the polarization of the probing radiation. This changes at subleading order. We show that the gravitational spin Hall effect of light shifts the critical impact parameter governing photon capture by a helicity-dependent amount, causing polarized radiation with opposite helicities to trace slightly different shadow boundaries -- even in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes. The correction is analytic, universal, and scales as $1/ω$: it depends only on a single geometric function evaluated at the photon-sphere radius. We derive this result from the spin Hall equations of motion, confirm it numerically through ray-tracing calculations, and extend the analysis to Reissner-Nordström black holes, where electric charge amplifies the effect by up to a factor of $2.5$ at extremality. We further develop a perturbative treatment for slowly rotating (Kerr) spacetimes, showing that frame dragging introduces a $\cos\varphi$ modulation of the shadow splitting that can reverse its sign on one side of the image for spins $χ\gtrsim 0.21$. Although the magnitude of the effect is small, the conceptual implication is clear: black-hole shadows are not purely geometric observables.

</details>


### [71] [Bondi and Novikov-Thorne accretion in regular black holes and Simpson-Visser spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02425)
*Serena Gambino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文比较了Bondi球状吸积模型（Bondi spherical accretion model）与Novikov-Thorne薄盘形式（Novikov-Thorne thin disc formalism）在正则黑洞（regular black hole）和Simpson-Visser时空（Simpson-Visser spacetime）中的表现，使用多种吸积流体状态方程（equation of state）。Bondi模型对时空几何和状态方程更为敏感，能更有效区分正则解与经典解；而Simpson-Visser解中，正则化参数ℓ对临界点位置的影响具有双向性，且电荷Q的效应不及ℓ显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在检验正则黑洞和Simpson-Visser时空背景下，不同吸积模型（Bondi模型与Novikov-Thorne模型）对时空几何和流体状态方程的敏感度差异，从而评估哪种模型更适合作为区分正则解与经典黑洞解的工具。

Method: 采用Bondi球状吸积模型和Novikov-Thorne薄盘形式两种吸积框架，针对正则黑洞和Simpson-Visser时空，分别引入多种吸积流体状态方程进行比较分析。

Result: Bondi模型比Novikov-Thorne模型对时空几何和状态方程更为敏感，因此更能有效区分正则黑洞解与经典黑洞解。在Simpson-Visser解中，增大正则化参数ℓ会使临界点位置既向内也向外移动；而带电的Simpson-Visser扩展（由电荷Q描述）产生的效应不如ℓ显著。

Conclusion: 在区分正则黑洞与经典黑洞解方面，Bondi吸积模型优于Novikov-Thorne薄盘模型；Simpson-Visser时空中的关键控制参数是正则化参数ℓ，而非电荷Q。

Abstract: We compare the Bondi spherical accretion model and the Novikov-Thorne thin disc formalism around regular black holes and Simpson-Visser spacetimes, using several equations of state for the accreting fluids. The Bondi model is significantly more sensitive to spacetime geometry and the equation of state, making it more effective at distinguishing between regular and classical solutions. For the Simpson-Visser solutions, however, increasing the regularisation parameter, $\ell$, shifts critical point positions both inward and outward. However, the charged Simpson-Visser extension, modeled by the charge $Q$, does not produce an effect comparable to that of $\ell$.

### [72] [Black Hole Thermodynamics via Tsallis Statistical Mechanics and Phase Transitions Probed by Optical Characteristics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02429)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Tsallis非广延统计力学（Tsallis non-extensive statistical mechanics）应用于黑洞热力学，以通过非广延参数$q$引入长程引力关联，从而超越标准面积律框架，揭示黑洞系统的更丰富热力学行为。

Method: 采用近视界光子气体模型（near-horizon photon-gas model），基于Tsallis统计力学推导出Reissner-Nordström黑洞的$q$-广义熵，并将光子球轨道周期和Lyapunov指数等光学可观测映射为热力学量，建立光学-热力学对应（optical–thermodynamic correspondence）。

Result: 得到的广义熵在符合面积律的同时，展现出小、中、大黑洞三个分支，并呈现范德瓦耳斯型（Van der Waals-like）相变，其临界指数为平均场（mean-field）标度；光学信号在定性层面复现了该热力学相结构。

Conclusion: 该框架将非广延熵、相变与天体物理光学联系起来，为强引力热力学提供了新视角，并暗示未来干涉实验可能通过光学特征对黑洞热力学相变进行观测检验。

Abstract: We investigate black hole thermodynamics within Tsallis non-extensive statistical mechanics using a near-horizon photon-gas model. We derive a $q$-generalized entropy for Reissner--Nordström black holes that is consistent with the area law while incorporating long-range gravitational correlations via the non-extensivity parameter $q$. The resulting thermodynamics exhibits three branches (small, intermediate, and large black holes) with Van der Waals-like phase transitions characterized by mean-field critical exponents. Furthermore, we demonstrate an optical--thermodynamic correspondence by mapping photon-sphere observables, such as orbital periods and Lyapunov exponents, to thermodynamic quantities. The optical signatures qualitatively reproduce the thermodynamic phase structure, suggesting potential observational probes in future interferometric experiments. This framework connects non-extensive entropy, phase transitions, and astrophysical optics, providing a new perspective on strong-gravity thermodynamics.

### [73] [Testing General Relativity Through Gravitational Wave Classification: A Convolutional Neural Network Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02453)
*Lavinia Heisenberg,Shayan Hemmatyar,Hector Villarrubia-Rojo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于机器学习的框架，用于从双黑洞并合引力波信号中检验广义相对论（GR）。通过引入响应函数（response function）形式体系，并训练卷积神经网络（CNN），该框架能够有效区分GR波形与包含受控相位变形（beyond GR, BGR）的波形。以响应函数作为输入表示，CNN的分类灵敏度比白化波形（whitened waveforms）提升了约33倍，并能在超低信噪比下探测引力的偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波检验广义相对论的方法对微弱偏离的探测灵敏度有限，且缺乏统一的形式体系来量化不同可观测量对GR修正的响应。因此，作者旨在开发一种机器学习框架，系统性地提升对超越广义相对论（BGR）信号——特别是微小的相位变形——的探测能力。

Method: 利用GWTC星表中173个双黑洞并合（BBH）事件的源参数生成真实的模拟GR波形，并施加受控相位变形构建BGR波形。引入响应函数（response function）形式体系，量化可观测量对GR修正的响应。将卷积神经网络（CNN）应用于两种输入表示：白化波形（whitened waveforms）和基于波形失配（waveform mismatch）导出的响应函数型可观测量。此外，通过贝叶斯最优误差分析、噪声中相干模式的平均方法，以及与单一特征分类器（作为人类表现的代理）的对比，研究分类的基本极限。

Result: 使用响应函数作为CNN输入，分类灵敏度比白化波形提升了约33倍，表明可观测量表示的选择与分类器架构同样重要。在所有变形尺度上，CNN的性能均优于最佳的单一特征分类器。将该框架推广到参数化后爱因斯坦（ppE）形式体系并应用于大质量引力理论（massive gravity），CNN能够在aLIGO设计灵敏度下探测到引力子质量（graviton mass）量级约为$m_g \sim 10^{-23}\;\mathrm{eV}/c^2$的偏离。

Conclusion: 该机器学习框架通过巧妙的输入表示设计（响应函数）显著提升了引力波检验GR的灵敏度。可观测量表示的选择是影响分类性能的关键因素，且神经网络方法优于传统单一特征方法。该框架可推广至多种物理激励理论，为未来引力波天文学中的基础物理检验提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We present a machine learning framework for testing general relativity (GR) with gravitational wave signals from binary black hole mergers. Using the source parameters of 173 BBH events from the GWTC catalog as a realistic astrophysical population, we generate simulated GR waveforms and construct beyond GR (BGR) waveforms by applying controlled phase deformations. We introduce a response function formalism that provides a systematic framework for quantifying how any observable responds to modifications of GR. We train convolutional neural networks (CNNs) on two input representations: whitened waveforms and a response function type observable derived from the waveform mismatch, which isolates the effect of phase deviations from the bulk signal. Using response functions as the CNN input improves the classification sensitivity by a factor of approximately 33 compared to whitened waveforms, demonstrating that the choice of observable representation is as important as the classifier architecture. We study the fundamental limits of this classification through Bayes optimal error analysis, averaging methods that reveal coherent patterns hidden in noise, and a comparison between CNN accuracy and a single feature classifier as a proxy for human performance. At all deformation scales, the CNN outperforms the best single feature approach. We extend the framework to physically motivated theories using the parameterized post Einsteinian (ppE) formalism and apply it to massive gravity, where the classifier detects deviations for graviton masses of order $m_g \sim 10^{-23}\;\mathrm{eV}/c^2$ with aLIGO design sensitivity.

Abstract: We construct slowly rotating traversable wormholes in the presence of an anisotropic fluid. Starting from a Teo-type stationary, axisymmetric extension of the Morris-Thorne metric, we perform a slow-rotation expansion, fix a gauge that preserves the geometric meaning of the radial coordinate, and introduce two complementary prescriptions for treating the throat (fixed and free). Abstract: We study the axial (magnetic) tidal Love numbers of a Schwarzschild black hole surrounded by a spherically symmetric matter distribution. While the formalism developed here is general, we specialize to the case of anisotropic fluids as a proxy for dark matter distributions, computing the Love numbers for different density profiles of astrophysical interest. We employ two complementary methods: a small-compactness expansion, yielding closed-form analytic expressions, and direct numerical integration of the perturbation equations. We discuss the connection between different formulations of the fluid perturbations and the resulting Love numbers. We further show that density profiles lacking compact support generically produce logarithmic terms in the asymptotic expansion of the perturbation variable, which obstruct the standard tidal matching procedure and whose origin we trace to the absence of a strictly vacuum exterior. Our findings highlight the importance of controlling the asymptotic structure of the matter distribution when defining tidal observables for black holes dressed by matter, and provide a general framework that can be applied to other spherically symmetric environments.

### [77] [Hadronic lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02807)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非线性西格玛模型与麦克斯韦理论最小耦合描述强子介质；推导包含强子修正的雷乔杜里方程；在程函近似下求解探针光子的积分曲线；以超流π子涡旋（superfluid pionic vortices）驱动的解析黑洞模型为例进行验证。

Conclusion: 该解析框架能够自洽描述强子介质中的引力透镜效应，建立了强子微观参数与宏观透镜观测之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We introduce an analytic approach to study gravitational lensing in the presence of a distribution of hadrons. The situation is analogous to the propagation of photons in a medium with a nontrivial Cooper-pair condensate, where the photon acquires an effective mass term that may depend on the coordinates if the condensate is not homogeneous. As a result, photons generally do not follow null geodesics in the hadronic medium. In this setup, hadrons are described by the nonlinear sigma model minimally coupled to Maxwell theory. The modified Raychaudhuri equation, including hadronic corrections, is derived, along with the integral curves of probe photons in the eikonal approximation. These results are consistent with the theory of gravitational lensing in plasma media, with the advantage that transport properties, such as the refractive index, can be expressed analytically in terms of the hadronic density without assuming a phenomenological modeling thereof. As an example, we study the hadronic lensing produced by an analytic black hole sourced by superfluid pionic vortices, and we obtain the hadronic correction to the deflection angle in the weak-field limit.

### [78] [Derivation of the Smarr formula from the Komar charge in Einstein-nonlinear electrodynamics theories and applications to regular black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02813)
*Gabriele Barbagallo,Tomás Ortín*

TL;DR: 本文构造了四维爱因斯坦引力耦合非线性电动力学（NLED）的广义Komar荷，并通过将耦合常数提升为动力学场并施加拉格朗日乘子约束，导出了包含该耦合常数贡献的Smarr公式，进而分析了规则Bardeen黑洞的热力学行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非线性电动力学（NLED）与爱因斯坦引力耦合的理论中，量纲耦合常数对Komar荷和Smarr公式的贡献此前仅通过齐次性论证（homogeneity arguments）得到，缺乏一般性构造方法。本文旨在建立一种系统框架，以广义Komar荷统一导出包含耦合常数贡献的Smarr公式，并用于分析规则黑洞的热力学性质。

Method: 将非线性电动力学理论中的量纲耦合常数提升为一个动力学场，并引入拉格朗日乘子（Lagrange multiplier）强制其在壳（on-shell）保持恒定，从而构造广义Komar荷。利用该广义Komar荷推导适用于渐近平坦黑洞和孤立子解（soliton solutions）的包含耦合常数贡献的Smarr公式。

Result: 成功构造了四维爱因斯坦-NLED理论中的广义Komar荷，并导出了包含耦合常数贡献的Smarr公式。该结果与之前基于齐次性论证的结论一致。在广泛的Einstein-NLED理论类别上验证了该公式，并通过对规则Bardeen黑洞的详细热力学分析，利用广义Komar荷的守恒性解释了规则黑洞在事件视界（event horizon）内部的规则性。

Conclusion: 提出了一种系统的方法，通过将耦合常数动力学化并借助拉格朗日乘子约束，构造广义Komar荷并导出包含耦合常数贡献的Smarr公式，为非线性电动力学-引力系统中的黑洞热力学提供了一般的框架。该工作还深化了对规则黑洞内部正则性机制的理解。

Abstract: We construct the generalized Komar charge of generic, non-linear theories of electrodynamics (NLED) in 4 dimensions coupled to Einstein gravity. The contribution of the dimensionful coupling constant present in all these theories is obtained by promoting it to a dynamical field which is forced to be constant on-shell by a Lagrange multiplier. We use this charge to derive a Smarr formula for asymptotically-flat black-hole and soliton solutions of these theories that includes the contribution of the coupling constant. Previously, this contribution had been found using homogeneity arguments. We test our results on a broad class of Einstein--NLED theories and analyze in detail the thermodynamics of the regular Bardeen black hole using the conservation of the generalized Komar charge to understand the regularity of regular black holes inside the event horizon.

</details>


### [79] [Gravitational-Bumblebee perturbations: Exact decoupling and isospectrality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02820)
*Hui-Fa Liu,Wentao Liu,Yu-Xiao Liu,Qi Su,Ding-fang Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在类史瓦西（Schwarzschild-like）背景下实现了完整度规与大黄蜂场（bumblebee field）扰动的精确解耦，得到四个解耦主方程，并发现引力主模式对非最小洛伦兹破缺耦合具有“动力学免疫”（dynamical immunity），奇偶宇称扰动保持严格等谱（isospectral），尽管洛伦兹破缺向量模式的传播速度被修改。

Method: 通过对类史瓦西背景下的完整度规和大黄蜂场扰动进行精确解析解耦，将耦合系统约化为四个解耦主方程（master equations），分别对应每个宇称宇称（parity sector）下的类史瓦西引力扇区（gravitational sector）和类麦克斯韦洛伦兹破缺矢量扇区（Lorentz-violating Maxwell-like vector sector）。

Result: 引力主模式对非最小洛伦兹破缺耦合表现出动力学免疫，奇偶宇称扰动保持严格等谱；洛伦兹破缺仅修改了矢量模式的传播速度，而引力铃宕（ringdown）频谱保持不变。两类模式的传播速度失配暗示了可观测的时间差特征。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个洛伦兹破缺耦合重构场却不改变引力铃宕频谱的罕见范例，并指出传播速度失配可作为探测大黄蜂矢量动力学（bumblebee vector dynamics）的时序特征，为多信使天文学（multi-messenger astronomy）时代检验自发洛伦兹对称性破缺提供了理论途径。

Abstract: In this paper, we present the exact decoupling of the full metric and bumblebee field perturbations in a Schwarzschild-like background. The coupled system reduces to four decoupled master equations, revealing in each parity sector a Schwarzschild-like gravitational sector and a Lorentz-violating Maxwell-like vector sector. While Lorentz violation modifies the propagation speed of the emergent vector modes, we demonstrate that the gravitational master modes exhibit a ``dynamical immunity'' to the non-minimal Lorentz-violating coupling, and that the odd- and even-parity perturbations remain strictly isospectral. Our work provides a rare example in which Lorentz-violating couplings reshape the field reconstruction while leaving the gravitational ringdown spectrum intact. This mismatch in propagation speeds suggests a possible timing signature of bumblebee vector dynamics in black hole perturbations, offering a theoretical route to testing spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking in the era of multi-messenger astronomy.

### [81] [Defect Triangles and Intersection-Space Hodge Atom Shadows for Calabi--Yau Conifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01455)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文针对射影Calabi-Yau三维流形锥化退化（conifold degeneration）证明了一个投影-三角语句（projection-triangle statement），并利用该语句构建了交空间（intersection-space）的Hodge原子包（Hodge atom shadow package）。在多种理论假设下，通过变分态射（variation morphism）的投影和八面体公理（octahedral axiom），该包与交上同调包（intersection-homology package）进行了比较，并在自偶特殊化-分裂假设下建立了对偶关系。对于经典125节点五次流形，中间度数的IC-交空间缺陷秩为202，识别出用于未来DT/BPS比较的几何传递对象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究射影Calabi-Yau三维流形锥化退化中交空间的Hodge原子结构，并建立其与交上同调包之间的系统比较框架，为未来DT/BPS（Donaldson-Thomas/Bogomol'nyi–Prasad–Sommerfield）对偶比较提供几何传递对象。

Method: 证明了一个投影-三角语句（projection-triangle statement），利用八面体公理（octahedral axiom）构造了交空间Hodge原子包（intersection-space Hodge atom shadow package）$\mathsf{HA}^{I}(X_0)$，并与交上同调包（intersection-homology package）$\mathsf{HA}^{IH}(X_0)$进行对比。在自偶特殊化-分裂假设下，通过对偶性$\mathbb D P^H_I\simeq Q^H_I(3)$实现刚-消失滤过（rigid–vanishing filtration）的隔离。

Result: 对于经典125节点五次流形（$125$-node quintic），中间度数的IC-交空间缺陷（IC–intersection-space defect）的秩为$202$。识别出$\mathcal C^H_Σ$和$Δ_{I/IC}(X_0)$作为几何传递对象。

Conclusion: 该构造保持在Hodge实现（Hodge realization）层面，所识别的几何传递对象为未来DT/BPS比较提供了基础。这一框架将锥化退化的代数与几何结构系统化地联系起来。

Abstract: We prove a projection-triangle statement for projective Calabi--Yau threefold conifold degenerations and use it to organize an intersection-space Hodge atom shadow package. This realizes the intersection-space atom shadow package $\mathsf{HA}^{I}(X_0)$ and compares it with the intersection-homology package $\mathsf{HA}^{IH}(X_0)$. Under the self-dual specialization-splitting hypothesis, the projected variation object satisfies $\mathbb D P^H_I\simeq Q^H_I(3)$, where $Q^H_I=\operatorname{Cone}(\operatorname{can}_I)[-1]$. Under the mixed-Hodge realization of Banagl's middle exact sequence, we isolate a rigid--vanishing filtration and identify the IIB vanishing atom with the realized kernel. For the classical $125$-node quintic, the middle-degree IC--intersection-space defect has rank $202$. The construction remains at Hodge-realization level and identifies $\mathcal C^H_Σ$ and $Δ_{I/IC}(X_0)$ as geometry-side handoff objects for future DT/BPS comparisons.
