### [82] [From Finite-Node Conifold Geometry to BPS Structures III: Mediated Triangle Transport and Graded Interaction Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02704)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文在前期工作提取的有限节点锥形退化（conifold degeneration）状态数据包 $A_\Sigma=(V_\Sigma,E_\Sigma,c_\Sigma)$ 基础上，引入下一层结构：一种分级成对相互作用包（graded pairwise interaction package），通过定义介导三角传输（mediated triangle transport, MTT）来精炼二元支撑信息。MTT 结合体介导的 schober 传输、局域探针、校正扩展阴影相容性及导出相互作用预函子（derived interaction profunctors），构造了相互作用复形 $\mathsf H_{ij}$ 及其上同调多项式 $P_{ij}(q)$，从而形成首个分级相互作用输入 $I_\Sigma^{\mathrm{gr}}$，为后续稳定性、BPS态及壁穿越（wall-crossing）理论奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期工作仅记录了支撑矩阵（support matrix）中是否存在介导通道，但未能刻画该通道的导出大小（derived size）、上同调次数（cohomological degree）或正合三角行为（exact-triangle behavior）。因此，本文动机在于引入一种更精细的相互作用结构，以弥补二元支撑信息的不足，并首次提供分级相互作用输入。

Method: 定义了介导三角传输（MTT），其包含四个组成部分：体介导的 schober 传输、局域探针（localized probes）、校正扩展阴影相容性（corrected-extension shadow compatibility）以及导出相互作用预函子（derived interaction profunctors）。对于每个有序对 $(i,j)$，构造 $\mathbb T_{ij}(X,Y):=\RHom_{\mathcal C_{p_j}}(\Psi_j\Phi_i(X),Y)$ 及探针相互作用复形 $\mathsf H_{ij}:=\mathbb T_{ij}(L_i,L_j)$。在有限 Hom-有界（bounded Hom-finite）约定下，定义上同调多项式 $P_{ij}(q)=\sum_m \dim H^m(\mathsf H_{ij})q^m$，并将其组装为 $I_\Sigma^{\mathrm{gr}}$。

Result: 证明了正合性及长正合相互作用序列（long exact interaction sequences），分离出一个三角可见非平凡判据（triangle-visible nonvanishing criterion），并表述了一个条件性桥定理（conditional bridge theorem），表明在规定的探针、内容与检测器假设下，支撑通道会产生非平凡的成对相互作用复形。由此得到的分级相互作用包 $(A_\Sigma,I_\Sigma^{(0/1)},I_\Sigma^{\mathrm{gr}})$ 构成了后续理论的首个分级输入。

Conclusion: 本文构建的分级成对相互作用包 $I_\Sigma^{\mathrm{gr}}$ 作为前期支撑数据的精炼推广，为后续的稳定性理论、BPS态计数及壁穿越理论提供了必要的分级相互作用输入。该框架为从二元支撑信息走向更丰富的上同调相互作用描述奠定了基础。

Abstract: In previous work, we extracted from a finite-node conifold degeneration the state-data package $A_Σ=(V_Σ,E_Σ,c_Σ)$ and then constructed the support-level interaction package encoded by a binary incidence structure and finite quiver-theoretic skeleton \cite{RahmanQuiverDataI,RahmanQuiverDataII}. The present paper introduces the next layer: a graded pairwise interaction package refining binary support. Since the support matrix records where a mediated channel is present, but not its derived size, cohomological degree, or exact-triangle behavior, we introduce \emph{mediated triangle transport} (MTT). An MTT datum combines bulk-mediated schober transport, localized probes, corrected-extension shadow compatibility, and derived interaction profunctors. For each ordered pair $(i,j)$, it produces $\mathbb T_{ij}(X,Y):=\RHom_{\mathcal C_{p_j}}(Ψ_jΦ_i(X),Y)$ and the probe interaction complex $\mathsf H_{ij}:=\mathbb T_{ij}(L_i,L_j)=\RHom_{\mathcal C_{p_j}}(Ψ_jΦ_i(L_i),L_j)$. We prove exactness and long exact interaction sequences, isolate a triangle-visible nonvanishing criterion, and formulate a conditional bridge theorem showing that supported channels yield nontrivial pairwise interaction complexes under the stated probe, content, and detector hypotheses. Under a bounded Hom-finite convention, the cohomology of $\mathsf H_{ij}$ defines $P_{ij}(q)=\sum_m \dim H^m(\mathsf H_{ij})q^m$, and these polynomials assemble into $I_Σ^{\mathrm{gr}}$. Thus $(A_Σ,I_Σ^{(0/1)},I_Σ^{\mathrm{gr}})$ provides the first graded interaction input for later stability, BPS, and wall-crossing theory.

Method: 采用变换器（transformer）模型，以低能谱（low-energy spectra）为输入特征，预测张量积理论（tensor product theory）的组成成分。组成理论由中心荷（central charge）和仿射李代数标记（affine Lie algebra labels）表征。通过加入少量领域外（out-of-domain）样本，提升模型对更大中心荷和未见过的有理共形场论（rational conformal field theories, RCFTs）类别的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 变换器在该组合重构任务上表现有效，为AdS/CFT对偶中的体态重构提供了一种新的潜在工具。

Abstract: We study the use of transformers to reconstruct the compositions of tensor products of two-dimensional rational conformal field theories (RCFTs) based on their low-energy spectra. The task is challenging due to its combinatorial nature. The constituent theories are characterized by their central charges and affine Lie algebra labels. We achieve 98% accuracy in recovering the constituents of tensor products theories constructed from Wess-Zumino-Witten models. We further demonstrate that our method generalizes to CFTs with larger central charge and unseen classes of RCFTs by adding a small number of out-of-domain examples. Our results show that transformers are effective at this task and point towards a new tool for bulk reconstruction in AdS/CFT.

### [85] [Twist Operator BOPE and Entanglement Entropy in 2D Interface CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01150)
*Mianqi Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文利用复制方法（replica method）研究了二维界面共形场论（2D interface CFT）中的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy），通过分析Rényi扭转算符（Rényi twist operator）的边界OPE（BOPE），发现了一个锚定在界面上（interface）的边界扭转算符（boundary twist operator），并以此给出了纠缠熵的O(1)贡献。文中进一步分析了不同区间的纠缠熵，并与先前的全息（holographic）结果进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用复制方法（replica method），具体通过对Rényi扭转算符（Rényi twist operator）施加边界OPE（BOPE）展开，发现了一个锚定在界面（interface）上的边界扭转算符（boundary twist operator），从而导出纠缠熵的O(1)贡献表达式。

Result: 以BOPE系数（BOPE coefficients）的形式给出了纠缠熵的O(1)贡献；进一步分析了不同区间（intervals）下的纠缠熵行为，并与先前的全息（holographic）结果进行了对比。

Conclusion: 研究表明，界面共形场论（interface CFT）中纠缠熵的O(1)贡献可由Rényi扭转算符的边界OPE（BOPE）系数完整描述，且其行为与全息（holographic）计算结果相符，证实了该方法的有效性。

Abstract: We address several aspects of entanglement entropy of 2D interface CFT using the replica method. Unlike the case of boundary CFT, we consider the boundary OPE (BOPE) of the Rényi twist operator and find a boundary twist operator anchored on the interface. This approach gives the $O(1)$ contribution to the entanglement entropy in terms of the BOPE coefficients of the twist operator. We further analyze entanglement entropy of different intervals and compare our findings with previous holographic results.

</details>


### [86] [Exact WKB and Quantum Periods for Extremal Black Hole Quasinormal Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01321)
*Yasuyuki Hatsuda,Tomohito Shiga*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将精确WKB分析（exact WKB analysis）应用于黑洞微扰理论中的谱问题，通过求解准正则模（quasinormal modes）的精确量子化条件，并利用Borel–Padé求和（Borel–Padé resummation）对极端Reissner–Nordström与Kerr黑洞标量扰动的WKB展开进行高阶计算，高精度地复现了准正则模频率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞准正则模（quasinormal modes）的频谱问题是黑洞微扰理论的核心，但传统WKB方法在精度和收敛性上存在局限。本文旨在通过精确WKB分析（exact WKB analysis）建立更严格的量子化条件，并借助Borel–Padé求和克服WKB展开的发散性，从而高精度求解复频率。

Method: 首先，将黑洞准正则模的边界条件转化为精确的量子化条件（exact quantization conditions），其中需要计算所谓的量子周期（quantum periods）或Voros符号（Voros symbols）。然后，针对极端Reissner–Nordström与Kerr黑洞的标量扰动，在WKB展开中将这些量计算到极高阶，并执行Borel–Padé求和（Borel–Padé resummation）以获得收敛结果。

Result: 通过Borel–Padé求和后的量子化条件成功且高精度地复现了正确的准正则模频率（quasinormal mode frequencies）。

Conclusion: 精确WKB分析结合Borel–Padé求和是一种有效的高精度方法，可求解黑洞准正则模的复频谱，为极端Reissner–Nordström与Kerr黑洞的标量扰动谱问题提供了可靠的计算框架。

Abstract: We apply exact WKB analysis to the spectral problem arising in black hole perturbation theory. The boundary conditions for quasinormal modes lead to exact quantization conditions for the complex frequencies. To solve these conditions, one needs to evaluate the so-called quantum periods, or Voros symbols. For scalar perturbations of extremal Reissner--Nordström and Kerr black holes, we compute these quantities up to very high orders in the WKB expansion and perform Borel--Padé resummation. The resulting resummed quantization conditions successfully reproduce the correct quasinormal mode frequencies with high precision.

</details>


### [87] [Hidden gauge invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01453)
*Karl-Henning Rehren*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在无需先验假设规范不变性的前提下，仅基于量子力学原理（特别是希尔伯特空间表示）重新推导标准模型粒子间的可重整化相互作用，并发现多数满足约束的相互作用隐含精确且未被破缺的“隐藏规范不变性”（hidden gauge invariance），即使在存在有质量矢量玻色子（massive vector bosons）时依然成立。该研究采用弦局域化相互作用（string-localized interactions）确保S矩阵（S-matrix）与弦无关，从而在不依赖不定度规空间（indefinite state spaces）和鬼场（ghosts）的框架下统一描述有质量与无质量的矢量玻色子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 规范不变性（gauge invariance）在粒子物理标准模型中被视为基本假设，但其根源与必要性问题尚未完全澄清。本文旨在探究能否不预先假设规范不变性而仅从量子原理出发推导出相互作用的约束，从而提供一种更自治且更基础的理解路径。

Method: 采用自治方法（autonomous approach），不预先假定规范不变性，而是基于希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）上的量子表示原理来约束可重整化相互作用（renormalizable interactions）。通过量子场的重新定义（redefinitions of quantum fields），揭示出满足约束的相互作用中隐藏的规范对称性；并引入弦局域化相互作用（string-localized interactions）以保证S矩阵的弦无关性。

Result: 发现大多数满足希尔伯特空间表示约束的可重整化相互作用隐含着精确且未破缺的规范不变性；即使存在有质量矢量玻色子，该隐藏规范不变性依然成立。此外，弦局域化框架下的S矩阵与不定度规空间中规范理论（gauge theory）的局域相互作用S矩阵一致。

Conclusion: 基于希尔伯特空间的自治方法表明，规范不变性并非必要的基本假设，而是量子原理的自然推论。有质量与无质量矢量玻色子的粒子物理学可以在不引入不定度规空间或鬼场的框架下得到统一理解。

Abstract: The role of gauge invariance is reconsidered by "deriving it without assuming it" within an autonomous approach to interactions of Standard Model particles. In this approach, the renormalizable interactions are purely constrained by quantum principles, notably the representation on a Hilbert space. It is shown that - surprisingly - most interactions fulfilling the constraints enjoy a "hidden" gauge invariance (uncovered via redefinitions of quantum fields). The hidden gauge invariance is exact and unbroken even in the presence of massive vector bosons. While the Hilbert space formulation requires the use of "string-localized interactions", its role is to secure that S-matrices are string-independent, and in fact coincide with S-matrices with local interactions from the gauge theory approach on indefinite state spaces. Thus, particle physics with massless and massive vector bosons can be understood without neither indefinite state spaces nor ghosts.

</details>


### [88] [Reductions in Khovanov-Rozansky operator formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01584)
*D. Galakhov,E. Lanina,A. Morozov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出将高阶Khovanov-Rozansky（KhR）纽结不变量理论重新表述为一个双层上同调（double cohomology）框架，其中“垂直”上同调由局部构造的幂零算子D定义，而“水平”上同调通过共轭变换χ(±)连接，最终组合成KhR多项式。该构造在全局上依赖于整个纽结图，但其所有构建模块（算子与态射）均具有局域性，从而允许局部约化，特别是在反平行锁缠结（antiparallel-lock tangles）和二分图（bipartite）情形下可实现从双复形到单复形的全局约化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Khovanov-Rozansky（KhR）理论中反直觉的矩阵分解（matrix factorization）替换为具有明确物理意义的局部算子，使复杂的不变量构造更直观且易于约化。

Method: 采用双复形（bicomplex）框架：为每个MOY分解（MOY resolution）局部构造幂零算子D，定义“垂直”上同调；通过共轭变换χ(±)连接不同分辨率的态射，沿超立方体（hypercube）边定义“水平”上同调；最终组合为KhR多项式。

Result: 所有构建模块（算子D与态射χ(±)）均为局域定义，但结果上同调全局依赖于整个纽结图；在Reidemeister等价、反平行锁缠结以及N=2及任意N的二分图情形下，可实现局部或全局约化，后者将KhR双复形约化为Khovanov（类）单复形。

Conclusion: 该局域构造为KhR理论提供了更简洁的物理诠释，并通过局部约化机制简化了计算，特别在二分图情形下建立了与经典Khovanov同调的直接联系。

Abstract: Sophisticated Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) description of knot invariants in the fundamental representation can be reformulated in terms of bicomplex with a simple physical meaning. Namely, the counterintuitive matrix factorization is substituted by simple operators $D$, locally constructed for every MOY resolution of a link diagram, which becomes nilpotent when the diagram has no external lines. Operators for different resolutions are related by equally simple conjugations $χ^{(\pm)}$. The KhR procedure then splits in two steps - defining ``vertical'' cohomologies of $D$, which are associated with particular resolutions and will be put at vertices of the hypercube, and conjugations $χ^{(\pm)}$, that define morphisms along its edges. As usual, standard combinations of morphisms are nilpotent, and one can define ``horizontal'' cohomologies - which are then combined into Poincaré polynomial, called KhR polynomial in application to links. This construction remains global in the sense that resulting cohomologies depend on the entire link diagram, but all its building blocks, including the operators and morphisms are local in the sense that they are defined for its particular vertices. Sometimes, this allows simple local reductions, allowing to eliminate or change particular vertices or sets of those. Along with the obvious case of Reidemeister equivalencies this happens also for antiparallel-lock tangles, what is responsible for simplification of bipartite calculus. In the $N=2$ and arbitrary $N$ bipartite cases, one can also provide global reductions transferring the local construction of the KhR double-complex to the global construction of the Khovanov(-like) single-complex.

</details>


### [89] [Higher-derivative $\mathcal{N}=1$ and $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric Maxwell-Chern-Simons theories at one loop in superspace](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01661)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用背景场量子化（background field quantization）方法，在高阶导数 $R_ξ$ 规范（higher-derivative $R_ξ$ gauge）下进行超场计算。高阶导数算子被定义为达朗贝尔算子的任意次多项式函数，且仅引入到规范扇区（gauge sector）中。

Conclusion: 论文表明，在高阶导数推广的麦克斯韦-陈-西蒙斯理论中，单圈有效势可以完全解析地求出，其形式依赖于多项式算子的根结构，这为理解高阶导数规范理论的量子性质提供了系统框架。

Abstract: We define a higher-derivative generalization of Maxwell-Chern-Simons theory in $\mathcal{N}=1$ and $\mathcal{N}=2$ superspaces. In particular, the chosen higher-derivative operator is a polynomial function of the d'Alembertian of arbitrary degree, and it is introduced exclusively in the gauge sector. The main goal is to explicitly compute the one-loop quantum corrections to the superfield effective potential for these theories. This is carried out by means of background field quantization in a higher-derivative $R_ξ$ gauge. The effective potential is obtained in closed form and expressed in terms of the roots of polynomial functions.

### [90] [A Non-local "Boundary'' Term for Two-Point Amplitudes in String Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01784)
*Yasu Gen,Hiroaki Matsunaga,Jojiro Totsuka*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在自由玻色子弦场论（free bosonic string field theory）中引入一种新的“边界”项（boundary term），该项通过BRST算符与阶跃函数算符的对易子构造为双线性形式，旨在恢复因插入弦性阶跃函数算符（stringy step-function operator）而破坏的循环性（cyclicity）。该边界项使作用量具有良好定义的变分原理（variational principle），并在壳（on-shell）弦场上正确再现了开弦与闭弦的树级两点振幅（tree-level two-point amplitude），在快子（tachyon）和无质量（massless）扇区中得到明确验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自由玻色子弦场论中，弦性阶跃函数算符的插入破坏了作用量的循环性，需要引入一项修正来恢复该性质。

Method: 构造一个双线性形式（bilinear form），具体涉及BRST算符（BRST operator）与阶跃函数算符（step-function operator）的对易子（commutator），作为新边界项。

Result: 所得作用量具有良好定义的变分原理；在壳弦场上，该边界项正确还原了开弦与闭弦的树级两点振幅，并在快子与无质量扇区中得到显式验证。

Conclusion: 所提出的边界项有效恢复了被弦性阶跃函数算符破坏的循环性，并确保了作用量的变分一致性以及振幅的正确性。

Abstract: We propose a new ``boundary'' term in free bosonic string field theory. Here, the term ``boundary'' refers to a contribution introduced to restore the cyclicity broken by the insertion of a stringy step-function operator, although it is not strictly localized as it involves an operator that selects positive-energy modes. We construct this term as a bilinear form involving the commutator of the BRST operator with the step-function operator. The resulting action has a well-defined variational principle. When evaluated on on-shell string fields, the proposed term reproduces the correct tree-level two-point amplitude for both open and closed strings. We verify this explicitly in the tachyon and massless sectors.

### [91] [Confinement of Massive Ghost in Quadratic Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01966)
*Ichiro Oda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在二次引力的协变正则形式（covariant canonical formalism）框架下，证明大质量鬼态（massive ghost）可通过BRST四重态机制（BRST quartet mechanism）被束缚到零模态（zero-norm states）中，从而恢复物理S矩阵（S-matrix）的幺正性（unitarity），并指出该机制与量子色动力学（QCD）中的色禁闭（color confinement）存在类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次引力（quadratic gravity）中存在违背幺正性的大质量鬼态，这破坏了物理S矩阵的幺正性。本文旨在解决该鬼态的禁闭问题，以恢复理论的幺正性。

Method: 基于二次引力的协变正则形式，利用BRST四重态机制分析大质量鬼态与Faddeev-Popov鬼态（Faddeev-Popov ghost）之间的束缚态。同时采用Bonora和Tonin的超场形式（superfield formulation），推导相关渐近场（asymptotic field）的动力学方程。

Result: 大质量鬼态与Faddeev-Popov鬼态之间存在束缚态（bound state），该束缚态使大质量鬼态被禁闭在零模态中，从而恢复幺正性。大质量鬼态的渐近场表现为大质量偶极场（massive dipole），而束缚态的渐近场满足大质量Klein-Gordon方程（massive Klein-Gordon equation）。

Conclusion: 本文表明二次引力中的大质量鬼态禁闭机制与QCD中色禁闭存在相似性：两者实际被禁闭的均为有质量（而非无质量）的规范场量子。

Abstract: In the framework of the covariant canonical formalism of quadratic gravity, we consider the problem of confinement of massive ghost which violates the unitarity of the physical S-matrix. It is shown that if there is a bound state between the massive ghost and Faddeev-Popov ghost the massive ghost is confined in the zero-norm states through the BRST quartet mechanism, thereby the unitarity being restored. Based on the superfield formulation by Bonora and Tonin, we show that the asymptotic field of the massive ghost must be a massive dipole whereas that of the bound state obeys a massive Klein-Gordon equation. This situation may be of some similarity to color confinement in quantum chromodynamics (QCD) where it is conjectured that not a massless but a massive gluon is in fact confined.

### [92] [All DDF/lightcone two-particle decay widths up to level $8$ in open bosonic string in critical dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02013)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We carry out an ``experimental analysis'' in which we explicitly compute all possible Abelian two-particle decay channels (excluding the tachyon) of open bosonic massive states up to level (8), amounting to approximately 2,000,000 cases. The aim is to develop intuition about which states are the most stable and to identify the dominant decay channels. Our results show that, for all levels considered, the ratio of decay widths between the slowest- and fastest-decaying states is of order one. In most cases, the dominant polarized decay channel accounts for at least $10\%$ of the total decay width, while the first five channels together contribute roughly 60%. Even when we sum about $10000$ polarized channels. Dominant polarized channels always involve at least one photon and all strings ultimately decay into a photon carrying energy at the string scale. The most stable states are made using the DDF/lightcone oscillators $A_{-1}$ and some $A_{-2}$ and are close relatives of the states on the leading Regge trajectory. Finally, we discuss how the computation on the lightcone differs from the equal-time computation due to ``surges'', i.e., decays into a tachyon and a higher-mass state, and we hypothesize that, in bosonic string theory, decays into tachyons constitute the dominant decay channels.

### [93] [Geometric QCD III: Exact transition amplitudes and the glueball spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02373)
*Alexander Migdal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在连续极限下完成了平面 Makeenko–Migdal 圈方程的分析，利用约束扭弦（confining twistor-string）表示计算量子涨落行列式，揭示了卷绕数（winding number）趋近无穷大时的极点奇异性，并分别对开弦介子扇区和纯杨-米尔斯闭弦扇区给出了精确的拓扑依赖谱学结果与胶球质量间隙的显式解析机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完成平面 Makeenko–Migdal 圈方程在连续极限下的分析，并基于约束扭弦（confining twistor-string）表示严格计算量子涨落行列式，以建立弦论框架下规范理论的精确可解结构。

Method: 采用约束扭弦表示计算量子涨落行列式；在闵可夫斯基空间中退化为有限维矩阵求积的离散乘积；利用 $\zeta$ 正则化（$\zeta$-regularization）处理权重（weight）；在卷绕数（winding number）$w$ 趋于无穷的大 $w$ WKB 极限下对路径积分进行局域化（localization）。

Result: $\zeta$ 正则化权重与卷绕数 $w$ 无关；在质量壳（mass shell）附近，$w \to \infty$ 产生极点奇异性（pole singularity），涨落方差（fluctuation variance）按 $1/w$ 被压制；开弦介子扇区拟合 40 个态，跨越五个拓扑扇区（topological sectors）$h=0, \pm 1, \pm 2$，全纯移位（holonomy shift）$h$ 决定了宇称族（parity families）间的精确几何简并（geometric degeneracy）；闭弦扇区证明共形刘维尔反常（conformal Liouville anomaly）驱动弦严格趋向三角最小值（trigonometric minimum）$q=0$，复椭球几何解析坍缩，给出线性雷吉轨迹（linear Regge trajectories）；平移零模测度（translation zero-mode measure）动态消去无质量标量鬼（massless scalar ghost）的跃迁振幅，产生纯胶子质量间隙（mass gap）；无参数胶球轨迹（glueball trajectories）恢复 Lüscher 截距（intercept）$\alpha(0)=1/12$。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了平面极限下弦论表示与规范理论精确可解性之间的完整桥梁：开弦介子扇区的拓扑简并与质量劈裂无需唯象自旋-轨道参数即可再现；闭弦扇区则首次为纯杨-米尔斯质量间隙提供了显式解析机制，且无参数胶球谱与 PDG 未分配等标量候选态（isoscalar candidates）具有启发性的对应关系。

Abstract: We complete the analysis of planar Makeenko--Migdal loop equations in the continuum limit. Using the confining twistor-string representation, we compute the quantum fluctuation determinant. In Minkowski space, this reduces to a discrete product of finite-dimensional matrix quadratures. The $ζ$-regularized weight is independent of winding number $w$. Near the mass shell, the pole singularity is generated by $w \to \infty$, suppressing fluctuation variance as $1/w$. The path integral localizes on the classical trajectory, rendering the pole spectrum and transition residues parametrically exact in the large-$w$ WKB limit.For the open-string meson sector, we fit 40 states across five topological sectors ($h=0, \pm 1, \pm 2$). The holonomy shift $h$ dictates exact geometric degeneracies between parity families, reproducing mass splittings without phenomenological spin-orbit parameters. Evaluated one-loop residues yield relative transition cross-sections, demonstrating nontrivial topology- and flavor-dependent scaling that captures heavy-mass quenching and phase-space enhancement for high-spin light states.For the pure Yang--Mills closed string, we demonstrate dynamical stability of the pure-gauge minimal surface in the planar limit: the conformal Liouville anomaly drives the string strictly to the trigonometric minimum ($q=0$). The complex elliptic geometry analytically collapses, yielding linear Regge trajectories. The translation zero-mode measure dynamically nullifies the transition amplitude of the massless scalar ghost, providing an explicit analytic mechanism for a purely gluonic mass gap. Anchoring parameter-free glueball trajectories to the string tension natively recovers the L"uscher intercept $α(0)=1/12$, yielding a macroscopic spectrum that provides a suggestive baseline for established PDG unassigned isoscalar candidates.

</details>


### [94] [Functional Renormalization Group for a Rank-4 Renormalizable Tensorial Group Field Theory with Derivative Necklace Couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02422)

Abstract: We apply the functional renormalization group to an Abelian Group Field Theory extended beyond the branched-polymer (melonic) sector by including interactions that are subdominant from a power-counting perspective but enhanced by derivative couplings. Focusing on a rank-4 model, we consider a class of non-melonic interactions with a necklace structure. Due to their index contraction pattern, their leading-order behavior is analogous to that of large-N random matrix models and is associated with a planar graph structure. Within this setting, we identify the emergence of a nontrivial ultraviolet fixed point, reminiscent of mechanisms previously observed in matrix models, and discuss its reliability within the present truncation. The robustness of this fixed point will be further investigated through modified Ward identities, following strategies previously developed in the melonic sector.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars are atypical nonthermal states embedded in the chaotic spectrum that evade conventional ergodicity. Their spectrum exhibits random-matrix signatures of chaos while supporting embedded integrable spectral branches. Boson stars further display anomalously low entanglement relative to black holes at the same energy density, and also robust revivals in Krylov complexity, revealing nonergodic dynamics. These spectral, entanglement, and dynamical diagnostics provide unified evidence for holographic quantum scars in a self-gravitating system. Abstract: We present the first complete non-redundant operator basis for the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) at finite temperature, using the imaginary-time formalism. By employing the Hilbert series method on the space-time manifold $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$, we classify all effective operators up to dimension-six. In constructing the basis, we consistently impose integration-by-parts and equations-of-motion constraints along spatial directions. We further analyze the impact of additional constraints, including the vanishing of the curl of the electric and magnetic fields and gauge choices for the temporal components on an operator basis. We also express them in terms of static three-dimensional spatial and zero-temperature SMEFT operators. ### [101] [de Sitter Vacua & pUniverses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02883)
*Jeremias Aguilera-Damia,Dionysios Anninos,Tarek Anous,Johnny Gleeson,Alan Rios Fukelman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对 p-Schwinger 模型进行理论分析：在 Minkowski 空间和全局 de Sitter 背景上分别研究其对称性结构及其破缺机制；将多味（N_f 味）变体耦合到具有正宇宙常数 Λ>0 的量子引力中，分析大 N_f 极限下的半经典 de Sitter 鞍点（semiclassical de Sitter saddle）。

Abstract: We analyze a simple extension of the Schwinger model, which we refer to as the $p$-Schwinger model, on a de Sitter background. In this theory, the charged massless fermions carry non-unit integer charge $p$. In Minkowski space, the $p$-Schwinger model has discrete zero- and one-form global symmetries that are spontaneously broken, yielding $p$ degenerate ground states. We demonstrate that these features persist upon placing the $p$-Schwinger model on a global de Sitter background, establishing that such discrete global symmetries can be spontaneously broken for quantum field theories in de Sitter space. In particular, the theory is endowed with $p$ distinct, but locally-indistinguishable, de Sitter invariant states, the de Sitter vacua, satisfying the Hadamard property. We couple a variant of the $p$-Schwinger model with ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$ flavors to quantum gravity with $Λ>0$, and demonstrate the existence of a semiclassical de Sitter saddle at large ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$. In the gravitational theory, the $p$ de Sitter invariant vacua are speculatively interpreted as microstates of the de Sitter horizon in the low-energy effective field theory.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索扭结全息对偶背景下开-闭-开三元性的实现机制，并建立开放弦描述与体时空几何涌现之间的直接联系。

Method: 从已解锥形上的B模型出发，构造两支横向膜片，导出两种等价的开放弦场论描述；在适当极限下简化为带有行列式插入的规范βγ系统（gauged βγ-systems）；通过对场论作用量进行在壳分析（on-shell analysis）获得ρ矩阵模型（ρ-matrix models）。

Result: 积分掉一支膜片上的开弦所生成的有效势能精确捕捉了该膜片对几何的反作用（backreaction），并将探针膜片的作用量匹配到变形锥形（deformed conifold）中的巨引力子（giant gravitons）的作用量。

Conclusion: 三元性中的第二开放弦描述可直接诊断涌现的体时空，为弦理论中开弦与闭弦之间的对偶关系提供了新的证据。

Abstract: We explore the ideas of open-closed-open triality within twisted holography. Starting from two transverse stacks of branes in the B-model on the resolved conifold, we obtain two equivalent open string descriptions. Both are full-fledged field theories. In the appropriate limit, they simplify to gauged $βγ$-systems with determinant insertions, as expected from open string field theory. The $ρ$-matrix models that have appeared previously in the literature appear from an on-shell analysis of the field-theory actions. Most importantly, we show that the effective potential generated by integrating out the open strings on the other stack of branes exactly captures their backreaction on the geometry. In particular, we match the action of the probe branes to that of giant gravitons in the $\textit{deformed}$ conifold. The second open string description of the triality thus directly diagnoses the emergent bulk spacetime.

### [103] [Probing Quantum Entanglement in $τ^+τ^-$ Pairs via the $ππ$ Channel at STCF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01233)
*Xiaokang Li,Chentao Bao,Hai Chen,Mingyi Liu,Dayong Wang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过全模拟蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）研究，论证了超陶-粲工厂（STCF）在质心能量 7 GeV 下可通过 ππ 道（τ±→π±ν）实现 τ+τ- 对中量子纠缠与贝尔不等式（Bell inequality）违背的高精度探测，重建并发度（concurrence）达 0.279±0.007。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠缠与贝尔不等式违背是高能相互作用中量子关联的灵敏探针，但目前尚缺乏在 STCF 上基于全模拟的可行性验证。

Method: 在提议的 STCF 上开展 e+e- → τ+τ- 的全模拟研究，质心能量 √s=7 GeV，聚焦自旋分析能力最大（|κ|=1）且末态拓扑最简单的 ππ 衰变道（τ±→π±ν），并建立从树图级量子电动力学（QED）预言到真实级与探测器级重建的一致性链条。

Result: 采用良解（good-solution）方法，经探测器级重建得到并发度为 0.279±0.007；同时简要报告了 ρρ 道的补充全模拟结果。

Conclusion: 上述结果表明 STCF 可为 τ 轻子对中量子关联的精密研究提供有竞争力的实验平台。

Abstract: Quantum entanglement and Bell-inequality violation in $τ^+τ^-$ pairs provide a sensitive probe of quantum correlations in high-energy interactions. We present a feasibility study of $e^+e^- \to τ^+τ^-$ at the proposed Super Tau-Charm Facility based on full Monte Carlo simulation at $\sqrt{s} = 7$ GeV, focusing on the $ππ$ channel ($τ^\pm \to π^\pmν$), which offers the maximal spin-analyzing power $|κ| = 1$ and the simplest final-state topology for validating the quantum-tomography framework. We establish a consistency chain from the tree-level QED prediction through truth-level and detector-level reconstruction, yielding a reconstructed concurrence of $0.279 \pm 0.007$ with the good-solution approach. A complementary full-simulation study of the $ρρ$ channel is also briefly reported. These results demonstrate that the STCF can provide a competitive platform for precision studies of quantum correlations in $τ$-lepton pairs.

### [104] [Data-Driven, Geometry-Aware Optimal-Transport Calibration of Flavor Tagger](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01363)
*Yeonjoon Kim,Un-ki Yang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种几何感知的框架，将味标记校准（flavor-tagger calibration）形式化为概率单纯形上的最优传输（optimal transport）问题，利用等距对数比坐标（isometric log-ratio coordinate system）和Aitchison距离实现连续、事件级别的校准，并通过期望最大化（EM）技术从控制区数据中提取味条件目标分布，以替代传统离散工作点或分箱校正方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有味标记校准通常仅在有限工作点（working points）上提供比例因子（scale factors），或对一维判别量做分箱校正，无法覆盖现代标记器多分量输出的完整连续校准。这种信息损失限制了需要高性能味标记的分析，使其只能使用少量预定义变量。

Method: 将校准问题转化为概率单纯形（probability simplex）上的最优传输问题，传输映射在等距对数比坐标中参数化并训练；在该坐标下Brenier传输的二次欧几里得代价等价于单纯形上的Aitchison距离，从而确保映射的几何最小变形。通过期望最大化（expectation-maximization, EM）技术从多个控制区数据中同时提取味条件目标分布：使用归一化流（normalizing flow）建模每个味组分，并估计区域混合分数。针对混合分数与柔性组分密度的联合估计中存在的弱约束方向，进一步引入线性化反馈算子分析，将拟合的组分协方差传播到提取的组分密度中，从而区分数据约束模式与先验主导模式。

Result: 基于模拟的闭合测试（closure study）显示，所提方法在专用控制区和独立验证混合物中均表现出改进的闭合性。

Conclusion: 该几何感知框架能够提供连续、事件级别的味标记校准，克服了传统方法的离散化局限，在高性能味标记需求的分析场景中具有优势。

Abstract: Flavor-tagging calibrations are often provided either as scale factors measured at a finite set of working points or as binned corrections to a chosen one-dimensional discriminant. However, this approach falls short of providing continuous, event-level calibration across the full multicomponent outputs of modern taggers. This limitation leads to information loss in analyses that demand high-performance flavor tagging, restricting analyses to a limited set of predefined variables.
  In this work, we propose a geometry-aware framework that formulates flavor-tagger calibration as an optimal transport problem on the probability simplex. The transport maps are parameterized and trained in the isometric log-ratio coordinate system. Because the quadratic Euclidean cost of Brenier transport in this coordinate system is equivalent to the Aitchison distance on the simplex, the learned map induces a minimal deformation under the Aitchison geometry. Furthermore, we extract flavor-conditional target distributions directly from control-region data using an expectation-maximization (EM) technique that simultaneously fits multiple control regions, models each flavor component with a normalizing flow, and estimates the regional mixture fractions. The extracted targets are subsequently used to learn flavor-factorized transport maps. Because the joint estimation of mixture fractions and flexible component densities admits weakly constrained directions, we further introduce a linearized feedback-operator analysis that propagates the fitted composition covariance into the extracted component densities, separating data-constrained modes from those dominated by the composition prior. The simulation-based closure study demonstrates improved closure in dedicated control regions and in independent validation mixtures.

</details>


### [105] [HepScript: A Dual-Use DSL for Human-AI Collaborative Data Analysis Workflows in High-Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01423)
*Junkun Jiao,Tong Liu,Ke Li,Weimin Song,Yipu Liao,Bolun Zhang,Beijiang Liu,Chang-Zheng Yuan,Yue Sun*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出以 HepScript 领域特定语言（DSL）作为高能物理数据分析的统一形式化接口，在 BESIII 实验中实现人类专家与 AI 智能体之间的高效协作：人类代码量减少 93%，AI 基于文献自主生成可执行规范的成功率达 95%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理（High-Energy Physics, HEP）的数据规模持续增长，迫切需要更高的分析效率；大语言模型（Large Language Models, LLMs）虽可通过智能体 AI（agentic AI）实现自动化，但在需要深度领域知识且紧密耦合于实验特定代码库的复杂科学工作流中表现不佳。

Method: 引入 HepScript——一种面向 HEP 数据分析工作流的双重用途领域特定语言（Domain-Specific Language, DSL）。HepScript 作为共享形式化接口（shared formal interface），将 HEP 分析逻辑抽象为受约束的语法，既对人类专家直观，又可被 AI 智能体可靠生成；该语言隐藏底层软件栈复杂性，将高层分析意图翻译为低层生产级代码。

Result: 在 BESIII 实验案例中，该抽象使所需手动编写的代码减少 93%；HepScript 的受约束语法定义了可处理的行动空间（tractable action space），使 AI 智能体能够直接从已发表文献中自主生成核心分析阶段的可执行规范，成功率达 95%。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种可扩展的人机协作路径：形式化定义的 DSL 作为人类专业知识、AI 自动化与生产环境之间的无歧义翻译层，使此前难以处理的自动化问题变得可解。

Abstract: The escalating data scale in High-Energy Physics (HEP) fuels a growing aspiration for higher analytical efficiency. While Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a path toward automation via agentic AI, they struggle with complex scientific workflows that require deep domain knowledge and are tightly coupled to experiment-specific codebases. To address this, we introduce a methodology centered on HepScript, a dual-use Domain-Specific Language (DSL) for HEP data analysis workflows. HepScript serves as a shared formal interface, abstracting HEP analysis logic into a constrained syntax that is both intuitive for human experts and reliably generable by AI agents. First developed for the Beijing Spectrometer III (BESIII) experiment, HepScript hides the complexity of the underlying software stack, translating high-level analysis intent into low-level, production-ready code. In our case studies, this abstraction reduces the required human-written code by 93\%. Crucially, HepScript's constrained grammar defines a tractable action space, enabling AI agents to autonomously generate executable specifications for core analysis stages directly from published literature with a 95\% success rate. Our work demonstrates a scalable pathway toward human-AI collaborative systems, where a formally specified DSL acts as an unambiguous translation layer between human expertise, AI automation, and production environment, rendering previously intractable automation problems solvable.

</details>

### [107] [Study of $t\bar{t}$ threshold effects in $eμ$ differential distributions measured in $\sqrt{s}=13$\,TeV $pp$ collisions with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02341)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究基于ATLAS实验在13 TeV质子-质子碰撞中测量的归一化eμ双轻子不变质量与方位角分布，扩展分析了对t t 阈值附近准束缚态（quasi-bound states）形成的敏感性。通过将数据与含或不含色单态准束缚态的t t 模型比较，发现含准束缚态的预言能更好描述实验数据；对双轻子不变质量分布的拟合表明该过程观测显著性超过3倍标准偏差，且测量截面与阈值区域的专门研究一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）上，利用ATLAS实验测得的归一化eμ双轻子不变质量与方位角分布，能否探测t t 阈值附近色单态准束缚态（colour-singlet quasi-bound states）的形成。

Method: 将实验测得的微分分布与两种理论模型进行比较：一种仅含微扰量子色动力学（perturbative QCD）对硬过程的预言，另一种则在硬过程中加入色单态准束缚态形成。通过拟合双轻子不变质量分布，提取准束缚态过程的观测显著性及截面。

Result: 含准束缚态形成的预言能更好描述实验数据；拟合双轻子不变质量分布显示准束缚态过程的观测显著性超过3倍标准偏差（three standard deviations），且测得的截面与阈值区域的专门研究结果一致。

Conclusion: 实验数据支持t t 阈值附近存在色单态准束缚态形成的证据，表明该类非微扰效应在双轻子衰变道中可被有效探测。

Abstract: The recent ATLAS measurement of the normalised $eμ$ dilepton invariant mass and azimuthal angle distributions in $\sqrt{s}=13$\,TeV $pp$ collisions at the Large Hadron Collider is extended to study the sensitivity to the formation of quasi-bound states near the $t\bar{t}$ threshold. The measured differential distributions are compared with $t\bar{t}$ models incorporating perturbative QCD predictions for the hard process, with or without the addition of colour-singlet quasi-bound states. The data are better described by the predictions incorporating quasi-bound-state formation. Fits to the dilepton invariant mass distribution show evidence for the latter process with an observed significance exceeding three standard deviations, and a measured cross-section in agreement with dedicated studies of the threshold region.

### [109] [Recent Results from NA62 in Kaon and Dump Mode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02415)
*Jonathan Leon Schubert*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于NA62实验在CERN SPS上采集的2016–2024年数据，报告了对超稀有衰变$K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$的最新测量结果，以及基于2021–2024年束流-dump模式数据对新物理粒子（质量150–2000 MeV，衰变至$h^\pm\ell^\mp$通道，符合重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton）场景）的搜寻；未观测到信号事件，对耦合强度设定了上限。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用NA62固定靶（fixed-target）实验在CERN SPS上采集的数据：2016–2024年数据用于$K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$测量；2021–2024年专用运行期间的数据用于束流-dump模式下的新物理粒子搜寻。搜寻覆盖衰变通道$h^\pm\ell^\mp$，其中$h^\pm\in(π^\pm,π^\pmπ^0,π^\pm2π^0,K^\pm)$，$\ell\in(e,μ)$。

Result: $K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$的测量结果与以往测量及标准模型预测一致。新物理粒子搜寻在所有信号通道中均未观测到事件，因此设定了该类粒子与标准模型耦合强度的上限。

Conclusion: NA62实验的最新数据进一步验证了标准模型对$K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$衰变的预测，同时通过束流-dump模式对重中性轻子场景中的新物理粒子给出了有竞争力的耦合上限约束。

Abstract: NA62 is a fixed-target kaon experiment at the CERN SPS. The recent measurement of the ultra-rare decay $K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$, based on data collected between 2016 and 2024 is reported. The measurement is compatible with previous measurements and the Standard Model. The experiment can also be operated in an alternative beam-dump mode. From this mode, a search for new-physics particles with masses in the range of 150 to 2000~MeV, based on data collected in dedicated runs between 2021 and 2024 is reported. The search focuses on their decays to $h^\pm\ell^\mp$, where $h^\pm\in(π^\pm,π^\pmπ^0,π^\pm2π^0,K^\pm)$, and $\ell\in(e,μ)$, which are expected in heavy neutral lepton scenarios. ### [110] [Surface background of the BULLKID detector array operated with moderate shielding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02468)
*D. Delicato,A. Acevedo-Rentería,M. Folcarelli,G. Del Castello,M. Cappelli,L. E. Ardila-Perez,L. Bandiera,C. Bonomo,M. Calvo,R. Caravita,F. Carillo,F. Cescato,U. Chowdhury,D. A. Crovo,A. Cruciani,A. D'Addabbo,M. De Lucia,M. del Gallo Roccagiovine,F. Ferraro,S. Fu,R. Gartmann,M. Giammei,M. Grassi,V. Guidi,D. L. Helis,T. Lari,L. Malagutti,A. Mazzolari,A. Monfardini,T. Muscheid,D. Nicolò,F. Paolucci,D. Pasciuto,L. Pesce,C. Puglia,D. Quaranta,C. M. A. Roda,S. Roddaro,M. Romagnoni,G. Signorelli,F. Simon,A. Tartari,E. Vázquez-Jáuregui,M. Vignati,K. Zhao*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了 BULLKID 探测器在表面实验室中采用中等辐射屏蔽的运行结果。该探测器由 60 个硅粒子吸收体组成，用于寻找暗物质（Dark Matter）和相干弹性中微子-核散射（CEνNS）。290 小时的本底数据表明，在 600 eV 至 2 keV 能区，测量与模拟符合良好；但 225 eV 至 600 eV 区间出现了与模拟不符的背景上升，但其特征不同于其他低温实验中的低能过剩（low energy excess）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低阈值低温探测器是搜索轻质量暗物质和相干弹性中微子-核散射（Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering，CEνNS）的关键实验手段。BULLKID 探测器旨在结合大质量与大阵列的优势，降低能量阈值并提升灵敏度。

Method: BULLKID 探测器由 60 个立方体硅粒子吸收体（每个 0.34 g）组成，采用低温动能电感探测器（kinetic inductance detector）读取信号。分析聚焦于阵列中 15 个单元的数据，其中两个中心单元用于评估本底，周围单元用作反符合veto。实验在表面实验室中进行，并使用了外部和内部辐射屏蔽。

Result: 在 290 小时的环境本底暴露中，从 2 keV 至 600 eV 的能区，测量谱与模拟的符合程度为 (6.8±0.4 stat. ±0.1 syst.) × 10⁴ counts / keV kg days。225 eV 至 600 eV 区间出现背景上升，与模拟不符，但该上升不具备其他低温实验中观察到的低能过剩（low energy excess）的关键特征。高能区谱形与模拟总体一致，并显示了铅屏蔽的典型粒子诱导 X 射线发射（particle-induced X-ray emission）。

Conclusion: BULLKID 探测器的中等屏蔽方案在表面实验室中实现了从 keV 到 sub-keV 能区的有效本底控制。225-600 eV 区间未解释的背景上升值得进一步研究，但其特征表明它可能不同于其他实验报道的低能过剩现象。

Abstract: We present the operation with moderate radiation shield in a surface laboratory of BULLKID (BULky and Low-threshold Kinetic Inductance Detector), a cryogenic detector for searches of light Dark Matter or Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering. The detector consists of an array of 60 cubic silicon particle absorbers of 0.34 g each, sensed by cryogenic kinetic inductance detectors. The analysis presented focuses on data from 15 elements of the array, with two central units used to evaluate the background and with their surrounding elements used as veto. The low energy spectrum resulting from an exposure of 290 hours to ambient backgrounds, acquired with the use of external and internal radiation shields, is compatible with the simulations at the level of $(6.8\pm0.4\,{\rm stat.}\pm0.1\,{\rm syst.})\times10^4$ counts / keV kg days from 2 keV down to an energy of 600 eV. The region between 225 eV and 600 eV shows a rise in background in disagreement with the simulations, while not sharing some of the key traits of the low energy excess observed in other cryogenic experiments. The high energy spectrum shape is in overall agreement with the simulations and displays the typical particle-induced X-ray emission of the surrounding lead.

</details>


### [111] [Cascade Pipeline for Leading-Order Matrix Element Evaluation on AMD Versal AI Engine Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02481)
*P. Leguina López,C. Vico Villalba,F. Hervás Álvarez,H. Gutiérrez Arance,S. Folgueras,L. Fiorini,A. Valero,J. Fernández Menéndez,F. Carrió,A. Oyanguren*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于AMD Versal AI Engine（AIE）阵列的级联流水线架构，用于加速高能物理事件生成器中领头阶矩阵元（\ggttg过程）的计算。在VCK190平台上映射80条独立流水线，实现了每秒1.0×10^6次矩阵元评估，相比单CPU核心获得34倍加速和7.7倍能效提升，数值精度与双精度参考一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代高能物理事件生成器（event generator）的计算瓶颈在于矩阵元（matrix element）的积分需要在不同相空间点（phase-space points）重复评估。随着大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）进入高亮度阶段，传统CPU扩展已无法满足能效需求，亟需探索高度并行的计算平台如图形处理器（GPU）或专用AI Engine阵列。

Method: 本文采用级联流水线架构（cascade pipeline architecture），将\ggttg过程的领头阶矩阵元计算分解为五级流水线，每级通过波函数-令牌协议（wavefunction-token protocol）在片上级联接口通信，以适应每片16 kB的程序内存限制。在AMD Versal AI Engine（AIE）阵列的VCK190平台上，将80条独立流水线映射到400个AIE瓦片（tile）上。

Result: 在54.8 W功耗下实现每秒1.0×10^6次矩阵元评估，相比单CPU核心获得34倍加速（speedup）和7.7倍能效（energy efficiency）提升。数值精度与\amcnlo双精度参考的平均相对误差（mean relative error）在百万分之一（parts-per-million）级别。

Conclusion: 基于AI Engine阵列的流水线架构可有效加速高能物理事件生成中的矩阵元计算，在保证数值精度的前提下显著提升吞吐量和能效，为应对高亮度LHC时代的计算需求提供了可行方案。

Abstract: A major computational bottleneck in modern High Energy Physics event generators arises from the integration of the matrix element, which requires repeated evaluations at different phase-space points to cover all possible initial- and final-state configurations. As the Large Hadron Collider enters its High-Luminosity phase, the demand for energy-efficient acceleration is expected to exceed the limits of conventional CPU scaling, motivating the use of highly parallel computing platforms such as graphics processing units (GPUs). In this work, we present an alternative approach based on a cascade pipeline architecture for evaluating leading-order matrix elements of the \ggttg process on AMD Versal AI Engine (\aie) arrays. Due to the 16\,kB per-tile program memory constraint, the computation is decomposed into a five-stage pipeline, with stages communicating via a wavefunction-token protocol over the on-chip cascade interface. Mapping 80 independent pipelines onto the 400 \aie tiles of the VCK190 platform yields a projected throughput of $1.0\times10^6$ matrix element evaluations per second at 54.8\,W, corresponding to a $34\times$ speedup over a single CPU core and a $7.7\times$ improvement in energy efficiency. Numerical agreement with the \amcnlo double-precision reference is validated at the parts-per-million level in mean relative error.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在 CMS 新物理搜索案例中，HEP-CoPilot 能够检索相关测量结果、直接从 HEPData 记录重建排除极限（exclusion limits），并执行跨论文的实验约束比较，无需人工数据整合即可实现一致的物理感知比较。

Conclusion: 检索增强型 AI 系统可作为粒子物理领域的科学副驾驶（scientific co-pilot），帮助导航复杂文献、结构化异构证据，并加速新物理搜索的解释管线。

Abstract: Modern searches for physics beyond the Standard Model produce rapidly expanding literature containing heterogeneous information, including textual analyses, numerical datasets, and graphical exclusion limits. Integrating these distributed sources remains a time-consuming and manual process for physicists.
  We present HEP-CoPilot, a retrieval-augmented multi-agent AI framework for the exploration and interpretation of high-energy physics literature. The system unifies textual information from publications, structured experimental data from HEPData, and reconstructed physics plots within a multimodal retrieval and reasoning architecture. By combining retrieval-augmented language models with coordinated agent workflows, it enables evidence-grounded reasoning over experimental analyses and structured interpretation of collider results.
  We evaluate the framework on recent CMS searches for physics beyond the Standard Model. Case studies show that HEP-CoPilot can retrieve relevant measurements, reconstruct exclusion limits directly from HEPData records, and perform cross-paper comparisons of experimental constraints. This enables consistent, physics-aware comparison across analyses without manual data integration.
  These results demonstrate that retrieval-augmented AI systems can function as scientific co-pilots for particle physics, facilitating navigation of complex literature, structuring heterogeneous evidence, and accelerating the interpretation pipeline for new physics searches.

### [113] [Search for a new heavy scalar resonance decaying into the Higgs boson and a new scalar particle in the $\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}$ final state using proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02848)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报道了在质心能量13 TeV的质子-质子对撞中，利用CMS探测器收集的138 fb$^{-1}$数据，搜索新重标量共振X衰变为125 GeV希格斯玻色子H和新标量粒子Y的过程，聚焦于$\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}$末态。未发现显著超出背景的迹象，最大超出对应X和Y质量分别为600 GeV和400 GeV，局部（全局）显著性为3.47（2.44）个标准差。结果在次最小超对称标准模型（next-to-minimal supersymmetric standard model, NMSSM）框架下进行了解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超出标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的新物理现象，特别是新标量共振X通过X→YH过程衰变，其中Y和H各衰变至底夸克对（$\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}$）。该搜索旨在检验次最小超对称标准模型（NMSSM）等理论预言的信号。

Method: 采用质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量13 TeV，积分亮度138 fb$^{-1}$，由CMS探测器在大型强子对撞机（LHC）Run 2期间收集。以$\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}$末态作为探测通道，扫描共振X质量范围400 GeV–1.6 TeV及标量粒子Y质量范围60 GeV–1.4 TeV。

Result: 观测结果与纯背景假设一致。最大超出对应X和Y质量分别为600 GeV和400 GeV，局部显著性3.47个标准差，全局显著性2.44个标准差。给出了95%置信水平（confidence level, C.L.）下生产截面乘以分支比（production cross section times branching fraction）的上限。

Conclusion: 未发现显著的新共振信号，背景假设未被排除。结果在NMSSM理论框架下给出了限制，为未来更高精度或更高能量的搜索提供了参考约束。

Abstract: A search for a new heavy scalar resonance (X) decaying into the 125 GeV standard model Higgs boson (H) and a new scalar particle (Y) in proton-proton collisions at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV is presented. The analysis is performed using a data sample corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$ collected with the CMS detector during LHC Run 2. The $\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}$ final state is used as a probe to search for phenomena beyond the standard model where, in the X $\to$ YH process, the Y and H each decay into a bottom quark-antiquark pair. A range of masses from 400 GeV to 1.6 TeV for the resonance X and from 60 GeV to 1.4 TeV for the scalar Y is investigated. The observations are in agreement with the background-only hypothesis. The largest excess, with a local (global) significance of 3.47 (2.44) standard deviations, is observed for hypothetical X and Y masses of 600 and 400 GeV, respectively. Upper limits at 95% confidence level on the production cross section times branching fraction are presented for signal mass hypotheses in the range of the search. Results are interpreted within the next-to-minimal supersymmetric standard model scenario.

Method: 本文采用综述（review）方法，首先简要概述磁单极子的理论依据，然后对实验探测尝试进行历史性回顾，重点聚焦于宇宙线实验（cosmic experiments）和对撞机实验（collider experiments）中的最新搜索技术，特别是基于CERN大型强子对撞机的相关研究。

Result: 尽管经过广泛搜索，磁单极子至今仍未被发现。目前最前沿的搜索工作主要集中在宇宙线实验以及大型强子对撞机（LHC）等高能对撞机实验中。

Conclusion: 磁单极子作为重要的未证实理论预言，其存在与否仍需更高灵敏度的实验进行检验。当前的研究前沿已聚焦于大型强子对撞机等装置，未来可能需要更精密的探测手段来验证这一基本物理问题。

Abstract: One of the basic properties of magnetism is that a magnet has always two poles, north and south, which cannot be separated into isolated poles, the magnetic monopoles. There are strong theoretical arguments in favour of monopoles' existence, but in spite of extensive searches they are yet to be found. In this review article, after highlighting briefly the theoretical foundations of monopoles, a historical overview of experimental endeavours to observe them is given, with emphasis on the state-of-the-art of searches in cosmic and collider experiments and in particular the Large Hadron Collider at CERN.

### [115] [The Mesoscopic Partition Function:A Combined Spatial and Phase-Space Cell Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00958)
*Bob Osano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于空间与相空间联合粗粒化（coarse-graining）的介观配分函数（mesoscopic partition function），用占据数（occupation numbers）上的离散求和替代正则相空间积分。在精细极限下该构造恢复标准正则配分函数。主要结果表明，介观配分函数在空间元胞上的可分解性等价于粗粒化自由能的可加性（extensivity），偏差由互信息（mutual information）量化的元胞间相关性决定。研究还推导出带有次可加修正项的广义欧拉关系，为介观热力学中粗粒化、分解性与可加性的统一提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典多体系统的正则配分函数在连续相空间中的积分形式难以直接处理粗粒化或有限尺度效应，缺乏一种能同时兼顾空间与相空间离散化的统一数学构造。

Method: 通过对空间和相空间进行联合粗粒化，将标准正则配分函数的连续积分替换为对占据数的离散求和，构造了一个介观配分函数。

Result: 介观配分函数在空间元胞上可分解当且仅当粗粒化自由能具有可加性，而不可分解部分由互信息度量的元胞间相关性控制；推导了含次可加修正项的广义欧拉关系。

Conclusion: 该工作为粗粒化、分解性与可加性三者之间的内在联系提供了统一的数学框架，有助于理解介观热力学中边界效应与相关性对自由能的影响。

Abstract: We introduce a mesoscopic partition function for classical many-body systems based on a combined spatial and phase-space coarse-graining, replacing the canonical phase-space integral with a discrete sum over occupation numbers. The construction recovers the standard canonical partition function in the fine-graining limit. Our main result shows that factorisation of the mesoscopic partition function across spatial cells is equivalent to extensivity of the coarse-grained free energy, with deviations governed by inter-cell correlations quantifiable via mutual information. We derive a generalised Euler relation with a subextensive correction encoding boundary and correlation effects. Together, these results provide a unified framework linking coarse-graining, factorisation, and extensivity in mesoscopic thermodynamics.

</details>


### [116] [When Independent Gaussian Models Break Down: Characterizing Regime-Dependent Modeling Failures in $φ^4$ Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01145)
*Anish Bhat,Ryo Ide,Zihan Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维格点φ⁴理论中自相互作用对频率表示（傅里叶模式）统计性质的影响，发现高斯独立模式假设的失效主要源于模式间的结构化依赖（structured dependencies）而非边缘非高斯性（marginal non-Gaussianity），并据此识别出三种不同的统计区域，为判断高斯模型何时失效以及设计非线性模型提供了标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际物理系统中，高斯性（Gaussianity）和基独立性（basis independence）的建模假设因自相互作用（self-interactions）而失效。作者旨在系统分析相互作用强度和系统尺寸如何共同影响场（field）的傅里叶模式（Fourier modes）的边际分布与联合分布，以明确传统模型在何种条件下不再适用。

Method: 以一维格点φ⁴理论（one-dimensional φ⁴ theory on a lattice）为具体研究对象，通过改变相互作用强度（interaction strength）和系统尺寸（system size），分析场在频率表示（即傅里叶模式）下的边际分布（marginal distributions）和联合分布（joint distributions）的变化。

Result: 依赖高斯独立傅里叶模式的模型主要因模式间的结构化依赖（structured dependencies）而失败，而非由于边缘非高斯性；尽管模式耦合（mode coupling）随系统尺寸增长，单个模式仍近似服从高斯分布（approximately Gaussian）。基于此，识别出三种不同的统计区域（three distinct regimes）。

Conclusion: 研究提供了一种计算上简单的诊断方法，用于判断高斯模型何时失效，并为未来非线性模型（nonlinear models）提出了具体的设计准则（design criterion）。

Abstract: In practical physical systems, modeling assumptions of Gaussianity and basis independence break down due to self-interactions. We study a specific instance of one-dimensional $φ^4$ theory on a lattice, analyzing how the interaction strength and system size jointly affect the marginal and joint distributions of frequency-based representation of the field (i.e., Fourier modes). We find that models relying on Gaussian and independent Fourier modes fail primarily from structured dependencies rather than marginal non-Gaussianity, since individual modes become approximately Gaussian despite mode coupling growing with size. Based on this, we identify three distinct regimes that delineate where traditional methods remain effective and where more expressive models are needed. Our results provide a computationally simple diagnostic to establish when Gaussian models are insufficient, and establish a concrete design criterion that future nonlinear models must satisfy.

</details>


### [117] [Threshold-Controlled Geometric Reorganization in 2D Bootstrap Percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01151)
*Fangfang Wang,Wei Liu,Kai Qi,Ying Tang,Zengru Di*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了二维自举渗流（bootstrap percolation）在阈值控制下发生的几何交叉（geometric crossover）：低阈值下体量和边界敏感可观测量（observables）集中在同一低密度窗口，高阈值下分裂为不同分支，边界组织成为高阈值下吸收态（absorbing state）的主导结构特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维自举渗流通常由体量（bulk）可观测量表征，但提高活化阈值（activation threshold）是否会导致吸收态几何结构发生质变尚不清楚。

Method: 通过分析不同阈值下体量和边界敏感可观测量的极值行为、有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）特征以及时间分辨机制追踪（time-resolved mechanism traces），研究了阈值控制的几何交叉现象。

Result: 低阈值时，体量与边界可观测量极值集中于单个低密度窗口；高阈值时分裂为不同分支，有限尺寸特征从最终活性密度（active density）涨落转向非单元素（non-singleton）边界可观测量，且涨落峰值下降。机制上，交叉伴随从扩展集体传播（extended collective propagation）到前沿耗竭（frontier exhaustion），再到准一步稳定化（quasi-one-step stabilization）的转变。

Conclusion: 边界组织是高阈值自举渗流吸收态的主要结构特征，仅凭传统体量可观测量无法全面捕捉吸收态的几何重组。

Abstract: Two-dimensional bootstrap percolation is usually characterized by bulk observables, but whether increasing the activation threshold qualitatively reorganizes the geometry of the absorbing state has remained unclear. Here we show that the response undergoes a threshold-controlled geometric crossover. At low thresholds, the extrema of bulk and boundary-sensitive observables remain confined to a single collective low-$p$ window. At high thresholds, they split into distinct branches, revealing multiple geometric response scales. Over the accessible system sizes, the dominant finite-size signatures shift from fluctuations of the final active density to non-singleton boundary observables, while the fluctuation peak itself decreases. Time-resolved mechanism traces show that this crossover is accompanied by a progression from extended collective propagation to frontier exhaustion and, at the highest threshold, to quasi-one-step stabilization. Our results identify boundary organization as the dominant structural signature of high-threshold bootstrap percolation and show that conventional bulk observables alone do not capture the full reorganization of the absorbing state.

</details>


### [118] [Effective attraction by repulsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01421)
*Rosalba Garcia-Millan,Luca Cocconi,Ziluo Zhang,Marius Bothe,Letian Chen,Zigan Zhen,Gunnar Pruessner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过精确微观理论，在一个最小模型（二维软体游走-翻滚粒子）中量化了运动诱导相分离（MIPS）中有效吸引力的出现，发现排斥增强时主导行为仍为有效排斥，有效吸引力仅作为对势重整化的高阶贡献出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 运动诱导相分离（Motility-Induced Phase Separation, MIPS）中排斥性自驱动粒子会聚集，此前类比平衡相分离将其归因于粒子间有效吸引力（effective attraction）的转变，但该关联的微观机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用精确微观理论（exact microscopic theory），研究最小模型：在周期边界（periodic domain）下放置两个软体游走-翻滚粒子（soft run-and-tumble particles），并对粒子间的对势（pair potential）进行重整化（renormalisation）分析。

Result: 当粒子间排斥力增大时，主导行为（leading-order behaviour）仍表现为有效排斥（effective repulsion），而有效吸引力仅作为对势重整化中的高阶贡献（higher-order contribution）出现。

Conclusion: 有效吸引力并非MIPS形成的直接主导机制，而是在粒子间相互作用的微观重整化过程中以高阶项形式体现，从而深化了对非平衡相分离微观起源的理解。

Abstract: Repulsive self-propelled particles tend to cluster, leading to Motility-Induced Phase Separation (MIPS). By analogy with equilibrium phase separation, the onset of MIPS has been associated with a transition to effective attraction between particles. Using an exact microscopic theory, we quantify the emergence of effective attraction in a minimal model: two soft run-and-tumble particles in a periodic domain. We show that, as repulsion increases, the leading-order behaviour is that of effective repulsion, while effective attraction emerges as a higher-order contribution to the renormalisation of the pair potential.

</details>


### [119] [Microscopic theory of soft run-and-tumble particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01422)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文采用微扰展开（perturbation expansion）方法，围绕相互作用耦合（interaction couplings）逐阶添加圈修正（loop corrections），迭代计算有效相互作用顶点。这一方法是对粒子动力学的精确表示（exact representation），使理论推导具备严格的数学基础。

Result: 通过有效相互作用顶点，计算了两点关联函数以完整刻画稳态（stationary state）；还计算了结构因子（structure factor）、重叠概率（overlap probability）和熵产生率（entropy production rate）等其他可观测量。

Abstract: Soft, repulsive run-and-tumble particles display emergent effective interactions as they appear to stick to each other in spite of the absence of attractive forces. This effective attraction emerges at strong enough repulsion and large self-propulsion. Complementing a companion paper that characterises effective attraction between two soft run-and-tumble particles [Garcia-Millan et al., Effective attraction by repulsion (2026)], here we provide a thorough derivation of our microscopic theory, which is an exact representation of the particle dynamics. We report the systematic calculation of the effective interaction vertices iteratively, in a perturbation expansion about the interaction couplings, by adding, order by order, loop corrections. We use the effective interaction vertices to calculate the two-point correlation function, fully characterising the stationary state. Other observables, such as the structure factor, overlap probability and entropy production rate are calculated as well.

### [120] [Entanglement dynamics after quenches with inhomogeneous Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01595)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不均匀哈密顿量下双部分系统中的纠缠动力学，旨在理解非均匀性如何影响量子多体系统中的纠缠产生与输运行为，特别是在流体动力学极限下的长时行为。

Method: 推导XX链和横向场伊辛链中纠缠熵的解析公式；通过求解稳态晶格薛定谔方程（stationary lattice Schrödinger equation）解析获得透射系数；利用准粒子图像解释纠缠产生机制；针对XXZ链采用时间相关密度矩阵重整化群（tDMRG）进行数值模拟。

Result: 强不均匀性抑制输运和纠缠增长；在非相互作用体系中的解析预测与数值结果一致；对于相互作用的XXZ链，定性上观察类似行为：纠缠增长在强不均匀极限下受抑制，但在中等时间尺度输运被抑制时纠缠仍持续增加。

Abstract: We investigate entanglement dynamics in bipartite systems governed by inhomogeneous Hamiltonians of the form $H = H_L + H_R$, where $H_{L/R}$ acts only on the left or right region and is homogeneous within each region. Focusing on the XX chain and the transverse-field Ising chain, we derive analytical formulas for the entanglement entropy between the two regions in the hydrodynamic limit of long times. In this regime, fermions incident on the interface undergo scattering, generating entanglement between reflected and transmitted modes. The resulting quasiparticle picture is controlled by the transmission coefficient, which we obtain analytically by solving the stationary lattice Schrödinger equation. Due to the bounded dispersion, strong inhomogeneity suppresses both transport and entanglement growth. We benchmark our analytical predictions against numerical simulations in paradigmatic setups. Finally, we extend the analysis to the interacting XXZ chain using tDMRG. The numerical data show qualitative agreement with the quadratic case: entanglement growth remains suppressed in the strongly inhomogeneous limit. Notably, however, entanglement continues to increase even when transport is suppressed, at least at intermediate times.

Abstract: On the grounds of nonadditive entropies -- appropriate for complex systems -- we investigate the electroencephalogram amplitudes of typical and ADHD children. The corresponding probability distributions are $q$-Gaussians, i.e., $ρ(x) \propto e_q^{-βx^2} \equiv [1+(q-1) βx^2]^{1/(1-q)}$, where $(q,β)$ are, respectively, the entropic index characterizing complexity and the inverse width. We show that $q$ tends to monotonically vary with $β$ for both typical and ADHD subjects, thus revealing critical behavior of the brain. Moreover, we verify that ADHD subjects have a higher complexity than the typical ones. Consistently, biomarkers for objective phychyatric diagnosis could emerge along this path. ### [122] [Long-range correlation and the spin conductivity in the XXZ chain from ballistic macroscopic fluctuation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01645)

Method: 采用弹道宏观涨落理论（ballistic macroscopic fluctuation theory）作为分析框架，对自旋-1/2 XXZ链在临界区（critical regime）的自旋关联函数进行积分（即自旋电导率，spin conductivity），并考察了等时两点自旋关联函数（equal-time two-point spin correlation function）在系统尺寸N无穷大时的O(1/N)标度行为。

Conclusion: 超扩散自旋输运由1/N标度的长程自旋关联（long-range spin correlation）驱动，这一发现为各向同性点处自旋输运的动态标度行为提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Based on the ballistic macroscopic fluctuation theory, the integration of the spin correlation function (spin conductivity) is analyzed for the spin-1/2 XXZ chain in the critical regime. In the time when the magnetization of an infinite spin chain fluctuates from an initial state with a wavelength as long as the infinite length $N$, the equal-time two-point spin correlation function is scaled up to $O(1/N)$. In the state where the ballistic spin transport decays at high temperature $T$, the diffusive transport remains on a large scale. We show that the spin conductivity is proportional to $1/T$ in the limit $T\to\infty$ and its high temperature proportionality constant diverges in the case where one-quasiparticle magnetization is infinitely large. This analysis informs that the superdiffusive spin transport is driven by the $1/N$-scaled long-range spin correlation and sheds a light on the dynamic scaling in spin transport at the isotropic point.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在二维点接触储库情形下，与一维类似存在三种耦合强度区间（弱、中、强）。三维及以上维度仅存在弱耦合区间，且该区间行为对接触的微观结构敏感。对于介观尺度接触储库，宏观涨落理论仍然有效。

Conclusion: 维度显著影响非平衡系统的行为：二维保留了一维的三区间结构，而高维（d≥3）仅剩弱耦合区间。接触的微观结构在高维弱耦合区起关键作用。宏观涨落理论（MFT）可有效描述介观储库系统，并可通过推广的可加性原理处理多介观储库情形。

Abstract: The non-equilibrium behavior of particle systems driven by reservoirs has been extensively studied in recent years. In one dimension, various regimes have been explored depending on the coupling strength to the reservoirs. In this paper, we investigate the role of the dimension and of the geometry of the contacts with the reservoirs. For the symmetric simple exclusion process with point contact reservoirs, we show that in dimension 2, as in one dimension, three different regimes occur depending on the coupling strength. On the other hand in dimensions 3 and higher, there exists only a weak coupling regime which is very sensitive to the microscopic structure of the contacts. We then argue that for reservoirs with mesoscopic size contacts the macroscopic fluctuation theory remains in force and we propose an extension of the additivity principle for multiple mesoscopic reservoirs.

Abstract: We analytically study the time evolution of the expectation values of observables in periodically kicked many-body quantum systems. Our derivation explains the criteria and the mechanism that lead to the infinite-temperature statistical average of observables at long times, irrespective of the initial state. When the criteria are violated, the observables oscillate with time. These oscillations are subharmonic and robust to small perturbations, suggesting the emergence of a discrete time crystal phase. We demonstrate these features explicitly in periodically kicked nonintegrable spin chains. For a spin chain with two kicks per cycle, we show that the kicked chain can exhibit an ergodic or a discrete-time crystal phase for the same kicking strengths, depending on the initial state preparation. Abstract: We exactly solve the nonequilibrium dynamics of a harmonically trapped self-propelled particle with anisotropic translational mobility in two dimensions, relevant to rodlike microswimmers and wheeled robots. The mean displacement and MSD reveal a quasi-steady plateau with vanishing fluctuations in the high-persistence regime. An exact calculation of steady-state fourth moment yields a negative excess kurtosis that varies non-monotonically with the ratio of mechanical to rotational relaxation timescales. This gives rise to a strictly sub-Gaussian steady-state position distribution, in which the particle with anisotropic mobility, in high persistence regime, is displaced into the high-potential region lying outside the stationary contour set by the activity and harmonic confinement. This is further corroborated by the relaxation of the MSD from the quasi-steady plateau to the steady-state regime.

Motivation: 为全面梳理 Wilson 圈在格点规范理论中探测禁闭的统计力学基础、强耦合与对偶解释、有限温度与连续极限标度行为，以及该领域的数学严格性进展。

Method: 采用综述（survey）方法，系统回顾格点规范系综（lattice gauge ensembles）的统计力学表述，分析强耦合展开（strong-coupling expansion）与对偶（duality）机制下的面积律（area laws），并讨论有限温度与连续极限（continuum scaling）的数值诊断技术。

Result: 格点规范理论中 Wilson 圈面积律的强耦合与对偶机制得到系统梳理；有限温度和连续极限下的标度诊断方法被整合；Wilson 圈禁闭的数学严格性现状被清晰概述。

Conclusion: Wilson 圈是理解格点规范理论中禁闭现象的核心工具，其统计力学框架与对偶方法为解决禁闭问题提供了坚实的理论基础，但数学严格性仍有待进一步发展。

Abstract: Wilson loops provide the central gauge-invariant probe of confinement in lattice gauge theory. This survey reviews the statistical-mechanical formulation of lattice gauge ensembles, the strong-coupling and duality mechanisms behind area laws, finite-temperature and continuum scaling diagnostics, and the mathematical status of Wilson-loop confinement.

</details>


### [128] [Aging Record Statistics in Saturating Self-Interacting Random Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02433)
*J. Brémont,R. Voituriez,O. Bénichou*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了饱和自相互作用随机行走中记录年龄（record age）τ_k的精确渐近分布，揭示了记忆效应如何破坏马尔可夫不变性并导致老化（aging）现象，发现了两个渐近区域，并提供了一个超越标度理论（scaling theory）的罕见精确分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）动力学中，记忆效应如何打破记录年龄τ_k与序号k之间的独立性、进而诱导老化现象，是一个基本但尚未解决的问题。

Method: 针对饱和自相互作用随机行走（saturating self-interacting random walks）这一广泛的非马尔可夫过程类别，推导了记录年龄τ_k的精确渐近分布（exact asymptotic distribution）。

Result: 发现了两个渐近区域：在短时间（τ远小于k²）区域，记录统计由探索区域的几何结构（geometry of the explored region）主导；在长时间（τ远大于k²）区域，记忆效应变为次主导，仅贡献非平凡的前因子修正（prefactor corrections）。

Conclusion: 该精确结果为超越标度理论提供了罕见的解析窗口，并扩展为一个能完整量化存在饱和自相互作用时老化动力学的框架。

Abstract: The record age tau_k, defined as the time between the k-th and k+1-st record-breaking events, is a central observable of extreme-value statistics. In Markovian processes, the absence of memory makes tau_k independent of k. How memory breaks this invariance and induces aging, meaning a dependence of tau_k on k, remains a fundamental question, closely connected to widely observed aging phenomena in non-Markovian dynamics. In this Letter, we derive the exact asymptotic distribution of tau_k for saturating self-interacting random walks, a broad class of non-Markovian processes. We uncover two asymptotic regimes, in agreement with recent scaling predictions: at short times (tau much smaller than k squared), record statistics are governed by the geometry of the explored region, while at long times (tau much larger than k squared), memory effects become subdominant and reduce to nontrivial prefactor corrections. Our exact result provides a rare analytic window beyond scaling theory and extends to a framework that fully quantifies aging dynamics in the presence of saturating self-interaction.

### [129] [Stochastic first-passage modeling of single-event burnout in SiC power MOSFETs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02478)
*Feiyi Liu,Min Guo,Shiyang Chen,Yuhan Jiang,Mingyang Liu,Yang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一个首达时间（first-passage）视角，用于解释碳化硅（SiC）功率 MOSFET 中单粒子烧毁（SEB）的随机阈值展宽现象。通过一个带吸收边界的约化电热反馈-弛豫模型，将确定性烧毁阈值扩展为概率性过渡带，并揭示了噪声诱发的亚阈值失效、失效时间尺度以及反馈-弛豫相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，SiC 功率 MOSFET 的单粒子烧毁由确定性阈值量来刻画。然而在恢复与失控的边界附近，随机变异（stochastic variability）使这一阈值描述具有概率性而非尖锐性。本文旨在解释这种阈值展宽现象背后的统计物理机制。

Method: 构建一个约化的电热反馈-弛豫模型（reduced electrothermal feedback-relaxation model），其中引入吸收边界（absorbing boundary）。模型整合了载流子倍增、雪崩反馈、局域加热、载流子损失及热弛豫过程，并利用随机的载流子项和热项来表示未解析的事件级变异（event-level variability）。

Result: 有限涨落将确定性烧毁阈值拓宽为概率性过渡带（probabilistic transition band）；出现噪声诱发的亚阈值失控（noise-induced subthreshold runaway），即名义上可恢复的条件仍可能通过罕见的随机涨落导致失效；首达时间分布（first-passage-time distribution）解析了烧毁的时间尺度，存活概率（survival probability）进一步区分了快速反馈主导的失控与延迟的随机失效。

Conclusion: 通过一个反馈-弛豫相图（feedback-relaxation phase diagram）组织可恢复、概率性和快速不稳定三种状态。该框架将粗粒化（coarse-grained）的电热动力学与概率性和时间分辨的失效可观测量联系起来，为 SiC 功率 MOSFET 单粒子烧毁中的阈值分散（threshold dispersion）提供了统计物理解释。

Abstract: Single-event burnout (SEB) in silicon carbide (SiC) power MOSFETs is often characterized by deterministic threshold quantities. Near the boundary between recovery and runaway, stochastic variability can make this threshold description probabilistic rather than sharp. This work introduces a first-passage perspective for stochastic threshold broadening in burnout. The process is described by a reduced electrothermal feedback-relaxation model with an absorbing boundary. The model combines carrier multiplication, avalanche feedback, localized heating, carrier loss, and thermal relaxation. Stochastic carrier and thermal terms represent unresolved event-level variability. The main finding is that finite fluctuations broaden the deterministic burnout threshold into a probabilistic transition band. Noise-induced subthreshold runaway also emerges, where nominally recoverable conditions can still fail through rare stochastic excursions. First-passage-time distributions resolve the time scale of burnout and survival probabilities further distinguish rapid feedback-dominated runaway from delayed stochastic failure. A feedback-relaxation phase diagram organizes recoverable, probabilistic, and rapidly unstable regimes. This framework provides a statistical-physics interpretation of threshold dispersion in single-event burnout of SiC power MOSFETs by linking coarse-grained electrothermal dynamics to probabilistic and time-resolved failure observables.

</details>


### [130] [Topological defects in out-of-equilibrium systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02482)
*Ylann Rouzaire*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该博士论文研究了二维非平衡系统中拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的行为，通过有噪声的Kuramoto晶格、可移动振子以及非互易O(2)模型，系统分析了活性（activity）、迁移率（mobility）和非互易性（non-reciprocity）如何影响序的维持与缺陷动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解二维非平衡系统中拓扑缺陷的行为，特别是在活性物质（active matter）背景下，活性、迁移率和非互易性如何破坏或维持长程序。

Method: 研究采用了三种模型：（1）具有短程耦合的有噪声Kuramoto晶格（noisy Kuramoto lattice）；（2）允许振子空间移动的扩展模型；（3）具有视觉锥耦合（vision-cone couplings）的非互易O(2)模型（non-reciprocal O(2) model），并推导了相应的连续场论。

Result: 在有噪声Kuramoto晶格中，固有频率异质性（intrinsic frequency heterogeneity）破坏了准长程序（quasi-long-range order），导致系统碎裂为有限畴区，缺陷在所有温度下解束缚（unbind）并表现出超扩散随机游走（superdiffusive random walks）。引入移动振子后，系统出现Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变并恢复准长程序。非互易O(2)模型中，非互易性选择缺陷形状、丰富湮灭过程并通过平流（advection）重塑斑图。

Conclusion: 活性和非互易性在非平衡系统中对拓扑缺陷的形成、演化以及有序化起着根本性的调节作用，迁移率是维持相干序的关键因素。

Abstract: In this PhD thesis, we study topological defects in two-dimensional non-equilibrium systems, focusing on active extensions of the XY model, including activity, mobility and non-reciprocity. In a noisy Kuramoto lattice with short-range coupling, intrinsic frequency heterogeneity destroys quasi-long-range order and fragments the system into finite domains. Defects unbind at all temperatures and exhibit superdiffusive random walks, advected by evolving domain boundaries. By contrast, when oscillators are allowed to move in space, the system undergoes a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition and regains quasi-long-range order, revealing the fundamental role of motility in sustaining coherence. We also analyse a non-reciprocal O(2) model with vision-cone couplings and derive a continuum theory that captures the same large-scale physics. Non-reciprocity selects defect shapes, enriches the annihilation process, and reshapes patterns through advection. Together, these results elucidate the fundamental role of activity and non-reciprocity in shaping topological defects and ordering in non-equilibrium systems.
  Keywords: Topological defects, XY model, Steep XY model, Kuramoto model, Non-reciprocal interactions, Active matter, Phase transitions, Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition, Non-equilibrium statistical mechanics

### [131] [A general thermodynamic approach for diffusion on a lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02579)
*Matías A. Di Muro,Miguel Hoyuelos*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通用热力学方法，通过将每个晶格位点视为开放热力学系统，利用化学势表示微观粒子相互作用，建立了Onsager矩阵（L）与其理想系统对应矩阵（L_id）之间的基本关系，成功应用于推导固体中替代扩散的Darken方程和表面扩散的Zhdanov模型非对角扩散矩阵，并通过数值模拟验证了分析预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 描述晶格上粒子扩散的输运过程（transport processes）时，微观粒子相互作用的影响难以直接处理；本文旨在提供一种通用热力学框架，将相互作用效应纳入化学势（chemical potential）中，从而简化输运系数的计算。

Method: 将每个晶格位点视为开放热力学系统（open thermodynamic system），以化学势表示微观相互作用；利用协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）的行列式建立Onsager矩阵与理想系统对应矩阵之间的基本关系，从而用理想值和热力学性质计算输运系数（transport coefficients）。

Result: 成功重现了固体中替代扩散（substitutional diffusion）的Darken方程（Darken equation），并推导了用于Langmuir粒子表面扩散（surface diffusion）的Zhdanov模型（Zhdanov model）中的非对角扩散矩阵（non-diagonal diffusion matrix）。针对Zhdanov模型，分析预测在不同相互作用势（interaction potentials）下均通过了数值模拟验证。

Conclusion: 该热力学框架能够统一且简洁地处理晶格扩散中的相互作用效应，为计算复杂输运系数提供了通用工具，且分析预测与数值模拟结果一致，证明了方法的有效性。

Abstract: This work presents a general thermodynamic approach to describe particle diffusion on a lattice, a model used to study transport processes in solids and on surfaces. By treating each lattice site as an open thermodynamic system, the effects of microscopic particle interactions are represented through the chemical potential. A fundamental relationship between the Onsager matrix ($L$) and its ideal-system counterpart ($L_\text{id}$, where interactions are neglected) using the determinant of the covariance matrix is demonstrated. This framework allows for the calculation of transport coefficients using the combination of their ideal values and thermodynamic properties. The general result is successfully applied to reproduce the Darken equation for substitutional diffusion in solids and to derive the non-diagonal diffusion matrix of the Zhdanov model for surface diffusion of Langmuir particles. In the last case, analytical predictions are further validated through numerical simulations across various interaction potentials.

### [132] [Geometric Formulation of Power-Efficiency Bounds in Carnot-like Engines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02732)
*R. X. Zhai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文将卡诺型热机的功率-效率约束表述为归一化分支耗散平面上的几何优化问题。通过将效率等高线视为直线，将固定功率下的最大效率问题转化为可容许直线的斜率边界问题。针对分支分辨的幂律耗散模型（各等温分支上的不可逆损失随分支时长以共同指数衰减，而非遵循标准反比律），在优化耗散不对称参数后，固定功率可达集退化为二维区域，斜率边界问题简化为线性规划。该框架给出了该模型下精确的功率-效率前沿，并针对代表性耗散指数（包括最大功率极限）提供了闭式约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有热机功率-效率关系的研究多依赖于标准反比耗散律，缺乏对更一般耗散行为的统一几何刻画。本文旨在将卡诺型热机的功率-效率约束表述为几何优化问题，并推广至分支分辨的幂律耗散场景。

Method: 在归一化分支耗散平面上将效率等高线表述为直线，将固定功率下的效率最大化转化为可容许直线的斜率边界问题；针对幂律耗散模型，通过优化耗散不对称参数将固定功率可达集简化为二维区域，进而将斜率边界问题归约为线性规划。

Result: 给出了该幂律耗散模型下精确的功率-效率前沿，并为代表性耗散指数（包括最大功率极限）推导出了闭式约束条件。

Conclusion: 所提出的几何优化框架能够统一处理更一般的热机耗散模型，并给出解析形式的功率-效率边界。

Abstract: We formulate the power-efficiency constraint of Carnot-like heat engines as a geometric optimization problem in the plane of normalized branch dissipations. Efficiency contours are straight lines in this plane, so maximizing efficiency at fixed power reduces to bounding the slope of an admissible line. We apply this framework to branch-resolved power-law dissipation, where the irreversible loss on each isothermal branch decays with the branch duration with a common exponent rather than following the standard inverse-time law. After optimizing over the dissipation-asymmetry parameter, the fixed-power attainable set becomes a two-dimensional region, and the resulting slope-bound problem reduces to linear programming. The framework yields the exact power-efficiency frontier within this model and gives closed-form constraints for representative dissipation exponents, including the maximum-power limit.

### [133] [Exact Microcanonical Formulation and Thermodynamics of Equispaced Finite-Level Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02736)
*J. Ricardo de Sousa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在热力学极限下，对具有p个等间距能级{0, ε, 2ε, ..., (p-1)ε}的N个无相互作用粒子系统进行精确微正则表述（microcanonical formulation）的方法。通过生成函数系数表示微正则多重度（microcanonical multiplicity），并利用鞍点分析（saddle-point analysis）导出熵和逆温度的解析表达式，统一描述了有限p系统的有界谱热力学行为及其随p→∞向无界谱的交叉过渡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）方法仅针对少数特定p值（如p=2、p=3及p→∞）有解，缺乏一个适用于任意能级数p的统一分析框架，以系统地研究有界能谱（bounded spectrum）系统的热力学性质及其极限行为。

Method: 将微正则多重度Ω_p(E,N)写为生成函数（generating function）的系数，随后通过鞍点分析对该表示进行渐进评估，导出每粒子熵s(u,p)和逆温度β(u,p)的解析表达式。

Result: 对于任意有限p，有界能谱导致在u_c=(p-1)/2处熵达到最大值，此时逆温度β=0并改变符号；当p→∞时，上谱界消失，有限能量下的熵最大值随之消失，负温度分支（negative-temperature branch）不复存在。该结果恢复了已知的p=2、p=3及p→∞的特殊情形。

Conclusion: 这是首次针对任意p给出的热力学极限下的微正则通用解，为等间距有限能级系统的热力学及其随p增大时从有界谱到无界谱的交叉过渡提供了一个统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We present an exact microcanonical formulation, in the thermodynamic limit, for a system of $N$ noninteracting particles with $p$ equally spaced energy levels $\{0,ε,2ε,\ldots,(p-1)ε\}$. Writing the microcanonical multiplicity $Ω_p(E,N)$ as the coefficient of a generating function and evaluating the resulting representation by saddle-point analysis, we derive analytical expressions for the entropy per particle $s(u,p)$ and inverse temperature $β(u,p)$, with $u=E/(Nε)$ in the interval $[0,p-1]$. The formulation applies to arbitrary $p$ and recovers the known cases $p=2$, $p=3$, and $p\to\infty$. For finite $p$, the bounded spectrum implies an entropy maximum at $u_c=(p-1)/2$, where $β$ vanishes and changes sign. In the limit $p\to\infty$, the upper spectral bound is lost, the finite-energy entropy maximum disappears, and no negative-temperature branch remains. To our knowledge, this is the first general thermodynamic-limit microcanonical solution for arbitrary $p$. It therefore provides a unified framework for the thermodynamics of equispaced finite-level systems and their bounded-spectrum crossover with increasing $p$.

</details>
