### [134] [Diffusion Operator Geometry of Feedforward Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01107)
*Kanishka Reddy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于扩散马尔可夫算子（diffusion Markov operator）的光滑算子几何框架，用于分析前馈神经网络表征的几何结构。通过Bakry-Emery Γ-演算从单一算子导出传输、谱、标签边界和局部尺度可观测量，并在高斯类条件快照模型下推导出封闭形式的类亲和度、泄露和粗谱，同时证明算子可观测量在特征扰动下光滑变化，而硬邻接图诊断可能不连续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，研究者利用邻接图（neighborhood graph）上的离散曲率研究神经网络表征几何，观察到类似里奇流（Ricci-flow）的层间行为。然而，离散方法在稳定性方面存在局限，需要一种更稳定、算子理论（operator-theoretic）的替代方案来系统分析前馈表征的几何结构。

Method: 对于每个特征云（feature cloud）快照，定义一个高斯核扩散马尔可夫算子（Gaussian-kernel diffusion Markov operator）。通过Bakry-Emery Γ-演算（Bakry-Emery Γ-calculus）从该单一算子导出传输、谱（spectral）、标签边界（label-boundary）和局部尺度（local-scale）可观测量。在平衡高斯类条件快照模型（balanced Gaussian class-conditional snapshot model）下，推导出类亲和度（class affinities）、泄露（leakage）和粗谱（coarse spectra）的封闭形式，这些量均由成对正则化马氏距离（pairwise regularized Mahalanobis separations）$c_\varepsilon^{(a,b)}$控制。

Result: 证明了算子可观测量在特征扰动下光滑变化，而硬邻接图诊断可能发生不连续变化。合成实验验证了封闭形式高斯桥接模型的有效性；在MNIST数据集上的实验表明，同一算子可观测量能够追踪训练过程、网络宽度和扰动稳定性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个稳定的算子几何框架（stable operator-geometric framework），用于分析前馈表征的几何结构，克服了离散邻接图方法的不稳定性问题。

Abstract: Neural networks transform data through learned representations whose geometry affects separation, contraction, and generalization. Recent work studies this geometry using discrete curvature on neighborhood graphs, suggesting Ricci-flow-like behavior across layers. We develop a smooth operator-theoretic alternative for feedforward representation snapshots. Each feature cloud induces a Gaussian-kernel diffusion Markov operator, and transport, spectral, label-boundary, and local-scale observables are derived from this single object via Bakry-Emery $Γ$-calculus. In a balanced Gaussian class-conditional snapshot model with shared covariance, the population operator has closed-form class affinities, leakage, and coarse spectra, all controlled by pairwise regularized Mahalanobis separations $c_\varepsilon^{(a,b)}$. We also prove that the resulting operator observables vary smoothly under feature perturbations, while hard neighborhood-graph diagnostics can change discontinuously. Synthetic experiments validate the closed-form Gaussian bridge, while learned MNIST experiments show that the same operator observables track training, width, and perturbation stability. Together, these results give a stable operator-geometric framework for analyzing feedforward representation geometry.

</details>


### [135] [A Theory of Saddle Escape in Deep Nonlinear Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01288)
*Divit Rawal,Michael R. DeWeese*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文推导了深度非线性网络中权值矩阵弗罗贝尼乌斯范数（Frobenius norm）不平衡性的精确恒等式，据此将激活函数分为四个普适类（universality class），并在置换对称子流形（permutation-symmetric submanifold）上将全矩阵流约化为标量常微分方程（scalar ODE），得到由瓶颈层（bottleneck layer）数量r而非总层数L决定的临界深度逃逸时间律（critical-depth escape time law）τ⋆ = Θ(ε^{-(r-2)})，且理论与数值模拟高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 浅层非线性网络与深层线性网络已得到充分研究，但将类似分析推广到深层非线性网络仍具挑战性。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 推导了深度网络中任意平滑激活函数（smooth activation）和任意可微损失（differentiable loss）下权值矩阵弗罗贝尼乌斯范数不平衡性的精确恒等式；据此将激活函数分为四个普适类；在置换对称子流形上结合近似平衡律（approximate balance law）将全矩阵流约化为标量ODE。

Result: 得到了由瓶颈层数量r而非总层数L控制的临界深度逃逸时间律τ⋆ = Θ(ε^{-(r-2)})；该指数在He正态初始化（He-normal initialization）下仍然成立，此时对称流形为流所保持但不具有吸引性（attracting）。数值模拟与理论计算高度一致。

Conclusion: 深层网络小初始化训练中的长平台（long plateau）与特征获取跃迁（feature-acquisition transition）可由瓶颈层架构尺度统一刻画，且该现象对初始化的对称性条件具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: In deep networks with small initialization, training exhibits long plateaus separated by sharp feature-acquisition transitions. Whereas shallow nonlinear networks and deep linear networks are well studied, extending these analyses to deep nonlinear networks remains challenging. We derive an exact identity for the imbalance of Frobenius norms of layer weight matrices that holds for any smooth activation and any differentiable loss and use this to classify activation functions into four universality classes. On the permutation-symmetric submanifold, the identity combines with an approximate balance law to reduce the full matrix flow to a scalar ODE, giving a critical-depth escape time law $τ_\star = Θ(\varepsilon^{-(r-2)})$ governed by the number $r$ of layers at the bottleneck scale rather than the total depth $L$. We find that this same $r-2$ exponent is recovered under He-normal initialization with $r$ bottleneck layers rescaled by $\varepsilon$, where the symmetry manifold is preserved by the flow but not attracting. We find close agreement between our theory and numerical simulations.

</details>


### [136] [Sequential Learning and Catastrophic Forgetting in Differentiable Resistor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01383)
*Maniru Ibrahim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究可微电阻网络（differentiable resistor networks）中的序列学习（sequential learning）问题，发现基于梯度的连续任务训练会产生灾难性遗忘（catastrophic forgetting），并揭示遗忘与任务冲突、适应程度、高电流边缘的局部电导变化以及网络拓扑结构密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可微物理网络（differentiable physical networks）这一简单设定中，探索可训练参数与物理平衡约束（physical equilibrium constraints）相互作用下的学习机制，特别是序列学习中的灾难性遗忘现象。

Method: 基于基尔霍夫定律（Kirchhoff's laws）构建可微电阻网络，通过梯度下降调整边缘电导（edge conductances）来学习输入-输出映射；采用均匀锚定（uniform anchoring）和归一化梯度加权锚定（normalised gradient-weighted anchoring）两种方法尝试减轻遗忘；并在多种图拓扑（Erdős–Rényi、小世界（small-world）、无标度（scale-free）、随机几何图（random-geometric graph））上进行比较实验。

Result: 遗忘受任务冲突和适应新任务的程度控制；两种锚定方法仅通过增加新任务的最终损失来减少遗忘，存在明确的遗忘-适应权衡（forgetting–adaptation trade-off）；遗忘与高电流边缘上的局部电导变化相关，对应主导输运路径（dominant transport pathways）的重新配置；当第二个任务反转第一个任务施加的输出顺序时，遗忘最严重；图拓扑改变遗忘-适应平衡。

Conclusion: 可微电阻网络可作为紧凑且物理可解释的测试平台（testbeds），用于研究可调物质（tunable matter）中的持续学习（continual learning）现象。

Abstract: Differentiable physical networks provide a simple setting in which learning can be studied through the interaction between trainable parameters and physical equilibrium constraints. We investigate sequential learning in differentiable resistor networks governed by Kirchhoff's laws. Although individual input--output mappings can be learned by gradient-based adjustment of edge conductances, sequential training on conflicting tasks produces catastrophic forgetting. We show that forgetting is controlled by task conflict and by the degree of adaptation to the new task. Uniform anchoring and normalised gradient-weighted anchoring reduce forgetting only by increasing the final loss on the new task, giving a clear forgetting--adaptation trade-off. We also show that forgetting is associated with localised conductance changes on high-current edges, giving a physical interpretation as reconfiguration of dominant transport pathways. Broader random-task ensembles show that the strongest forgetting occurs when the second task reverses the output ordering imposed by the first task. Finally, comparisons across Erdős--Rényi, small-world, scale-free, and random-geometric graph ensembles show that topology changes the forgetting--adaptation balance. These results position differentiable resistor networks as compact, physically interpretable testbeds for studying continual learning in tunable matter.

</details>

### [137] [Model-agnostic cooling algorithms for strongly interacting fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01029)
*Henning Schlömer,Liyuan Chen,Susanne F. Yelin,Hong-Ye Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需谱信息的随机化、对称性保持的耗散冷却算法，利用随机采样能级分裂的局域耦合算符驱动强关联费米子体系趋向低能流形，并在多种关联费米子模型上展现出普适的冷却行为，为可编程量子设备上制备强关联费米子态提供了一种通用策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强相互作用费米子（strongly interacting fermions）体系（如高温超导体）的低能态编码了其关键微观性质，但经典方法难以求解。虽然量子模拟（quantum simulation）和 engineered dissipation 提供了一条有前景的路径，但现有冷却协议通常依赖准粒子谱（quasiparticle spectrum）知识或自由费米子极限的映射，缺乏通用性。

Method: 提出一种随机化的、对称性保持的冷却算法（randomized, symmetry-preserving cooling algorithm），无需任何谱信息，仅通过将局域耦合算符（local coupling operators）耦合到具有随机采样能级分裂（randomly sampled energy splittings）的辅助自由度（ancilla degrees of freedom）上，驱动一般费米子体系趋向其低能流形。

Result: 在金属相、密度波相、配对相、超导相和相分离相等多种与高温超导体相关的规范关联费米子模型上进行基准测试，观察到普适的冷却行为（universal cooling behavior）：单调的能量弛豫（monotonic energy relaxation）、低能谱权重的集中（concentration of spectral weight at low energies）、以及关联基态序（correlated ground-state order）的稳定化。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，随机化耗散冷却（randomized dissipative cooling）可作为在可编程量子设备（programmable quantum devices）上制备强关联费米子态（strongly correlated fermionic states）的一种通用策略。

Abstract: Strongly interacting fermions underpin some of the most challenging problems in condensed matter physics, such as high-temperature superconductivity. The low-energy states of these systems encode their essential microscopic properties, yet remain largely inaccessible to classical methods. Quantum simulation offers a promising path forward, and among state-preparation strategies, engineered dissipation has emerged as a particularly compelling approach. Existing cooling protocols, however, typically rely on knowledge of the quasiparticle spectrum or mappings to free-fermion limits. In this letter, we introduce a randomized, symmetry-preserving cooling algorithm that requires no spectral information, using only local coupling operators to ancilla degrees of freedom with randomly sampled energy splittings to drive generic fermionic systems toward their low-energy manifold. We benchmark the protocol on canonical correlated fermionic models relevant to high-temperature superconductors, spanning metallic, density-wave, paired, superconducting, and phase-separated phases. Across all models, we observe universal cooling behavior: monotonic energy relaxation, concentration of spectral weight at low energies, and stabilization of correlated ground-state order. Our results establish randomized dissipative cooling as a general strategy for preparing strongly correlated fermionic states on programmable quantum devices.

</details>

### [139] [Interplay of Valley, Orbital, Spin, and Layer Degrees of Freedom in Ta$_2$CS$_2$ MXene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01271)
*Kunal Dutta,Anupam Mondal,Sayantika Bhowal,Subhradip Ghosh,Indra Dasgupta*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 论文通过第一性原理计算表明，非中心对称MXene材料Ta₂CS₂能够同时容纳谷（valley）、自旋（spin）、轨道（orbital）和层（layer）多个耦合自由度，并在自旋-轨道耦合作用下产生谷依赖和层依赖的自旋分裂；此外，内禀电极化可作为调控参数实现对这些自由度的控制，进而产生可开关的谷依赖轨道矩和类塞曼自旋分裂，并最终体现为轨道霍尔效应和自旋霍尔效应，为下一代自旋轨道电子学器件奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何在二维材料中同时容纳并调控多个耦合自由度（valley、spin、orbital、layer），以揭示其相互作用机制和可调性，从而为新型自旋轨道电子学（spin-orbitronics）器件的设计提供物理基础。

Method: 基于第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析MXene Ta₂CS₂的电子结构，研究谷-轨道耦合（valley-orbital coupling）和轨道-层耦合（orbital-layer coupling）的相互作用，并考察内禀电极化（intrinsic electric polarization）作为外部调控参数对多个自由度的控制效果。

Result: 在Ta₂CS₂中发现了多种耦合自由度，包括谷-轨道耦合和轨道-层耦合；自旋-轨道相互作用导致谷依赖和层依赖的电子带自旋分裂；内禀电极化能够调控这些自由度，产生可开关的谷依赖轨道矩和类塞曼自旋分裂（Zeeman-like spin splitting）；这些轨道和自旋织构（textures）分别表现为轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）和自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）。

Conclusion: 非中心对称MXene材料是研究多个自由度相互作用及其可调性的理想平台，能够产生丰富的轨道和自旋输运现象，为下一代自旋轨道电子学器件的开发开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We show that the MXene Ta$_2$CS$_2$ provides an excellent platform for hosting multiple coupled degrees of freedom, viz., valley, spin, orbital, and layer. The interplay among these degrees of freedom gives rise to a range of intriguing properties in reciprocal space, including valley-orbital and orbital-layer coupling. In the presence of spin-orbit interaction, these couplings lead to valley-dependent and layer-dependent spin splitting of the electronic bands. We further show that the intrinsic electric polarization in Ta$_2$CS$_2$ introduces an additional tuning parameter, enabling control over these coupled degrees of freedom and resulting in switchable valley-dependent orbital moments and Zeeman-like spin splitting. We demonstrate that these nontrivial orbital and spin textures manifest in the orbital and spin Hall effects, respectively. Our results establish noncentrosymmetric MXenes as a promising platform for exploring the interplay among multiple degrees of freedom, their tunability, and the resulting orbital and spin transport phenomena in these two-dimensional materials, thereby paving the way for next-generation spin-orbitronic devices.

Abstract: Electronic and structural degrees of freedom are often intimately coupled in strongly correlated systems, which result in intriguing macroscopic and microscopic phenomena. Using the well-studied material VO$_2$ as a prototype, here we explore the domain distribution across the metal-insulator transition (MIT). We use macroscopic as well as microscopic techniques, such as first-order reversal curve (FORC) and infrared imaging, to probe the domain distributions across the MIT. This study compares MIT in thin films of VO$_2$ with different grain sizes grown by pulsed laser deposition and dc sputtering. We explore the relation between the nature of the FORC distribution and the corresponding thermal hysteresis due to interactions between the supercooled metallic domains and surrounding insulating matrix. Our multi-probe study with quantitative analysis provides a correlation between the growth, domain interaction, and domain nucleation process in MIT.

### [141] [Collinear ferromagnetism with reduced moment length in kagome magnet Nd3Ru4Al12](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01447)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决关于Kagome晶格磁体Nd3Ru4Al12磁基态（magnetic ground state）的争议，纠正此前文献提出的不等磁矩长度模型。

Method: 采用单晶中子衍射（single-crystal neutron diffraction）并结合极化中子（polarized neutrons）实验；通过分析极化中子散射中的翻转比（flipping ratio）来验证磁结构模型。

Result: 该材料被确认为共线铁磁体（collinear ferromagnet），即“hex-FM”态，具有均匀磁矩长度mc = 2.1 μB/Nd和序参量波矢Q = 0；翻转比分析结果与hex-FM态一致，排除了此前提出的“ortho-FM”态。

Abstract: We determine the magnetic ground state of the kagome lattice magnet Nd3Ru4Al12 by single-crystal neutron diffraction, supported by experiments with polarized neutrons. We identify this material as a collinear ferromagnet ("hex-FM") with uniform moment length mc = 2.1 μB/Nd and ordering vector Q = 0, in contrast to a previous, seminal report that proposed unequal moment lengths on two Nd sites, here called the "ortho-FM" state. Our analysis of the flipping ratio in polarized neutron scattering is consistent with the hex-FM state. The results provide a microscopic basis for understanding the large fluctuation-induced Hall and Nernst responses near TC = 41 K, as previously reported for Nd3Ru4Al12.

### [142] [Topological Ising superconductivity in two-dimensional p-wave magnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01686)
*Kyoung-Min Kim,Gibaik Sim,Moon Jip Park*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文研究了方形晶格p波磁体中的超导不稳定性，发现奇宇称交换场可在无强自旋-轨道耦合条件下诱导拓扑超导电性，主导不稳定性为可调谐的s+p_x Ising态，并在特定条件下进入具有马约拉纳边缘态的节点拓扑超导相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由非相对论性交换场（non-relativistic exchange field）产生的费米面自旋劈裂能否在不依赖强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的情况下，为拓扑超导电性（topological superconductivity）提供新途径。

Method: 对具有在位和最近邻吸引相互作用的方形晶格p波磁体（square-lattice p-wave magnet）进行超导不稳定性（superconducting instabilities）分析。

Result: 奇宇称交换场移除了自旋劈裂电子结构中的反演对称性，允许单态和三态序参量在单一A1对称性通道内混合；主导不稳定性为耦合的s+p_x Ising态，其单态-三态平衡可通过最近邻吸引的相对强度连续调节；当三态间隙振幅超过单态时，该Ising态转变为具有马约拉纳边缘模（Majorana edge modes）的节点拓扑超导相；垂直于交换场的塞曼场（Zeeman field）可诱导Z2拓扑超导相。

Conclusion: 非相对论性交换场为拓扑超导电性提供了一种不依赖强自旋-轨道耦合的新机制，所获得的拓扑超导相具有可调谐性和丰富的边缘态拓扑保护特性。

Abstract: Fermi-surface spin splitting generated by non-relativistic exchange fields provides a new route to topological superconductivity without relying on strong spin-orbit coupling. Here, we study superconducting instabilities of a square-lattice $p$-wave magnet with onsite and nearest-neighbour attractive interactions. The odd-parity exchange field removes inversion symmetry in the spin-split electronic structure, allowing singlet and triplet order parameters to mix within a single $A_1$ symmetry channel. The leading instability is a coupled $s+p_x$ Ising state, whose singlet-triplet balance is continuously tunable by the relative strength of the nearest-neighbour attraction. When the triplet gap amplitude exceeds the singlet one, this Ising state undergoes a transition into a nodal topological superconducting phase with Majorana edge modes protected by momentum-resolved winding numbers. These modes extend over finite momentum intervals bounded by the surface projections of bulk point nodes. We further show that a Zeeman field perpendicular to the exchange field can induce a $Z_2$ topological superconducting phase, even in the regime where a single gap dominates.

</details>


### [143] [Field-induced metal-insulator transition, Chern insulators, and topological semimetals in a clean magnetic semiconductor GdGaI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01804)
*Kazuki Guzman,Hiroaki Ishizuka*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文基于低载流子密度磁半导体 GdGaI 中发现的四子格三重-𝑞（triple-𝑞）磁序，构建了一个耦合 Γ 点 Ga 4p 空穴口袋与三个 M 点 Gd 5d 电子口袋的有效理论。在反铁磁伞状态（零净磁化）下，模型呈现出陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）相（𝐶=0 和 𝐶=±4）与金属相之间的转变；通过 Γ 点解析低能理论，揭示了拓扑相边界由双重简并的双外尔半金属（double-Weyl semimetal）描述，自然解释了陈数（Chern number）跳跃 Δ𝐶=4。外加磁场调控倾角（canting angle）可驱动绝缘体-金属转变，并稳定额外的 𝐶=±2 陈绝缘体相。这些结果将 GdGaI 及其同族化合物识别为在洁净磁半导体中实现拓扑相和场致金属-绝缘体转变的高度可调平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低载流子密度半导体中的非共面磁序（non-coplanar magnetic order）为自旋-电荷耦合重塑电子结构并诱导非平庸拓扑相提供了平台。近来在磁半导体 GdGaI 中发现了四子格三重-𝑞 磁序，这激发了构建有效理论以理解该体系中拓扑相的起源与调控机制的需求。

Method: 构建了一个耦合 Γ 点 Ga 4p 空穴口袋与三个 M 点 Gd 5d 电子口袋的有效理论，包含四个交换通道（exchange channels）。针对反铁磁伞状态（antiferromagnetic umbrella state，零净磁化）模型，推导了 Γ 点的解析低能理论，并分析了陈数（Chern number）变化与拓扑相边界。

Result: 模型在零净磁化下呈现出 𝐶=0 和 𝐶=±4 的陈绝缘体相，其间由金属区域隔开。Γ 点低能理论显示拓扑相边界由两个简并的双外尔半金属描述，自然解释了陈数跳跃 Δ𝐶=4。在 𝑝-𝑑 交换耦合缺失时，费米能级附近出现钉扎的类节线态（nodal-line-like state），将 𝐶=±4 相在倾角 𝜃=arccos(1/3) 处二分。外加磁场调控倾角可驱动陈绝缘体相发生绝缘体-金属转变，而平庸绝缘体基本不受影响；当均匀磁化交换耦合变得可观时，还稳定了 𝐶=±2 的陈绝缘体相。

Conclusion: GdGaI 及其同族化合物可被用作高度可调的平台，用于在洁净磁半导体中实现多种拓扑相（陈绝缘体、双外尔半金属）以及场诱导的金属-绝缘体转变（field-induced metal-insulator transition）。

Abstract: Non-coplanar magnetic order in low-carrier-density semiconductors provides a platform on which spin-charge coupling can reshape the electronic structure and induce nontrivial topological phases. Motivated by the recent discovery of the four-sublattice triple-$q$ order in the magnetic semiconductor GdGaI, we study an effective theory that couples a Ga $4p$ hole pocket at the $Γ$ point to three Gd $5d$ electron pockets at the $M$ points through four exchange channels. For the antiferromagnetic umbrella state with zero net magnetization, the model hosts trivial ($C = 0$) and $C = \pm 4$ Chern insulator phases separated by metallic regions; by deriving an analytical low-energy theory at the $Γ$ point, we show that the topological phase boundary is described by two degenerate double-Weyl semimetals, naturally explaining the $ΔC = 4$ jump in the Chern number. In addition, a nodal-line-like state pinned near the Fermi level emerges in the absence of the $p$-$d$ exchange coupling, which separates the $C=\pm4$ phases for $θ=\arccos(1/3)$ into two. Tuning the canting angle by an external magnetic field drives an insulator-to-metal transition out of the Chern insulator phase while leaving the trivial insulator largely intact, and stabilizes an additional $C = \pm 2$ Chern insulator phase when the uniform-magnetization exchange couplings become appreciable. These results identify GdGaI and its sister compounds as highly tunable platforms for realizing topological phases and field-induced metal-insulator transitions in clean magnetic semiconductors.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将两个退耦合的Wen棋盘模型（Wen plaquette models）堆叠，通过引入位错修改哈密顿量（Hamiltonian），产生局域化扭结缺陷并诱导层间相互作用；利用分支割线（branch cuts）作为任意子置换源，通过计算量子维度及构建双环算子（double loop operators）分析缺陷的非阿贝尔融合规则。

Abstract: In this work, we explore a microscopic realization of three types of anyonic symmetries in a $\mathbb{Z}_2\times\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological order, corresponding to a double toric code. These symmetries act as nontrivial permutations on the anyon labels of the parent state. We consider a setup consisting of two decoupled Wen plaquette models stacked on top of each other and introduce dislocations that modify the Hamiltonian, giving rise to localized twist defects, eventually inducing interactions between the layers. In this context, branch cuts act as sources of anyon permutations when they cross it. ### [145] [Validity and Limits of Low Order Hybridization Expansion Approaches for Multi-Orbital Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02228)
*Dolev Goldberger,Ido Zemach,Lei Zhang,Yang Yu,Emanuel Gull,Guy Cohen,André Erpenbeck*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过解耦轨道极限推导了多轨道杂质求解器中低阶展开方法（NCA和OCA）的解析结果，发现其精度受最弱关联轨道控制，该轨道的快速衰减行为会通过截断展开产生的虚假耦合传递给所有其他轨道，抑制Kondo共振等关联效应。数值验证了在双轨道模型中的适用参数区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非交叉近似（non-crossing approximation, NCA）和单交叉近似（one-crossing approximation, OCA）等低阶杂化展开方法被广泛用作强关联系统（strongly correlated systems）的杂质求解器（impurity solvers），但它们在真实多轨道（multi-orbital）环境中的准确性尚不清楚。

Method: 以解耦轨道极限（decoupled orbital limit）作为受控参考点，推导将多轨道限制传播子（restricted propagators）和格林函数（Green's functions）与单轨道对应量关联的解析结果，识别导致低阶方法在多轨道设置中失效的图论机制（diagrammatic mechanisms），并通过代表性双轨道稳态模型系统进行数值验证。

Result: 低阶方法的精度由关联最弱的轨道（即 retardation Green's function 衰减最快的轨道）决定：该轨道的性质通过截断展开（truncated expansion）产生的虚假耦合（spurious coupling）被传递给所有其他轨道，从而抑制Kondo共振（Kondo resonance）等关联效应。即使在单轨道计算中使用相同近似方案被认定为强关联的轨道上，这一现象也会发生。

Conclusion: 该结果为评估单轨道计算结果在何种条件下可推广到多轨道环境提供了实用指南，并为高阶多轨道杂质求解器的开发与验证提供了基准。

Abstract: Low-order hybridization expansion methods such as the non-crossing approximation (NCA) and the one-crossing approximation (OCA) are widely used impurity solvers in the study of strongly correlated systems, yet their accuracy in genuine multi-orbital settings remains poorly understood. Using the decoupled orbital limit as a controlled reference point, we derive analytic results connecting multi-orbital restricted propagators and Green's functions to their single-orbital counterparts, identify the diagrammatic mechanisms responsible for the breakdown of low-order methods in multi-orbital settings, and determine their regimes of applicability. Our central finding is that the accuracy of these methods is governed by the least correlated orbital: i.e., the orbital with the most rapidly decaying retarded Green's function. That orbital's properties are transferred to all other orbitals through a spurious coupling generated by the truncated expansion, thereby suppressing correlation-induced features such as the Kondo resonance. This occurs even in orbitals that are themselves strongly correlated within single-orbital calculations using the same approximation scheme. We confirm this numerically across representative two-orbital model systems in the steady-state, systematically identifying the parameter regimes in which low-order methods succeed or fail. Our results provide a practical guide for assessing when insights from single-orbital calculations carry over to multi-orbital settings, and serve as a benchmark for the development and validation of higher-order multi-orbital impurity solvers.

</details>

Result: 在金属区整个范围内 m*/m 接近单位值，呈现浅的非单调密度依赖——在 r_s ≈ 1 附近存在极小值随后缓慢回升——反映了自能中交换与动态屏蔽（dynamical screening）的相互作用，且不支持强烈的单调抑制行为。

Conclusion: 该结果支持金属均匀电子气的物理图像：占主导的电荷关联（charge correlations）主要集中在近前向散射（nearly forward scattering），仅产生较弱的 F₁^s 分量。

Abstract: The quasiparticle effective mass $m^*$ of the three-dimensional uniform electron gas (UEG) is a fundamental Fermi-liquid parameter whose value and density dependence have remained controversial for decades. Using renormalized perturbation theory with explicit counterterms, we determine $m^*$ in the metallic regime ($r_s \le 6$) from first principles by two complementary routes -- the self-energy and the forward-scattering four-point vertex via the $p$-wave spin-symmetric Landau parameter $F_1^s$ -- that agree within uncertainties at each density through sixth renormalized order. The resulting $m^*/m$ remains close to unity throughout the metallic regime, with a shallow non-monotonic density dependence -- a minimum near $r_s\approx 1$ followed by a gentle upturn -- reflecting the interplay of exchange and dynamical screening in the self-energy, and disfavoring strong monotonic suppression. This finding supports a physical picture for the metallic UEG in which dominant charge correlations are concentrated in nearly forward scattering and generate only a weak $F_1^s$ component.

### [147] [Exchange-frustrated quadrupoles on the honeycomb lattice: Flavor-wave spectra, classical degeneracies and parton constructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02336)

Abstract: We study the quadrupolar Kitaev model, an $S=1$ honeycomb-lattice model with frustrated bond-dependent quadrupolar interactions. Using complementary methods and expanding around controlled limits, we uncover several intertwined structures. First, a semiclassical variational analysis based on $\mathrm{SU}(3)$ flavor theory reveals an extensively degenerate manifold of classical mean-field ground states, suggesting that quantum fluctuations may stabilize a quantum-disordered phase. Second, in the bond-anisotropic limit, perturbation theory is used to derive effective low-energy Hamiltonians, which crucially depend on the presence (or absence) of a residual symmetry $\mathcal{M}$ of combined lattice reflection and discrete spin rotation. A Majorana parton construction uncovers an exact $\mathbb Z_2$ gauge structure and motivates possible confined and deconfined phases driven by gauge-charge condensation, consistent with the effective theories obtained in anisotropic limit. Further, within the same parton formalism, different Majorana mean-field ansätze produce both gapless and gapped candidate quantum-disordered states, distinguished by linear versus projective implementations of $\mathcal M$. Our results highlight frustrated quadrupolar interactions as a route to quantum-disordered phases, relevant to $S \geq 1$ Kitaev materials and Rydberg-array quantum simulators.

### [148] [Entanglement signature of fully and partially dimerized phases in frustrated spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02581)
*Wuttichai Pankeaw,Teparksorn Pengpan,Pruet Kalasuwan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The von Neumann entanglement entropy of exact valence-bond ground states is studied in two frustrated one-dimensional spin chains: the spin-1/2 Majumdar-Ghosh (MG) model and the spin-3/2 J1-J2-J3 chain in its fully dimerized (FD) and partially dimerized (PD) phases. Using matrix-product-state representations, the entropy is computed as a function of system size for three complementary bipartitions - half-chain, single-site, and pairwise - under both open and periodic boundary conditions. In all cases, the entropy saturates to a finite constant in the thermodynamic limit, confirming area-law behavior. The saturation values, extracted via finite-size scaling, are directly related to the underlying virtual-spin bond structure. The MG model and FD phase exhibit similar entanglement behavior, differing primarily in saturation magnitude determined by spin value and bond multiplicity, and both display even-odd oscillations and exponential convergence with system size. In contrast, the PD phase shows qualitatively distinct signatures, including multiple half-chain saturation values depending on the bond type at the cut, asymmetric edge contributions in the single-site entropy, and a multi-band structure in the pairwise entropy reflecting the coexistence of single- and double-singlet bonds. These results establish entanglement entropy as a robust signature of frustrated bond architecture, enabling clear distinction among dimerized phases with different spin magnitude, bond multiplicity, and dimerization patterns.

### [149] [NESSi 2.0: The Non-Equilibrium Systems Simulation package version 2.0](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02606)
*Fabian Künzel,Michael Schüler,Denis Golež,Yuta Murakami,Sujay Ray,Christopher Stahl,Jiajun Li,Hugo U. R. Strand,Philipp Werner,Martin Eckstein*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过引入内存截断（memory truncation）和非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady states）描述技术，扩展了非平衡格林函数模拟平台NESSi，将计算复杂度从O(N_t^3)降低至O(N_t N_c^2)，从而克服了大时间跨度动力学模拟的计算瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于非平衡格林函数（Nonequilibrium Green's functions）的模拟在面对大时间跨度动力学（如亚飞秒电子动力学到皮秒集体模动力学）时，由于Kadanoff-Baym方程中记忆积分的存在，计算复杂度随时间步数N_t呈三次方增长（O(N_t^3)），内存需求呈二次方增长（O(N_t^2)），严重限制了长时模拟的可行性。

Method: 本文采用两种技术扩展NESSi平台：（i）对Kadanoff-Baym方程中的记忆积分进行截断，最多保留N_c个时间步长，将计算复杂度降至O(N_t N_c^2)，内存需求降至O(N_c^2)；（ii）引入描述非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady states）的功能，这类态具有时间平移不变性（time-translational invariance），适用于输运设置和缓慢演化的预平衡态（prethermal states）的近似描述。

Result: 通过记忆截断，在结果关于截断参数N_c收敛的前提下，可将模拟显著延长至更长时间尺度；同时，非平衡稳态功能的引入使得模拟适用于输运场景及缓慢演化的非平衡态。

Conclusion: 本文提出的扩展方案有效缓解了非平衡格林函数模拟的计算瓶颈，为研究激光诱导固体动力学等长时量子多体动力学问题提供了更高效的数值工具。

Abstract: Nonequilibrium Green's functions provide a powerful framework for studying quantum many-body dynamics including the laser-induced dynamics in solids. The Non-Equilibrium Systems Simulation package (NESSi) offers an efficient platform for such simulations, ranging from perturbative approaches like nonequilibrium $GW$ to nonequilibrium dynamical mean-field theory. However, simulations based on nonequilibrium Green's functions become computationally demanding when the dynamics span a large temporal range, such as from sub-femtosecond electron dynamics to the picosecond dynamics of collective modes. Due to the memory integral in the Kadanoff-Baym equations, which serve as equations of motion for nonequilibrium Green's functions, the computational cost scales as $\mathcal{O}(N_t^3)$ with the number of timesteps $N_t$, and the memory requirement scales as $\mathcal{O}(N_t^2)$. In this work, we extend NESSi by incorporating techniques that aim to overcome this bottleneck: (i) By truncating the memory integrals in the KBE to a maximum of $N_c$ timesteps, the computational complexity is reduced to $\mathcal{O}(N_tN_c^2)$, and the memory requirement to $\mathcal{O}(N_c^2)$. Provided that the results converge with respect to the cutoff $N_c$, memory truncation allows to extend the simulations to significantly longer times. (ii) We introduce functionalities to describe nonequilibrium steady states, i.e. time-translationally invariant nonequilibrium states. Such states are relevant for transport settings, and they provide an approximate description of slowly evolving (prethermal) nonequilibrium states.

Motivation: 强关联量子电子系统在非扩散输运（non-diffusive conduction）状态下，电磁扰动同时激发时间（频率依赖）和空间（波矢依赖）的电子动力学响应，其非局域电动力学响应尚未被精确确定。本文旨在解决这一理论空白。

Method: 基于局域频率依赖相互作用和电荷/质量守恒假设，利用重整化相互作用顶点的Bethe-Salpeter方程（Bethe-Salpeter equations）确保守恒律，并引入Kubo形式论（Kubo formalism）计算双粒子关联函数（如密度、电流、动量、应力）。通过分析顶点修正在动量空间中的对称性条件推导其消失判据。

Result: 证明了在单粒子色散具有反演对称性（inversion symmetry）且裸相互作用顶点在动量空间中特定点群变换（反演、镜像反射、二重或更高重旋转）下为奇函数时，顶点修正通常在q=0处消失。对于二次型色散，电流-电流关联函数中的顶点修正对任意q和ω均恒为零。进一步讨论了判据对对称性破缺、多带效应及动量守恒的鲁棒性，并应用于朗道能级霍尔黏度（Hall viscosity）。

Conclusion: 给出了费米液体（Fermi liquids，具有明确定义准粒子峰）和非费米液体（non-Fermi liquids，缺乏准粒子）在任意局域自能下的通用非局域关联函数显式表达式，为强关联量子流体电动力学响应的理论计算提供了精确框架。

Abstract: In non-diffusive conduction regimes of strongly correlated quantum electron systems, electromagnetic perturbations simultaneously probe the electronic dynamics in time and space: the exchanged energy $\hbar ω$ excites retarded, i.e., frequency-dependent, many-body interactions, while the probing spatial modulation renders the response spatially nonlocal, i.e., dependent on the external wave vector $\vec{q}$. This work determines the exact nonlocal electrodynamic response of such dynamical quantum fluids under the assumptions of local, frequency-dependent interactions and charge/mass conservation. The latter is ensured by Bethe-Salpeter equations for renormalized interaction vertices, entering the Kubo formalism for two-particle correlation functions (e.g., for density, currents, momentum, stress). Within such framework, it is shown that vertex corrections generally vanish at $q=0$ for single-particle dispersions with inversion symmetry and for bare interaction vertices that are odd with respect to specific point group transformations in momentum space, including inversion for vector vertices, and mirror reflections or two- or higher-fold rotations for tensor vertices. In addition, for quadratic dispersion vertex corrections identically vanish from the current-current correlation function, at any momentum $\vec{q}$ and frequency $ω$. The robustness of these criteria against further symmetry breaking, multiband effects, and additionally imposing momentum conservation, is discussed, with application to the Hall viscosity of Landau levels. Explicit expressions for generic nonlocal correlation functions are derived for Fermi liquids (with well-defined quasiparticle peaks) and non-Fermi liquids (devoid of quasiparticles), for arbitrary local self-energies.

</details>


### [151] [Exotic magnetism and persistent short-range spin correlations in a frustrated honeycomb lattice antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02683)
*M. Barik,Q. Faure,F. Damay,J. P. Embs,S. Petit,P. Khuntia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过宏观热力学测量和非弹性中子散射，系统研究了S=5/2扭曲蜂窝状磁体CaZn₂Fe(PO₄)₃的磁性和自旋动力学，发现竞争交换相互作用、弱伊辛型各向异性与自旋涨落之间的耦合导致非常规场致相变和自旋倾斜态，并将体系置于平均场三临界点附近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维高自旋二分蜂窝状网络（two-dimensional high-spin bipartite honeycomb networks）中各向异性（anisotropy）、竞争交换相互作用（competing exchange interactions）与自旋涨落（spin fluctuations）的耦合为检验经典与量子磁性理论模型提供了新平台，但相关实验体系尚不充分。

Method: 采用晶体结构解析、磁化强度（magnetization）、比热（specific heat）与非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）等多种实验手段，并结合自旋波计算（spin-wave calculations）对CaZn₂Fe(PO₄)₃进行综合分析。

Result: 磁化测量显示Fe³⁺（S=5/2）磁矩间以反铁磁相互作用为主；磁化率凹陷及其场演化表明存在非常规场致相变（field-induced transition）；零场比热在T_N≈1.67 K处出现反铁磁相变，且在场下演化并稳定出场致自旋倾斜态（field-induced spin-canted state）；热力学测量显示转变温度以上存在短程自旋关联；非弹性中子散射验证了反铁磁有序；自旋波计算揭示竞争交换相互作用引发的磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）与弱伊辛型各向异性（weak Ising-like anisotropy）。

Conclusion: 竞争相互作用与各向异性的耦合导致非常规场致行为，并将体系置于平均场三临界点（mean-field tricritical point）附近的J₂/J₁–J₃/J₁相图中，为高自旋阻挫蜂窝状磁体中非常规态的研究开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Two-dimensional high-spin bipartite honeycomb networks, where anisotropy, competing exchange interactions, and spin fluctuations interplay, provide an alternative platform to test theoretical models that distinguish between classical and quantum magnetism in the context of emergent many-body phenomena and exotic excitations. Here, we report the crystal structure, magnetization, specific heat, and inelastic neutron scattering measurements of the $S = 5/2$ distorted honeycomb magnet $\mathrm{CaZn_2Fe(PO_4)_3}$. Magnetization measurements reveal dominant antiferromagnetic interactions between the $\mathrm{Fe^{3+}}$ ($S = 5/2$) moments. The development and field evolution of a dip in the magnetic susceptibility under an external magnetic field indicate an unconventional field-induced transition, further supported by anomalies observed in magnetization isotherms. Zero-field specific heat measurements show an antiferromagnetic transition at $T_N \approx 1.67 \mathrm{K}$, which evolves under applied magnetic field, suggesting stabilization of a field-induced spin-canted state. Thermodynamic measurements reveal short-range spin correlations above the transition temperature. Inelastic neutron scattering results further corroborate antiferromagnetic ordering, consistent with specific heat data. Spin-wave calculations indicate competing exchange interactions that introduce magnetic frustration, along with weak Ising-like anisotropy. The interplay of competing interactions and anisotropy gives rise to exotic field-induced behavior and places the system in close proximity to a mean-field tricritical point in the $J_2/J_1$--$J_3/J_1$ phase diagram, opening a route to unconventional states in high-spin frustrated honeycomb magnets.

### [152] [Benchmarking the Dual Fermion approach on the Falicov-Kimball model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02717)
*Akshat Mishra,Hugo U. R. Strand,Erik G. C. P. van Loon*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过将阶梯双费米子（ladder Dual Fermion）方法与动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）在Falicov-Kimball模型上进行基准测试，并与精确经典蒙特卡洛（classical Monte Carlo）解进行对比，评估了双费米子方法的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强电子关联（strong electronic correlations）通常需要非微扰（non-perturbative）处理。双费米子方法建立在物理动机驱动但在原则上不可控的近似之上，因此需要仔细的基准测试以理解该方法的优势与局限性。

Method: 使用阶梯双费米子方法与动力学平均场理论计算Falicov-Kimball模型的热力学、电子结构（electronic structure）和磁化率（susceptibility），特别是联合频率与动量（combined frequency and momentum）结构，并将结果与精确经典蒙特卡洛解进行对比。

Result: 双费米子方法在热力学、电子结构和磁化率方面明显优于动力学平均场理论；但在掺杂体系中，关于轨道密度（orbital density）与化学势（chemical potential）之间的关系，双费米子方法的准确性不如预期。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了对于具有不等价轨道（inequivalent orbitals）的模型，需要对动力学平均场理论的图解扩展（diagrammatic extensions）进行严格的基准测试，这对材料建模至关重要。

Abstract: Strong electronic correlations generally require non-perturbative treatment. Local correlations are captured by dynamical mean-field theory while nonlocal correlations can be treated with diagrammatic extensions such as the Dual Fermion approach. Dual Fermion is built on physically motivated, but in principle uncontrolled approximations, so careful benchmarking is needed to understand the strengths and limitations of the method. In this work, we benchmark ladder Dual Fermion and dynamical mean-field theory for the Falicov-Kimball model with the exact classical Monte Carlo solution. We focus on the thermodynamics, electronic structure and susceptibility, especially at the combined frequency and momentum structure, and find that Dual Fermion clearly outperforms dynamical mean-field theory. Somewhat surprisingly, Dual Fermion is not as accurate for the relation between orbital density versus chemical potential in the doped system. These results demonstrate the need for rigorous benchmarking of diagrammatic extensions of dynamical mean-field theory for models with inequivalent orbitals, which is essential for modelling materials.

</details>


### [153] [Interlayer Five-Spin Polaron in Superconducting Bilayer Nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02891)
*Jiarui Li,Christopher T. Parzyck,Eder G. Lomeli,Yidi Liu,Taehun Kim,Heemin Lee,Zengqing Zhuo,Eun Kyo Ko,Yaoju Tarn,Cheng-Tai Kuo,Ronny Sutarto,Chunjing Jia,Vivek Thampy,Brian Moritz,Yijun Yu,Jun-Sik Lee,Valentina Bisogni,Thomas P. Devereaux,Harold Y. Hwang,Wei-Sheng Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究利用共振X射线散射（resonant X-ray scattering）技术，在双层镍氧化物超导薄膜La₂PrNi₂O₇中证实自旋密度波序与超导性存在相分离（phase segregation），并发现氧化学计量比（oxygen stoichiometry）是调控层间耦合与电子结构的关键参数，提出配体空穴形成的层间五自旋极化子态（five-spin polaron state）是超导基态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Ruddlesden-Popper型镍氧化物中发现高温超导电性后，理解磁基态与多轨道物理（multi-orbital physics）之间的相互作用是建立超导微观机制的关键问题。双层镍氧化物中自旋密度波（spin density wave, SDW）序在非超导区域显著存在，但其与超导配对的关系尚不明确，这一问题亟待解决。

Method: 采用共振X射线散射技术检测超导双层镍氧化物薄膜La₂PrNi₂O₇中SDW序的存在；通过对比超导样品与缺氧样品，结合Ni-L₃和O-K边光谱学（spectroscopy）表征电子结构差异。

Result: 超导电性出现在无SDW、氧化学计量比正常的区域，而氧缺乏会促进SDW序，表明SDW与超导性存在相分离。Ni-L₃和O-K边光谱揭示了两个区域间沿c轴方向电子结构的显著差异。氧化学计量比是控制层间耦合与电子结构的关键参数。

Conclusion: 结合理论分析，提出配体空穴主要位于层间顶角氧原子（inter-bilayer apical oxygen）上，形成一种稳健的层间五自旋极化子态，该态作为超导双层镍氧化物的基态。

Abstract: The discovery of high-$T_c$ superconductivity in Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates has sparked substantial effort towards understanding unconventional electronic states beyond a traditional cuprate-like d^9 configurational ground state. An understanding of the interplay between magnetic ground states and multi-orbital physics is key for establishing a microscopic mechanism for superconductivity. In the bilayer nickelates, spin density wave (SDW) order is a prominent feature in the non-superconducting regime. However, its relation to superconducting pairing remains an open question. Here, we use resonant x-ray scattering to examine the existence of SDW order in superconducting bilayer nickelate thin films La$_2$PrNi$_2$O$_7$ (LPNO). Comparing superconducting and oxygen-deficient LPNO thin films, we find that superconductivity occurs in SDW-free, oxygen-stoichiometric regions, whereas oxygen-deficiency promotes SDW order, indicating phase segregation of SDW and superconductivity. Furthermore, Ni-$L_3$ and O-$K$ edge spectroscopy reveals distinct electronic structures - particularly along the $c$-axis - between the two domains. Our results identify oxygen stoichiometry as a key parameter controlling interlayer coupling and thus the electronic structure of bilayer nickelates. In concert with theory, we propose that a ligand hole primarily resides at the inter-bilayer apical oxygen, forming a robust interlayer five-spin polaron state, which serves as the ground state for superconducting bilayer nickelates.

### [154] [Autonomous Reliability Qualification of Ga$_2$O$_3$-based Hydrogen and Temperature Sensors via Safe Active Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00868)
*Davi Febba,William A. Callahan,Anna Sacchi,Andriy Zakutayev*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种安全主动学习（Safe Active Learning, SAL）框架，用于在耦合热与氢气应力下自主表征整流型Ga₂O₃器件的可靠性。该方法将整流特性作为物理驱动的安全观测量，利用高斯过程（Gaussian process）代理模型建模其随时间的演化，并结合自适应完成时间窗口、置信下限安全检测、信任区域约束及两阶段策略实现安全探索。仿真与实验验证表明，SAL能够在保证安全的前提下扩展探索区域，并构建可用于长期退化建模的数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在严苛耦合应力（热与氢气）环境下，对整流型Ga₂O₃基器件进行自主可靠性表征时，需避免探索过程中的不安全测量，同时获取有效的退化数据。现有方法难以同时满足安全约束与数据高效采集的需求，因此需要一种安全感知的主动学习框架来平衡探索效率与安全性。

Method: SAL框架包含以下技术组件：以整流特性作为安全观测量，使用高斯过程（Gaussian process）代理模型建模其随时间的演化；采用自适应完成时间窗口处理条件依赖的、不确定的实验时长；通过时间窗口置信下限（lower-confidence-bound）进行安全检测；利用信任区域（trust region）锚定已验证的安全条件；采用两阶段策略，从保守安全探索过渡到逐步放宽的整流目标。此外，在离线阶段构建了具有条件依赖的Kohlrausch–Williams–Watts均值与残差协方差核的结构化高斯过程模型，用于长期预测。

Result: 在仿真中，SAL在保证安全的同时有效扩展了探索区域。在Pt/Cr₂O₃:Mg/β-Ga₂O₃器件的自动化高温探针台实验中，第一阶段仅发生一次由异常电流-电压扫描引起的不安全测量，第二阶段则有意探测了较低整流区域。离线模型成功捕捉了辅助验证数据集中的长期饱和退化趋势。

Conclusion: SAL框架实现了安全感知的自主实验，既支持保守的可靠性表征，又为后续退化建模提供了数据基础。该方法虽在整流型Ga₂O₃器件上验证，但可推广至其他具有可测量原位安全观测量的系统。

Abstract: We present a Safe Active Learning (SAL) framework for autonomous reliability characterization of rectifying Ga$_2$O$_3$-based devices under coupled thermal and hydrogen stress. SAL treats rectification as a device-physics-motivated safety observable and models its evolution over elapsed time, temperature, and H$_2$ concentration using a Gaussian-process surrogate. To handle condition-dependent and uncertain experiment durations, the method combines an adaptive completion-time window, time-window lower-confidence-bound safety checks, a trust region anchored to previously verified safe conditions, and a two-phase strategy that transitions from conservative safe exploration to progressively relaxed rectification targets as the device degrades. We first evaluate SAL in simulation, where it safely expands the explored region while learning the evolving rectification surface. We then demonstrate SAL experimentally on an automated high-temperature probe-station platform using a Pt/Cr$_2$O$_3$:Mg/$β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ device. In the reported campaign, phase 1 incurred only one unsafe measurement associated with spurious current-voltage sweeps, while phase 2 intentionally probed lower-rectification regimes. Finally, we use the curated SAL dataset for offline long-horizon forecasting of device response at a target voltage using a structured Gaussian-process model with a condition-dependent Kohlrausch--Williams--Watts mean and a residual covariance kernel. The model captures long-time, saturating degradation trends in an auxiliary validation dataset, illustrating how safety-aware autonomous experimentation enables both conservative characterization and subsequent degradation modeling. Although demonstrated for a rectifying Ga$_2$O$_3$ device, SAL is applicable to other systems where a measurable in situ safety observable can be defined.

</details>

### [155] [Bounds on massive graviton-like particles from searches for axion-like particles coupling to photons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00549)
*Jordan Gué,David d'Enterria*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将自旋-0 轴子类似粒子（ALP）与光子耦合的实验限制重新解释为对自旋-2 引力子类似粒子（GLP）与标准模型场之间普适耦合的约束，利用 Primakoff 和 Gertsenshtein 效应的形式类比，将 ALP 参数空间上的现有及未来实验界限映射到 GLP 平面上，并评估了未来实验对轻质量 GLP 的灵敏度潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对自旋-0 轴子类似粒子（ALPs）的搜索已覆盖极广的质量范围和多种实验设置，但自旋-2 引力子类似粒子（GLPs）在大质量区间所受的实验约束相对薄弱。本文旨在利用两类粒子在产生与探测机制上的形式类比，将已有且日益丰富的 ALP 实验限制系统地重新诠释为对 GLP 的约束，从而在不引入过多模型依赖的前提下填补自旋-2 粒子参数空间的实验空白。

Method: 采用最小模型依赖的重新演绎（recasting）方法，基于 Primakoff 效应和 Gertsenshtein 效应所导致的光子-轴子/引力子转换在形式上的类比，将 ALP 质量-光子耦合平面上的约束直接翻译到 GLP 质量-普适耦合参数空间。分析覆盖了从腔体探测器、太阳望远镜（helioscopes）、磁力计、光学干涉仪、束流 dump、固定靶及对撞机实验，到天体物理和宇宙学限制在内的全部质量范围。

Result: 在当前实验中，ALP 搜索对自旋-2 粒子施加的约束并未强于第五力（fifth-force）检验。但未来磁力计、双光束干涉仪和上转换（upconversion）实验对质量小于约 10⁻⁸ eV 的轻 GLP 具有极高灵敏度，耦合下限可达 α_G/M_P ≈ 10⁻³² GeV⁻¹，且未来探测器对质量型引力子的灵敏度高于对轴子的灵敏度。对 TeV 量级的大质量引力子，单举双光子衰变搜索可提供互补约束。

Conclusion: 现有 ALP 搜索无法超越第五力实验对自旋-2 粒子的限制，但未来特定实验对轻质量 GLP 具有显著增强的探测能力；高能标下双光子衰变搜索则是对传统自旋-2 共振搜索的有力补充。

Abstract: Limits on spin-0 axion-like-particles (ALPs) coupling to photons are reinterpreted as constraints on massive spin-2 graviton-like-particles (GLPs) with universal coupling $α_\text{G}/M_\text{P}$ (where $M_\text{P}$ is the reduced Planck mass) to the Standard Model fields. A minimally model-dependent recasting is performed, exploiting the formally analogous production and detection mechanisms for both particle types, based on the Primakoff and Gertsenshtein effects, i.e., photon-axion/graviton conversion. Constraints originally derived in the ALP mass vs. photon-coupling plane ($m_\text{a}, g_{\text{a}γ}$) are translated into the corresponding bounds in the GLP ($m_\text{G}, α_\text{G}/M_\text{P}$) parameter space over the full mass range, $m_\text{a,G} \approx 10^{-20}$--$10^{14}$eV probed in current and future experimental setups including cavity-based detectors (haloscopes and resonant upconversion devices), helioscopes, magnetometers, optical interferometers, beam dumps, fixed-target, and collider experiments, as well as astrophysical and cosmological constraints. Generic scenarios are considered in which GLPs are a dark matter candidate and not. Whereas current ALP searches do not set stronger bounds on massive spin-2 particles than fifth-force tests, future magnetometers, two-beam interferometers, and upconversion experiments have the potential to provide very strong sensitivity, down to $α_\text{G}/M_\text{P} \approx 10^{-32} \text{GeV}^{-1}$, for light graviton-like particles with $m_\text{G}\lesssim 10^{-8}$eV. These future detectors exhibit comparatively greater sensitivity to massive gravitons than to axions. For massive gravitons at the TeV scale, exclusive diphoton decay searches, employed in ALP studies, offer a complementary approach to standard searches for spin-2 resonances in other inclusive final states.

</details>


### [156] [Nuclear geometry driven symmetry plane correlations in OO and Ne--Ne collisions at the Large Hadron Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00866)
*Suraj Prasad,Raghunath Sahoo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究基于NLEFT和PGCM核几何构型，利用AMPT模型在5.36 TeV下模拟OO和Ne–Ne碰撞中的对称面关联（SPCs），发现Ne–Ne碰撞中$\langle \cos[4(ψ_2 - ψ_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$更大，而OO碰撞中$\langle \cos[6(ψ_3 - ψ_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$更大，表明$^{20}$Ne核存在强形变，$^{16}$O核存在四面体结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称面关联（symmetry-plane correlations, SPCs）是敏感的观测量，可反映介质输运性质，且由核重叠区域的参与者平面关联（participant-plane correlations, PPCs）驱动。本研究旨在探索氧–氧（OO）和氖–氖（Ne–Ne）碰撞中是否存在由核几何驱动的SPCs。

Method: 基于核晶格有效场论（Nuclear Lattice Effective Field Theory, NLEFT）和投影生成坐标法（Projected Generator Coordinate Method, PGCM）的核几何构型，利用多相输运模型（A Multi-Phase Transport Model, AMPT）在$\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV下模拟OO与Ne–Ne碰撞，计算$\langle \cos[4(ψ_2 - ψ_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$和$\langle \cos[6(ψ_3 - ψ_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$。

Result: Ne–Ne碰撞的$\langle \cos[4(ψ_2 - ψ_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$值大于OO碰撞，而OO碰撞的$\langle \cos[6(ψ_3 - ψ_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$值大于Ne–Ne碰撞。此外，对尖端–尖端（tip-tip）和体–体（body-body）碰撞构型的事件分析进一步支持了上述结果。

Conclusion: 观测到的SPCs差异表明$^{20}$Ne核具有强形变（strongly deformed shape），而$^{16}$O核具有四面体结构（tetrahedral structure）。

Abstract: Symmetry-plane correlations (SPCs) are key observables sensitive to the medium's transport properties and are driven by participant-plane correlations (PPCs) in the nuclear overlap region. This study explores the possibility of nuclear-geometry-driven SPCs in Oxygen--Oxygen (OO) and Neon--Neon (Ne--Ne) collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV using nuclear geometry simulations based on Nuclear Lattice Effective Field Theory (NLEFT) and Projected Generator Coordinate Method (PGCM) configurations. We investigate $\langle \cos[4(ψ_2 - ψ_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ and $\langle \cos[6(ψ_3 - ψ_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ in OO and Ne--Ne collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV using the A Multi-Phase Transport (AMPT) model. We find that Ne--Ne collisions exhibit larger $\langle \cos[4(ψ_2 - ψ_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ values than OO collisions, whereas $\langle \cos[6(ψ_3 - ψ_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ is larger in OO than in Ne--Ne collisions. This behavior indicates a strongly deformed shape of the $^{20}$Ne nucleus and a tetrahedral structure of the $^{16}$O nucleus. We also explore SPCs for events with tip-tip and body-body collision configurations, which further support these findings.

</details>


### [157] [$CP$ violation in neutral kaon mixing in $D^0\rightarrow K_SK_S$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00989)
*Yuval Grossman,Guglielmo Papiri,Stefan Schacht*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了中性Kaon混合（neutral kaon mixing）引发的$D^0 \rightarrow K_S K_S$衰变中的CP破坏（CP violation）效应。研究表明，该效应仅源于D衰变中的二阶弱相互作用（second-order weak interactions），其量级约为$10^{-6}$，远小于当前实验灵敏度和粲（charm）物理CP破坏的预期贡献，因此可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 明确$D^0 \rightarrow K_S K_S$衰变中由中性Kaon混合引起的CP破坏效应的大小，以判断其对实验测量的影响是否是显著的。

Method: 通过理论计算分析中性Kaon混合在D介子衰变中诱导CP破坏的贡献机制，确认该贡献仅来自二阶弱相互作用，并估算其量级。

Result: 中性Kaon混合引起的CP破坏贡献量级约为$10^{-6}$。

Conclusion: 该效应与当前实验灵敏度及粲物理中CP破坏的预期贡献相比均可忽略，不会对现有测量造成显著干扰。

Abstract: We study CP violation induced by neutral kaon mixing in $a_{CP}(D^0 \rightarrow K_S K_S)$. We show that the contribution from neutral kaon mixing arises only in connection with second-order weak interactions in $D$ decays. We estimate this effect to be at the $10^{-6}$ level, and thus negligible compared to current experimental sensitivity and to the expected contribution from CP violation in the charm sector.

### [158] [Probing Saturation Effect in Heavy Meson Pair Correlation in Forward $pA$ Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01527)
*Zhan Gao,Cyrille Marquet,Yu Shi,Bo-Wen Xiao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在色玻璃凝聚有效理论框架下，结合统一的Sudakov重求和（Sudakov resummation），研究了前向质子-核（pA）碰撞中重介子对（heavy meson pair）的方位角关联，发现理论结果与LHCb实验数据吻合良好，并预测了重味介子对在高能前向快度区的关联行为，观测到核修正因子中存在明显的质量层级（mass hierarchy），为探测胶子饱和（gluon saturation）信号提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前向质子-核（proton-nucleus, pA）碰撞中的双粒子方位角关联（two-particle angular correlations）长期以来被认为是探索胶子饱和效应（gluon saturation effects）的敏感观测量。尤其在对向（back-to-back）区域，软胶子辐射与饱和效应共同贡献。然而，现有研究对重味介子（heavy meson）的关联行为仍缺乏系统的理论处理，亟需结合更精确的QCD理论框架进行深入分析。

Method: 在色玻璃凝聚（Color Glass Condensate, CGC）有效场论框架下，引入统一的Sudakov重求和（Sudakov resummation）方法，对前向pA碰撞中重介子对的方位角关联进行理论计算。该方法同时考虑了软胶子辐射和饱和效应的贡献，适用于D介子对及底夸克衰变产生的J/ψ对等过程。

Result: 理论结果与LHCb合作组在正反质子（pp）和pA碰撞中测量的D⁰D̄⁰对Δφ数据，以及pp碰撞中b夸克衰变产生的J/ψ对数据吻合良好。进一步预测了前向快度区（forward rapidity region）DD̄和BB̄的关联。核修正因子（nuclear modification factor）R_pA呈现明显质量层级：R_pA|_{m_b} < R_pA|_{m_c}，表明重味介子对在小x区域对饱和效应具有更强的敏感性。随着快度增加，压低效应更加显著，质量层级保持稳健。

Conclusion: 该研究通过理论计算与实验数据的系统比较，验证了CGC加Sudakov重求和框架对重介子对关联的描述能力；质量层级的发现为利用重味介子对关联在前向pA碰撞中寻找胶子饱和信号提供了重要的理论依据和可检验的预言。

Abstract: Forward two-particle angular correlations in $pA$ collisions have long been recognized as a particularly sensitive observable for exploring gluon saturation effects. In the back-to-back regime, two-particle correlations receive substantial contributions from both soft-gluon radiation and saturation effects. In this work, we study heavy meson pair correlation in forward proton-nucleus collisions by incorporating a unified Sudakov resummation for heavy meson pair correlations in the Color Glass Condensate effect theory. Our results are in good agreement with the $Δφ$ data measured by the LHCb Collaboration for $D^0 \bar D^0$ pairs in forward $pp$ and $pA$ collisions, as well as $J/ψ$ pairs from $b\bar b$ decays in forward $pp$ collisions. Furthermore, we present predictions for $D\bar D$ and $B\bar B$ correlations in the forward rapidity regions at the Large Hadron Collider. A pronounced mass-hierarchy is observed in the nuclear modification factor, $R_{pA}\big|_{m_b}<R_{pA}\big|_{m_c}$, indicating stronger sensitivity to saturation effects at small $x$. As the rapidity increases, the suppression becomes more pronounced while the mass hierarchy remains robust. This study will help us to search for the saturation signal via heavy-meson pair correlations in forward $pA$ collisions.

</details>


### [159] [Multimodal Fragmentation of All-Heavy Pentaquarks: Uncertainty-Aware Predictions for Hadron Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01539)
*Francesco Giovanni Celiberto*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种含不确定性感知的领头幂次碎裂描述，用于研究强子对撞机中全粲五夸克态（S波 |cccc\bar{c}⟩）的碎裂过程。构建了多模态共线碎裂函数集合PQ5Q1.1，同时纳入了微扰与非微扰不确定性，并通过(sym)JETHAD接口在NLL/NLO⁺精度下预言HL-LHC与未来FCC上的半包容五夸克加喷注产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对全粲五夸克态（all-charm pentaquark states）这类奇特强子（exotic hadron）的碎裂过程尚缺乏系统性、不确定性可控的理论预言，尤其是在高能强子对撞机环境下。

Method: 构建多模态共线碎裂函数集合PQ5Q1.1，通过缺失高阶效应（F-MHOUs）估计微扰不确定性，通过控制横向动量结构（F-NPWF）建模非微扰波函数，并在复制品（replica-like）框架内一致地组合两者。初始能标下粲夸克碎裂输入被细化以同时描述紧致多夸克（compact multiquark）与双夸克驱动（diquark-driven）产生机制。利用(sym)JETHAD接口在NLL/NLO⁺精度下分析半包容五夸克加喷注产生。

Result: 在HL-LHC与未来FCC上给出了NLL/NLO⁺精度下全粲五夸克态的半包容产生预言，并系统量化了微扰与非微扰两类不确定性。底夸克扇区因对非微扰建模更为敏感而留待未来研究。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个灵活的不确定性可控预言框架，桥接了奇特强子结构、重味碎裂（heavy-flavor fragmentation）与高能QCD理论，为全粲五夸克态这一奇特强子通道的未来实验搜寻奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We present an uncertainty-aware description of leading-power fragmentation for all-charm pentaquark states ($S$-wave $|cccc\bar{c}\rangle$) at hadron colliders. We construct a multimodal set of collinear fragmentation functions, PQ5Q1.1, incorporating both perturbative and nonperturbative uncertainties. Perturbative effects are estimated via missing higher-order variations (F-MHOUs), while the nonperturbative wave function is modeled through controlled modifications of its transverse-momentum structure (F-NPWF), consistently combined within a replica-like framework. The initial-scale input for constituent charm fragmentation is refined to describe both compact multiquark and diquark-driven production mechanisms. We employ the (sym)JETHAD interface to study NLL/NLO$^+$ semi-inclusive pentaquark-plus-jet production at the HL-LHC and future FCC. The bottom sector is left to future dedicated studies due to its enhanced sensitivity to nonperturbative modeling. Our results provide a flexible framework for uncertainty-controlled predictions, bridging exotic-hadron structure, heavy-flavor fragmentation, and high-energy QCD.

### [160] [New Directions in Kaon Physics: Interference in $K^0\toμ^+μ^-$ as a New Golden Mode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01744)
*Teppei Kitahara*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用 $K_L^0$ 与 $K_S^0$ 之间的干涉项来提取稀有衰变 $K^0_{L/S} \to \mu^+\mu^-$ 中的短距离物理信息。该干涉项对 $s \to d \mu^+\mu^-$ 过程中的直接 $CP$ 破缺（direct $CP$ violation）敏感，从而将原本受长距离贡献主导的衰变通道转变为干净的短距离物理探针。研究总结了干涉的基本机制、LHCb 实验中的味标记策略（flavor-tagging strategy），并给出了对 CKM 参数 $|A^2\lambda^5\bar\eta|$ 的约束精度以及 $K_L^0 \to \gamma\gamma$ 三点振幅符号歧义的解决前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有衰变 $K^0_L \to \mu^+\mu^-$ 和 $K^0_S \to \mu^+\mu^-$ 传统上难以用于提取短距离物理（short-distance physics），因为它们被双光子交换的长距离贡献（long-distance contributions）所主导。本文旨在通过引入 $K_L^0$–$K_S^0$ 干涉项来克服这一困难。

Method: 定性分析了 $K_L^0$–$K_S^0$ 干涉的基本机制；提出了适用于 LHCb 类实验装置的味标记策略（flavor-tagging strategy）；基于该方法给出了对 CKM 参数组合 $|A^2\lambda^5\bar\eta|$ 以及 $K_L^0 \to \gamma\gamma$ 三点振幅符号歧义的预期灵敏度。

Result: 预计 LHCb 实验能够将 CKM 参数 $|A^2\lambda^5\bar\eta|$ 约束在标准模型（Standard Model, SM）值的约 35% 精度内；在高亮度 LHC（high luminosity LHC）运行结束时，能够以超过 $3\sigma$ 的显著性解决标准模型预言 $\mathcal{B}(K_L^0 \to \mu^+\mu^-)_{\rm SM}$ 中的离散符号歧义（discrete ambiguity）。

Conclusion: 通过 $K_L^0$–$K_S^0$ 干涉，原本被长距离贡献掩盖的衰变通道可转化为 $CP$ 破缺短距离物理的干净探针。该方法有望在 LHCb 上对 CKM 参数实现有效约束，并解决 $K_L^0\to\mu^+\mu^-$ 中的符号歧义问题。

Abstract: The rare decays $K^0_L \toμ^+μ^-$ and $K^0_S \toμ^+μ^-$ have long been regarded as difficult channels to extract short-distance physics because they are dominated by long-distance contributions via two-photon exchanges. A qualitatively new feature arises once the interference between $K_L^0$ and $K_S^0$ is taken into account. The interference term is sensitive to genuine direct $CP$ violation in $s \to d μ^+ μ^-$ processes and turns this channel into a clean probe of the $CP$-violating short-distance physics. In this contribution, I summarize the basic mechanism of the $K_L^0$--$K_S^0$ interference, the flavor-tagging strategy at LHCb-like setup, and the projected sensitivities for a kaon-unitarity-triangle parameter combination $|A^2λ^5\barη|$ and also for the sign ambiguity of the $K_L^0 \to γγ$ three-point amplitude. As a result, it is expected that the CKM parameter $|A^2λ^5\barη|$ could be constrained by LHCb at the level of about $35\%$ of its Standard Model (SM) value, and the discrete ambiguity in $\mathcal{B}(K_L^0 \to μ^+μ^-)_{\rm SM}$ could be resolved at more than $3σ$ by the end of the high luminosity LHC.

</details>


### [161] [Pair creation via Amplitude-Modulated Periodic and Quasiperiodic Pulse Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02515)
*Deepak Sah*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过量子动能方法（quantum kinetic approach）研究了由正负交替电场脉冲串驱动的非微扰对产生（nonperturbative pair production），比较了周期性和准周期（Fibonacci序）时间序对动量谱与粒子产额的影响。结果表明，时间序主要调控动量空间中的谱权重分布，而总产额主要由有效场强决定，长程时间序可作为多脉冲施温格对产生（Schwinger pair production）的有效控制参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索交替符号电场脉冲串中的时间序（周期性 vs. 准周期性）如何影响非微扰电子-正电子对产生过程，特别是动量谱结构和总产额，以揭示长程时间序在多脉冲施温格对产生中的控制作用。

Method: 采用量子动能方法（quantum kinetic approach）对严格周期脉冲序列（振幅按(E_1, E_2)模式规则交替）和准周期脉冲序列（遵循Fibonacci替换规则的确定性非周期序列，展现长程序但无精确重复）进行数值模拟，分析纵向动量谱和粒子产额。

Result: 周期性脉冲串产生规则调制的多缝（Ramsey型）干涉谱；Fibonacci序则产生碎片化结构和部分动量空间局域化（localization）。增大脉冲数（N=20）使周期性驱动产生更尖锐的干涉条纹，准周期序则导致更强的局域化和更不规则的谱特征。粒子产额对场强比呈强非线性依赖：弱调制下两种时间序产额几乎一致；强场下准周期序产额略高于周期序。

Conclusion: 时间序主要重新分配动量空间中的谱权重，而总积分产额主要由有效场强主导。长程时间序可作为多脉冲施温格对产生的有效控制参数，为未来高强激光实验中设计定制脉冲序列提供指导。

Abstract: We study nonperturbative pair production driven by alternating-sign electric field pulse trains. Using a quantum kinetic approach, we analyze both the longitudinal momentum spectrum and the particle yield for pulse sequences with either strictly periodic temporal structure, in which the pulse amplitudes alternate in a regular and repeating (E_1, E_2) pattern, or quasiperiodic (Fibonacci-ordered) structure, where the amplitudes follow a deterministic but aperiodic sequence generated by the Fibonacci substitution rule, exhibiting long-range order without exact repetition. For N=12 pulses, periodic trains generate regularly modulated spectra characteristic of multi-slit (Ramsey-type) interference, whereas Fibonacci sequences produce fragmented structures and partial momentum-space localization. Increasing the pulse number to N=20 further enhances these effects: periodic driving yields sharper and higher-contrast interference fringes, while quasiperiodic ordering leads to stronger localization and increasingly irregular spectral features.The particle yield exhibits a strongly nonlinear dependence on the field-strength ratio. For weak modulation , both temporal orderings produce nearly identical yields. For stronger fields, a modest crossover behavior is observed, with quasiperiodic sequences yielding slightly larger values than the periodic case. Overall, temporal ordering primarily redistributes spectral weight in momentum space, while the integrated yield is governed predominantly by the effective field strength. These results establish long-range temporal ordering as an effective control parameter in multipulse Schwinger pair production and provide guidance for designing tailored pulse sequences in future high-intensity laser experiments.

</details>

### [162] [Effects of surface viscosities on the motion of a droplet enclosing a translating particle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01196)
*Ali Gürbüz,Hervé Nganguia,Guangpu Zhu,Lailai Zhu,Y. N. Young,On Shun Pak*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了界面流变学对Stokes流中由粘性液滴包裹平移刚性颗粒构成的复合颗粒运动的影响，基于Boussinesq-Scriven本构律建立界面模型，通过解析解和谱边界积分法揭示了表面剪切粘度与膨胀粘度在不同构型（同心/偏心）下的差异化作用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解界面流变学（interfacial rheology）——特别是表面剪切粘度（surface shear viscosity）和表面膨胀粘度（surface dilatational viscosity）——如何影响复合颗粒（compound particle）在低雷诺数流中的运动，填补该领域对界面性质与受限几何效应耦合机制认识的不足。

Method: 采用Stokes流假设，液滴界面通过Boussinesq-Scriven本构律（Boussinesq-Scriven constitutive law）建模；对同心构型（concentric configuration）推导出精确解析解，对偏心构型（eccentric geometry）采用谱边界积分法（spectral boundary integral method）进行扩展分析，系统考察受限程度、粘度对比和界面性质的影响。

Result: 同心构型下，诱导液滴速度与表面剪切粘度无关，而表面膨胀粘度根据受限程度与粘度比的耦合可增强或抑制液滴运动；偏心构型下，表面剪切粘度的影响凸显，且随偏心率的增加而一致地增强液滴运动。解析与数值结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: 界面流变学、受限几何（confinement）以及对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）共同决定了复合颗粒系统的动力学行为。研究结果为理解具有复杂界面的活性复合颗粒提供了机制性见解，并建立了定量基准。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of interfacial rheology on the motion of a compound particle consisting of a viscous droplet enclosing a translating rigid particle in the Stokes flow regime. The droplet interface is modeled using the Boussinesq-Scriven constitutive law, incorporating both surface shear and dilatational viscosities. An exact analytical solution is derived for the concentric configuration, and the analysis is extended to eccentric geometries using a spectral boundary integral method, enabling a systematic examination of confinement, viscosity contrast, and interfacial properties. For concentric configurations, we show that the induced droplet velocity is independent of surface shear viscosity, while surface dilatational viscosity can either enhance or suppress the droplet motion depending on the interplay between confinement and viscosity ratio. This behavior is rationalized in terms of competing effects between reduced interfacial mobility and increased driving force required to maintain the prescribed particle speed. In contrast, when the particle is eccentrically positioned within the droplet, a dependence on surface shear viscosity emerges, leading to a consistent enhancement of droplet motion that becomes more pronounced with increasing eccentricity. The analytical and numerical results are in excellent agreement and reveal how interfacial rheology, confinement, and symmetry breaking jointly govern the dynamics of compound particle systems. These findings provide mechanistic insight and establish a quantitative benchmark for future studies of active compound particles with complex interfaces.

</details>

### [163] [Influence of Coherent Elastic Strain on Phase Separation in BCC Nb-V Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01031)
*Siya Zhu,Raymundo Arróyave*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个将相干弹性应变（coherent elastic strain）纳入相图计算的热力学框架，应用于BCC Nb-V合金体系，表明相干弹性显著抑制相分离、缩小混溶隙（miscibility gap）并降低临界温度，同时揭示平衡分解组分为温度与整体合金成分的函数，改变了传统相平衡解读方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有显著晶格失配（lattice mismatch）的合金体系中，相干弹性应变（coherent elastic strain）是相分离热力学中一个重要但常被忽略的贡献因素；现有相图计算主要依赖CALPHAD化学自由能，缺乏对相干弹性兼容性的系统整合。

Method: 发展了一个将相干弹性兼容性（coherent elastic compatibility）直接纳入相图计算的热力学框架，并与传统的CALPHAD化学自由能相结合。

Result: 在BCC Nb-V体系中，相干弹性显著抑制相分离，缩小混溶隙，并将临界温度降低至接近实验观测值；平衡分解组分为温度和整体合金成分的函数，两相边界不再代表唯一的共存组分。

Conclusion: 相干弹性（coherent elasticity）是晶格失配体系中关键的热力学因素，该工作为相干相图建模（coherent phase-diagram modeling）提供了一个通用框架。

Abstract: Coherent elastic strain is an important but often neglected contribution to phase-separation thermodynamics in alloy systems where decomposed phases have appreciable lattice mismatch. We develop a thermodynamic framework that incorporates coherent elastic compatibility directly into phase-diagram calculations alongside conventional CALPHAD chemical free energies. Applied to the BCC Nb-V system, the framework shows that coherent elasticity substantially suppresses phase separation, narrows the miscibility gap, and lowers the critical temperature toward experimentally observed values. Beyond these quantitative effects, the coherent constraint qualitatively alters the interpretation of phase equilibria: the equilibrium decomposition compositions become functions of both temperature and overall alloy composition, so the two-phase boundary no longer represents unique coexistence compositions. These results establish coherent elasticity as a key thermodynamic factor in lattice-mismatched systems and provide a general framework for coherent phase-diagram modeling.

</details>

While oxygen and caesium atoms form a typical crystal lattice, the dynamics of the hydrogen atoms are more complex. Here we show that the covalent and hydrogen bonds are continually interconverting, meaning that the water and hydroxyl are interconverting by proton exchange. The order-disorder transition of the water and hydroxyl proceeds by chemical reaction rather than rotation or diffusion of the molecules. A hydrogen can rotate out of the layer, leaving a vacant site in the 2D layer. Such a hydrogen vacancy can diffuse rapidly by single molecule rotation, leading to fast-ionic conduction. Abstract: Organic semiconductors (OSCs) are widely explored for flexible optoelectronic technologies, with performance governed not only by molecular design, but also by solid-state packing, which can give rise to polymorphism. Here, we discover, isolate, and resolve the crystal structure of a previously unrecognised bulk polymorph of DNTT, termed blue DNTT owing to its characteristic blue emission. Abstract: Altermagnets are a class of materials with compensated magnetic moments, in which spin sublattices are related by specific symmetries other than inversion or translation. This allows time-reversal symmetry to be broken without a net magnetization. Here, we synthesize single crystals of Fe1-xCrxSb2 and investigate their electrical transport and magnetic properties, with a focus on Fe0.85Cr0.15Sb2. Abstract: Having been extensively studied during last decades in the fields of thermoelectics and ionic conductors, the $α$ phase of Cu$_{2}$Se with antfluoride crystal structure has recently emerged as a topological zero-gap semimetal with a quadratic contact point which exists at the Fermi surface of its bulk electronic spectrum. Here we argue based on density functional electronic structure calculation that the $β$ phase of Cu$_{2}$Se realized in a recently discovered rhombohedral structure shows a Dirac semimetal behavior of the electrons near the Fermi level. These topological semimetals are currently generating a lot of interest due to unusual transport phenomena, such as strong quantum oscillations, large magnetoresistance effect and ultrahigh carrier mobilities with their Fermi velocities potentially exceeding graphene. We show that there exist Fermi arc states at the surface spectrum of $β-$Cu$_{2}$Se that are topologically protected by the bulk Dirac points. ### [168] [Rational Mechanics of Material Strength in Brittle Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01156)
*Arash Yavari,Aditya Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文在有限弹性（finite elasticity）框架下重新表述了材料强度（material strength），证明强度须由应力与应变对共同决定，并系统分析了其几何、本构及对称性基础，将经典应力判据作为特例纳入统一理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料强度在断裂力学（fracture mechanics）尤其是脆性固体的裂纹成核（crack nucleation）问题中具有重要新意义，但经典理论仅基于应力定义强度，缺乏空间协变性（spatial covariance）的严格基础。本文旨在建立一套自洽的有限弹性强度理论。

Method: 采用空间协变性分析方法，要求强度函数依赖于应力及其对应的应变度量，从而统一处理基于第一Piola–Kirchhoff、第二Piola–Kirchhoff和Cauchy应力的不同表述。通过定义强度超曲面（strength hypersurface）为本构可容许应力流形（constitutively admissible stress manifold）的子集，并研究安全域（safe domain）的几何性质。在比例缩减假设（proportional-reduction hypothesis）下分析各向同性固体的星形安全域，并扩展至非弹性脆性固体及小应变极限情形。

Result: 在标准正则性假设及充分大应力不可容许的要求下，强度超曲面是该流形上的光滑紧致超曲面。对于各向同性固体，安全域在比例缩减假设下是星形（star-shaped）的。残余应力与特征应变（eigenstrains）通过材料度量（material metric）改变强度曲面。小应变极限下理论退化至经典应力判据。

Conclusion: 本研究为材料强度提供了有限弹性中的协变理论框架，统一了基于不同应力测度的强度判据，并为各向同性、各向异性及非弹性脆性固体的强度分析建立了严谨的几何与本构基础。

Abstract: Material strength is a classical concept with renewed importance in fracture mechanics, particularly in crack nucleation in brittle solids. We formulate material strength in finite elasticity and examine its geometric, constitutive, and symmetry-theoretic foundations. Spatial covariance requires a strength function to depend on both stress and the corresponding strain measure, so that strength is governed by the pair (stress,strain), not stress alone, and only then can representations based on different stress measures be consistently related, with classical stress-based criteria recovered as a special case. We analyze covariance under spatial diffeomorphisms and relate formulations based on the first Piola--Kirchhoff, second Piola--Kirchhoff, and Cauchy stresses. For stress-based criteria, we define the strength hypersurface as a subset of the constitutively admissible stress manifold and study the associated safe domain. Under standard regularity assumptions and the requirement that sufficiently large stresses are inadmissible, the strength surface is a smooth compact hypersurface of this manifold. For isotropic solids, we show that the safe domain is star-shaped under a proportional-reduction hypothesis. We extend the formulation to anelastic brittle solids, showing that residual stresses and eigenstrains modify the strength surface through the material metric, and discuss anisotropic strength via material symmetry. Finally, in the small-strain limit, the theory reduces to classical stress-based criteria.

Abstract: Light elements play an important role in influencing the macroscale properties of engineering alloys through grain boundary (GB) segregation phenomena. However, the scarcity and scattered nature of ab initio datasets for light elements in steels makes reproduction and extraction of general trends from the literature difficult. Here, we present a comprehensive ab initio evaluation of the segregation energies and cohesive effects for H, He, B, C, N, O, P, S, extensively sampling both substitutional and interstitial sites in six model coincident site lattice (CSL) ferritic iron GBs using density functional theory (DFT). Cohesive effects are evaluated in both a quantum-chemistry bond-order and rigid Rice-Wang interfacial cohesive strength framework. Our calculations indicate that, compared at the same concentration, B and C enhance GB cohesion, N, P, H are mildly detrimental, and He, O, S as powerful decohesive agents/embrittlers. Sampling both interstitial and substitutional starting positions is necessary to accurately capture segregation spectra. Commonly utilised sampling criteria such as site volumes prove insufficient for identifying deepest GB binding sites. Solutes placed in either kind of site can induce large relaxations to the same final configuration, resulting in site classification ambiguity. The nearest neighbour distance of a solute to its neighbours after relaxation is shown to be a controlling factor for the lower threshold of segregation energies at sites. The freely available DFT dataset and analysis repositories are expected to advance understanding of GB segregation behaviours of light elements in steels and serve as a resource for developing machine learning interatomic potentials.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无机晶体的逆设计（inverse design）要求生成满足目标属性且兼具多样性与物理合理性的结构，但属性条件约束往往会降低现有生成模型所能达到的结构质量，使得逆设计比从头生成（ab initio generation）更具挑战性。

Method: 提出一种扩散框架（diffusion framework），通过共享的评分网络（score network）联合去噪晶体结构变量与位点分辨的局域电子描述符（site-resolved local electronic descriptors），采用Bader电荷（Bader charge）与原子态密度（atomic DOS, density of states）作为代表性描述符。

Result: 在带隙和形成能条件生成下，联合模型在多数目标条件中取得了比纯结构基线更高的成功率，同时提升了满足唯一性、新颖性、热力学稳定性与物理有效性（VSUN准则）的结构比例。生成的Bader电荷与DFT参考值之间的MAE为5.5e-2 e，生成的原子态密度在模态准确度范围内捕捉了DFT参考的粗粒频谱轮廓。

Conclusion: 局域电子描述符可作为有效的生成变量，发挥双重作用：通过增加结构多样性拓宽可探索的材料空间；在联合去噪过程中引导结构轨迹朝向电子上合理的构型，从而缓解属性目标与结构质量之间的权衡。

Abstract: Inverse design of inorganic crystals, in which structures are generated to satisfy a target property while preserving diversity and physical plausibility, remains more demanding than ab initio generation, as property conditioning can degrade the structural quality that current generative models otherwise achieve. We propose a diffusion framework that jointly denoises crystal-structure variables and site-resolved local electronic descriptors through a shared score network. As representative descriptors, we adopt Bader charge and atomic density of states (atomic DOS). Under both band-gap and formation energy conditioned generation, the joint models achieved higher success rates than the structure-only baseline in most target conditions, while simultaneously increasing the fraction of generated structures that satisfy uniqueness, novelty, thermodynamic stability, and physical validity (VSUN criteria). A dummy-variable control confirms that these gains originate from the electronic content of the descriptors rather than from auxiliary site-wise variables. The generated Bader charges agree with DFT references with an MAE of 5.5e-2 e on stable structures, and the generated atomic DOS captures the coarse spectral profile of the DFT reference around the modal accuracy range, although finer details and accuracy vary with elemental species. These results establish local electronic descriptors as effective generative variables that serve two complementary roles: broadening the explored materials space through increased structural diversity, and mitigating the trade-off between property targeting and structural quality by guiding the structural trajectory toward electronically plausible configurations during joint denoising.

</details>


### [172] [SR-CGCNN: Shared Recurrent Convolution in Crystal Graph Neural Networks for Materials Property Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01304)
*Satadeep Bhattacharjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过提出共享循环晶体图卷积神经网络（SR-CGCNN），验证了重复应用相同学习到的局部更新可以在大幅减少参数量的前提下，接近标准深层CGCNN的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统晶体图卷积神经网络（CGCNN）通过堆叠独立参数化的卷积层来增加信息传播深度，导致参数量随深度线性增长。本文旨在探究：重复应用同一组学习到的局部更新，是否能够在减少参数的同时，保留深层CGCNN的大部分性能收益。

Method: 提出共享循环CGCNN（SR-CGCNN），将晶体图卷积的主权重在多个循环消息传递步骤（recurrent message-passing steps）中共享绑定，而图的构建、池化操作和预测头保持不变，以便与标准CGCNN基线进行受控对比。

Result: 在Materials Project衍生的形成能和带隙数据集上，三步SR-CGCNN接近标准三层CGCNN的精度，但仅使用其34.5%的可训练卷积参数。形成能测试平均绝对误差从0.0945变为0.0986 eV atom⁻¹，带隙误差从0.4346变为0.4503 eV。

Conclusion: 重复共享消息传递可以作为一种参数高效的近似方式来替代堆叠式CGCNN深度，为晶体图卷积提供了一种紧凑的循环解释。

Abstract: Crystal graph neural networks predict materials properties by propagating information through local atomic environments. In conventional crystal graph convolutional neural networks (CGCNNs), this propagation depth is increased by stacking independently parameterized convolutional layers. This coupling between message-passing depth and parameter count raises a simple question: can repeated application of the same learned local update recover most of the benefit of a deeper CGCNN? We address this question by introducing a shared-recurrent CGCNN (SR-CGCNN), in which the main crystal-graph convolutional weights are tied across recurrent message-passing steps. The graph construction, pooling operation, and prediction head are kept unchanged, allowing a controlled comparison with standard CGCNN baselines. On Materials Project-derived formation-energy and band-gap datasets, a three-step SR-CGCNN approaches the accuracy of a standard three-layer CGCNN while using only $34.5\%$ of its trainable convolutional parameters. The formation-energy test mean absolute error changes from $0.0945$ to $0.0986~\mathrm{eV\,atom^{-1}}$, while the band-gap error changes from $0.4346$ to $0.4503~\mathrm{eV}$. These results indicate that repeated shared message passing can provide a parameter-efficient approximation to stacked CGCNN depth, offering a compact recurrent interpretation of crystal graph convolution.

### [173] [Analyticity and symmetry of band extrema in gapped solids: when does the effective mass approximation hold?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02576)
*Jakob Kjærulff Svaneborg,Kristian Sommer Thygesen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文证明在标准第一性原理哈密顿量（包括DFT和G₀W₀）下，非简并极值点处的能带色散具有解析性，从而确立了有效质量近似（effective mass approximation）的严格数学基础；进一步利用群论推导了32个晶体学点群下有效质量张量的对称性允许形式，并以单层MoS₂为例展示了电子和空穴有效质量在K点必然各向同性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有效质量近似（effective mass approximation）广泛应用于半导体和绝缘体中的载流子输运、光学响应和激子模型，但其有效性依赖于能带色散（band dispersion）Eₙ(k)在相关极值点处是否解析。该问题缺乏严格的数学证明，因此需要从第一性原理（ab initio）哈密顿量的层面检验解析性条件是否成立。

Method: 从数学上证明标准第一性原理哈密顿量（包括采用局域或杂化交换关联泛函的密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）以及带边G₀W₀准粒子能（quasiparticle energy））在非简并非简并（non-degenerate）极值点处具有解析性；并运用群论（group theory）确定32个晶体学点群（crystallographic point group）下有效质量张量（effective mass tensor）的对称性允许形式。

Result: 能带非解析性（band non-analyticity，或称翘曲（warping））必然源自简并性（degeneracy）；建立了32个点群下有效质量张量的对称性约束规则，可作为第一性原理计算的严格一致性检验。以单层MoS₂的K点为例，证明在DFT和G₀W₀水平上电子和空穴的有效质量必须严格各向同性（strictly isotropic）。

Conclusion: 有效质量近似在标准第一性原理框架下具有严格的解析性基础；对称性约束为第一性原理计算中的有效质量张量提供了强有力的验证手段，并揭示了MoS₂等二维材料中有效质量的各向同性性质。

Abstract: The effective mass approximation is widely used across models of carrier transport, optical response, and excitons in semiconductors and insulators, but its validity hinges on the assumption that the band dispersion $E_n(\mathbf{k})$ at the relevant extremum is analytic. We prove that analyticity holds at any non-degenerate extremum for the standard ab initio Hamiltonians, including density functional theory with local or hybrid exchange-correlation functionals and for band-edge $G_0W_0$ quasiparticle energies in gapped systems. Band non-analyticity (or warping) in these settings is therefore intrinsically tied to degeneracy. We then use group theory to determine the symmetry-allowed form of the effective mass tensor for each of the 32 crystallographic point groups, providing a stringent consistency check on first-principles calculations. As a representative application, we show that the electron and hole effective masses at the $K$ point of monolayer MoS$_2$ must be strictly isotropic at the DFT and $G_0W_0$ levels.
