### [174] [Revealing the kinetics of interfacial surfactant phase transitions through multiscale simulations and in-situ plasmonic sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01458)
*Esmée Berger,Narjes Khosravian,Ferry Anggoro Ardy Nugroho,Joakim Löfgren,Christoph Langhammer,Paul Erhart*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究建立了一种基于等离激元（plasmonic）的原子级理论框架，通过光学特征（光谱峰位移）定量映射固液界面表面活性剂自组装（self-assembly）的相态与相变动力学。以十六烷基三甲基溴化铵（cetyltrimethylammonium bromide, CTAB）在二氧化硅表面为模型体系，结合原子模拟、电子结构计算和连续电动力学，将分子形态预测为光谱峰位移，并通过实验验证了稳态峰位移与时间分辨弛豫动力学。该方法的普适性源于对近场介电对比度（dielectric contrast）的依赖，且可透过介电覆盖层工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面活性剂在固液界面的自组装调控着界面稳定性、输运与反应性，但原位（in situ）解析界面表面活性剂相态及其转变动力学仍具挑战。

Method: 以CTAB在二氧化硅表面为原型体系，结合原子模拟（atomistic simulations）、电子结构计算（electronic-structure calculations）与连续电动力学（continuum electrodynamics），将分子形态——包括堆积与水合状态的差异——映射为等离激元近场（plasmonic near field）内有效介电常数（effective permittivity）的变化，从而预测对应文献报道表面相的光谱峰位移。实验上通过步进浓度变化验证稳态峰位移，并利用时间分辨峰位移的指数弛豫提取转变动力学。

Result: 实验确认了步进浓度变化下稳态峰位移的预测顺序与幅度；从时间分辨峰位移的指数弛豫中提取了相变动力学。关键机制特征在于，从不渗透双层（impermeable bilayer）转变为含通道的水可进入相（water-accessible, channel-containing phase）时，光谱位移方向发生反转，这与水合驱动局部有效介电常数降低的机制一致。

Conclusion: 该方法依赖于等离激元近场中的介电对比度，且可透过介电覆盖层工作，因此为水相条件下实时识别界面表面活性剂相态及其动力学提供了一条广泛适用的路径。

Abstract: Surfactant self-assembly at solid-liquid interfaces governs interfacial stability, transport, and reactivity across many technologies, yet resolving interfacial surfactant phases and their transition kinetics in situ remains challenging. Here, we establish an atomistically grounded plasmonic framework that quantitatively maps interfacial surfactant phases and phase transitions onto optical signatures. Distinct morphologies differ in packing and hydration, modifying the effective permittivity within the optical near field and producing surfactant phase-specific plasmonic extinction peak shifts. Using cetyltrimethylammonium bromide on silica as a prototypical surfactant-surface system, we combine atomistic simulations, electronic-structure calculations, and continuum electrodynamics to translate molecular morphologies into predicted spectral shifts for literature-reported surface phases. We experimentally confirm the predicted ordering and magnitude of steady-state peak shifts during stepwise concentration changes, and extract transition kinetics from exponential relaxations of the time-resolved peak shift. A key mechanistic signature is reversal of the spectral shift direction upon transition from an impermeable bilayer to a water-accessible, channel-containing phase, consistent with hydration-driven reduction of the local effective permittivity. Because the approach relies on dielectric contrast in the plasmonic near field and works through a dielectric overlayer, it provides a broadly applicable route for real-time identification of interfacial surfactant phases and their kinetics in aqueous conditions.

### [175] [Deterministic Realization of Complex Local Strain Fields and Bandgap Profiles in Two-Dimensional Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01465)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新型经典与量子器件概念要求对二维材料的 optoelectronic properties（光电特性）实现精确的空间控制，但通过局域多轴应变分布（multiaxial strain distributions）进行确定性工程调控仍面临挑战。现有方法难以在悬浮范德华膜中定量、可预测地设计应变和带隙分布。

Result: 成功量化了双轴与单轴应变计因子。双组分解析模型对复杂几何结构（包括相邻纳米结构间的相互作用）中的带隙偏移预测误差小于12%。同时验证了该方法可推广至其他二维材料体系。

Conclusion: 纳米结构设计提供了一种定量、确定性的框架（quantitative, deterministic framework），能够实现二维材料中设计好的应变与带隙分布，从而为新型器件概念中的光电特性空间控制提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Emerging classical and quantum device concepts demand precise spatial control over the optoelectronic properties of two-dimensional (2D) materials, but deterministic engineering via local multiaxial strain distributions remains challenging. Using Ga$_2$Se$_2$, we demonstrate a material-agnostic platform in which nanostructure geometry deterministically prescribes in-plane strain profiles in suspended van der Waals membranes. We first use hyperspectral photoluminescence mapping and experimentally-constrained finite element analysis to quantify the experimental biaxial and uniaxial strain gauge factors that relate strain to the change in bandgap. We next show that a two-component analytical model can predict, with less than 12% error, spatially-resolved bandgap shifts arising from multiaxial strain distributions in complex geometries, including the interactions between adjacent nanostructures. Finally, we demonstrate that this approach can be extended to other materials. The results demonstrate that nanostructure design provides a quantitative, deterministic framework for the realization of designed strain and bandgap distributions in 2D materials.

### [176] [Generalized continuum theory of phonon angular momentum in crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01678)
*Mamoru Matsuo,Naoki Nishimura,Ai Yamakage,Takeo Kato*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过引入局域SO(3)材料框架，建立了一个描述晶体中声子角动量（phonon angular momentum）的广义连续统理论，将声学位移模与光学转动模统一于长波连续描述中，并利用转动对称性与诺特定理（Noether's theorem）确定了连续声子角动量密度的构成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有连续理论缺乏对晶体中转动光学自由度（rotational optical degrees of freedom）的统一描述，无法在长波极限下同时容纳声学位移模式与晶胞转动模式及其角动量贡献。

Method: 在宏观位移场之外引入局域SO(3)材料框架（local SO(3) material frame），构建广义连续统理论；在线性化极限下，利用共旋变形梯度（co-rotated deformation gradient）和转动梯度（rotational gradient）恢复Eringen微变形与扭曲张量；基于转动对称性和诺特定理推导连续声子角动量密度。

Result: 各向同性微极弹性（isotropic micropolar elasticity）作为特例出现；声子角动量密度包含位移-极化贡献（displacement-polarization contribution）与内禀微转动贡献（intrinsic microrotation contribution）；理论识别了微转动退化为晶格涡量（lattice vorticity）的锁定极限（locking limit），以及导致手性声子分裂（chiral phonon splitting）的非恰当对称性破缺项（improper-symmetry-breaking terms）。

Conclusion: 该框架为统一描述晶体中声学与光学转动模式、理解声子角动量的连续起源以及手性声子分裂机制提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We formulate a generalized continuum theory of phonon angular momentum in crystals by introducing a local SO(3) material frame in addition to the macroscopic displacement field. The local frame represents rotational optical degrees of freedom of the unit cell and brings acoustic displacement modes and optical rotational modes into a common long-wavelength continuum description. In the linearized limit, the co-rotated deformation gradient and the rotational gradient associated with the local material frame recover the Eringen microdeformation and wryness tensors; isotropic micropolar elasticity then appears as a special case. Rotational symmetry and Noether's theorem determine the continuum phonon angular-momentum density, including both the displacement-polarization contribution and the intrinsic microrotation contribution. The theory further identifies the locking limit in which microrotation reduces to lattice vorticity and the improper-symmetry-breaking terms responsible for chiral phonon splitting.

We then discuss future prospects in spin caloritronics from the viewpoints of measurement techniques, physics, materials science, and engineering applications. ### [178] [Physics-Constrained Learning of Dose-Dependent Spectral Degradation in Metal--Organic Frameworks from In Situ Low-Loss EELS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01697)
*Gabriel T. dos Santos,Roberto dos Reis,Vinayak P. Dravid*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该框架提供了剂量依赖、谱学约束的MOF退化描述，同时界定了固定窗口低损失EELS在缺乏独立化学态验证时的分配能力极限。

Abstract: Electron-beam irradiation limits atomic-resolution characterization of beam-sensitive hybrid materials, yet quantitative models that connect \textit{in situ} spectroscopy to dose-dependent degradation remain scarce. Here we use a physics-informed neural network (PINN) to model beam-induced spectral evolution in MIL-101(Fe) from an in situ low-loss electron energy-loss spectroscopy (EELS) dose series. Each spectrum is reduced to fixed-window low-loss descriptors, $\tilde n_{\mathrm{eff},j}(Φ)=\int_{\mathcal{W}_j}S(E,Φ)\,dE$, evaluated over nominal $π$--$π^{*}$, C--C, C--O, and M--O windows. These descriptors are relative window-integrated low-loss spectral areas, not absolute f-sum-rule effective electron numbers. For each spectral channel, a latent integrity variable $C_i(Φ)$ obeys the same uncoupled power-law degradation equation in normalized dose space, $dC_i/dφ=-k_i C_i^{p_i}$, regularized by monotonicity, boundedness, and a single hierarchy prior $k_{\mathrm{C\text{-}O}}\geq k_{\mathrm{C\text{-}C}}$. Applied to nine dose frames spanning 152--1368~e$^-$/Å$^2$, the ensemble PINN identifies C--O and C--C as the most strongly dose-sensitive linker-associated channels, with half-integrity thresholds of approximately $1.0\times10^3$~e$^-$/Å$^2$. The 1--3~eV $π$--$π^{*}$-labelled window increases with dose and is therefore interpreted as a mixed low-energy response, likely involving oscillator-strength redistribution rather than direct monotonic loss of a single bond population. The framework provides a dose-dependent, spectroscopy constrained description of MOF degradation while also defining the limits of what fixed-window low-loss EELS can assign without independent chemical-state validation.

</details>


### [179] [Universal Design Principles for High-Quality Persistent Spin Textures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01724)
*Cheng-Ao Ji,Lingling Tao,James M. Rondinelli,Xue-Zeng Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个通用模型来描述由不同k点自旋轨道场相互作用形成的高质量持久自旋织构（PST），并在多种点群体系中识别出此类结构。非极性手性化合物Na2Sn2O3和AgClO4（D2d对称性）展现出大区域高质量PST及创纪录的长自旋寿命（0.5–7.4 ns和0.9–2.5 ns），同时化学替代和压力调控被证明是有效的工程化手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久自旋织构（PST）可实现极长自旋寿命，对自旋电子学（spintronics）应用至关重要，但兼具大布里渊区（BZ）范围、小自旋偏差和长自旋寿命的高质量PST材料仍然稀缺。

Method: 提出了一个通用模型（universal model），用于捕捉不同k点自旋轨道场（spin-orbit fields）相互作用下高质量PST区域的形成机制，并在多种点群体系中验证了该框架的有效性。

Result: 非极性手性化合物Na2Sn2O3展现出约0.02 Å⁻²的高质量PST区域，可通过几何手性（geometric chirality）切换实现反转；AgClO4（D2d对称性）具有0.016 Å⁻²的PST区域。两者分别拥有0.5–7.4 ns和0.9–2.5 ns的自旋寿命，为PST材料中报道的最长值之一。化学替代和施加压力均可有效工程化高质量PST。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了高质量PST的普适性原理（universal principle），并提供了跨多种点群的有前景材料，为下一代自旋电子学器件奠定了基础。

Abstract: Persistent spin texture (PST) describes a unique spin-momentum locking in momentum space that maintains a uniform spin orientation through portions of the Brillouin zone (BZ), enabling exceptionally long spin lifetimes which are essential for applications in spintronics. However, materials exhibiting large BZ regions of high-quality PST, characterized by minimal spin deviation and long spin lifetimes, remain scarce. Here a universal model is introduced to capture the formation of superior PST regions arising from the interplay of spin-orbit fields at different k points. Within this framework, high-quality PSTs are identified in several systems belonging to various point groups. Notably, the nonpolar-chiral compound Na2Sn2O3 exhibits ~0.02 Å-2 high-quality PST region, which can be reversed by the switching of geometric chirality, while AgClO4 (D2d symmetry) exhibits a 0.016 Å-2 PST region. Significantly, Na2Sn2O3 and AgClO4 host persistent spin helices with spin lifetimes of 0.5-7.4 ns and 0.9-2.5 ns, respectively, among the longest reported for PST materials. In addition, both chemical substitutions and the application of pressure are demonstrated as effective routes for engineering high-quality PST. Our findings not only establish a universal principle for high-quality PST, but also provide promising materials across various point groups for the next-generation spintronic devices.

### [180] [Geometric Percolation Threshold Defines Half-Metallic Window in Vacancy-Doped Titanium disulfides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01754)
*Shrestha Dutta,Rudra Banerjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过几何逾渗（geometric percolation）机制解释了二维材料空位掺杂中从绝缘体到半金属铁磁体的相变，指出在单层$1T$-\ptis~中，当缺陷网络形成跨越簇时才会出现半金属性（half-metallicity），并确定了半金属工作的窄浓度窗口（$11\%<x<15\%$）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料的缺陷工程（defect engineering）通常会产生局域磁矩，但半金属铁磁性（half-metallic ferromagnetism）至今难以实现，实验上常得到顺磁绝缘体。本文旨在解决这一矛盾，揭示绝缘体-半金属转变的内在机制。

Method: 将三维稀磁半导体（diluted magnetic semiconductors）的逾渗框架推广至二维空位掺杂体系，通过晶体场对称性破缺（crystal-field symmetry breaking, $O_h \to C_{4v}$）稳定 Ti $3d_{z^2}$ 轨道以产生局域磁矩，并利用超胞尺寸效应（supercell-size effect）验证逾渗机制。

Result: 半金属性在临界空位浓度 $x_c \approx 12.5\%$ 时通过逾渗转变实现：多数自旋杂质带从局域态（$W<0.1$ eV）转变为色散带（宽1.5 eV，100%自旋极化），少数自旋带隙为1.0 eV。超胞效应进一步证实：$2\times2$ 胞呈反铁磁序，$4\times4$ 胞呈铁磁序。居里温度（Curie temperature）估计超过300 K，浓度超过20%时出现几何堵塞不稳定性（geometric jamming instability）。

Conclusion: 半金属性仅在 $11\%<x<15\%$ 的窄窗口内稳定存在，几何连通性（geometric connectivity）可作为缺陷工程化二维自旋电子学（defect-engineered 2D spintronics）的定量设计原则。

Abstract: Defect engineering of two-dimensional materials routinely produces local magnetic moments, yet itinerant half-metallic
  ferromagnetism remains elusive -- experiments frequently yield paramagnetic insulators. We resolve this paradox for vacancy-doped
  monolayer $1T$-\ptis~by demonstrating that the insulator-to-half-metal transition is governed by universal geometric percolation
  of the defect network, extending the percolation framework established for three-dimensional diluted magnetic semiconductors into
  the 2D vacancy-doped regime. Half-metallicity emerges via a two-step mechanism: crystal-field symmetry breaking
  ($O_h \to C_{4v}$) selectively stabilizes the Ti $3d_{z^2}$ orbital, generating robust local moments ($0.94~μ_B$), but
  spin-polarized transport requires these moments to form a spanning cluster. At critical vacancy concentration $x_c \approx
  12.5\%$, a percolation transition drives the majority-spin impurity band from flat, localized levels ($W < 0.1$~eV) to a
  dispersive 1.5~eV-wide band with 100\% spin polarization and a minority-spin gap of 1.0~eV. The
  percolation mechanism is independently corroborated by a striking supercell-size effect: at identical concentration, $2\times2$
  cells yield antiferromagnetic order while $4\times4$ cells mandate ferromagnetism, reflecting the presence or absence of a
  spanning cluster. We estimate a Curie temperature exceeding 300~K from the exchange coupling, and identify a geometric jamming
  instability at $x > 20\%$ that fragments the network. These results define a narrow functional window ($11\% < x < 15\%$) for
  half-metallic operation and establish geometric connectivity as a quantitative design principle for defect-engineered 2D
  spintronics.

### [181] [Spin-orbit coupling effects in altermagnets: Interplay of weak spin and orbital ferromagnetism with relativistic splitting of electron states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01780)
*L. M. Sandratskii,K. Carva,V. M. Silkin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过结合相对论性DFT计算与自旋空间群（spin space groups）对称性分析，在原子磁矩和单电子态两个层面上研究了交变磁体（altermagnets）中弱铁磁性（weak ferromagnetism, WFM）的相对论性形成机制，揭示了自旋与轨道磁矩形成的基本差异，并发现WFM矩随自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）强度呈现非单调依赖关系，其中准对称性（QS）计算表明仅考虑与奈尔矢量（Néel vector）共线的SOC分量时自旋WFM消失而轨道WFM仍存在。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在深入理解交变磁体中相对论性效应的形成机制，特别是弱铁磁性现象背后的物理根源。

Method: 采用相对论性密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，并结合基于自旋空间群的对称性分析；在原子层面计算弱铁磁态的磁结构（同时考虑自旋与轨道原子磁矩），在单电子态层面引入电子态磁结构（MSES）概念并分析其相对论性转变。

Result: WFM矩随SOC强度呈现非单调依赖关系；准对称性计算中仅考虑与奈尔矢量共线的SOC分量时，自旋WFM消失而轨道WFM仍存在，揭示了两者形成机制的根本差异；非相对论性计算中金属与配体的共线自旋MSES及配体补偿轨道MSES在相对论性条件下转变为非共线三维MSES；布里渊区一般k点处偶然自旋简并（accidental spin degeneracies）的相对论性劈裂在MSES形成中起重要作用；能带结构中避免交叉（avoided crossings）区域的形成与WFM矩的非单调行为相关。

Conclusion: 交变磁体中自旋与轨道磁矩的形成机制存在本质差异；金属-配体杂化（metal-ligand hybridization）在交变磁性（altermagnetism）性质形成中具有重要作用；大多数计算以MnTe为模型体系完成。

Abstract: The aim of the paper is to contribute to reaching a deeper understanding of the formation of relativistic effects in altermagnets. The focus of the paper is on the phenomena of weak ferromagnetism (WFM) and relativistic DFT calculations combined with the symmetry analysis on the basis of spin space groups. The consideration is performed on two different levels. On the first level, the atomistic magnetic structure of weak ferromagnetic state is calculated. Both spin and orbital atomic moments are taken into account. We study the dependence of the WFM moment on the strength of the SOC and obtain a peculiar nonmonotonous type of dependence. An interesting result is obtained in quasisymmetry (QS) calculation where only the component of the SOC collinear to the Néel vector is taken into account. In QS calculation the spin WFM is absent while the orbital WFM is present. This reveals a principal difference in the formation of the spin and orbital magnetic moments. On the second level, the study is focused on the properties of individual electron states. We introduce the notion of the magnetic structure of the electron state (MSES). It is shown how the collinear spin-MSESs of both metal and ligand atoms and compensated orbital-MSES of the ligand obtained in the nonrelativiatic calculation transform into complex noncollinear 3D MSESs of both spin and orbital nature. An important role in the formation of MSESs is played by the relativistic splitting of the accidental spin degeneracies at general {\bf k} points filling the volume of the Brillouin zone. The formation of the regions of avoided crossings in the relativistic band structure is related to the nonmonotonous behavior of the WFM moment. The importance of the metal-ligand hybridization in the formation of the AM properties is discussed. Most of the calculations are performed for MnTe.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种完全从头算的SLD方法，集成于VASP软件中；在每个时间步，通过自洽的约束矩密度泛函计算（constrained-moment density-functional calculations）获取原子间力（interatomic forces）和有效磁场（effective magnetic fields）。

Abstract: Coupled spin-lattice dynamics (SLD) underlie a wide range of magnetic phenomena, yet a unified first-principles framework that propagates both degrees of freedom without empirical parameterization has remained elusive. We present a fully ab initio SLD approach integrated into VASP, in which interatomic forces and effective magnetic fields are obtained at each time step from self-consistent constrained-moment density-functional calculations. The method is validated on four materials spanning ferromagnetic, non-collinear, and geometrically frustrated orders, recovering the correct magnetic ground state in every case from random initial conditions. SLD trajectories also provide physically correlated training data for magnetic machine-learning potentials, as demonstrated for BiFeO$_3$ by a reduction of up to approximately one order of magnitude in energy MAE over training on randomized spin configurations. This framework opens a practical first-principles route to finite-temperature spin-lattice coupled phenomena in magnetic materials.

### [183] [Compositionally tuned phase transformations enhance pyroelectric energy harvesting from low-grade heat](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01791)

Abstract: Phase-transforming pyroelectric materials have emerged as promising candidates for low-grade thermal energy harvesting. Here we report compositionally tunable phase transformations in Ba$_{1-x}$Sr$_x$TiO$_3$ ($x \in [0, 0.3]$), revealing evolution from first-order to second-order character. Abstract: Engineering liquid metal alloys offers a transformative pathway for plasma-facing components (PFC) by enabling chemically tailored surfaces that can simultaneously optimize plasma-material interactions, reduce divertor heat flux, and enhance core plasma confinement, thereby advancing the commercial viability of nuclear fusion power plants. We validated them using formation energies and elastic constants. We then employed reactive molecular dynamics simulations to resolve the coupled effects of surface segregation and impurity-driven chemistry at fusion-relevant temperatures. We also introduced an overlap-based segregation index that captures interfacial compositional separation directly from atomistic density distributions. This metric reveals a clear hierarchy of segregation regimes across all systems and presents a unified view of segregation across all observations reported herein. ### [185] [Reversible fully spin polarization in strain-engineered two-dimensional fully compensated magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01872)

Motivation: 在对称补偿磁体中实现可控的自旋极化及其反转是自旋电子学的重要目标，但传统方法面临对称性约束。本文旨在利用单轴应变解除二维系统中磁子晶格的等价性，驱动交变磁体（altermagnet, AM）向全补偿亚铁磁体（fully compensated ferrimagnet, fFIM）转变，从而实现完全自旋极化及其可逆切换。

Method: 采用对称性分析（symmetry analysis）和最小紧束缚模型（minimal tight-binding model）建立理论框架；结合自旋群分析（spin-group analysis）、第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和玻尔兹曼输运理论（Boltzmann transport theory），在代表性候选材料AM Mn₂SeO和铁弹性fFIM V₂SO中验证机制的普适性。

Result: 单轴应变使二维AM态转变为fFIM态，实现完全自旋极化；沿正交方向施加应变可获得两个能量简并但自旋极化方向相反的fFIM态，实现可逆自旋切换。两个对称性相关的fFIM态可视为不同的铁弹变体（ferroelastic variants），表明该机制可推广至铁弹性fFIM体系。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一个普适的对称性驱动框架，用于应变控制和可逆的全自旋极化输运；应变工程化的AM和铁弹性fFIM系统为易失性和非易失性自旋电子学（volatile and nonvolatile spintronic applications）提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Achieving controllable spin polarization and its reversal in symmetry-compensated magnets. Here we demonstrate, using symmetry analysis and a minimal tight-binding model, that uniaxial strain removes these constraints by inducing inequivalence between magnetic sublattices in two-dimensional (2D) system, driving an altermagnetic (AM) state into a fully compensated ferrimagnetic (fFIM) state and enabling fully spin polarization. Furthermore, strain along orthogonal directions gives rise to two energetically degenerate fFIM states with opposite spin polarization, enabling reversible spin switching. More importantly, the two symmetry-related fFIM states can be regarded as distinct ferroelastic variants, suggesting that this model or mechanism can be extended to ferroelastic fFIM systems. The generality of this mechanism is confirmed by combining spin-group analysis, first-principles calculations, and Boltzmann transport theory in representative candidates, including AM Mn$_2$SeO and ferroelastic fFIM V$_2$SO. Our results reveal a universal symmetry-driven framework for strain-controlled and -reversible fully spin-polarized transport and identify strain-engineered AM and ferroelastic fFIM systems as a promising platform for volatile and nonvolatile spintronic applications.

</details>


### [186] [Polymorphic crystallites model for monolayer amorphous materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01881)
*Le-Ye Zhu,Xi Zhang,Yun-Peng Wang,Jieheng Shi,Junwei Zhang,Shixuan Du,Yu-Yang Zhang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于第一性原理（first-principles）总能量的机器学习势（machine learning potential），结合能量驱动动力学蒙特卡洛（energy-driven kinetic Monte Carlo）主动学习框架，对非晶多元素单层体系进行建模分析。

Result: 提出了多晶型晶粒（polymorphic crystallite）模型，发现单层非晶氮化硼由 $o-B_2N_2$ 和 $o-B_4N_4$ 结构基元（structural motifs）的晶粒共存构成；单层非晶LiCl存在六方和四方晶粒共存；单层非晶BCN包含类石墨烯（graphene-like）、类六方氮化硼（h-BN-like）和类硼烯（borophene-like）晶粒组合。

Conclusion: 多晶型晶粒模型在两个额外的多元素非晶单层体系中得到进一步验证，表明其具有普适性。这些发现拓展了经典非晶结构模型的图景，为非晶材料的微观结构提供了新的认识。

Abstract: Modeling the atomic structure of amorphous materials has long been a critical challenge in materials science. Recent advances in monolayer amorphous materials enable direct observation of their atomic structures, paving the way for a better understanding of their atomic-scale models. Here, we investigate amorphous multielement monolayers using machine learning potential from first-principles total energies via energy-driven kinetic Monte Carlo based active-learning framework. A polymorphic crystallite model is proposed to describe the atomic configuration of monolayer amorphous boron nitride, as it consists of coexisting crystallite of $o-B_2N_2$ and $o-B_4N_4$ structural motifs. Generality of the polymorphic crystallite model is further validated in two other multielement monolayer amorphous systems. Monolayer amorphous LiCl shows coexisting hexagonal and tetragonal crystallites, while monolayer amorphous BCN contains a combination of graphene-like, h-BN-like, and borophene-like crystallites. These findings expand the classical picture of amorphous structure models and offer new insight into the microscopic structure of amorphous materials.

### [187] [Liquid-phase encapsulation of $π$-conjugated dyes in boron nitride nanotubes: Ensemble and single-nanotube optical characterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01906)
*Friedrich Schöppler,Lukas Stumpf,Lucas Fuhl,Elena Behr,Charlotte Allard,Christoph Lambert,Richard Martel,Tobias Hertel*

TL;DR: 本研究通过联合系综光谱和单纳米管偏振显微术，系统分析了十种染料分子填充氮化硼纳米管（BNNTs）的光物理性质。在齐聚噻吩体系中，发现其形成弱发射系综，有效辐射速率受到抑制，排除了明亮J-聚集体的可能性；单纳米管成像揭示有序但结构异质的受限系综；尼罗红则呈现溶剂化变色电荷转移态的介电调谐行为。研究将染料@BNNT体系定性为光学惰性的纳米受限系统，其中分子有序性、介电受限和客体-客体耦合可通过系综与单纳米管光谱加以区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管氮化硼纳米管（boron nitride nanotubes, BNNTs）可为分子染料提供宽禁带、光学透明的准一维主体，且主体本身几乎不参与电子过程，但染料@BNNT体系是否产生明亮的J-或H-聚集体，还是形成依赖于链长和局部堆积的结构异质发射系综，这一问题尚未完全解决。

Method: 采用系综消光（extinction）光谱、光致发光（photoluminescence）光谱、量子产率测量以及时间相关单光子计数（TCSPC）导出的辐射与非辐射速率；结合偏振分辨单纳米管显微术（polarization-resolved single-nanotube microscopy）；从十种染料筛选中选取四联噻吩、六联噻吩、八联噻吩和尼罗红作为研究对象。

Result: 在齐聚噻吩系列中，受限效应以链长依赖的方式改变光谱和激发态动力学：三种齐聚噻吩均形成弱发射系综，有效辐射速率受抑制，其中6T显示出最显著的辐射与非辐射衰减之间的重新分布。整个系列未观察到辐射速率增强或荧光寿命缩短，排除了明亮J-聚集体归属。单纳米管偏振显微术揭示强偏振发射但存在管间与管内变化，表明齐聚噻吩@BNNT为有序但结构异质的受限系综。尼罗红的主要响应为溶剂化变色电荷转移态的介电调谐，而非聚集体形成。

Conclusion: 染料填充的BNNTs应被定性为光学惰性的纳米受限系统（optically quiet nanoconfined systems），在该体系中，分子有序性、介电受限和客体-客体耦合可通过系综与单纳米管光谱的联合分析加以区分。

Abstract: Boron nitride nanotubes (BNNTs) provide wide-bandgap, optically transparent one-dimensional hosts for molecular dyes, limiting direct electronic participation of the host. Whether dye@BNNT systems produce bright, well-defined J- or H-aggregates or instead heterogeneous emissive ensembles whose character depends on chain length and local packing remains only partly resolved. We address this question using ensemble extinction, photoluminescence, quantum-yield measurements, and TCSPC-derived radiative and non-radiative rates, together with polarization-resolved single-nanotube microscopy on encapsulated quaterthiophene, sexithiophene, octithiophene, and Nile Red, selected from a ten-dye screening. In the oligothiophene series, confinement modifies spectra and excited-state dynamics in a length-dependent manner, with all three oligothiophenes forming weakly emissive ensembles with suppressed effective radiative rates and 6T showing the strongest redistribution between effective radiative and non-radiative decay. The absence of radiative-rate enhancement or fluorescence-lifetime shortening across the series disfavors bright J-aggregate assignments. Polarization-resolved single-nanotube microscopy reveals strongly polarized emission, but with tube-to-tube and intratube variations, identifying oligothiophene@BNNTs as ordered yet structurally heterogeneous confined ensembles. Nile Red provides a complementary case in which the dominant response is dielectric tuning of a solvatochromic charge-transfer state rather than oligothiophene-like aggregate formation. These findings establish dye-filled BNNTs as optically quiet nanoconfined systems in which molecular ordering, dielectric confinement, and guest-guest coupling can be distinguished through combined ensemble and single-nanotube spectroscopy.

### [188] [Microscale bending plasticity and fracture behavior of amorphous aluminum oxide films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01917)
*Nidhin George Mathews,Erkka J. Frankberg,Vivek Devulapalli,Chandan Kumar,Barbara Putz,Aloshious Lambai,Sergei Khakalo,Mattia Cabrioli,Bjarke Holl Christensen,Janne-Petteri Niemelä,Arnold Milenko Müller,Fabio Di Fonzo,Ivo Utke,Erkki Levänen,Gaurav Mohanty*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过微悬臂梁弯曲实验，首次证明了脉冲激光沉积（PLD）和原子层沉积（ALD）非晶氧化铝（a-Al2O3）薄膜在微尺度下的弯曲塑性，而溅射沉积（SD）薄膜则表现为弹性脆性断裂。三种薄膜的缺口断裂韧性值相近（3.1±0.2 MPa·m^0.5），表明裂纹尖端塑性受到抑制，沉积方法和缺陷分布是决定变形行为的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究已证实脉冲激光沉积（PLD）非晶氧化铝（a-Al2O3）在微尺度下具有压缩塑性，但对其弯曲塑性及断裂行为的理解尚不充分。本文旨在系统探索不同沉积方法制备的a-Al2O3薄膜在微尺度下的弯曲塑性和断裂行为，以揭示缺陷与沉积工艺对塑性机制的影响。

Method: 采用三种沉积方法——脉冲激光沉积（pulse laser deposition, PLD）、原子层沉积（atomic layer deposition, ALD）和溅射沉积（sputter deposition, SD）——制备非晶氧化铝（a-Al2O3）薄膜，通过原位微悬臂梁弯曲实验（in situ microcantilever bending experiment）在室温下测试其微尺度弯曲塑性和断裂行为，并对缺口微悬臂梁进行弯曲测试以评估断裂韧性。

Result: 所有PLD a-Al2O3微悬臂梁在弯曲中表现出显著延性，总应变超过10%而未断裂；ALD样品中一半表现为弹性脆性断裂，另一半呈现弯曲塑性，说明缺陷分布强烈影响变形行为；所有SD样品因柱状生长微结构而表现为弹性脆性断裂。缺口弯曲测试显示三种薄膜均发生脆性断裂，断裂韧性值相等（3.1±0.2 MPa·m^0.5），排除了局部裂纹尖端塑性。

Conclusion: 微尺度弯曲响应高度依赖薄膜沉积方法，缺陷的存在显著抑制塑性机制。制造过程中最小化缺陷是开发耐损伤非晶氧化物的关键。然而，PLD和ALD微悬臂梁在包含拉伸应力分量的弯曲条件下仍表现出塑性，说明非晶氧化铝的塑性变形机制具有更普遍的适用性，并非完全由沉积方法决定。

Abstract: Recent work has demonstrated microscale compressive plasticity in pulse laser deposited (PLD) amorphous alumina (a-Al2O3). This work explores microscale bending plasticity and fracture behavior of a-Al2O3 films deposited using three different methods-PLD, atomic layer deposition (ALD) and sputter deposition (SD). The three deposition routes produced amorphous films with similar stoichiometric compositions. We demonstrate, for the first time, bending plasticity in PLD and ALD a-Al2O3 films at microscale using in situ microcantilever bending experiments at room temperature. All tested PLD a-Al2O3 microcantilevers showed substantial ductile behavior in bending by accommodating total strains >10% without fracture. Half of the tested ALD a-Al2O3 cantilevers exhibited elastic brittle fracture while the other half showed bending plasticity, indicating that the observed deformation behavior is strongly influenced by the presence and distribution of defects within the tested volume. All SD a-Al2O3 microcantilevers showed elastic brittle failure attributed to their columnar growth microstructure. The microscale bending response was found to be highly dependent on the film deposition method highlighting the role of defects in suppressing plasticity mechanisms. Notched microcantilever bending tests on all three films showed brittle failure with similar fracture toughness value of 3.1 +/- 0.2 MPa.m0.5, effectively ruling out any localized crack tip plasticity. These findings underscore the importance of minimizing defects during fabrication in order to develop damage tolerant amorphous oxides. Nonetheless, the observation of bending plasticity in both PLD and ALD microcantilevers, which include a tensile stress component as well, suggests that the plastic deformation mechanisms in amorphous alumina are more general and are not exclusively governed by the deposition method.

*Alex Hallett,Nicola A. Spaldin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理（first principles）计算，分析原子位电多极矩（electric multipole moment）和磁多极矩（magnetic multipole moment），识别这些多极矩与手性（chirality）之间的关联。

Result: 反铁序排列的原子位电环偶极矩可作为反铁轴旋转的序参量（order parameter）；整体手性序由反极性电偶极矩与电环偶极矩的复合序（composite order）参量化。

Conclusion: 评估了多种提出的手性序参量，排除了部分候选者，并为未来探索指出了最有前景的方向。

Abstract: We present a first principles study of the ferrochiral phase transition in chiral BaTiOCu$_4$(PO$_4$)$_4$, which has been shown using X-ray diffraction to proceed via the antiferroaxial rotation of antipolar structural units. We analyze the atomic-site electric and magnetic multipole moments to identify connections between these multipoles and chirality and corroborate the previous experimental interpretation. We show that antiferroically ordered atomic-site electric toroidal dipole moments act as an order parameter for the antiferroaxial rotations, and that the overall chiral order is parameterized by the composite order of the antipolar electric dipole and electric toroidal dipole moments. Finally, we evaluate the suitability of various proposed order parameters for chirality, show that some can be excluded and suggest the most promising directions for future exploration.

### [191] [Dynamic Mechanical Response of Spinodal Architectures Across Length and Time Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02031)
*Vatsa Gandhi,Rishi Kommalapati,Carlos M. Portela,Vikram Deshpande*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和有限元计算，系统研究了旋节线（spinodal）构型材料在不同长度尺度（100微米微观尺度与30毫米宏观尺度）和应变率（10^{-3} s^{-1}至10^{4} s^{-1}）下的力学响应，发现宏观尺度试样在高应变率下强度提升近十倍，其机制源于从基材应变率敏感性主导向惯性主导行为的转变，并建立了类似流体力学中依赖于结构长度尺度的行为相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高通量表征不同长度尺度下的构型材料（architected materials）虽然有助于快速筛选拓扑结构用于工程应用，但实验室缩放试样与实际应用场景在长度尺度和加载条件上存在差异，导致直接比较困难。本文旨在揭示基材应变率敏感性（strain-rate sensitivity）、拓扑长度尺度和施加变形速率之间的相互作用机制。

Method: 采用旋节线构型（spinodal architected morphology）作为研究对象，制造了长度尺度为100微米（microscale）和30毫米（macroscale）的试样，在10^{-3} s^{-1}至10^{4} s^{-1}的应变率范围内进行实验表征，并结合有限元（finite element）计算分析力学响应机制，最终建立行为参数相图（maps）。

Result: 微观尺度试样在高应变率下强度仅适度增加，而宏观尺度试样在等效应变率下强度提升了近十倍。有限元计算表明，这一增强源于宏观尺度试样中从基材应变率敏感性主导向惯性主导行为（inertia-dominated behavior）的转变，而在所研究的应变率范围内，微观尺度试样未观察到这一转变。

Conclusion: 从基材应变率敏感性主导向惯性主导行为的转变与流体（fluids）中的现象具有类比性，即依赖于结构长度尺度（structural length scale）。该发现为理解跨长度和时间尺度的物理响应参数提供了见解，有助于设计能够提取结构应用相关动态特性的新型实验室实验。

Abstract: High-throughput characterization of architected materials across a wide range of length scales enables rapid screening of topologies for engineering applications. Scaled-down specimens manufactured and evaluated in laboratory environments enable this iteration, but application scenarios may involve differing length scales and loading conditions that complicate direct comparisons. Here, we use a spinodal architected morphology to determine the interplay among the constituent material's strain-rate sensitivity, the topological length scale, and the imposed deformation rates. We report characterization spanning strain rates from $10^{-3}$ s$^{-1}$ to $10^{4}$ s$^{-1}$ on spinodal architected specimens with length scales of 100 $μ$m (microscale) and 30 mm (macroscale). The experiments show that while microscale specimens exhibit moderate increase in strength at high strain rates, macroscale specimens exhibit a nearly tenfold increase in strength at equivalent strain rates. Finite element calculations reveal that this increase is linked to a transition from a response governed by constituent material strain-rate sensitivity to inertia-dominated behavior in macroscale specimens, a transition not observed in microscale specimens at the strain rates investigated here. Using extensive finite element calculations, we develop maps to establish the parameters governing the regimes of behavior, illustrating that the transition from behavior governed by constituent material rate sensitivity to inertia-dominated behavior has analogies to fluids in that it depends on a structural length scale. Our findings provide insights into the physical parameters that govern responses across length and time scales, towards the development and design of new laboratory experiments that extract relevant dynamic properties for structural applications.

### [192] [Multiscale computational approaches to magnetic behaviour in Cobalt Ferrite (CoFe$_2$O$_4$) nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02065)
*Soham Chandra,Soumyajit Sarkar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个整合密度泛函理论（DFT+U）、原子尺度的自旋模型、统计力学（statistical mechanics）与连续介质微磁学（continuum micromagnetics）的多尺度计算框架，用于预测钴铁氧体（CoFe₂O₄）从电子到宏观尺度的磁学功能特性，并通过案例验证了预测精度，讨论了现有挑战与未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钴铁氧体因其高磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）、磁弹性耦合（magnetoelastic coupling）和热稳定性，在自旋电子学（spintronics）、磁热疗（magnetic hyperthermia）、能量收集和催化等领域具有重要应用。然而，其复杂的功能机制跨越多个尺度和长度，单一方法难以全面预测，因此需要建立一个多尺度且具备预测能力的计算框架。

Method: 首先利用DFT+U计算交换常数Jᵢⱼ、磁晶各向异性常数K₁和磁弹性系数B₁，并考虑阳离子反位（cation inversion）、应变（strain）和关联效应（correlation effects）。随后将这些参数输入广义海森堡哈密顿量（generalized Heisenberg Hamiltonians），进行蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）和朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特（Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert）模拟，研究纳米颗粒和薄膜中的有限尺寸效应、磁滞、矫顽力和热疗响应。最后通过粗粒化策略（coarse-graining）桥接到微磁学模型，保证参数一致性。

Result: 案例研究表明了尺寸依赖的各向异性增强、表面自旋无序（surface spin disorder）、应变可调开关以及掺杂趋势，揭示了实验难以独立获取的设计原理。通过对居里温度（Curie temperature）、各向异性常数、矫顽力（coercivity）和磁致伸缩（magnetostriction）等基准量的验证，确认了预测准确性。

Conclusion: 该多尺度计算框架能够预测钴铁氧体在不同尺度的磁学功能特性，弥补了纯实验方法的不足。同时指出了当前挑战，包括U参数敏感性、真实表面化学、自旋-晶格耦合（spin-lattice coupling）和大规模集成问题，并提出了DFT+DMFT、耦合动力学和机器学习势（machine-learned potentials）等未来研究方向。

Abstract: Cobalt ferrite (CoFe$_2$O$_4$) is a prototypical ferrimagnetic spinel oxide whose exceptional magnetic anisotropy, magnetoelastic coupling, and thermal stability underpin applications in spintronics, magnetic hyperthermia, energy harvesting, and catalysis. This chapter presents a comprehensive computational framework that integrates electronic$-$structure calculations with atomistic spin modeling, statistical mechanics, and continuum micromagnetics to predict magnetic functionality across length and time scales. Starting from density functional theory with Hubbard corrections (DFT$+$U), we derive exchange constants J$_{ij}$, magnetocrystalline anisotropy K$_1$, and magnetoelastic coefficients B$_1$, accounting for cation inversion, strain, and correlation effects. These parameters feed into generalized Heisenberg Hamiltonians, enabling Monte Carlo and Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert simulations of finite-size effects, hysteresis, coercivity, and hyperthermia response in nanoparticles and thin films. Coarse-graining strategies bridge to micromagnetic modeling, ensuring consistent parameter flow without empirical fitting. Computational case studies demonstrate size-dependent anisotropy enhancement, surface spin disorder, strain-tunable switching, and doping trends, revealing design principles inaccessible to experiment alone. Validation against benchmarks, e.g. Curie temperature, anisotropy constants, coercivity, magnetostriction, confirms predictive accuracy. Current challenges, e.g., U$-$parameter sensitivity, realistic surface chemistry, spin-lattice coupling, and large-scale integration are discussed alongside emerging directions including DFT$+$DMFT, coupled dynamics, and machine-learned potentials.

</details>


### [193] [Ab initio evidence for spin-polarized and soft-mode instabilities in D-type carbon schwarzite C136](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02082)
*Eugene Yashin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算发现，D型碳施瓦茨石（carbon schwarzite）C136是一种具有平带（flat-band）特征的金属性碳网络，其自旋极化态能量更低，并表现出显著的虚频软模（imaginary-frequency soft mode），表明该材料处于自旋破缺与晶格破缺的不稳定性边缘，可能成为竞争性量子相（如磁性、电荷密度波乃至超导）的候选平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碳施瓦茨石因其负高斯曲率（negative Gaussian curvature）能够重新组织π电子能带结构，为平带物理（flat-band physics）、增强态密度（density of states）及竞争性破缺对称相（broken-symmetry phases）提供天然平台，因此有必要对其电子结构与晶格稳定性进行第一性原理计算研究。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）的第一性原理计算，对一个136原子D型碳施瓦茨石单胞进行了非自旋极化与自旋极化计算；同时使用Phonopy和Quantum ESPRESSO软件，通过78个对称性约化的位移构型进行有限位移声子计算（finite-displacement phonon calculations）。

Result: 非自旋极化计算显示金属性电子结构，在费米能级（Fermi level）附近存在显著平带特征和高态密度；自旋极化计算收敛到磁态，总磁化强度约为每单胞11.01玻尔磁子（Bohr magneton），绝对磁化强度约为每单胞12.15玻尔磁子，该磁态能量低于非自旋极化态约0.03687 Ry（约0.50 eV）；声子计算揭示理想结构存在大量虚频模式，最软模位于q = [0.5, 0.5, 0.5]处，频率约为-11.90 THz。

Conclusion: 理想C136并非简单的简谐稳定金属碳相，而是一个靠近自旋与晶格破缺不稳定性边界的平带碳网络，可能涉及Stoner型平带磁性（Stoner-like flat-band magnetism）和Peierls或电荷密度波型结构重构（Peierls- or charge-density-wave-like structural reconstruction），是磁性、软模重构及可能超导相竞争的候选体系。

Abstract: Carbon schwarzites are three-dimensional sp2-bonded carbon networks with negative Gaussian curvature. Because negative curvature can reorganize the pi-electron manifold, these materials provide a natural platform for flat-band physics, enhanced density of states, and competing broken-symmetry phases. Here I report first-principles calculations for a 136-atom D-type carbon schwarzite cell using density-functional theory. Non-spin-polarized calculations show a metallic electronic structure with pronounced flat-band features and high density of states near the Fermi level. A spin-polarized calculation converges to a magnetic solution with total magnetization of approximately 11.01 Bohr magnetons per 136-atom cell and absolute magnetization of approximately 12.15 Bohr magnetons per cell. The spin-polarized state is lower in energy than the corresponding non-spin-polarized solution by approximately 0.03687 Ry, or about 0.50 eV per cell. Finite-displacement phonon calculations using Phonopy and Quantum ESPRESSO, with 78 symmetry-reduced displaced configurations, further reveal substantial imaginary-frequency modes in the ideal submitted structure. The softest mode in the calculated band path occurs near q = [0.5, 0.5, 0.5], with frequency approximately -11.90 THz. These results indicate that ideal C136 is not a simple harmonically stable metallic carbon phase. Instead, it appears to be a flat-band carbon network close to spin and lattice broken-symmetry instabilities. Possible interpretations include Stoner-like flat-band magnetism and Peierls- or charge-density-wave-like structural reconstruction. Superconductivity is not claimed here as an established ground state; rather, the results identify C136 and related D-type schwarzites as candidate platforms where magnetism, soft-mode reconstruction, and possible doped or structurally stabilized superconducting phases compete.

Abstract: Magnetic topological insulators provide a unique platform to explore the interplay between magnetism and topology. MnBi$_2$Te$_4$, known for its A-type antiferromagnetic (AFM) ground state, undergoes a striking transformation when single crystals are grown in an applied magnetic field. Despite retaining the same crystal structure, field-grown MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ exhibits a ferromagnetic (FM) ground state with a Curie temperature of $\sim$ 12.5 K, confirmed by magnetization, magnetic torque, electrical resistivity, and specific heat measurements. First-principles calculations support these findings, revealing that magnetic-field-assisted synthesis can effectively reconfigure the ground-state spin order and thereby modify the material's electronic properties, as reflected in the de Haas-van Alphen oscillation seen in the magnetic torque.

### [195] [Composition-Weighted Symbolic Regression for General-Purpose Property Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02267)
*Yang Huang,Jingrun Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种基于成分加权的符号回归（composition-weighted symbolic regression）框架，能够直接从化学组成中学习可解析的物性预测表达式，同时统一回归与分类任务，并在材料发现中兼具可解释性与竞争性精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有材料物性预测的黑箱模型（black-box models）虽然精度高，但缺乏可解释性；而传统符号回归方法通常需要预定义描述符，难以直接从化学组成出发进行端到端学习。

Method: 框架联合学习解析函数形式（analytical functional forms）与任务相关的元素权重（task-dependent elemental weightings），无需预定义描述符；通过引入最大值/最小值算子（max/min operators）自然施加非负带隙、有界分类概率等约束；采用混合蒙特卡洛树搜索-遗传编程（hybrid Monte Carlo tree search–genetic programming）算法，结合梯度优化与并行计算实现高效搜索。

Result: 在 MatBench 基准任务上，与最先进的黑箱模型相比取得了竞争性的精度，同时输出显式解析表达式。在 III-V 族半导体合金上的应用表明，模型能够生成平滑的成分-物性变化趋势，所学元素权重呈现具有化学意义的周期性规律。

Conclusion: 该框架为材料发现与物性筛选提供了一条可扩展且可解释的路径，弥合了预测精度与物理可解释性之间的差距。

Abstract: We introduce a composition-weighted symbolic regression framework for interpretable prediction of materials properties directly from chemical composition. The method jointly learns analytical functional forms and task-dependent elemental weightings without predefined descriptors. By incorporating max/min operators, it naturally enforces constraints such as non-negative band gaps and bounded classification probabilities, unifying regression and classification tasks. Efficient search is achieved through a hybrid Monte Carlo tree search--genetic programming algorithm with gradient-based refinement and parallel computation. Benchmarks on MatBench tasks show competitive accuracy relative to state-of-the-art black-box models while yielding explicit analytical expressions. Applied to III--V semiconductor alloys, the model produces smooth composition-dependent trends and learned elemental weights with chemically meaningful periodic behavior. This framework provides a scalable and interpretable route for materials discovery and property screening.

### [196] [Quantum Limits of Electronic Transport in Nanostructured Macroscopic Conductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02295)
*Agnieszka E. Lekawa-Raus,John S. Bulmer,Teresa Kulka,Magdalena Marganska,Nick Papior,Dwight G. Rickel,Fedor F. Balakirev,Jacek A. Majewski,Krzysztof Koziol,Karolina Z. Milowska*

TL;DR: 本文结合量子相干输运、热无序和磁场效应的统一原子论框架，与60 T超高磁场磁输运测量，揭示碳纳米管纤维中的宏观电荷输运主要由结区量子干涉主导，而非仅由缺陷或掺杂决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维材料宏观组装体（如碳纳米管纤维）中电荷输运的微观机制尚不明确，传统唯象模型无法将电子结构与宏观磁输运（magnetotransport）显式关联起来。

Method: 发展了一个统一的原子论框架（unified atomistic framework），将量子相干输运（quantum-coherent transport）、热无序（thermal disorder）和磁场效应相结合，并在宽温区、高达60 T的超高磁场下对碳纳米管纤维进行了磁输运测量。

Result: 正磁电阻（positive magnetoresistance）受结重叠长度控制，而负磁电阻（negative magnetoresistance）主要源于晶格失配异质结（lattice-mismatched heterojunctions），而非仅由弱局域化（weak localisation）引起。大规模数值数据集的统计分析表明，实验观测到的正二次磁电阻源于结输运（junction transport）。

Conclusion: 无序低维网络中的宏观输运主要由结级量子干涉（junction-level quantum interference）主导，而非仅由缺陷或掺杂决定。

Abstract: Macroscopic assemblies of one- and two-dimensional materials promise to translate nanoscale electronic properties into device-scale performance, yet the microscopic principles governing charge transport in such networks remain unresolved. In these systems, conductivity is often interpreted using phenomenological models that do not explicitly connect electronic structure to macroscopic magnetotransport. Here we develop a unified atomistic framework that links quantum-coherent transport, thermal disorder and magnetic-field effects, and combine it with ultrahigh-field magnetotransport measurements up to 60 T over a broad temperature range on carbon nanotube fibres. We show that positive magnetoresistance is controlled by junction overlap length, whereas negative magnetoresistance arises predominantly from lattice-mismatched heterojunctions rather than weak localisation alone. Statistical analysis of a large-scale numerical dataset reveals that the experimentally observed positive quadratic magnetoresistance originates from junction transport. These results show that macroscopic transport in disordered low-dimensional networks is governed primarily by junction-level quantum interference rather than solely by defects or doping.

### [197] [Persistent Spin Texture and Spin-Orbital Hall Responses on the AgI (110) Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02368)
*Manish Kumar Mohanta*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算与解析建模，系统研究了AgI (110)表面的结构、电子及自旋-轨道输运性质。该体系因非中心对称和非对称性而展现出稳健的持久自旋织构（persistent spin texture, PST），可实现近乎无限的自旋寿命。研究还表明该体系具有可观的自旋霍尔电导率（spin Hall conductivity, SHC）和轨道霍尔电导率（orbital Hall conductivity, OHC），且PST对双轴应变、结构畸变和多层形成具有鲁棒性，而垂直电场可诱导向Rashba型自旋织构的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有报道的持久自旋织构（PST）材料主要基于硫族化合物，卤化物半导体能否作为PST宿主材料尚不清楚。本研究旨在探索卤化物体系中的PST现象，以扩展自旋电子学（spintronics）的材料平台。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合解析建模；引入有效自旋-轨道耦合哈密顿量（effective spin-orbit coupled Hamiltonian）描述能带中的各向异性自旋劈裂和动量偏移；提出两个新的PST解析模型并与现有模型进行对比。

Result: AgI (110)表面展现出鲁棒的持久自旋织构（PST），具有单向自旋构型和抑制的自旋弛豫；体系具有可观的自旋霍尔电导率（SHC）和轨道霍尔电导率（OHC）；PST对双轴应变、结构畸变和多层形成具有鲁棒性，但垂直电场可破坏对称性保护，驱动其向Rashba型自旋织构转变。

Conclusion: 本研究证实卤化物半导体AgI (110)可作为持久自旋织构（PST）的宿主材料，显著扩展了自旋电子学应用的材料库。该体系在实现长寿命自旋输运和可调谐自旋-轨道功能方面具有潜力，为低维卤化物体系中的自旋电子学研究提供了新平台。

Abstract: A systematic investigation of the structural, electronic, and spin-orbital transport properties of the AgI (110) surface is presented using first-principles calculations combined with analytical modelling. The non-centrosymmetric and nonsymmorphic nature of the system gives rise to a robust persistent spin texture (PST), characterized by a unidirectional spin configuration and suppressed spin relaxation, enabling an effectively infinite spin lifetime. Unlike previously reported PST materials, which are predominantly based on chalcogen compounds, this work demonstrates that a halide semiconductor can host PST, thereby significantly expanding the materials platform for spintronic applications. The underlying mechanism is captured using an effective spin-orbit coupled Hamiltonian, which reproduces the anisotropic spin splitting and momentum shift observed in the band structure. This work introduces two new analytical models describing PST and compares them with existing models, offering new perspectives on PST arising from spin-orbit interaction. In addition, the system exhibits sizable intrinsic spin Hall conductivity (SHC) and orbital Hall conductivity (OHC), highlighting its potential for efficient charge-to-spin and charge-to-orbital conversion. The PST is found to be robust against biaxial strain, structural distortion, and multilayer formation, while a vertical electric field breaks the symmetry protection and drives a transition to a Rashba-type spin texture. These findings establish AgI (110) as a promising platform for realizing long-lived spin transport and tunable spin-orbit functionalities in the low-dimensional halide systems.

Method: 采用导电原子力显微镜（conductive atomic force microscopy, c-AFM）探测α-Si忆阻器中导电细丝的空间分布。

Result: 电荷传输由有限数量的离散细丝主导而非均匀导电；细丝平均面密度约为每平方微米3200根；同一忆阻器内同时存在挥发性和非挥发性细丝。

Conclusion: 实验数据及两类细丝的性质可通过多重陷阱辅助隧穿（multiple trap assisted tunnelling）模型加以解释，该模型对两种细丝的物理性质给出了合理的估算。

Abstract: Cation-based Ag/Cu filaments formed in an insulating $α$-Si matrix are widely used as memristors in crossbar arrays for efficient in-memory computing. However, the stochastic nature of filament formation and rupture gives rise to device-to-device and cycle-to-cycle variation. Despite successful implementation of large-scale memristor arrays, systematic studies of filament parameters and their spatial distribution in the memristors are scarce. In this work, we use conductive atomic force microscopy (c-AFM) to probe the spatial distribution of conductive filaments in $α$-Si memristors. The charge transport is dominated by a limited number of discrete filaments rather than by uniform conduction across the device area. The systematic analysis of the experiment gives the mean surface density of the conductive filaments $\sim$3200 per $μ\text{m}^2$. Both volatile and non-volatile filaments can be found within one memristor. The experimental data and the nature of volatile and non-volatile filaments may be explained within the model of multiple trap assisted tunnelling. The model yields reasonable estimates for physical properties for both types of filaments.

</details>

### [201] [Designing explicit functionals for the charge density in terms of a potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02492)
*Muhammed Hüseyin Güneş,Ayoub Aouina,Vitaly Gorelov,Matteo Gatti,Lucia Reining*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了如何利用均匀电子气（homogeneous electron gas）的模型数据，直接构建非均匀材料中电荷密度关于Kohn-Sham势的显式泛函，无需求解Kohn-Sham薛定谔方程。通过一系列从Thomas-Fermi近似到Connector Theory的近似方案，在立方氦（cubic helium）这一典型强非均匀材料中验证了该方法随近似层级提升而系统改进的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际多体系统（many-body systems）中，利用模型数据（如均匀电子气数据）构建交换关联势的局域密度近似（Local Density Approximation, LDA）是一种重要策略。本文旨在探索能否直接将模型数据用于构造材料可观测量（observables）的泛函，特别是电荷密度关于Kohn-Sham势的显式泛函，从而避免求解Kohn-Sham薛定谔方程。

Method: 以均匀电子气的Lindhard密度-密度响应函数（Lindhard density-density response function）为核心构件，设计了一系列逐步逼真的近似方案：完全近视（nearsighted）表达式（等价于Thomas-Fermi近似）、泛函泰勒展开（functional Taylor expansions），以及Connector Theory（见[Aouina等, npj Computational Materials 11, 242 (2025)]）的多种近似。所有方案中电荷密度均无需通过求解Kohn-Sham方程获得。

Result: 以立方氦（cubic helium）这一典型强非均匀材料为测试对象，计算结果随近似层次的提高而系统性地改善。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一条有前景的路径，用于构建既相对简便计算又易于分析的电荷密度泛函表达式。

Abstract: One of the most powerful strategies to address properties of real many-body systems is to incorporate data obtained for models, for example, to use data of the homogeneous electron gas in order to build the Local Density Approximation for the Kohn-Sham exchange-correlation potential. In the present work, we examine to what extent we can use model data to design functionals directly for observables of materials. In particular, we study different approximations for the charge density of real inhomogeneous materials expressed as a simple, explicit functional of a given Kohn-Sham potential, using as central building block the Lindhard density-density response function of the homogeneous electron gas. Our increasingly realistic set of approximations includes a fully nearsighted expression equivalent to the Thomas-Fermi approximation, functional Taylor expansions, and different approximations to the Connector Theory developed in [Aouina \textit{et al.}, npj Computational Materials {\bf 11}, 242 (2025)]. In all cases, the charge density is obtained without ever solving the Kohn-Sham Schrödinger equation. Results for cubic helium, a prototypical strongly inhomogeneous material, systematically improve with higher levels of approximation, indicating that this is a promising route to obtain expressions that are relatively simple to calculate and to analyze.

Abstract: Following the Fukushima Daiichi disaster, an increasing number of studies concentrate on the development of Accident Tolerant Fuel (ATF) cladding materials for nuclear fuel, aiming to prevent the oxidation of zirconium during incidents such as Loss of Coolant Accident (LOCA) and to effectively lower the amount of heat and hydrogen released during emergency core cooling (ECC). Zirconium alloy cladding with a protective chromium (Cr) coating is considered one of the promising candidates, largely due to its relatively short timeline for deployment in nuclear power plants. In this study, Cr-coated and uncoated Zircaloy-4 claddings were evaluated using high temperature X-ray diffraction (HT-XRD) in vacuum over a temperature range from RT to 1100oC. The temperatures corresponding to the formation of oxide phases are >200oC and >600oC for the uncoated and Cr-coated samples, respectively. SEM and TEM characterisation of the sub-surface in Cr-coated specimen after HT-XRD revealed Fe segregation, formation of Zr(Fe,Cr)2 Laves phase and nano-bubbles at the former Cr / Z4 interface.

### [203] [A Unified microscopic picture of cation and anion migration in MAPbI$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02685)
*Viren Tyagi,Geert Brocks,Shuxia Tao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用基于神经网络势（neural network potentials）的分子动力学模拟，研究了MAPbI₃中由I和MA空位或间隙原子引发的离子迁移，发现多数缺陷在室温下快速扩散，迁移势垒仅0.15–0.20 eV，其中MA间隙原子通过多离子协同机制实现高速迁移，而MA空位迁移未被观测到；结果修正了混合卤化物钙钛矿中离子输运的传统图像，强调了集体分子运动在快速离子迁移中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钝化卤化物钙钛矿（halide perovskites）中的缺陷并限制其迁移率以延长器件寿命已成为主要研究方向，对点缺陷（point defects）的结构与迁移率进行建模是达成上述目标的重要基础。

Method: 采用了基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）数据训练的神经网络势（neural network potentials）驱动的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，对MAPbI₃中由I和MA空位（vacancies）或间隙原子（interstitials）触发的离子迁移过程进行建模。

Result: 多数缺陷种类在室温下快速扩散，迁移势垒在0.15–0.20 eV之间；MA间隙原子尽管本身是分子，却因涉及多个MA离子的协同迁移机制（concerted migration mechanism）而表现出极高的迁移率；未观测到MA空位迁移；I相关缺陷的扩散显著依赖于电荷态（charge state），而MA相关缺陷的扩散则无此依赖。

Conclusion: 这些结果修正了混合钙钛矿（hybrid perovskites）中离子输运的传统图像，并强调了集体分子运动（collective molecular motion）在实现快速离子迁移中的关键作用。

Abstract: Passivating defects and restricting defect mobilities in halide perovskites to increase device lifetimes has become a main field of research. Modeling structure and mobility of point defects is an essential contribution to this endeavor. We employ molecular dynamics, based on neural network potentials trained on density functional theory data, to model ion migration in MAPbI$_3$ triggered by I and MA vacancies or interstitials. Most of these species diffuse rapidly at room temperature, with migration barriers between 0.15 and 0.20 eV. MA interstitials are highly mobile despite their molecular nature, owing to a concerted migration mechanism involving multiple MA ions. No evidence of MA vacancy migration is obtained. Whereas diffusion of I-related defects appreciably depends on their charge state, diffusion of MA defects does not. These results revise the conventional picture of ion transport in hybrid perovskites and highlight the role of collective molecular motion in enabling fast ionic migration.

### [204] [Unified Mapping of Multi-Site Electrocatalytic Activity Using a Single Descriptor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02688)
*A. Dana,D. Terrones,S. Gelin,I. Dabo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通用且精确的映射方法，通过有效吸附自由能描述符和约化描述符映射，将电催化剂活性分析从单站点推广到多站点体系，建立了覆盖-一致火山关系和多峰活性趋势，为复杂合金催化剂的Sabatier分析提供了可解释的筛选框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统单站点描述符无法捕捉多吸附位点体系中不同吸附环境之间的非线性耦合效应，导致对合金催化剂等复杂体系的活性预测存在根本性不足。

Method: 从平均场统计力学（mean-field statistical mechanics）模型出发，引入有效吸附自由能描述符（effective adsorption free energy descriptor），显式纳入横向吸附质-吸附质相互作用（lateral adsorbate-adsorbate interactions），构建覆盖-一致火山关系（coverage-consistent volcano relationships）。进一步将吸附能学和相互作用强度定义为二维活性景观（two-dimensional activity landscape），形成“火山脊”（volcano ridge）。针对多站点体系，提出约化描述符映射（reduced descriptor mapping），将多维活性景观投影到单一有效坐标上，同时保留位点异质性（site heterogeneity）和横向相互作用的物理内涵。

Result: 该方法成功揭示了吸附能学和相互作用强度共同驱动的“火山脊”结构，并证明多站点体系中的非线性耦合导致传统单站点描述符无法表征的多峰活性趋势。约化描述符映射在降维的同时保持了底层物理机制，将Sabatier型分析推广至任意成分复杂度的合金催化剂。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种物理可解释的路径，用于筛选具有任意成分复杂度的电催化材料，系统化了复杂合金催化剂的活性分析。

Abstract: We present a precise and general method to map the activity of electrocatalysts across multiple sites. Starting from a mean-field statistical mechanics model, we introduce an effective adsorption free energy descriptor that explicitly incorporates lateral adsorbate-adsorbate interactions, enabling the construction of coverage-consistent volcano relationships. Extending this approach, we show that adsorption energetics and interaction strength define a two-dimensional activity landscape that gives rise to a "volcano ridge" that captures the coupled influence of binding and interactions on catalytic performance. For multi-site systems, we demonstrate that the inherently nonlinear coupling between distinct adsorption environments leads to multi-peaked activity trends that cannot be represented by conventional single-site descriptors. To address this, we introduce a reduced descriptor mapping that projects the multidimensional activity landscape onto a single effective coordinate while preserving the underlying physics of site heterogeneity and lateral interactions. The resulting framework generalizes Sabatier-type analysis to complex alloy catalysts and provides a physically interpretable route for screening electrocatalytic materials of arbitrary compositional complexity.

### [205] [Structural evolution of Ti/Cu multilayers as a function of period thickness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02788)
*Sergei S. Sakhonenkov,Aidar U. Gaisin,Anita O. Petrova,Vasilii A. Matveev,Elena O. Filatova*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过磁控溅射合成周期厚度为4–52.5 nm的Ti/Cu多层膜，系统研究了周期厚度对形貌、结晶、织构及周期保持性的影响。结果表明，周期厚度通过调控界面过渡区形成、结晶行为和生长诱发的形态不稳定性之间的平衡，决定了多层膜的结构演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Ti/Cu多层膜的周期厚度如何影响其形貌、结晶行为、织构发展以及周期结构的保持性，以理解周期厚度对多层膜结构演变的内在调控机制。

Method: 采用磁控溅射（magnetron sputtering）合成周期厚度为4–52.5 nm的Ti/Cu多层膜，并利用互补的透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy, TEM）技术结合X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction, XRD）和X射线反射测量（X-ray reflectometry, XRR）对结构演变进行分析。

Result: 周期厚度为4 nm时，多层膜的周期对比度显著降低，归因于界面区域扩展、部分Cu-Ti互混以及明确层状结构被抑制。10 nm时多层结构得以保持，但受累积粗糙度和层波纹影响，Cu晶格发生局部修饰。随着周期增大，多层膜趋于规整，Cu以面心立方（fcc）结构为主并出现强Cu(111)织构，Ti则从衬底附近的非晶或弱结晶态向表面附近的有序织构态演变。

Conclusion: Ti/Cu多层膜的周期厚度通过调控界面过渡区、结晶行为与形态不稳定性之间的竞争，直接决定了多层膜的结构质量与演变路径。较小的周期易导致互混和周期性丧失，较大的周期则有利于结晶和织构发展。

Abstract: Ti/Cu multilayers with periods ranging from 4 to 52.5 nm were synthesized by magnetron sputtering to examine how the period thickness affects morphology, crystallization, texture development, and preservation of periodicity. The structural evolution was analyzed using complementary transmission electron microscopy techniques with X-ray diffraction and reflectometry. The results show that the period thickness governs the balance between interfacial transition-region formation, crystallization, and growth-induced morphological instabilities. At the smallest period of 4 nm, the structure has strongly reduced periodic contrast, which may be attributed to extended interfacial regions, partial Cu-Ti intermixing, and suppression of well-defined layer formation. At 10 nm, the multilayer structure is preserved but remains affected by accumulated roughness and layer waviness; local modification of the Cu lattice is suggested to be significant relative to the bilayer period, likely due to mixed Cu-Ti interfacial regions and/or coherent strain. With increasing period, the multilayers become more regular, and the layers show progressive crystallization and texture development during growth. Cu crystallizes predominantly in the fcc structure with a strong Cu(111) contribution, whereas Ti exhibits a more complex structural evolution, from an amorphous or weakly crystallized state near the substrate toward a more ordered and textured state closer to the surface.

### [207] [Coupled Arnol'd cat maps on circulant graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00965)
*Kimon Manolas,Emmanuel Floratos*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了环图（circulant graph）节点上耦合的Arnol'd猫映射（Arnol'd cat maps, ACMs）的混沌性质。通过要求系统演化矩阵是辛的（symplectic），确定了耦合矩阵，并将其自然地解释为环图的邻接矩阵。数值模拟表明，由于环图的平移对称性（translational symmetry），熵产生（entropy production）并不随图连通性（connectivity）的增加而增加，这一结果与直觉相悖。此外，还分析了动力系统有限环形相空间（toroidal phase space）上演化矩阵的周期谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索耦合在环图节点上的Arnol'd猫映射系统的混沌特性，尤其是图拓扑结构如何影响系统的混沌动力学行为。

Method: 基于辛矩阵（symplectic matrix）约束确定耦合矩阵；通过数值模拟计算Lyapunov谱（Lyapunov spectra）和Kolmogorov-Sinai熵（K-S entropy）；在有限环形相空间上分析演化矩阵的周期谱。

Result: 数值模拟发现一个反直觉结果：由于环图的平移对称性，熵产生并不随图连通性的增加而增大。

Conclusion: 环图的平移对称性抑制了耦合ACM系统在高连通性下的混沌熵增长；系统在有限环形相空间上的周期结构也受到图拓扑的显著影响。

Abstract: This paper investigates the chaotic properties of Arnol'd cat maps (ACMs) coupled on the nodes of a circulant graph. By demanding that the system's evolution matrix be symplectic, we determine the coupling matrix, which is naturally interpreted as the adjacency matrix of a circulant graph. Specifically, the study analyses the system's Lyapunov spectra and Kolmogorov-Sinai (K-S) entropy. Numerical simulations yield the counterintuitive result that the entropy production does not increase as the connectivity of the graph increases, due to the translational symmetry of the circulant graph. Moreover, we analyse the spectra of the periods of the evolution matrix on a finite toroidal phase space of the dynamical system.

</details>

### [208] [Formation and Redshift Evolution of Dark Matter Spikes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01023)
*Gonzalo Herrera,Abdelaziz Hussein,Lina Necib,Elliot Y. Davies,Xuejian Shen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一个半解析框架，将暗物质密度尖峰（dark matter density spike）的形成推广至包含有限种子质量、恒星尖峰（stellar cusp）和非圆形轨道，并通过求解耦合的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equations）研究其长期宇宙演化。结果表明，恒星引力加热（stellar gravitational heating）在数吉年内将内坡指数（inner slope）驱动至 γ_χ≃1.5，使尖峰过密度（overdensity）比经典预期低2–4个数量级，但仍高于NFW类尖峰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典暗物质尖峰预测假设零质量种子（zero-mass seed）且仅考虑纯暗物质环境，未追踪周围恒星对尖峰长期动力学的反馈影响。为弥补这一缺陷，需要建立一个更真实的框架以评估间接和直接探测信号的可信度。

Method: 构建半解析框架：首先将绝热尖峰形成（adiabatic spike formation）推广至包含有限种子质量（finite seed masses）、恒星尖峰（stellar cusp）和非圆形轨道（non-circular orbits）；随后通过求解暗物质与恒星相空间分布（phase-space distributions）的耦合Fokker-Planck方程，并结合由宇宙恒星形成率（cosmic star formation rate）调制的加热率（heating rate），研究尖峰的后续宇宙演化。

Result: 保守起始于经典Gondolo-Silk尖峰并对天体物理不确定性做边缘化（marginalization），发现恒星引力加热在数吉年（Gyr）内将内坡指数驱动至γ_χ≃1.5（例如，在红移z≃10处形成的尖峰，至z≲2时即达此状态），导致过密度比经典预期低2–4个数量级，但仍高于NFW类尖峰。论文还提供了与散射、衰变和湮灭信号相关的柱密度（column density）和J因子（J-factor）的红移依赖基准值（redshift-dependent benchmarks）。

Conclusion: 对银河系核区暗物质间接探测信号的任何稳健解读都必须考虑上述演化效应。经典尖峰预测因忽略恒星加热而显著高估信号强度，但修正后的尖峰仍比NFW轮廓提供更强的探测信号。

Abstract: Dark matter density spikes forming around adiabatically growing black holes can dramatically enhance indirect and direct detection signals. Canonical predictions, however, assume a zero-mass seed in a purely dark matter environment and do not track the long-term dynamical impact of surrounding stars. We present a semi-analytic framework that first generalizes adiabatic spike formation to include finite seed masses, stellar cusps, and non-circular orbits, and then studies the subsequent cosmic evolution by solving coupled Fokker-Planck equations for the dark matter and stellar phase-space distributions, with a heating rate modulated by the cosmic star formation rate. Starting conservatively from canonical Gondolo-Silk spikes and marginalizing over astrophysical uncertainties, we find that stellar gravitational heating drives the inner slope towards $γ_χ\simeq 1.5$ within a few Gyrs (e.g by $z \lesssim 2$ for spikes formed at $z\simeq 10$), yielding overdensities two to four orders of magnitude below canonical expectations but still well above an NFW-like cusp. We provide redshift-dependent benchmarks for the column density and $J$-factor relevant to scattering, decay and annihilation signatures. Any robust interpretation of indirect dark matter signals from galactic nuclei must account for this evolution.

</details>


### [209] [Constraints on Ultralight Scalar and Dark Photon Dark Matter from PPTA-DR3 and EPTA-DR2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02172)
*Xiao-Song Hu,Siyuan Chen,Kuo Liu,Xingjiang Zhu,Shi-Yi Zhao,Wu Jiang,John Antoniadis,N. D. Ramesh Bhat,Amodio Carleo,Shi Dai,Valentina Di Marco,Huanchen Hu,Wenhua Ling,Yang Liu,Saurav Mishra,Christopher J Russell,Ryan M. Shannon,Clemente Smarra,Jingbo Wang,Lin Wang,Andrew Zic*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）数据对超轻暗物质（ULDM）进行贝叶斯搜索，未发现显著统计证据，并给出了标量ULDM和暗光子暗物质（DPDM）的95%置信上限约束，其中PPTA-DR3的约束在大部分质量范围内较早期数据显著改善，EPTA数据首次提供了DPDM约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 冷暗物质模型在大尺度上成功描述宇宙，但在亚星系尺度面临挑战。超轻暗物质（ultralight dark matter, ULDM）粒子质量约为10^(-22) eV，是解决小尺度问题的有前景方案。脉冲星计时阵列（Pulsar Timing Array, PTA）不仅能探测纳赫兹引力波，也可作为ULDM信号的灵敏探针。

Method: 采用贝叶斯搜索方法，利用PTA数据集分析两类ULDM信号：标量ULDM引起的振荡引力势（oscillatory gravitational potential），以及暗光子暗物质（dark photon dark matter, DPDM）中介的第五力（fifth-force）相互作用。分析中纳入脉冲星距离信息以更好地建模ULDM密度分布。

Result: 未发现具有统计显著性的ULDM证据，因此在95%置信水平上给出了相关参数的上限。对标量ULDM的分析并未排除其构成全部暗物质的可能性。PPTA-DR3约束在大部分质量范围内较PPTA-DR2（2018 Preview）有显著提升，且与其他PTA的无关限（uncorrelated limits）一致。首次使用EPTA数据给出了DPDM约束，EPTA-DR2和PPTA-DR3获得的DPDM边界与现有约束相当。

Conclusion: 当前PTA数据未探测到ULDM信号，但标量ULDM作为暗物质全部组分的场景仍未被排除。PPTA-DR3提供了改进的约束，EPTA首次给出DPDM约束，结果与已有研究可比。

Abstract: The cold dark matter model successfully describes the Universe on large scales, yet faces challenges at sub-galactic scales. Ultralight dark matter (ULDM), with particle masses around $10^{-22} \mathrm{eV}$, offers a promising solution to these small-scale issues. Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs), designed to detect nanohertz gravitational waves, can also provide a sensitive probe for ULDM signals. In this work, we perform a Bayesian search for ULDM using PTA data sets, focusing on two types of signals: the oscillatory gravitational potential from scalar ULDM and the fifth-force interaction mediated by dark photon dark matter (DPDM). We incorporate pulsar distances in the analysis to better model the ULDM density. No statistically significant evidence for ULDM has been found, therefore we place 95% confidence-level upper limits on the relevant parameters. For scalar ULDM, our analysis does not exclude the scenario in which ULDM constitutes all of dark matter. The constraints from PPTA-DR3 show significant improvements over the earlier PPTA-DR2 (2018 Preview) across most of the mass range, and are consistent with the recent uncorrelated limits from other PTAs. We also present for the first time the DPDM constraints using EPTA data. The obtained bounds on the DPDM from the EPTA-DR2 and PPTA-DR3 are comparable to existing constraints.

</details>


### [210] [Tracing Primordial Gravitational Waves via non-Gaussian Signatures of Halo Bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02882)
*Mariam Abdelaziz,Pritha Bari,Sabino Matarrese,Angelo Ricciardone*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究从理论上推导了原始引力波（PGWs）通过二阶效应诱导的标量密度扰动产生的非高斯性（NG）对暗物质晕大尺度成团性的影响。研究表明，这种张量诱导的非高斯性会在晕偏折（halo bias）中产生显著的尺度依赖修正，对于高红移稀有晕可达O(1)量级，且其信号无法被标准原始非高斯性（PNG）模板捕捉，从而将晕偏折建立为探测原始引力波的新探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始引力波（primordial gravitational waves, PGWs）在二阶微扰下可产生标量密度扰动（scalar density perturbations），该扰动呈非高斯特征。然而，这种张量诱导的非高斯性（tensor-induced non-Gaussianity）在大尺度结构（large-scale structure）中的观测效应尚未被充分研究。本文旨在探索该效应对暗物质晕（dark matter halos）大尺度成团性的影响，并评估其作为原始引力波探测工具的潜力。

Method: 聚焦于具有尖峰原始张量谱（peaked primordial tensor spectrum）的暴胀（inflationary）场景，通过密度场双谱（bispectrum）推导出由张量诱导非高斯性产生的领先阶尺度依赖（scale-dependent）晕偏折（halo bias）修正。该修正源于密度对比度（density contrast）对张量场的二次依赖，其本质是非高斯的（intrinsically non-Gaussian）。

Result: 对于低红移大质量暗物质晕，偏折修正约为百分之一量级（percent-level）；但对于高红移（z=7）的稀有暗物质晕（rare halos），该修正可达O(1)量级。该信号的尺度依赖特征与标准原始非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity, PNG）模板所描述的模式显著不同。

Conclusion: 晕偏折（halo bias）可作为一种新颖的原始引力波（PGWs）探针，通过对大尺度结构（large-scale structure）的观测为暴胀时期（inflationary epoch）提供互补的探测窗口。该效应无法被现有的标准非高斯性模板所涵盖，因此具有独立的观测价值。

Abstract: Primordial gravitational waves (PGWs) generate scalar density perturbations at second order. Since the induced density contrast is quadratic in the tensor field, it is intrinsically non-Gaussian. We study the imprint of this tensor-induced non-Gaussianity (NG) on the large-scale clustering of dark matter halos through its correction to halo bias. Focusing on inflationary scenarios with a peaked primordial tensor spectrum, we derive the leading scale-dependent contribution sourced by the bispectrum of the induced density field. While yielding a percent-level bias correction for massive low-redshift halos, this effect can reach an $\mathcal{O}(1)$ modulation for rare, high-redshift halos at $z=7$. Notably, the resulting signature exhibits a distinct scale dependence that is not captured by standard primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG) templates. Our results establish halo bias as a novel probe of PGWs through their imprint on the large-scale structure, providing a complementary window into the inflationary epoch.

</details>

### [211] [Two-Photon-Induced Direct 3D Printing of Freeform High-Index Phase-Change Sb2S3 Nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01054)
*Abhrodeep Dey,Andrea Dellith,Anne Sauer,Uwe Hübner,Henrik Schneidewind,Markus A Schmidt,Astrid Bingel,Volker Deckert,Jer-Shing Huang,Wei Wang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于溶液相双光子诱导固化的硫属化物相变材料（PCM）直接三维打印方法，能够快速、无掩模、低成本地制造具有亚微米分辨率的自由形状光子器件，实现了高折射率超表面（metasurface）的快速原型设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硫属化物相变材料（chalcogenide PCM）因超高折射率（refractive index, RI）和可见-近红外波段低光损耗而成为纳米光子学（nanophotonics）的重要材料，但当前基于二维薄膜图案化的方法限制了三维自由形状微纳结构的快速原型制造，从而制约了几何设计自由度和器件功能。

Method: 开发了一种基于双光子诱导固化的直接打印方法（dip in two photon-induced solidification, DITPS），使用特制的三硫化二锑（Sb₂S₃）前驱体溶液，通过溶液相直接打印将硫属化物PCM成型为功能结构。

Result: 成功在金和ITO基底上直接打印出具有不同线截面轮廓的Sb₂S₃螺旋结构，以及单步打印的平面菲涅尔波带片（Fresnel zone plate, FZP）和计算生成全息超表面（computer generated hologram metasurface, CGHM）。

Conclusion: 该DITPS自由形状打印方法实现了高折射率超表面的快速三维原型制造，并为将高折射率相变材料集成到现有光子架构与器件平台中开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Chalcogenides have recently emerged as an important class of phase-change materials (PCMs) for nanophotonics, owing to their very high refractive index (RI) and low optical loss in the visible to near-infrared range. They exhibit an ultralarge RI change (> 0.7) upon phase transition, which can be triggered by multiple stimuli such as electrical bias, laser illumination or thermal heating. These properties make them highly appealing materials for flat optics and metasurface applications. Current nanophotonic implementations of chalcogenide PCMs mostly rely on two-dimensional (2D) or quasi three-dimensional (3D) thin film patterning based on the coating of chalcogenide materials from a solid-state target. This limits fast prototyping of 3D freeform micro- and nanostructures, thus restricting geometric design freedom and device functionality. Here, we demonstrate a solution-phase direct printing of chalcogenide PCMs into functional structures. The method is based on dip in two photon-induced solidification (DITPS) of a specially synthesized antimony trisulfide (Sb2S3) precursor solution. Direct printing with DITPS is simple, maskless, fast and cost effective, enabling true freeform 3D printing of photonic devices with sub micron resolution. We show direct writing of Sb2S3 helices with different wire cross section profiles on gold and ITO substrates, as well as functional planar Fresnel zone plates (FZPs) and computer generated hologram metasurfaces (CGHMs) in a single printing step. This freeform DITPS approach thus enables rapid 3D prototyping of high index metasurfaces and opens a route to integrating high-index PCMs into existing photonic architectures and device platforms.

</details>


### [212] [Strong light-matter interactions in hybrid polaritonic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01583)
*Ben Johns,Andrea Schirato,Federico Toffoletti,Tommaso Giovannini,Mirko Vanzan,Margherita Marsili,Giovanni Parolin,Giulia Dall'Osto,Ajay Kumar Poonia,Chiara Cappelli,Francesca Baletto,Stefano Corni,Elisabetta Collini,Margherita Maiuri,Nicolò Maccaferri*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文综述了强光-物质耦合产生的极化激元（polaritons）现象，系统介绍了支撑极化激元形成的多种光腔架构（如光子微腔、等离激元纳米结构、开放腔和超表面），讨论了无机半导体、有机聚集体和杂化体系在强耦合与超强耦合下的关键物理现象（相干动力学、振动耦合、暗态库、极化激元介导的能量与电子传输），并展示了强耦合对电荷传输、能量流和化学反应活性的调控作用，最后总结了中间耦合和暗-强耦合等新兴研究前沿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强光-物质耦合能够产生兼具光子和物质特性的极化激元（polaritons），为调控光学、电学和化学性质提供了全新途径。本文旨在系统梳理支撑极化激元形成的主要架构与材料体系，归纳关键物理现象与研究方法，并展示强耦合在电荷传输、能量流和化学反应中的调控能力，从而为该领域的发展提供全景式综述。

Result: 研究发现强耦合能够显著调控电荷传输（charge transport）、能量流（energy flow）和化学反应性（chemical reactivity）。此外，中间耦合（intermediate coupling）和暗-强耦合（dark-strong coupling）等新兴机制进一步拓展了杂化光-物质物理学（hybrid light-matter physics）的研究版图。

Conclusion: 强光-物质耦合为操控材料的光学、电学和化学性质提供了丰富的物理图景。随着中间耦合、暗-强耦合等新机制的出现，杂化光-物质物理学的研究边界将进一步拓宽，有望在量子光学、能源转化和分子催化等领域催生新的应用。

Abstract: Strong light-matter coupling gives rise to polaritons - hybrid excitations whose mixed photonic and matter character enables control over optical, electronic and chemical properties. This Feature Article surveys the main architectures supporting polariton formation, including photonic microcavities, plasmonic nanostructures, open cavities and metasurfaces, and outlines how inorganic semiconductors, organic aggregates and hybrid systems access strong and ultrastrong coupling. Key phenomena such as coherent dynamics, vibronic interactions, dark-state reservoirs and polariton-mediated energy and electron transport are discussed, together with the experimental and theoretical tools used to study them. We highlight examples where strong coupling modifies charge transport, energy flow and chemical reactivity, and we summarize emerging regimes, including intermediate and dark-strong coupling, that broaden the landscape of hybrid light-matter physics.
