### [213] [Excited states engineering maximizes singlet generation by triplet fusion in conjugated systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01998)
*Alessandra Ronchi,Masashi Mamada,Michel Frigoli,Angelo Monguzzi*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通用分子设计策略，通过选择性取代调控萘衍生物湮灭剂的激发态能级结构，使其强烈倾向于单重态形成，从而最大化三重态-三重态湮灭（TTA）单重态生成产率（达0.83）。与合适的三线态敏化剂结合后，该系统在非相干宽带激发下实现了390 nm处的稳定紫外/可见光上转换，绝对上转换产率约0.19，激活激发强度阈值低于0.1倍太阳光，满足太阳能技术需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光子上转换（photon upconversion）在成像、防伪、信息加密及太阳能技术中有重要应用，其中基于敏化三重态-三重态湮灭（sensitized triplet-triplet annihilation, sTTA-UC）的机制因可在低强度非相干光下工作而尤为突出。然而，如何有效提高sTTA-UC中单重态生成产率仍是关键挑战。

Method: 采用选择性取代（selective substitution）策略，设计了一种萘衍生物湮灭剂（annihilator），通过调控其激发态能级结构（excited state energy landscape）使其强烈倾向于单重态形成（singlet formation），从而最大化三重态-三重态湮灭（TTA）过程产生的单重态产率。

Result: 工程化湮灭剂的TTA单重态生成产率达0.83；结合合适的三线态敏化剂（triplet sensitizer）后，系统在非相干宽带激发下实现390 nm处稳定的紫外/可见光上转换，绝对上转换产率（absolute upconversion yield）约0.19，激活激发强度阈值（activation excitation intensity threshold）低于0.1倍太阳光。

Conclusion: 该分子设计策略显著提升了TTA单重态生成效率，所得上转换系统的性能指标（低激发阈值、高上转换产率）完全满足太阳能驱动技术的应用要求，为设计高效上转换材料提供了通用路径。

Abstract: Photon upconverters are anti Stokes emitters capable of generating photons with higher energy than those absorbed. This behavior can be achieved through different mechanisms, which are extensively studied for applications in imaging, anticounterfeiting, information encryption and most importantly, solar energy technologies. Among these mechanisms, photon upconversion based on sensitized triplet-triplet annihilation (sTTA-UC) is particularly attractive because it operates under low intensity, incoherent light. In sTTA UC, two optically dark triplet states of a conjugated annihilator fuse upon collision to populate a higher energy fluorescent singlet, with the triplets initially generated via energy transfer from a lower energy sensitizer.
  Here we introduce a general molecular design strategy to maximize singlet generation through TTA. By selective substitution, we engineered a naphthalene derived annihilator with an excited state energy landscape that strongly favors singlet formation, achieving yields up to 0.83. When combined with an appropriate triplet sensitizer, the system delivers stable UV/visible upconversion peaking at 390 nm, with an absolute upconversion yield about 0.19 and an activation excitation intensity threshold lower than 0.1 suns under non-coherent broadband excitation fully compatible with the requirements of solar powered technologies.

</details>


### [214] [Effects of interface regularity on the bulk-edge correspondence in continuum photonic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02100)
*Matthew Frazier,Guillaume Bal*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文研究连续光子系统中横向磁波在有限宽度界面上的拓扑不变量与边缘态，发现磁场偏置的连续变化使体边对应关系（BEC）稳定成立，而磁场偏置的不连续性则引入高度局域化的边缘模，需定义新的反常体边对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究几乎只考虑两种电磁介质间的尖锐界面（sharp transition），本文旨在探索更一般的几何情形——磁场偏置（magnetic field bias）在有限宽度界面内任意变化时，连续光子系统的拓扑性质与边缘态行为。

Method: 对两种不同偏置旋磁材料（gyrotropic materials）间的有限宽度界面中横向磁波（transverse magnetic wave）传播进行分析，分别考察磁场偏置连续变化与存在间断（discontinuity）两种情形下的拓扑不变量（topological invariants）及边缘态（edge states）。

Result: 当磁场偏置在体区域间连续变化时，定义明确的陈不变量（Chern invariants）使体边对应关系（Bulk Edge Correspondence, BEC）稳健成立；而磁场偏置的不连续性会引入高度局域化于间断处的边缘模，其谱性质改变了BEC。

Conclusion: 分析了上述边缘模的谱性质，定义了包含拓扑不变量与磁场偏置间断贡献的连续光子系统中新的反常体边对应关系（anomalous BEC）。

Abstract: In this study we analyze the topological invariants and edge states of transverse magnetic wave propagation in continuum photonic systems at a finite-width interface between two gyrotropic matrials with different magnetic bias. Where previous studies have almost exclusively considered sharp transitions between two different electromagnetic media, we consider the more general geometry where the magnetic field bias is allowed to vary arbitrarily in a finite-width interface between to bulk regions. We find that when the magnetic field bias varies continuously between the two bulk regions, the Bulk Edge Correspondence (BEC) holds robustly with respect to well-defined Chern invariants. However, discontinuities in the magnetic field bias introduce edge modes which are highly localized at the associated discontinuity and whose spectral properties alter the BEC. We analyze the spectral properties of these edge modes and define a new anomalous BEC in continuum photonic systems which includes contributions from topological invariants and discontinuities in magnetic field bias.

</details>


### [215] [The infinitesimal environmental dust as a photonic bath at infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02265)
*Gaomin Tang,Yuhua Ren,Jian-Sheng Wang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文将远场热辐射中的环境“尘埃”模型映射为无穷远处的光子热浴（photonic bath at infinity），在非平衡光子格林函数（nonequilibrium photonic Green's function）形式体系下严格求解了空间积分，发现尘埃贡献可简化为局域自能（local self-energy），并证明该热浴等效于黑体（black body）。该框架为远场热辐射提供了简洁的分析与数值计算工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远场热辐射（far-field thermal radiation）中，物体辐射的电磁波传播至无穷远，需要将远区建模为有效热浴。早期工作提出用无穷小环境“尘埃（dust）”来刻画这一热浴，但涉及无穷大空间的积分难以解析或数值求解。因此，亟需一种更简洁且计算可行的形式化方案。

Method: 在非平衡光子格林函数（nonequilibrium photonic Green's function）框架下，将环境尘埃映射为无穷远处的光子热浴；通过显式计算尘埃的空间积分，将其贡献简化为局域自能（local self-energy），并推导出三维物体与平面系统对应的解析表达式；同时在附录B中基于表面格林函数（surface Green's function）框架提供了替代推导，以验证理论自洽性。

Result: 尘埃的空间积分被显式计算后，其贡献简化为一个简单的局域自能；该光子热浴展现出黑体（black body）特性，并在远场热辐射中的作用得到阐明。对于三维物体和平面系统，分别给出了局域自能的解析表达式。

Conclusion: 无穷远处光子热浴的引入为远场热辐射提供了一个便捷的分析与数值计算框架；附录中的表面格林函数推导进一步证明了该结果的的理论自洽性，且无需依赖尘埃模型。

Abstract: In far-field thermal radiation, electromagnetic waves emitted by an object propagate to infinity, requiring the far region to be modeled as an effective thermal bath. This bath was proposed as infinitesimal environmental "dust", but explicit calculations with such distributed dust involve integrals over infinite space that are difficult to evaluate. In this work, we map this environmental dust to a photonic bath at infinity within the nonequilibrium photonic Green's function formalism. By explicitly evaluating the spatial integral over the dust, we show that its contribution reduces to a simple local self-energy, for which we derive analytical expressions for both three-dimensional objects and planar systems. We further demonstrate that the bath behaves as a black body and clarify its role in far-field thermal radiation. An alternative derivation based on the surface Green's function framework is also provided in Appendix B, demonstrating the theoretical consistency of the results without invoking the dust model. The photonic bath at infinity provides a convenient framework for both analytical and numerical calculations in far-field thermal radiation.

### [216] [Free-standing circular Bragg gratings enabling efficient GaAs quantum dot entangled photon pair sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02360)
*Sai Abhishikth Dhurjati,Moritz Langer,Yared G. Zena,Ahmad Rahimi,Liesa Raith,Martin Bauer,Frank H. P. Fitzek,Riccardo Bassoli,Caspar Hopfmann*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于砷化镓（GaAs）单量子点（quantum dot）的自支撑环形布拉格光栅（circular Bragg grating, CBG）腔体，通过单步干法刻蚀实现方向性发射，无需底部反射镜或多层加工；实验测得光致发光增强达700倍，激子精细结构分裂（fine-structure splitting）从7.3 μeV降至1.3 μeV，为可扩展的明亮纠缠光子对源提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定性量子光源（deterministic quantum light source）是量子通信网络的关键组件；现有圆环形布拉格光栅（CBG）结构依赖多层工艺或倒装键合（flip-chip bonding），引入有害应变并限制可扩展性，亟需一种简化制备、低应变的单片（monolithic）方案。

Method: 采用单步自上而下（top-down）刻蚀工艺，利用深宽比依赖刻蚀（aspect-ratio-dependent etching, ARDE）实现垂直结构不对称性，从而在不设底部反射镜的条件下获得方向性发射；同时通过有限时域差分（finite-difference time-domain, FDTD）模拟优化腔体几何参数。

Result: FDTD模拟预测自由空间提取效率达68%，耦合至透镜单模光纤（NA=0.6）的效率为40%。实验显示确定性格点耦合的QD-CBG器件光致发光（photoluminescence）强度较未处理平面量子点增强700倍，积分计数率达45 MHz。激子精细结构分裂从7.3 μeV降至1.3 μeV，平均相干时间为70 ps。

Conclusion: 自支撑GaAs CBG平台结合了优化的FDTD设计、精准纳米加工与稳健的光学性能，是一种高度可扩展的明亮、相干纠缠光子对源方案。

Abstract: Deterministic and bright quantum light sources based on scalable semiconductor technologies are a crucial building block for future quantum communication networks. While circular Bragg gratings (CBGs) are highly effective for extracting light from solid-state quantum emitters, conventional architectures rely on complex multi-layer processing or flip-chip bonding, which introduce detrimental strain and limit scalability. Here, we present a fabrication-minimal approach to realize monolithic, free-standing CBG cavities with deterministically positioned single GaAs quantum dots (QDs). By utilizing aspect-ratio-dependent etching (ARDE) in a single-step top-down process, we achieve the necessary vertical structural asymmetry for directional emission without requiring bottom reflectors. Finite-difference time-domain (FDTD) simulations validate this geometry, predicting free-space extraction efficiencies up to $68 \, \%$ and coupling efficiencies of $40 \, \%$ into a lensed single-mode fiber ($\text{NA} = 0.6$). Experimentally, the deterministically coupled QD-CBG devices yield a photoluminescence intensity enhancement of up to $\times 700$ compared to unprocessed planar QDs, reaching integrated count rates of $45 \, MHz$. Furthermore, the suspended membrane architecture effectively relaxes residual strain, significantly reducing the average exciton fine-structure splitting from $7.3 \, μeV$ in planar QDs to $1.3 \, μeV$ in the CBGs. Interferometric measurements confirm that the fabrication process preserves the optical quality of the emitters, with average coherence times of $70 \, ps$. By bridging optimized FDTD design with precise nanofabrication and robust optical performance, these results establish free-standing GaAs CBGs as a highly scalable platform for bright and coherent entangled photon pair sources.

### [217] [Frequency locking in lasing ZnO nanowire pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02445)
*Ann-Kathrin Kollak,Lukas R. Jäger,Hark Hoe Tan,Carsten Ronning*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文首次在亚10纳米间隙的ZnO纳米线激光器对中实现了光学耦合与频率锁定（frequency locking），观察到全锁定与部分锁定现象，并发现耦合对多模激射的抑制效应，表明该机制是动态而非静态的，为纳米级可调控光源提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管频率锁定在宏观激光系统中已被广泛用于稳定和调控相干发射，但其在纳米尺度下的实现与适用性尚属未知，亟需探索。

Method: 实验上采用间距小于10纳米的ZnO纳米线激光器对，通过空间调控光学激发（optical excitation），在极端近场（extreme near field）条件下观察耦合与频率锁定行为。

Result: 观察到全锁定与部分锁定两种频率锁定模式；在耦合纳米线对中实现了单模激射（single-mode lasing），抑制了独立纳米线的多模激射（multi-mode lasing）；揭示了锁定行为是动态建立的，而非基于如游标效应（Vernier effect）等静态滤波机制。

Conclusion: 频率锁定是纳米线激光器中一种鲁棒且可调的机制，为集成纳米光子系统中稳定可控的纳米级光源开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Frequency locking between coupled laser systems provides a powerful mechanism for stabilizing and controlling coherent emission, yet its implementation and applicability down to the nanoscale remains unknown and unexplored. Here, we demonstrate optical coupling and frequency locking in closely spaced ZnO nanowire lasers operating in the extreme near field (gap < 10 nm). We observe both full and partial frequency locking, manifested as the alignment of all or a subset of the lasing modes, by spatially controlling the optical excitation. We also observe single-mode lasing in a coupled nanowire pair where the multi-mode lasing of individual nanowires is suppressed. In contrast to previously reported coupled-cavity nanowire lasers, where spectral control arises from static filtering mechanisms such as the Vernier effect, our results indicate a dynamically established relationship between actively lasing nanowires. These findings establish frequency locking as a robust and tunable mechanism in nanowire lasers, opening new routes toward stabilized and controllable nanoscale light sources for integrated nanophotonic systems.

### [218] [Strong enhancement of Er3+ emission at room temperature in Si3N4 metasurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02535)
*Fengkai Wei,Xinru Ji,Tobias J. Kippenberg,Duk-Yong Choi,Carsten Ronning*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文报道了通过离子注入法制备的三价铒掺杂氮化硅超表面在通信波长处实现了室温光致发光的显著增强，最大增强因子约为18，寿命缩短近十倍，主要归因于Purcell效应，并提供了一条与CMOS工艺兼容的有源光源集成路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现高效、CMOS兼容的有源光源是光子集成电路的关键挑战之一。稀土离子（如Er3+）在通信波段（约1.5 μm）的光致发光效率受限于其本征辐射速率慢和低吸收截面，因此需要借助纳米光子结构增强局域光学态密度（local density of optical states, LDOS）。

Method: 采用离子注入（ion implantation）方法将三价铒（Er3+）掺入氮化硅（Si3N4）超表面（metasurface），该超表面由周期排列的纳米圆柱（nanocylinder）阵列构成，设计支持米氏共振（Mie-type resonance），以调控光学态密度。通过优化纳米圆柱半径并在热退火后测量光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）增强因子，并结合时域分辨PL测量以及不同离子注入深度的对比实验，验证增强机制。

Result: 在纳米圆柱半径390 nm时，PL增强因子达到约18，与仿真结果高度吻合。时间分辨PL测量显示发光寿命缩短了近十倍，证实增强主要源于Purcell效应（Purcell effect）。此外，Er3+离子注入深度从20 nm增至80 nm时，发光强度提高了四倍，表明发射强度对注入深度有强烈依赖。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种通过超表面共振和离子注入深度调控实现高效PL增强的鲁棒方法，为在CMOS兼容平台中集成高效有源光源提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We report a significant enhancement of room-temperature photoluminescence from trivalent erbium-doped (Er3+) silicon nitride (Si3N4) metasurfaces at the telecommunication wavelength prepared via ion implantation. The metasurfaces, consisting of periodic nanocylinder arrays, are designed to support Mie-type resonances that tailor the local density of optical states. By systematically optimizing the nanocylinder radii, we achieve a photoluminescence (PL) enhancement factor of ~18 at a radius of 390 nm after thermal annealing, which is in excellent agreement with our simulations. Time-resolved PL measurements reveal a nearly ten-fold reduction in luminescence lifetime, confirming that the enhancement is primarily driven by the Purcell effect. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the PL intensity is strongly dependent on the Er3+ ion implantation depth, with a four-fold increase in emission observed from 20 nm to 80 nm ion range. These results provide a robust pathway for integrating efficient, active light sources into CMOS-compatible photonic device.

### [219] [Self-acceleration of Hardening Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00976)
*Giovanni Maria Tomaselli,Thomas F. M. Spieksma*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文发现，沉浸在轻粒子背景中的开普勒双星系统，其长期演化动力学远比传统两参数模型（硬化率与偏心率增长率）丰富：介质会对双星质心施加净力、诱发近点进动、旋转轨道平面，且这些确定性效应在均匀各向同性介质中仍然存在——双星自身不对称性提供了推进力。自加速、进动与动力学摩擦的耦合驱动质心沿外螺旋运动。对于超大质量黑洞双星，该位移主导布朗运动并接近影响半径，暗示其可能显著偏离宿主星系中心，并影响最终秒差距问题。此外，此前文献报道的小质量比双星圆化效应是截断长寿命遭遇的数值伪影，所有双星实际上均经历偏心率增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，双星在轻粒子背景中的硬化过程仅用两个参数（硬化率和偏心率增长率）描述，如星系合并后超大质量黑洞双星的演化。本文旨在揭示该过程中被忽略的丰富长期动力学行为，包括质心自加速、进动和轨道平面旋转等效应。

Method: 结合对称性论证与广泛的三体散射实验（three-body scattering experiments），对嵌入轻粒子背景中的开普勒双星（Keplerian binary）系统进行动力学分析。

Result: 发现介质对双星质心施加净力、诱发近点进动（apsidal precession），并在质心速度存在面外分量时旋转轨道平面。这些效应在均匀各向同性介质中仍然存在。自加速、进动与动力学摩擦（dynamical friction）的耦合驱动质心沿外螺旋运动。对于超大质量黑洞双星，该位移主导布朗运动并接近影响半径。所有双星经历偏心率（eccentricity）增长，此前报道的小质量比双星圆化是截断长寿命遭遇的数值伪影。

Conclusion: 该结果丰富了双星硬化的标准图像，对多个天体物理场景有重要意义，包括引力波源种群和超大质量黑洞双星的最终秒差距问题（final-parsec problem）。双星可能显著偏离宿主星系中心，且位移会扩大恒星损失锥（loss cone）。

Abstract: A Keplerian binary immersed in a bath of lighter particles hardens by ejecting them through gravitational slingshots. This process drives, for example, the evolution of supermassive black hole binaries following galaxy mergers, and has long been described with just two parameters: the hardening rate and the eccentricity growth rate. Here we show that the secular dynamics is substantially richer. Combining symmetry arguments with extensive three-body scattering experiments, we demonstrate that the medium exerts a net force on the binary's center of mass (CoM), induces apsidal precession, and rotates the orbital plane when the CoM velocity has an out-of-plane component. Remarkably, these deterministic effects persist even in a perfectly uniform and isotropic medium, as the binary's own asymmetry provides the propulsion. The interplay of self-acceleration, precession, and dynamical friction drives the CoM along an outward spiral. For supermassive black hole binaries, this displacement dominates over Brownian motion and approaches the radius of influence, suggesting they may be significantly offset from their host galaxies' centers. The displacement also enlarges the stellar loss cone, with direct implications for the final-parsec problem. We further show that the previously reported circularization of small-mass-ratio binaries is a numerical artifact of truncating long-lived encounters: all binaries undergo eccentricity growth. Our results enrich the standard picture of binary hardening and have implications in a variety of astrophysical contexts, including gravitational-wave source populations.

### [220] [Emergent population dynamics of random walkers with cooperative reproduction and spatial selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01770)
*Ohad Vilk,Baruch Meerson*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文将N支分支布朗运动（branching Brownian motion）模型扩展至高阶无性繁殖（higher-order asexual reproduction），发现繁殖阶数的增加会导致入侵前沿（invasion fronts）发生根本性变化：超越二元繁殖（binary reproduction）后前沿消失，二元情形下速度与扩散无关，三元繁殖（ternary reproduction）则展现临界行为（critical behavior），包括超临界态（supercritical regime）的局域化“入侵子弹”（invasion bullet）、次临界态（subcritical regime）的扩散传播及临界态（criticality）的前沿连续族。结果表明，自然界中分裂与二元繁殖的普遍性反映了入侵动力学的根本约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展标准N支分支布朗运动模型至更高阶无性繁殖，以探究繁殖阶数如何改变种群入侵前沿的动力学行为，并解释自然界中为何二元分裂繁殖占主导地位。

Method: 将分支布朗运动模型中的二元分支（binary branching）推广至一般性高阶无性繁殖（higher-order reproduction），通过理论分析不同繁殖阶数下入侵前沿的传播速度与空间分布特征，并对三元繁殖情形进行临界标度（critical scaling）分析。

Result: 随着繁殖阶数增大，入侵前沿出现质变：二元以上繁殖无法维持典型前沿结构；二元繁殖的前沿速度与扩散系数无关；三元繁殖呈现临界行为——超临界态形成强局域化的“入侵子弹”，次临界态表现为普通扩散，临界态则存在连续的前沿解族。

Conclusion: 自然界中分裂（division）与二元繁殖的广泛存在，并非偶然，而是源于高阶繁殖在入侵动力学上所受的根本性约束，即高阶繁殖无法支持稳定的传播前沿。

Abstract: We extend the $N$ branching Brownian motions model of population invasion to higher-order asexual reproduction. Increasing reproduction order leads to qualitative changes: invasion fronts generically cease to exist beyond binary reproduction; and in the binary case itself, their speed becomes diffusion-independent. Ternary reproduction shows critical behavior, with collapse into a strongly localized `invasion bullet' in the supercritical regime, diffusive spreading in the subcritical regime, and a continuous family of fronts at criticality. These results suggest that the dominance of division and binary reproduction in nature reflects fundamental constraints on invasion dynamics.

### [221] [Scattering matrix elements and energy spectrum of one-dimensional hybrid PT-symmetric finite systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00919)
*Vladimir Gasparian,Esther Jódar,Antonio Pérez-Garrido*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用特征行列式方法（characteristic determinant approach），完整描述了一维PT对称（PT-symmetric）混合有限系统中的散射矩阵元（scattering matrix elements）和电子能谱（electron energy spectrum）。作者得到了能谱的闭式解析表达式，并给出了在特定条件下谱奇点（spectral singularities）的解析形式，以及刚性晶格置于有限盒子中模型的量子化条件（quantization condition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对PT对称系统（PT-symmetric systems）的散射性质已有广泛关注，但在一维混合有限系统中，散射矩阵元和能谱的完整解析描述仍然缺乏。作者旨在利用特征行列式方法填补这一空白，提供从解析闭式到谱奇点和量子化条件的统一刻画。

Method: 采用特征行列式方法（characteristic determinant approach）对一维PT对称混合有限系统进行解析建模。系统构型为中间区域为实势（被动区，passive region），左右两侧分别为增益（gain）和损耗（loss）区域。通过解析推导获得能谱的闭式表达式，并在特定复数势实部与虚部比例条件下，导出谱奇点的解析形式。同一方法框架下还推导了刚性晶格置于有限盒子模型中的量子化条件。

Result: 获得了系统能谱的闭式解析表达式（closed-form expression）。在特定条件及复数势实部与虚部的特定比例下，找到了谱奇点的解析表达式，此时混合结构中的散射矩阵元在特定实能量处趋于无穷大。此外，得到了有限盒子中刚性晶格模型的量子化条件的紧凑解析表达式。

Conclusion: 特征行列式方法能够有效地统一描述一维PT对称混合有限系统中的散射矩阵元和能谱，并给出谱奇点和量子化条件的解析形式，为理解此类非厄米（non-Hermitian）系统中的谱性质提供了完整的理论基础。

Abstract: In this work, we provide a complete description of the scattering matrix elements and electron energy spectrum in one dimensional PT-symmetric hybrid finite systems, using the characteristic determinant approach. We present an analytical formulation of the problem and obtain a closed-form expression for the energy spectrum of the system, consisting of a region of real potential (passive region) surrounded by regions of gain and loss on the left and right, respectively. It has been shown that under certain conditions and a specific ratio between the real and imaginary parts of the complex potentials, it is possible to find analytical expressions for the spectral singularities at which the scattering matrix elements of the hybrid structure tend to infinity at a specific real energy. Within the framework of the same approach, we present a compact analytical expression for the quantization condition that determines the energy spectrum of a model corresponding to the placement of a rigid lattice within a finite-sized box.

### [222] [Non-Equilibrium Thermodynamic Extremal Principles During Filament Formation in ECM Memristors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01087)
*Justin Brutger,Xiao Shen*

Conclusion: 金属细丝形貌的形成受非平衡热力学极值原理驱动，具体表现为熵产生与能量耗散率的最小化，这为理解ECM忆阻器的开关机制提供了新的理论视角。

While the performance characteristics of these devices are widely investigated, the driving principles behind the morphology of the filament formation process remain unclear. ### [223] [Topological flat bands emerging at the inversion of stacking order in rhombohedral graphite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01115)

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算，研究了天然石墨中菱方相富集区域附近多种堆叠构型的能带结构，发现两种不同菱方序（rhombohedral ordering）界面处会在布里渊区K和K'点附近出现拓扑起源的平带（flat bands），并通过将紧束缚模型映射到Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链解释了其物理机制。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究组合两种石墨结构及修改菱方序列的多种堆叠构型；同时构建垂直于石墨烯层方向的菱方板条（rhombohedral slab）的简单紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），并将其映射到Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）链上进行理论分析。

Result: 当两种不同的菱方序（如ABCABC...与CBACBA...）结合时，在两种畴（domain）之间的界面附近、布里渊区（Brillouin zone）的K和K'点处，出现了具有拓扑起源的平带（flat bands）。

Conclusion: 菱方序界面上拓扑起源的平带可能是相关体系中高温超导现象的关键电子结构特征，而SSH链映射为理解该物理机制提供了清晰的理论框架。

Abstract: Motivated by the indications of high-Tc superconductivity in natural graphite enriched in the rhombohedral phase, we study the band structure of several stacking configurations that combine two of the three graphite structures as well as modifications of the rhombohedral sequence (from ABCABC... to CBACBA...), using first-principles calculations. We focus in particular on the possible emergence of flat bands near the Fermi level. When the two different rhombohedral orderings are combined, flat bands of topological origin emerge at the interface between the two domains, near the K and K' points of the Brillouin zone. Mapping a simple tight-binding model of a rhombohedral slab along the direction perpendicular to the graphene layers onto a Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain provides a transparent understanding of the underlying physics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子干涉效应对单分子磁体晶体管中电流输运的影响机制，特别是贝里相位干涉导致的电流完全阻断现象。

Method: 采用密度矩阵方法（density matrix approach），结合微扰理论（perturbation theory）处理自旋在不同路径间隧穿引起的基态能级分裂；构建描述贝里相位干涉的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），并利用开源Python软件QmeQ进行数值模拟。

Result: 横向磁场（transverse magnetic field）控制的贝里相位干涉能够在单分子磁体置于相反极化（oppositely polarized）电极之间时完全阻断电流流动；数值模拟结果与解析结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: 基于有效哈密顿量的理论框架可以准确描述贝里相位干涉对电流的阻断效应，为量子干涉在单分子磁体器件中的调控提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this paper we theoretically and numerically investigate transport signatures of quantum interference on the current through a single molecule magnet transistor tunnel coupled to oppositely polarized leads in the presence of a local transverse and longitudinal magnetic field. Our calculations are based in a density matrix approach where we treat the ground state energy splitting induced by tunneling of the spin between different paths with the aid of perturbation theory. Using this approach we show that it is possible to use an effective Hamiltonian which describes the Berry phase interference as a function of the transverse magnetic field which completely blocks the current flow when we place the single molecule magnet between oppositely polarized leads. Finally, we use this effective Hamiltonian in an open source Python software (QmeQ) that allows us to calculate the current through the single molecule magnet with oppositely polarized leads tunnel coupled to the single molecule magnet. The analytical results are well reproduced by our numerical simulations.

### [225] [Tracking thermal transport in colloidal quantum dot films using in-situ time-resolved X-ray diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01141)

TL;DR: 本研究利用时间分辨X射线衍射（time-resolved X-ray diffraction）作为一种非接触式方法，直接探测了在类器件环境中胶体量子点（colloidal quantum dots）的加热与冷却过程，并测量了量子点薄膜的热导率（~0.55 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹）及液相中量子点的界面热导（~15 MW m⁻² K⁻¹），为热管理策略提供了原位实验依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用时间分辨X射线衍射（time-resolved X-ray diffraction）作为非接触式方法，通过提取亚纳秒时间尺度下的德拜-沃勒因子（Debye-Waller Factors），直接捕捉脉冲光激发后核/壳结构CdSe/CdS量子点的加热与冷却过程。

Conclusion: 时间分辨X射线衍射可用于在类器件环境中非接触式地表征量子点的热响应，为未来热管理策略（thermal management strategies）提供原位实验洞察。

Abstract: Colloidal quantum dots (QDs) and their thin-films are increasingly used in electronic and photonic devices replacing traditional bulk semiconductors. However, thermal properties of the QDs are comparatively underexplored relative to device development efforts. This study shows the use of time-resolved X-ray diffraction as a contact-free method to probe the thermal response of QDs in device-like environments, providing in-situ insights for future thermal management strategies. Through the extraction of Debye-Waller Factors on a sub-nanosecond timescale, we use time-resolved X-ray diffraction to directly capture the heating and cooling of core/shell CdSe/CdS QDs following pulsed optical excitation. In a QD thin-film that actively provides optical gain, the thermal conductivity is found to be as low as 0.55 $\mathrm{W\,m^{-1}\,K^{-1}}$, because of the poor heat flow within close-packed QD solids. For QDs dispersed in liquids, interfacial thermal conductance is found to dominate the thermal relaxation with a conductance on the order of 15 $\mathrm{MW\,m^{-2}\,K^{-1}}$.

### [226] [Phase-shift instanton approach to tunneling duality in Read--Rezayi state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01206)
*Ryoi Ohashi,Hiroki Isobe,Ryota Nakai,Kentaro Nomura*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文针对分数量子霍尔态点接触几何中的准粒子与电子隧穿对偶性展开研究，引入“相移瞬子（phase-shift instanton）”处理非阿贝尔边缘算子，重新表述了Moore-Read对偶性并给出了k=3 Read-Rezayi态的显式对偶描述。基于该对偶描述，解析计算出强耦合区域中的非线性微分电导，发现由于隧穿粒子必须是真费米子，Moore-Read态和Read-Rezayi态的电导行为普遍收敛到G ∝ V^4标度律，揭示了一种非阿贝尔分数量子霍尔边缘的拓扑约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究分数量子霍尔态（fractional quantum Hall states）点接触几何中准粒子（quasi-particle）与电子隧穿（electron tunneling）之间的对偶性，特别是处理非阿贝尔边缘算子（non-Abelian edge operators）时面临的理论挑战。

Method: 引入“相移瞬子”（phase-shift instanton）方法，将初级场（primary fields）的相位因子纳入瞬子气体（instanton gas）框架，从而重新表述Moore-Read对偶性并导出k=3 Read-Rezayi态的对偶描述。

Result: 明确了准粒子隧穿如何在瞬子中产生特征相移，以及强准粒子隧穿如何映射为弱电子隧穿；基于此对偶描述，解析计算了强耦合区域的非线性微分电导，发现Moore-Read态和Read-Rezayi态的输运行为普遍收敛到G ∝ V^4标度律。

Conclusion: 隧穿粒子跨越真空间隙（vacuum gap）必须是真费米子（true fermion）这一物理要求导致了普遍的G ∝ V^4输运标度行为，该普适输运特征揭示了非阿贝尔分数量子霍尔边缘背后的一种基本拓扑约束（topological constraint）。

Abstract: We study the duality between quasi-particle and electron tunneling in point-contact geometries of fractional quantum Hall states. To treat non-Abelian edge operators, we introduce a "phase-shift instanton" that incorporates phase factors from primary fields into the instanton gas framework. Using this method, we reformulate the Moore--Read duality and obtain an explicit dual description for the $k=3$ Read-Rezayi state. Our results clarify how quasi-particle tunneling produces characteristic phase shifts in instantons and how these shifts map strong quasi-particle tunneling to weak electron tunneling. Based on this dual description, we analytically evaluate the non-linear differential conductance in the strong-coupling regime. We reveal that, due to the physical requirement that the tunneling particle across the vacuum gap must be a true fermion, the transport behavior universally converges to a $G \propto V^4$ scaling for both the Moore--Read and Read--Rezayi states. This universal transport signature highlights a fundamental topological constraint underlying non-Abelian fractional quantum Hall edges.

### [227] [Vector Magnonics: Electrical Injection and Control of Spin Flow in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01225)
*Yanmeng Lei,Rui-Chun Xiao,Weiwei Lin,Tao Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过量子动力学计算预测，在交错磁体（altermagnet）中，自旋累积可以电注入一种包含纵向和显著横向分量的“矢量”或“多方向”磁振子自旋流（magnon spin current）；该横向电流在远离源处会出现符号反转，并可通过重新取向奈尔矢量（Néel vector）来开关。虽然传统反铁磁体中也存在这种横向电流，但交错磁体中由于宇称-时间对称性（parity-time symmetry）破缺，其横向响应增强了两个数量级，这为实验区分交错磁体与传统反铁磁体提供了明确的输运判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交错磁体中存在手性分裂的磁振子（chirally split magnons），有望为信息处理提供独特功能，但关键的输运特征——对于实验识别与操控至关重要——尚不清楚。

Method: 基于量子动力学（quantum-kinetic）计算方法，分析交错磁体中由自旋累积电注入的磁振子自旋流的纵向与横向分量，并与传统反铁磁体进行对比。

Result: 在交错磁体中，自旋累积可注入包含纵向和显著横向分量的“矢量”磁振子自旋流；该横向电流在远离源处发生符号反转，且可通过奈尔矢量取向开关调控。与传统反铁磁体相比，交错磁体中的横向响应因宇称-时间对称性破缺而增强约两个数量级。

Conclusion: 该巨大的横向增强效应为检测磁振子自旋分裂（magnon spin splitting）和奈尔矢量取向提供了决定性的输运指纹，为实验上区分交错磁体与传统反铁磁体给出了清晰判据。

Abstract: Altermagnets host chirally split magnons that promise unique functionalities for information processing. However, their distinctive transport signatures, crucial for experimental identification and manipulation, remain elusive. Here, we predict that a spin accumulation electrically injects a ``vector" or multidirectional magnon spin current into an altermagnet, comprising both longitudinal and sizable transverse components. Notably, this transverse current exhibits a sign reversal away from the source and can be switched on or off by reorienting the Néel vector. While such a transverse current is found to be not forbidden even in conventional antiferromagnets, we demonstrate through quantum-kinetic calculations that in altermagnets, the transverse response is enhanced by two orders of magnitude due to broken parity-time symmetry. This giant enhancement provides a decisive transport fingerprint for detecting magnon spin splitting and Néel-vector orientation, offering a clear criterion to experimentally distinguish altermagnets from conventional antiferromagnets.

### [228] [Decoherence due to the sudden coupling of an impurity to a metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01612)
*Felipe D. Picoli,Gustavo Diniz,Luiz N. Oliveira*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文利用无自旋共振能级模型（spinless resonant level model）研究量子杂质系统（quantum impurity system）在杂化突变淬火（sudden quench）下的非平衡动力学与退相干过程，并提出混合线性-对数离散化方法抑制有限尺寸效应，从而统一描述从相干拉比振荡到不可逆退相干的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子杂质系统在淬火后因粒子-空穴激发导致退相干（dephasing），但有限尺寸体系中离散能谱会引起准周期动力学和恢复现象，掩盖了真实的相干损失。本文旨在揭示并抑制这些有限尺寸赝象，从而获得从相干振荡到不可逆退相干的统一理解。

Method: 采用无自旋共振能级模型刻画杂质与金属之间的杂化突变淬火；引入混合线性-对数离散化（mixed linear-logarithmic discretization）使激发能不相称（incommensurate），从而抑制恢复（revivals）；结合精确可解的二能级极限与数值方法处理大晶格体系。

Result: 在有限尺寸体系中，离散能谱导致准周期动力学和恢复现象；混合线性-对数离散化有效抑制了有限尺寸赝象；从二能级极限下的相干拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）到大晶格中的阻尼与弛豫，展示了从相干到不可逆退相干的连续过渡。

Conclusion: 通过分析存活概率（fidelity）和杂质占据数，论文建立了淬火后量子杂质系统从相干振荡到有效不可逆退相干（decoherence）的完整图景，为理解开放量子系统中的退相干机制提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium dynamics and loss of coherence in a quantum impurity system using the spinless resonant level model subject to sudden quenches of the hybridization between the impurity and the metal. The survival probability (fidelity) and impurity occupation are analyzed as probes of the dephasing induced by particle-hole excitations. For finite systems, the loss of coherence loss is only apparent, as discrete spectra lead to quasi-periodic dynamics and revivals when phases realign. We show that a mixed linear-logarithmic discretization suppresses these finite-size artifacts by rendering excitation energies incommensurate, thereby reducing revivals. Starting from the exactly solvable two-level limit exhibiting coherent Rabi oscillations, we extend the analysis to large lattices, where damping and relaxation emerge. Combining analytical and numerical results, we provide a unified picture of the crossover from coherent oscillations to effectively irreversible decoherence.

### [229] [Coherent exciton spin dynamics and three-dimensional quantum state tomography in a single InAlAs quantum dot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01801)
*J. Njala,Y. Yamamoto,R. Kaji,S. Adachi,H. Sasakura*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用时间分辨量子态层析成像（time-resolved quantum state tomography）研究了单个InAlAs/AlGaAs量子点（quantum dot）中的激子自旋相干动力学（exciton spin dynamics）。在双LO声子准共振激发（two-LO-phonon quasi-resonant excitation）下，观察到显著的量子拍（quantum beats），并通过全局拟合（global fitting）证实自旋演化由各向异性交换相互作用（anisotropic exchange interaction）主导。尽管初始圆偏振度受限，但后续自旋相干寿命（spin coherence lifetime, 1.1 ns）超过了激子寿命（exciton lifetime, ~767 ps），且未观测到奥弗豪瑟移位（Overhauser shift），表明局部核环境（local nuclear environment）影响可忽略。该结果为利用差分偏振信号进行自旋轨迹三维重建提供了定量基准，展示了准共振激发在半导体纳米结构中实现稳定自旋初始化的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子点中激子自旋相干动力学是实现自旋初始化、操纵和读出，进而利用自旋自由度进行量子信息处理的基础。本文旨在通过高精度的量子态层析成像方法，定量揭示准共振激发条件下单个自旋系统的演化机制，并评估核环境的影响。

Method: 采用时间分辨量子态层析成像（time-resolved quantum state tomography）技术，在双LO声子准共振激发（two-LO-phonon quasi-resonant excitation）下，测量单个InAlAs/AlGaAs量子点中中性激子的圆偏振（circular）和对角线偏振（diagonal）分量。通过三个正交偏振基（orthogonal polarization bases）下的全局拟合（global fitting）程序，统一描述由各向异性交换相互作用（anisotropic exchange interaction）主导的哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）支配的自旋演化。

Result: 观测到量子拍（quantum beats）现象，反映精细结构劈裂（fine-structure splitting）Δ≈19.6 μeV。初始圆偏振度（degree of circular polarization）约为0.28，受载流子冷却过程中的快速弛豫过程限制。后续自旋相干寿命（spin coherence lifetime）为1.1±0.2 ns，超过激子寿命（exciton lifetime）~767 ps。自旋形成时间（spin-formation time）显著短于仪器响应函数（instrument response function），且未观测到可辨别的奥弗豪瑟移位（Overhauser shift），表明局部核环境（local nuclear environment）影响可忽略。

Conclusion: 本文为利用差分偏振信号（differential polarization signals）进行自旋轨迹三维重建（three-dimensional reconstruction of spin trajectories）提供了定量基准，证实了准共振激发（quasi-resonant excitation）在半导体纳米结构中实现稳定自旋初始化（stable spin initialization）的可行性。

Abstract: We investigate the coherent exciton spin dynamics in a single InAlAs/AlGaAs quantum dot using time-resolved quantum state tomography. Under two-LO-phonon quasi-resonant excitation of neutral exciton, we observe pronounced quantum beats in the circular and diagonal polarization components, reflecting the fine-structure splitting ($Δ\approx 19.6 \ μ\text{eV}$). By employing a global fitting procedure across three orthogonal polarization bases, we demonstrate that the spin evolution is consistently described by a unified Hamiltonian dominated by the anisotropic exchange interaction. While the initial degree of circular polarization is limited to $\approx 0.28$ due to fast relaxation processes during carrier cooling, the subsequent dynamics reveal a long-lived spin coherence ($1.1 \pm 0.2$ ns) that exceeds the exciton lifetime ($\sim 767$ ps). Our analysis reveals that the spin-formation time is significantly shorter than the instrument response function, and the absence of a discernible Overhauser shift confirms a negligible influence from the local nuclear environment under the present conditions. These results provide a quantitative benchmark for the three-dimensional reconstruction of spin trajectories using differential polarization signals, demonstrating the feasibility of using quasi-resonant excitation for stable spin initialization in semiconductor nanostructures.

### [230] [Orbital-Splitter Current in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01812)
*Koushik Ghorai,Sayan Sarkar,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在共线交变磁体（collinear altermagnets）中提出了轨道分裂电流（orbital-splitter current, OSC），即自旋分裂电流的轨道对应物，并利用密度矩阵（density-matrix）框架推导了其Drude贡献和轨道贝里曲率（orbital Berry curvature）贡献。研究表明，d波交变磁体FeSb₂因镜面对称（mirror symmetry）抑制Drude通道而实现纯本征OSC，其响应强各向异性且在某些场向下超过自旋分裂电流近四倍；此外，OSC可在交变磁体-铁磁体异质结构中产生类阻尼力矩，并与自旋分裂电流协同显著缩短磁化翻转时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自旋分裂电流（spin-splitter current）在共线交变磁体中已被广泛研究，但对应的轨道输运（orbital transport）机制尚未被探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，提出轨道分裂电流的概念并分析其物理起源与材料实现。

Method: 采用密度矩阵（density-matrix）理论框架，分别推导了轨道分裂电流的Drude项和轨道贝里曲率（orbital Berry curvature）贡献项；以d波交变磁体FeSb₂为例进行具体计算，分析其对称性约束与各向异性响应。

Result: FeSb₂中由于镜面对称（mirror symmetries）迫使轨道磁矩（orbital magnetic moment）为零，Drude通道被完全抑制，因此OSC表现为纯本征（purely intrinsic）响应；OSC响应具有强各向异性（strongly anisotropic），在特定场向下其幅值约为自旋分裂电流的四倍；OSC能在交变磁体-铁磁体异质结构中产生类阻尼力矩（damping-like torque），与自旋分裂电流共同作用时可显著缩短磁化翻转时间（magnetization switching time）。

Conclusion: 轨道分裂电流是交变磁体中一类与自旋分裂电流平行但来源不同的本征输运现象，在特定材料中可获得远超自旋通道的响应强度，并在自旋轨道力矩（spin-orbit torque）器件中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: In collinear altermagnets, the real-space rotational symmetry of opposite spin sublattices generates a large nonrelativistic spin-splitter current. Orbital transport in this setting has remained largely unexplored. Here, we introduce the orbital-splitter current (OSC), an orbital analogue of the spin-splitter current, and derive its Drude and orbital Berry curvature contributions using a density-matrix framework. We show that the $d$-wave altermagnet $\mathrm{FeSb}_2$ realizes a purely intrinsic OSC because mirror symmetries suppress the Drude channel by forcing the orbital magnetic moment to vanish. The OSC response is strongly anisotropic and, for selected field orientations, exceeds the spin-splitter current by nearly a factor of four. We further show that the OSC generates a damping-like torque in an altermagnet-ferromagnet heterostructure and, when combined with the spin-splitter current, significantly reduces the magnetization switching time.

</details>


### [231] [Synthetic Flat Bands, Hierarchical Topology, and Phase-Fluctuation-Insensitive Quantized Transconductance in Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02095)
*Subhadeep Chakraborty,Aabir Mukhopadhyay,Udit Khanna,Sourin Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了三端约瑟夫森结（three-terminal Josephson junction, 3-TJJ）合成布里渊区中博戈留波夫-德让纳（Bogoliubov-de Gennes, BdG）谱的拓扑相层级结构：能隙以上连续谱实现具有量子化单极子电荷的陈绝缘体相，而亚能隙安德烈夫束缚态由量子化偶极不变量表征；通过破缺时间反演对称性诱导合成平带，在电压偏置下实现时间平均跨导的量子化，并产生全局“甜 plateau”效应，为对称性保护的安德烈夫量子比特提供了鲁棒架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索三端约瑟夫森结（3-TJJ）合成布里渊区中的拓扑相结构，并利用其拓扑性质实现对超导量子器件的功能调控，特别是构建对相位噪声不敏感的对称性保护安德烈夫量子比特（symmetry-protected Andreev qubit）。

Method: 通过分析三端约瑟夫森结的博戈留波夫-德让纳（BdG）谱，在合成布里渊区中识别能隙以上连续谱的陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）相及其量子化单极子电荷（monopole charges ±1），并刻画亚能隙安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states, ABS）的量子化偶极不变量（dipolar invariant）；通过破缺时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）诱导合成平带（synthetic flat bands）。

Result: 合成平带抑制了全域相位偏置空间中的直流约瑟夫森电流；在电压偏置下，时间平均跨导（time-averaged transconductance）呈现鲁棒的量子化行为，类似于量子化霍尔电导平台；平带产生了全局性的相位不敏感“甜 plateau”（sweet plateau），超越了传统超导量子比特的局部甜点。

Conclusion: 三端约瑟夫森结的合成布里渊区中存在丰富的拓扑相层级结构，利用平带效应可实现相位不敏感的全局甜 plateau，为构建对称性保护的安德烈夫量子比特提供了鲁棒的器件架构。

Abstract: We uncover hierarchy of topological phases within the synthetic Brillouin zone of a three-terminal Josephson junction's (3-TJJ's) Bogoliubov-de Gennes spectrum. We demonstrate that the above-gap continuum realizes a Chern insulator phase with quantized monopole charges (\pm 1), while the subgap Andreev bound states (ABS) are characterized by a quantized dipolar invariant. By breaking time-reversal symmetry at the junction, we induce synthetic flat bands that suppress DC Josephson currents across the entire phase-bias space. Furthermore, under voltage bias, the junction exhibits a robust quantization of the time-averaged transconductance that is reminiscent of a quantized Hall conductance plateau owing to the flat band limit and its dipole phase. As a byproduct, the flat band produces a global "sweet plateau" of phase insensitivity, surpassing localized sweet spots of conventional superconducting qubits and enabling a robust architecture for symmetry-protected Andreev qubits.

</details>


### [232] [3D Quantum Hall Effect with Two Distinct Plateaus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02188)
*Jun-Hong Li,Yi-Yuan Chen,Peng-Lu Zhao,Hai-Zhou Lu,X. C. Xie*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释 $\mathrm{HfTe_5}$ 中三维量子霍尔效应（3D quantum Hall effect）实验中出现的第二个霍尔电导平台（约为第一个平台的 $3/5$）以及纵向电阻率被抑制的异常现象，这些现象此前被解读为可能的三维分数化（3D fractionalization）信号。

Method: 提出磁场驱动的 Lifshitz 转变（Lifshitz transition）导致自旋向下（spin-down）的空穴型第零朗道能带（zeroth Landau band）穿越费米能（Fermi energy），进而最低的自旋向上与自旋向下朗道能带之间发生能带嵌套（nesting），诱导出自旋密度波（spin-density wave）。通过计算霍尔电阻率和纵向电阻率并与实验对比，以及运用重整化群（renormalization group）分析来支持绝缘基态的结论。

Result: 计算得到的霍尔电阻率和纵向电阻率重现了实验行为；重整化群分析支持自旋密度波导致的绝缘基态（insulating ground state）解释。

Conclusion: 沿磁场方向朗道能带的可调谐性（tunability）使得三维量子霍尔效应展现出比二维对应物更丰富的现象学，值得进一步探索。第二个电导平台并非源于三维分数化，而是自旋密度波序导致的绝缘基态。

Abstract: The recent discovery of the 3D quantum Hall effect in $\mathrm{HfTe_5}$ has also revealed puzzling signatures of possible 3D fractionalization. Beyond the first plateau associated with the lowest Landau band, Hall conductivity exhibits a second plateau with a value of about $3/5$ of the first, accompanied by a suppressed longitudinal resistivity. Here, we attribute this second plateau to an insulating ground state arising from spin-density-wave order. We show that a magnetic-field-driven Lifshitz transition causes the spin-down holelike zeroth Landau band to cross the Fermi energy and that the resulting nesting between the lowest spin-up and spin-down Landau bands induces a spin-density wave. We calculate the Hall and longitudinal resistivity and reproduce the experimental behaviors. Our renormalization-group analysis further supports this insulating ground state. Our work reveals that the tunability of Landau bands along the magnetic-field direction endows the 3D quantum Hall effect with a broader phenomenology than its 2D counterpart and merits further exploration.

### [233] [Voltage-Tunable Nonequilibrium Dispersion Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02315)
*Christine M. E. Little,Daniel S. Kosov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了非平衡态格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）理论，用于描述两个纳米结构之间的色散相互作用（dispersion interactions），每个结构均为由外加偏压驱动至非平衡稳态的开放量子系统。研究揭示了相互作用能量可分解为电荷噪声（charge noise）和电荷耗散（charge dissipation）贡献，并发现非平衡条件可在数量级上增强吸引性色散相互作用，甚至导致排斥性相互作用及符号反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有色散相互作用理论主要基于平衡态假设，缺乏对非平衡条件下（如外加偏压驱动的纳米结构）色散相互作用的理论描述。

Method: 从双粒子非平衡态格林函数出发，推导出以单个系统的极化传播子（polarisation propagators）表示的一般化相互作用能表达式，并引入广义Kubo-Martin-Schwinger比值（generalised Kubo-Martin-Schwinger ratio）刻画非平衡态下细致平衡的偏离。

Result: 相互作用能可分解为电荷噪声与电荷耗散贡献，提供推广了平衡态London图像的涨落-耗散解释。模型计算表明，外加电压可将吸引性色散相互作用增强约一个数量级。非平衡条件下可产生排斥性色散相互作用，且电子引线中的粒子数反转可驱动色散相互作用的符号反转。

Conclusion: 非平衡条件显著改变纳米结构间的色散相互作用性质，既能增强其强度，也能导致从吸引到排斥的符号反转，为调控纳米尺度相互作用提供了新的物理机制。

Abstract: We develop a nonequilibrium Green's function theory for dispersion interactions between two nanostructures, each an open quantum system driven into a nonequilibrium steady state by an applied bias voltage. Starting from the two-particle nonequilibrium Green's function, we derive a general expression for the interaction energy in terms of the polarisation propagators of the individual systems. The interaction energy admits a physically transparent decomposition into charge noise and charge dissipation contributions, providing a fluctuation-dissipation interpretation that generalises the equilibrium London picture. Model calculations for coupled molecular junctions demonstrate that the applied voltage can enhance the attractive dispersion interaction by nearly an order of magnitude relative to equilibrium. In thermal equilibrium, the dispersion interaction is universally attractive, irrespective of the specific form of the nanostructure Hamiltonians or their coupling to reservoirs. Out of equilibrium, we introduce a generalised Kubo-Martin-Schwinger ratio that parametrises the departure from detailed balance. We show that, in contrast to equilibrium, nonequilibrium conditions can lead to a repulsive dispersion interaction. Finally, we discuss the conditions under which population inversion in the electronic leads can drive a sign reversal of the dispersion interaction.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（如leviton）依赖精确电压驱动产生单电子激发，缺乏对热脉冲的灵活操控手段。本文旨在利用光场与电子系统的相互作用，实现可控的温度调制以产生电荷中性热脉冲。

Method: 通过光场诱导电子储层（electronic reservoir）的可控时变温度，产生电中性热脉冲并发射至介观导体（mesoscopic conductor）中。采用紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）描述两个由量子点接触（quantum point contact）连接的电子储层，计算时变电流及其涨落。

Result: 基于紧束缚模型的数值计算表明，光场诱导的温度调制能够产生可探测的热脉冲，并在输出端观测到时变电流及其涨落特征。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了实现按需热量电子学（on-demand caloritronics）的可行路径——利用能量而非电荷承载量子信息，并为探测热驱动导体中的时分辨热输运（time-resolved heat transport）和量子相干性（quantum coherence）奠定了基础。

Abstract: We propose to generate heat pulses in mesoscopic conductors using light fields. In contrast to single-electron excitations such as levitons, which are created by accurate voltage drives, our approach relies on modulating the temperature of an electronic reservoir. To this end, we show that the interactions with a light field can induce a controllable time-dependent temperature in an electrode. The temperature modulations generate charge-neutral heat pulses that can be emitted into a mesoscopic conductor and detected in the outputs. We illustrate our approach by evaluating the time-dependent currents and their fluctuations using a tight-binding model of two electronic reservoirs connected by a quantum point contact. Our work establishes a route towards on-demand caloritronics, where energy rather than charge carries quantum information, and it paves the way for probing time-resolved heat transport and quantum coherence in thermally driven conductors.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于紧束缚-马芬-锡轨道（tight-binding muffin-tin orbitals）基组的量子力学散射计算，模拟非平衡自旋和轨道电流在过渡金属中的输运和衰减过程。

Conclusion: 轨道电流的衰减行为与自旋电流定性不同，其短程衰减特征为轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）的物理机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: We use quantum mechanical scattering calculations implemented in a basis of tight-binding muffin-tin orbitals to calculate nonequilibrium spin and orbital currents in transition metals with a view to understanding the length scale on which they decay. In the case of spin currents, the relaxation length, called the spin-flip diffusion length, is reasonably well understood. We apply our experience with spin currents to study orbitally-polarized currents and find that they behave qualitatively differently. Upon injection from a lead, orbital currents decay within a few atomic layers contradicting the current interpretation of experimental results which appear to show exponential decay on the length scale of the spin-flip diffusion length and longer. When spin-orbit coupling is included, the injected orbital current is partially converted into a spin current within a few atomic layers. This insight provides a new perspective on the physics of the orbital Hall effect.

### [237] [Floquet-Multiple Andreev Reflections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02642)
*Régis Mélin,Romain Danneau,Morteza Kayyalha*

TL;DR: 本文提出在弹道多端约瑟夫森结中，由电压偏置导致的超导相位差周期性演化可提供内禀的Floquet驱动，并通过四重态（quartet）及高阶多对（multipair）过程产生特征性的Floquet-多次安德烈夫反射（Floquet-MAR）有限偏压电导和噪声共振现象。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 考虑一个构建在弹道二维正常导体（连续电子态）上的三端约瑟夫森结，通过分析四重态及高阶多对过程，研究Floquet-多次安德烈夫反射（Floquet-MAR）导致的有限偏压电导和噪声共振，并以偏压电压和电化学势为参数进行表征。

Result: 证实了四重态和高阶多对过程可以产生由偏压电压和电化学势参数化的Floquet-MAR有限偏压电导和噪声共振特征。

Conclusion: 该微观图像为在弹道多端约瑟夫森结中实现和探测Floquet-MAR物理开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: Floquet theory describes quantum systems governed by time-periodic Hamiltonians, much as Bloch theory describes spatially periodic solids. In voltage-biased multiterminal Josephson junctions, the Josephson relation causes superconducting phase differences to evolve periodically in time, thereby providing an intrinsic Floquet drive. In this Letter, we consider three-terminal Josephson junctions formed on a ballistic two-dimensional normal conductor with a continuum of electronic states. We show that the quartet and higher-order multipair processes yield characteristic Floquet-multiple Andreev reflection (Floquet-MAR) finite-bias conductance and noise resonances that are parameterized by the bias voltage and electrochemical potential. This microscopic picture opens a route toward implementing and probing Floquet-MAR physics in ballistic multiterminal Josephson junctions.

</details>

Electrical performances of fabricated RTD, starting from cryogenic to room temperatures, show a significant milestone via exhibiting huge PVR values of 178 at 4K and 24 at RT with more possible improvement in the field of room temperature quantum technology. Momentum conserved and non conserved tunneling from highly n-doped Si through multiple valleys of 1L-MoS2 provides a tremendous opportunity in gate-induced manipulation in Spin-Valley Qubit technology operational at deep cryogenic temperatures (mK).

Abstract: Surface acoustic wave (SAW) resonators provide a compact platform for confining microwave-frequency phonons and are widely used in radio-frequency technologies, but their operation at gigahertz frequencies and cryogenic temperatures remains challenging. ### [240] [Absence of Quantum-Metric-Induced Intrinsic Longitudinal Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02750)
*Ping Tang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文通过量子力学微扰理论证明，量子度量（quantum metric）诱导的本征纵向非线性响应严格为零，而本征霍尔响应则允许存在，解决了当前量子度量非线性输运理论中的不一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明量子度量可能同时产生本征非线性霍尔效应和纵向输运，然而这一结论在理论上存在不一致性，需要澄清量子度量诱导的本征纵向响应是否存在。

Method: 采用标准的量子力学微扰理论（quantum-mechanical perturbation theory），在非线性响应的所有阶次上进行分析，不依赖具体的能带结构细节。

Result: 量子度量诱导的本征纵向响应严格为零，而对应的本征霍尔响应是允许的；该结论来源于本征电流的无耗散特性（dissipationless nature），且独立于能带结构细节，在非线性响应的所有阶次都成立。

Conclusion: 该工作解决了当前量子度量诱导非线性输运理论公式中的不一致性，并建议重新审视近期归因于量子度量的本征纵向响应的实验或理论报告。

Abstract: Nonlinear charge transport in solids has emerged as a powerful probe of the quantum geometric properties of Bloch electrons. While the Berry curvature underlies the intrinsic anomalous Hall effect, recent studies have suggested that the quantum metric may generate both \emph{intrinsic} nonlinear Hall and longitudinal transport. Here, using standard quantum-mechanical perturbation theory, we demonstrate that the quantum-metric-induced intrinsic longitudinal response identically vanishes, even though the corresponding intrinsic Hall response is allowed. This conclusion follows from the dissipationless nature of intrinsic currents and holds independently of band structure details and to all orders in the nonlinear response. Our work resolves existing inconsistencies in the theoretical formulation of quantum-metric-induced nonlinear transport and suggests a reexamination of recently reported intrinsic longitudinal responses attributed to the quantum metric.

### [241] [Triplet-assisted leakage during singlet-triplet qubit readout with a quantum point contact](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02785)
*Karol Kawa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文扩展了横向双量子点中单态-三态量子比特的量子点接触（quantum point contact, QPC）读出理论，通过引入三态（triplet）构型隧穿至相邻点中更高能级的过程。该附加通道会产生能量允许的泄漏路径，从而改变分支依赖的电荷和电流噪声特征，即使泡利阻塞（Pauli blockade）在基态流形内仍然有效。模型包含每个点中的两个单粒子能级，推导了相应的单态和三态块结构以及林德布拉德主方程（Lindblad master equation），并通过量子跳跃模拟（quantum-jump simulations）解析单个读出事件的动力学。互补的利乌维尔稳态分析（Liouvillian steady-state analysis）识别了隧穿至激发态定性改变读出特征的参数区间，其交叉由能级间距决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 模型设定每个量子点包含两个单粒子能级；推导了单态和三态的块结构以及林德布拉德主方程；运用量子跳跃模拟解析单个读出事件的动力学；并结合利乌维尔稳态分析确定隧道耦合激发态定性改变读出特征的参数区间。

Result: 三态隧穿至更高能级会创建能量允许的泄漏路径，即使泡利阻塞仍在基态流形内有效，该路径也会改变分支依赖的电荷和电流噪声特征；交叉行为由能级间距决定。

Conclusion: 所扩展的读出理论揭示了三态隧穿至激发态对量子点接触读出特征产生定性改变的条件与机制，为更准确地理解和优化单态-三态量子比特的读出过程提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Quantum point contact readout theory for singlet-triplet qubits in a lateral double quantum dot is extended by including tunneling of triplet configurations into a higher-energy level of the neighboring dot. This additional channel creates energetically allowed leakage pathways that modify the branch-dependent charge and current-noise signatures, even when the Pauli blockade remains effective within the ground-state manifold. The model contains two single-particle levels in each dot. The resulting singlet and triplet block structure is derived together with a Lindblad master equation. Quantum-jump simulations are then used to resolve the dynamics of individual readout events. A complementary Liouvillian steady-state analysis identifies the regime in which tunneling to the excited level qualitatively changes the readout signatures, with the crossover determined by the level spacing.

### [242] [Emergent Kinetic Constraints and Subspace Fragmentation in Rydberg Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01366)
*Wen-Jie Geng,Zhenming Zhang,Wei Yi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了强相互作用里德伯原子阵列（Rydberg atom array）中希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert-space fragmentation）现象，指出碎片的存在与维度依赖于全局里德伯耦合的失谐（detuning）与相互作用之间的竞争，并采用辅助费米子描述（auxiliary fermion description）揭示了碎片化背后的涌现动力学约束，为非遍历多体动力学的工程化提供了系统理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强相互作用的里德伯原子阵列中，动力学往往被限制在退耦合的希尔伯特子空间（decoupled Hilbert subspaces）内，这为非遍历性（nonergodicity）提供了有趣的范例。然而，这些子空间的存在条件及其碎片化特征尚不清楚，需要系统性地理解其尺度行为及背后的动力学约束。

Method: 通过考虑全局里德伯耦合的可变失谐（variable detuning），分析失谐与相互作用对希尔伯特子空间存在性的影响；计算碎片维度随系统规模增大的多种标度行为；采用辅助费米子描述（auxiliary fermion description）揭示子空间碎片化及碎片约束动力的涌现动力学约束（emergent kinetic constraints）。

Result: 希尔伯特子空间的存在依赖于失谐与相互作用的共同作用；这些子空间表现出强烈的碎片化特征，碎片维度随系统规模增大呈现多种标度行为；系统的约束动力学由碎片的维度与连通性共同决定；辅助费米子描述成功揭示了碎片化及其约束动力的涌现动力学约束机制。

Conclusion: 该研究系统性地理解了里德伯阵列中的希尔伯特空间碎片化现象，并为超越PXP模型（PXP model）的非遍历多体动力学工程化提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In a strongly interacting Rydberg atom array, the dynamics are often constrained to the decoupled Hilbert subspaces, representing an intriguing paradigm for nonergodicity. By considering a variable detuning of the global Rydberg coupling, we show that, not only is the existence of these Hilbert subspaces dependent on the interplay of detuning and interaction, but they are also strongly fragmented, with the fragment dimensions exhibiting various scaling behaviors with increasing system size. The resulting constrained dynamics of the system are thus governed by the dimension and connectivity of these fragments. We then adopt an auxiliary fermion description to reveal the underlying emergent kinetic constraints for the subspace fragmentation and fragment-confined dynamics. Our results provide a systematic understanding of Hilbert-space fragmentation in Rydberg arrays, and shed light on engineering nonergodic many-body dynamics beyond the PXP model.

### [243] [Enhancing supercurrent-based inertial sensing via interactions in atomtronic angular accelerometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02048)
*S. Carmona-López,A. Matos-Abiague,F. Isaule,L. Morales-Molina*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文理论研究了环形光晶格中受角向交流驱动和外部旋转的超冷原子超流，证明通过将驱动频率调谐至布洛赫频率（Bloch frequency）的整数分数可产生显著净原子流，并发现弱相互作用可突破单粒子系统的傅里叶极限（Fourier limit），将角加速度计灵敏度提升至少两个数量级，超越了此前基于超冷原子的设计方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何利用受驱动环形光晶格中超冷原子的超流（supercurrent）来开发高精度原子电子学（atomtronics）角加速度传感器。

Method: 采用Bose-Hubbard模型（Bose-Hubbard model）框架下的解析分析与数值模拟相结合的方法，研究角向交流驱动（angularly ac-shaken）环形晶格中原子流对外部旋转的响应特性。

Result: 当驱动频率调谐至布洛赫频率（Bloch frequency）的整数分数时出现显著净原子流，远离共振时流平均趋近零；单粒子情形下共振宽度与平均时间成反比，形成傅里叶极限（Fourier limit）；引入弱相互作用后灵敏度超越该傅里叶极限，相较单粒子情形提升至少两个数量级。

Conclusion: 研究为开发基于原子流、具有相互作用增强灵敏度的新型惯性传感器（inertial sensors）铺平了道路。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate supercurrents of ultracold atoms in angularly ac-shaken ring lattices subjected to external rotation. Our results demonstrate how these supercurrents can be harnessed for the development of high-precision atomtronic angular accelerometers. Using both analytical and numerical approaches within the Bose-Hubbard model framework, we demonstrate that a significant net atomic current arises when the lattice driving frequency is tuned to an integer fraction of the Bloch frequency, while the current averages to nearly zero away from such a resonance. In the single-particle regime, the resonance width scales inversely with the averaging time, thereby setting a fundamental Fourier-limited bound on the measurement's sensitivity. Strikingly, our numerical simulations demonstrate that this Fourier limit - a fundamental barrier in the non-interacting system - can be surpassed by introducing weak interactions between atoms. In the interacting regime, the sensitivity surpasses the Fourier-limited scaling with the averaging time, achieving an improvement of at least two orders of magnitude over the single-particle scenario, and exceeding the performance of previously proposed ultracold-atom-based angular accelerometers. These findings pave the way for developing new atomic-current-based inertial sensors with interaction-enhanced sensitivity.

### [244] [Dynamical universality in a driven quantum fluid of light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02397)
*Ivan Gnusov,Paolo Comaron,Antonio Gianfrate,Dimitrios Trypogeorgos,Marzena Szymanska,Paolo Cazzato,Milena De Giorgi,Daniele Sanvitto,Dario Ballarini*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过实验测量了半导体微腔中激子-极化激元（exciton-polariton）形成的驱动量子光流体在相变阈值以下的临界动力学行为，发现关联长度与弛豫时间满足普适标度关系 τ ∝ ξ^z，动力学指数 z ≈ 2，表明非守恒序参量的扩散型动力学，将平衡态临界动力学拓展至驱动光学系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 普适标度（universal scaling）是相变物理的核心思想之一，但迄今为止，对此临界行为的直接实验探测主要局限于平衡态多体系统（equilibrium many-body systems），尤其是静态临界行为；研究者希望探索在非平衡驱动系统中普适性如何涌现。

Method: 实验使用半导体微腔中的激子-极化激元（exciton-polaritons）构成的驱动量子光流体（driven quantum fluid of light）；通过探测凝聚阈值以下以涨落为主导的无序相（fluctuation-dominated disordered phase），直接测量关联长度 ξ 的静态增长和弛豫时间 τ 的动态减慢。

Result: 实验发现关联长度 ξ 与弛豫时间 τ 满足普适标度关系 τ ∝ ξ^z，测得动力学指数（dynamical exponent）z ≈ 2，表明该系统呈现非守恒序参量（non-conserved order parameter）的扩散型动力学（diffusive dynamics）。

Conclusion: 该结果将临界动力学（critical dynamics）的物理图景从平衡态物质拓展至驱动光学系统（driven optical systems），在量子凝聚体（quantum condensates）与激光器（lasers）之间建立了桥梁。

Abstract: Universal scaling near phase transitions is one of the central ideas of physics, linking the growth of spatial correlations to the slowing down of dynamics. So far, direct experimental access to this critical behavior has remained largely confined to equilibrium many-body systems, and especially to static critical behavior. Here we probe how universality emerges in a driven quantum fluid of light formed by exciton--polaritons in a semiconductor microcavity. By probing the fluctuation-dominated disordered phase below the condensation threshold, we directly measure both the static growth of the correlation length $ξ$ and the dynamical slowing down of the relaxation time $τ$. We find that these quantities obey the universal relation $τ\propto ξ^{z}$ with dynamical exponent $z \approx 2$, revealing diffusive dynamics of a non-conserved order parameter. Our results extend the physics of critical dynamics from equilibrium matter to driven optical systems, bridging quantum condensates and lasers.

</details>

### [245] [Stochastic Cluster Expansion for Excited State Energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01064)
*Annabelle Canestraight,Russell Miller,Libor Veis,Vojtech Vlcek*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文扩展了随机簇展开（stochastic cluster expansion, SCE）框架，从基态关联能推广至激发能隙（excitation gaps），通过轨道空间簇贡献的层次化结构直接表达能量差，从而避免了对大型或化学预选活性空间（active spaces）的依赖。该方法在电荷转移复合物和并苯（polyacenes）上验证，获得的单重态-三重态能隙（singlet-triplet gaps）与全系统结果一致，且收敛快速、可系统改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联系统的激发态电子结构面临两个根本困难：多体希尔伯特空间（many-body Hilbert space）的指数级扩展，以及构建系统可控活性空间（active spaces）的难度。现有方法难以在不依赖大型或预选活性空间的情况下高效计算激发能。

Method: 基于先前为基态关联能开发的随机簇展开（SCE）框架，将形式扩展至激发能隙。能量差直接表示为轨道空间簇贡献的层次化结构；激发能由涉及最小前沿化学子空间（frontier chemical subspace, FCS）的降秩计算（低秩计算）精确处理，并结合随机采样（stochastic sampling）处理剩余轨道环境。

Result: 在电荷转移复合物和并苯体系上验证了该方法。获得的单重态-三重态能隙与全系统计算结果一致，且随着低阶簇项（low-order cluster terms）迅速收敛。

Conclusion: 该方法消除了对大型或化学预选活性空间的需求，提供了强关联体系中激发态计算的一种可系统改进（systematically improvable）的框架。

Abstract: Excited-state electronic structure in strongly correlated systems remains challenging due to the exponential scaling of the many-body Hilbert space and the difficulty of constructing systematically controlled active spaces. Building on the stochastic cluster expansion (SCE) framework previously developed for ground-state correlation energies, we extend the formalism to excitation gaps by expressing energy differences directly as a hierarchy of orbital-space cluster contributions. In this formulation, excitation energies are reconstructed from reduced-rank calculations involving a minimal frontier chemical subspace (FCS), treated exactly, together with stochastic sampling of the remaining orbital environment. This approach eliminates the need for large or chemically preselected active spaces. We demonstrate the method on charge-transfer complexes and polyacenes, where accurate singlet-triplet gaps are obtained that agree with full-system results. The method converges with low-order cluster terms and provides a systematically improvable framework for excited states in correlated systems.

</details>

### [246] [The Haar measure of the $p$-adic rotation group $\textrm{SO}(3)_p$ via nautical angles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01385)
*Lorenzo Guglielmi,Stefano Mancini,Vincenzo Parisi,Ilaria Svampa*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过航海（Cardano）参数化显式构造了紧致p进旋转群SO(3)_p上的哈尔测度（Haar measure），利用其与p进四元数乘性群模去标量群（ℍ_p^×/ℚ_p^×）的拓扑群同构，导出了变量变换公式和雅可比（Jacobian）行列式，最终给出了具有因式化密度形式的归一化哈尔测度显式公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为p进旋转群SO(3)_p提供显式的哈尔测度构造，以满足非阿基米德（non-Archimedean）模型中需要显式角度描述的不变积分（invariant integration）的应用需求。

Method: 采用航海（Cardano）参数化方法，利用SO(3)_p与p进四元数模去标量群ℍ_p^×/ℚ_p^×之间的拓扑群同构，结合p进四元数乘性群ℍ_p^×上已知的哈尔测度，在p进框架下推导相应的变量变换公式并计算雅可比行列式。

Result: 给出了SO(3)_p上以航海坐标参数化的归一化哈尔测度的显式公式，该测度在三个角度上具有因式化的密度形式。

Conclusion: 该构造为需要角度显式描述的不变积分的非阿基米德模型提供了一个具体的工具。

Abstract: We study the explicit construction of the Haar measure on the compact $p$-adic rotation group $\textrm{SO}(3)_p$ by nautical (Cardano) parametrization. Exploiting its topological group isomorphism with $\mathbb{H}_p^\times/\mathbb{Q}_p^\times$ of $p$-adic quaternions modulo scalars, we derive the corresponding change of variables formulas and compute the associated Jacobian in the $p$-adic setting, which we combine with the known Haar measure on the multiplicative group of $p$-adic quaternions $\mathbb{H}_p^\times$. This yields an explicit formula for the normalized Haar measure on $\textrm{SO}(3)_p$ in nautical coordinates, with a factorized density in the three angles. Our construction provides a concrete tool suited for applications of non-Archimedean models where an explicit angular description of invariant integration is required.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一维位置依赖质量系统在非自伴哈密顿量框架下的可解性，利用抽象阶梯算子策略寻找特征值与特征向量。

Method: 采用抽象阶梯算子方法，不假设哈密顿量自伴，聚焦于算子可因子化的情形；引入赝玻色算子进行分析，并构造双相干态。

Result: 发现赝玻色算子在该分析中发挥重要角色，成功构造了与这些算子关联的双相干态，并给出了显式实例。

Conclusion: 抽象阶梯算子策略可有效处理非自伴、可因子化的一维位置依赖质量哈密顿量，赝玻色算子和双相干态在该类问题中具有适用性。

Abstract: We consider the Hamiltonian $H$ of a particle in one dimension with a position dependent mass for which we apply the recent strategy of the so-called {\em abstract ladder operators}, in the attempt to find its eigenvalues and eigenvectors. We don't assume that $H$ is self-adjoint, while we focus on the case of a factorizable operator. We show then that pseudo-bosonic operators play a relevant role in this analysis, and we construct bi-coherent states attached to these operators. Explicit examples are discussed.

### [248] [Properties of tensorial free cumulants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01887)
*Thomas Buc-d'Alché,Luca Lionni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统性地将自由概率论（free probability）推广到随机张量（random tensors）领域，建立了不同理论框架之间的联系，将已有结果推广至任意阶涨落，并计算了具有非平凡协方差的高斯随机张量的张量自由累积量（tensorial free cumulants），提供了具体的非平凡例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，针对不同不变性下随机张量的自由概率论推广，出现了多种理论观点，但它们是否导向相同的张量自由累积量和张量自由性（tensorial freeness）概念尚不明确。已有方法（Collins、Gurau 及第二作者提出）仅针对某些分布和部分矩（moments）进行了研究，缺乏系统全面的分析。

Method: 将 Collins、Gurau 等人基于有限尺寸量（finite size quantities）和不变群平均的方法与 Nechita 和 Park 提出的方法建立联系；将已有结果以及 Nechita 和 Park 的结果推广至任意阶涨落（arbitrary orders of fluctuations）；研究具有更大不变群（invariance groups）的分布；详细阐明与张量 HCIZ 积分和 BGW 积分自由能渐近行为（asymptotics）的联系；给出张量乘积的张量自由累积量公式。

Result: 计算了具有非平凡协方差的高斯随机张量（Gaussian random tensors）的张量自由累积量，证明它们提供了张量自由累积量取非平凡值的具体分布例子。

Conclusion: 本文建立了不同张量自由概率论框架之间的系统联系，将相关结果推广到任意阶，并为非平凡张量自由累积量提供了具体的分布实例。

Abstract: In the past two years, several points of view have been proposed to address the question of the generalization of the theory of free probability to random tensors with different invariances, and it is unclear at this point whether they lead to the same notions of tensorial free cumulants and freeness. One way to approach this problem, developed by Collins, Gurau and the second named author for local unitary invariant random tensors, relies on finite size quantities involving averages over the invariance group, and whose asymptotics naturally possess the properties expected for tensorial generalizations of free cumulants of arbitrary orders. At this point, this approach has only been carried out for certain distributions, and for a subset of the moments that define such theories, and a more systematic and exhaustive study is lacking.
  This is the program initiated in this paper: we link this approach to the one proposed by Nechita and Park; extend a number of their results as well as those of the aforementioned paper to arbitrary orders of fluctuations, thereby generalizing higher order free cumulants; push further the study of distributions with larger invariance groups; detail the link with the asymptotics of the free-energies of the tensor HCIZ and BGW integrals; and provide formulae for tensorial free cumulants of products of tensors.
  Another important question is that of the definition of concrete distributions whose tensorial free-cumulants take non-trivial values. We compute the tensorial free cumulants for Gaussian random tensors with non-trivial covariances, and show that they provide such examples.

</details>


### [249] [A constructive approach to generalized principal connections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01983)
*Lorenzo Fatibene,Hartwig Winterroth*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过局部坐标变换律研究广义主丛（generalized principal bundle）与广义主联络（generalized principal connection）的全局几何性质，证明了李群纤维丛（Lie group fiber bundle）是广义主丛，并建立了广义主联络与李群纤维丛联络之间的关联，为经典场论中的广义规范理论（generalized gauge theory）奠定几何基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在澄清广义主丛与广义主联络的全局几何性质，特别是通过局部坐标变换律（local coordinate transformation laws）来刻画这些结构，并为将广义主联络纳入经典场论（classical field theories）的纤维丛（fiber bundle）框架、进而发展广义规范理论提供必要的几何基础。

Method: 引入广义主丛坐标（generalized principal bundle coordinates）并推导其变换律；通过证明李群纤维丛（进而包括向量丛（vector bundle））是广义主丛，以及具有连通典型纤维（connected typical fiber）的李群纤维丛是某个适当主丛的相伴丛（associated bundle），建立结构分类；利用水平提升（horizontal lifts）和局部条件刻画李群纤维丛联络与广义主联络。

Result: 得到了广义主丛坐标及其变换律；证明了李群纤维丛（以及任何向量丛）均为广义主丛，且具有连通典型纤维的李群纤维丛是某个主丛的相伴丛；给出了广义主联络与李群纤维丛联络之间关联的直接刻画；在本文框架中恢复了已知结果，即广义主联络仅与李群纤维丛联络相关联，且在标准主丛上退化为通常的主联络（principal connection）。

Conclusion: 本文建立的几何框架有助于理解广义主联络在经典场论纤维丛处理中的角色，为向广义规范理论的概念推进提供了必要的理论支撑。

Abstract: We address the recently introduced notions of generalized principal bundle and generalized principal connection by keeping track of global geometric properties through local coordinate transformation laws. This approach leads us to introduce generalized principal bundle coordinates and to find their transformation laws. Besides, we show that any Lie group fiber bundle (and hence, in particular, any vector bundle) is a generalized principal bundle and we give a proof of the fact that any Lie group fiber bundle with connected typical fiber is an associated bundle to a suitable principal bundle. Moreover, we present a direct way to characterize Lie group fiber bundle connections and generalized principal connections in terms of horizontal lifts and of local conditions. Finally, we recover in our setting some already known results, including that generalized principal connections are associated only to Lie group fiber bundle connections and that they reduce to usual principal connections on standard principal bundles. Our results are needed in order to understand how generalized principal connections might fit in the fiber bundle treatment of classical field theories, aiming towards a notion of generalized gauge theory.

</details>


### [250] [On the Ultraviolet Problem for the Ground State Energy of the Translation-Invariant Pauli--Fierz Model at Zero Total Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02349)
*Volker Bach,Miguel Ballesteros,Merten Mlinarzik*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了无外势情况下Pauli–Fierz模型的基态能量，重点分析了总动量算符谱值p=0时的情形。通过Bogoliubov–Hartree–Fock近似，证明了能量泛函关于参数η和z的非凸性，识别并移除了非凸项，得到了严格凸的修正泛函，并证明了唯一极小元的存在性。进一步构造了关于η的显式偏极小元，将问题简化为单变量优化。最终估计显示，修正能量的最小值在紫外截止Λ→∞时渐近行为为Λ^{3/2}。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确估计Pauli–Fierz模型在无外势情况下的基态能量，特别是其关于紫外截止（ultraviolet cutoff）Λ的依赖关系，是量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics）中理解电子-光子相互作用基本性质的重要理论问题。

Method: 采用Bogoliubov–Hartree–Fock近似，利用Bogoliubov变换（由正Hilbert–Schmidt算子z参数化）和Weyl变换（由向量η参数化）作用于真空生成纯准自由态（pure, quasifree states），对Pauli–Fierz算子在总动量p=0的分量进行变分分析。

Result: 证明了原始能量泛函关于η和z不是凸函数；识别并移除非凸项后，修正泛函保持完整相互作用项且是严格凸的，存在唯一极小元。构造了关于η的显式偏极小元，将问题简化为单变量η的优化。修正能量的最小值在Λ→∞时渐近增长为Λ^{3/2}。

Conclusion: 通过修正能量泛函并消除非凸性，成功地将原多变量变分问题简化为单变量优化，并得到了基态能量关于紫外截止的标度行为，即渐近地正比于Λ^{3/2}。

Abstract: We study the ground state energy of the Pauli--Fierz model in the absence of external potentials. We consider the fiber decomposition of the Pauli--Fierz operator with respect to the spectral values, $p$, of the total momentum operator and focus on the case $p = 0$. The corresponding variational problem is analyzed to estimate the dependence of the ground state energy on the ultraviolet cutoff $Λ$. We employ a Bogoliubov--Hartree--Fock approximation using pure, quasifree states generated by Bogolubov transformations (parametrized by a positive Hilbert--Schmidt operator $z$) and Weyl transformations (parametrized by a vector $η$) applied to the vacuum. We prove that the resulting energy functional is not a convex function of $η$ and $z$. We identify the non-convex term and remove it from the energy functional. The modified functional retains the full interaction term and is shown to be strictly convex. We study the ground state of the modified functional and prove the existence of a unique minimizer. Furthermore, we construct an explicit partial minimizer (with respect to $η$, for fixed $z$), which allows us to eliminate $z$ and reduce the minimization problem to a single variable, $η$. Finally, we estimate the minimum of the modified energy functional in terms of the ultraviolet cutoff $Λ$ and demonstrate that, up to a constant factor, it grows asymptotically as $Λ^{3/2}$, as $Λ\to \infty$.

</details>


### [251] [Low-Order Conservation Law Multipliers for a Generalized Fifth-Order KP Family](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02473)
*Nitin Serwa*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了一类广义五阶Kadomtsev–Petviashvili族（其一维约化包括Lax、Sawada–Kotera和Kaup–Kupershmidt方程）的局部守恒律乘子（local conservation law multiplier），通过直接乘子法（direct multiplier method）对零阶乘子进行分类并构造守恒向量，证明微分阶数不超过二的乘子必然降为一阶，并在一般情形下将一阶乘子进一步约化至零阶族，同时识别出导致低阶刚性的结构来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对广义KP族（generalized Kadomtsev–Petviashvili family）中高阶非线性方程的守恒律乘子进行系统分类，是一维约化方程（Lax、Sawada–Kotera、Kaup–Kupershmidt）之外的推广研究，旨在揭示该类方程在乘子结构上的低阶刚性（low-order rigidity）及其数学根源。

Method: 采用直接乘子法（direct multiplier method），首先在自然多项式子类（natural polynomial subclass）中对与因变量无关的零阶乘子（zeroth-order multiplier）进行分类并构造代表性的守恒向量（conserved vector）。随后通过严格证明表明微分阶数不超过二的乘子必然降为一阶。在三次导数非线性项（cubic derivative nonlinearity）系数非零时完成了无限制的一阶分类（unrestricted first-order classification），并在互补情形的一般代数子分支（generic algebraic sub-branch）上建立了相同的约化结果。

Result: 在所述一般性情形（generic regimes）下，所有一阶乘子（first-order multiplier）均可约化至零阶乘子族，从而揭示了乘子问题的低阶刚性的结构来源。研究同时指出一个有限的例外分支列表（finite list of exceptional branches）仍未解决。

Conclusion: 该工作为广义五阶KP族的守恒律乘子建立了清晰的分类框架，证明了一般参数情形下乘子结构存在显著的刚性（rigidity），并定位了导致该刚性的关键结构因素，为后续完全分类提供了方向和边界条件。

Abstract: We study local conservation law multipliers for a generalized fifth-order Kadomtsev--Petviashvili family whose one-dimensional reductions include the Lax, Sawada--Kotera, and Kaup--Kupershmidt equations. Using the direct multiplier method, we classify zeroth-order multipliers that are independent of the dependent variable within a natural polynomial subclass and construct representative conserved vectors. We then prove that every multiplier of differential order at most two is necessarily of differential order at most one. An unrestricted first-order classification is obtained when the coefficient of the cubic derivative nonlinearity is nonzero, and the same reduction is established on a generic algebraic sub-branch of the complementary case. In these regimes, all first-order multipliers reduce to the zeroth-order family. A finite list of exceptional branches remains open. The results identify the structural sources responsible for the low-order rigidity of the multiplier problem in the generic regimes treated here.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 对多项式势情形，推导出了广义Kontsevich模型的显式表达式，并给出了所预期对应关系的完整证明。对于可容许变形势情形，建立了变形版本的r-旋理论（deformed r-spin theory）作为相应几何理论。

Conclusion: 该工作为广义Kontsevich模型、拓扑递归与r-旋曲线模空间几何之间的等价性提供了显式构造与严格证明，并揭示了该框架在变形势下的自然扩展，深化了对可积系统与模空间几何关联的理解。

Abstract: By employing polynomial-reduced KP integrability, combined with the string equation, this work establishes explicit relationships between the generalized Kontsevich model, the topological recursion of the spectral curve, and the geometry of moduli spaces of $r$-spin curves. For the generalized Kontsevich model with a polynomial potential, we derive an explicit formulation and provide a proof of these widely expected correspondences. Furthermore, the method is extended to the cases with admissible deformed potentials, where the corresponding geometric theory is a deformed version of $r$-spin theory.

</details>


### [253] [On Algebras of Functions over Infinite Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02816)
*Dimitrios Giannakis,Mohammad Javad Latifi Jebelli,Michael Montgomery*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在可分希尔伯特空间上引入了一族由高斯测度协方差算子与单位圆盘上全纯函数构造的再生核希尔伯特空间，并研究了其作为再生核希尔伯特代数的乘法封闭性及扭曲正则对易关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无限维分析中，构造具有良好代数结构的函数空间是一个核心问题。本文旨在将再生核希尔伯特空间（reproducing kernel Hilbert space, RKHS）推广到无限维定义域，并赋予其点态乘法封闭性以形成代数结构，进而为研究量子场论中的正则对易关系提供新的函数空间框架。

Method: 利用可分希尔伯特空间$\mathbb{H}$上的高斯测度（Gaussian measure）的协方差算子（covariance operator），结合单位圆盘上的全纯函数（holomorphic function）$\Lambda$，构造一族再生核希尔伯特空间$\mathcal A_\Lambda$。通过施加特定条件确保该空间在点态乘法下封闭，从而赋予其再生核希尔伯特代数结构。进一步在该代数上研究扭曲正则对易关系（twisted canonical commutation relations），其中产生算符与湮灭算符均为有界算子。

Result: 成功构造了定义在可分希尔伯特空间无限维区域上的全纯函数再生核希尔伯特空间族$\mathcal A_\Lambda$；在核函数满足一定条件时，$\mathcal A_\Lambda$在点态乘法下封闭，构成再生核希尔伯特代数；在该代数上建立了产生算符与湮灭算符均有界的扭曲正则对易关系。

Conclusion: 该工作为无限维全纯函数空间上的代数结构提供了新构造，有界算子的扭曲正则对易关系为量子场论等领域的代数方法提供了潜在工具。

Abstract: We introduce a family of reproducing kernel Hilbert spaces $\mathcal A_Λ$ of holomorphic functions defined on an infinite--dimensional domain in a separable Hilbert space, $\mathbb{H}$. The reproducing kernel of $\mathcal A_Λ$ is constructed using the covariance operator associated with a Gaussian measure on $\mathbb{H}$, along with a holomorphic function $Λ$ on the unit disk. Under certain conditions on the kernel, $\mathcal A_Λ$ is closed under pointwise multiplication, giving it the structure of a reproducing kernel Hilbert algebra (RKHA). We also study twisted canonical commutation relations on these RKHAs, where the creation and annihilation operators are both bounded.

</details>
