### [254] [Impurity-Scattering Assisted Umklapp Scattering as the Origin of Low-Temperature Resistivity in the Normal-State of Cuprate Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01316)
*Xingyu Ma,Minghuan Zeng,Huaiming Guo,Shiping Feng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文从铜氧化物超导体的微观电子结构出发，研究了从欠掺杂赝能隙相到过掺杂奇异金属相的正常态低温电阻率行为，提出杂质散射辅助的反节点附近自旋激发导致的umklapp散射是核心机制，分别解释了欠掺杂区T平方行为和过掺杂区T线性行为的成因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物超导体正常态电阻率在欠掺杂赝能隙相（pseudogap phase）呈现T平方（T-quadratic）行为，而在过掺杂奇异金属相（strange-metal phase）呈现T线性（T-linear）行为，然而对这些不同行为的完整理解仍是一个具有挑战性的问题。

Method: 基于铜氧化物超导体的微观电子结构（microscopic electronic structure），从欠掺杂赝能隙相到过掺杂奇异金属相，对正常态低温电阻率进行了理论分析，引入了杂质散射（impurity scattering）和umklapp散射（umklapp scattering）机制。

Result: 电阻率行为需要同时依赖杂质散射和umklapp散射：杂质散射将分布函数的修正限制在反节点（antinodal）区域附近，而杂质散射辅助的自旋激发umklapp散射是低温电阻率行为的核心。温度标度（temperature scale）的掺杂依赖性与反节点自旋赝能隙交叉温度（spin pseudogap crossover temperature）的行为类似。在过掺杂奇异金属相中，温度标度以上区域电阻率为T线性；在欠掺杂赝能隙相中，温度标度以下区域自旋赝能隙打开，降低了反节点附近的自旋激发态密度，削弱了电子与反节点相关自旋激发的umklapp散射强度，从而产生T平方行为。

Conclusion: 该机制统一解释了铜氧化物超导体欠掺杂赝能隙相与过掺杂奇异金属相中不同的低温电阻率行为，指出杂质散射辅助的自旋激发umklapp散射及自旋赝能隙的打开是理解这些输运性质的关键。

Abstract: The transport experiments reveal that the low-temperature resistivity in the normal-state of cuprate superconductors is quadratic in temperature (T-quadratic) in the underdoped pseudogap phase, while it is linear in temperature (T-linear) in the overdoped strange-metal phase, however, the full understanding of these different behaviours is still a challenging issue. Here starting from the microscopic electronic structure of cuprate superconductors, the low-temperature resistivity in the normal-state is investigated from the underdoped pseudogap phase to the overdoped strange-metal phase. It is shown that the mechanism requires both the impurity scattering and the umklapp scattering: the impurity scattering is needed to restrict the modification of the distribution function to at around the antinodal region,while the impurity-scattering assisted umklapp scattering from a spin excitation is at the heart of the behaviour in the low-temperature resistivity, where the doping dependence of the temperature scale exists, and presents a similar behavior of the antinodal spin pseudogap crossover temperature. In the low-temperature region above the temperature scale in the overdoped strange-metal phase, the resistivity is T-linear, however, in the low-temperature region below the temperature scale in the underdoped pseudogap phase, the opening of the spin pseudogap lowers the spin excitation density of states at around the antinodal region, which reduces the strength of the electron umklapp scattering from a spin excitation associated with the antinode, and thus leads to a T-quadratic behaviour of the resistivity.

</details>


### [255] [Metallic crossover through the tilt-free transition in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ at high pressure and temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01651)
*Bastien Michon,Yingpeng Yu,Beatrice D'Alò,Elena Stellino,Gergely Németh,Bosen Wang,Jianping Sun,Jinguang Cheng,Paolo Postorino,Ferenc Borondics,Francesco Capitani*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过高压高温拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）和同步辐射红外光谱（synchrotron-based infrared spectroscopy），系统研究了双层镍氧化物La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$在压力驱动下的结构相变与电子性质演化，揭示了结构转变与金属化、载流子密度大幅增加以及电子-声子耦合增强之间的强耦合关系，建立了统一的结构-电子性质图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$在高压下出现高温超导电性（high-T$_c$ superconductivity），但其相边界（phase boundaries）以及结构变化对电子性质的影响尚不明确，亟需通过实验手段系统研究结构与电子性质的协同演化。

Method: 结合高压与高温拉曼光谱和同步辐射红外反射光谱（infrared reflectivity spectroscopy），对La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$在不同压力和温度条件下的结构相变与电子响应进行原位测量。

Result: 拉曼测量确认了压力驱动的结构相变，并观察到Fano线形（Fano line shapes）的出现，表明电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）增强；高温数据揭示了Amam相在544 K以上存在未报道过的上限温度；红外反射率测量证实了伴随的金属化（metallization）过程，载流子密度（carrier density）提高了两个数量级，标志着从坏金属（bad metal）到好金属（good metal）的转变。

Conclusion: 研究建立了La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$中结构相变与电子性质强耦合的统一图像，阐明了结构转变对金属化及超导电性出现的关键作用。

Abstract: La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, a bilayer nickelate with Ruddlesden-Popper structure, undergoes a pressure-induced structural transition from a tilted Amam phase to an untilted Fmmm (or I4/mmm) phase near 10-15 GPa, concomitant with the emergence of high-T$_c$ superconductivity (T$_c$ $\sim$ 80 K). Despite intense interest, the phase boundaries and the impact of structural changes on the electronic properties remain unclear. Here, we combine high-pressure and high-temperature Raman and synchrotron-based infrared spectroscopies to map the structural and electronic evolutions. Raman measurements confirm the pressure-driven structural transition and reveal the emergence of Fano line shapes, indicating enhanced electron-phonon coupling. High-temperature data show analogous spectral signatures above 544 K, suggesting an unreported upper temperature limit of the Amam phase within the T-P phase diagram of this system. Infrared reflectivity measurements evidence a concomitant metallization, with a tremendous two-order-of-magnitude increase in carrier density, marking a crossover from a bad metal to a good metal. These results establish a unified picture of the structural transition and its strong coupling to the electronic properties.

</details>


### [256] [Two distinct superconducting regimes in Ti4Co2O under pressures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01893)
*Lifen Shi,Keyuan Ma,Binbin Ruan,Zhen Wang,Pengtao Yang,Zhian Ren,Jianping Sun,Gang Li,Fabian O. von Rohr,Bosen Wang,Jinguang Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过对Ti4Co2O超导体的电输运测量，发现其超导转变温度Tc与上临界场Bc2(0)对压力表现出非单调依赖关系，识别出两个不同的超导相，并通过第一性原理计算揭示其与态密度演化密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Ti4Co2O超导体中超导转变温度Tc和上临界场Bc2(0)对压力的依赖行为，以揭示该体系在外界刺激（压力）作用下的超导特性及其物理机制。

Method: 采用电输运测量研究Tc和Bc2(0)的压力依赖性；利用室温同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron X-ray diffraction）检测晶体结构稳定性；结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析态密度（density of states）随压强的演化。

Result: Tc呈现非单调的压力依赖：先以dTc/dP=0.034 K/GPa上升，在10–20 GPa迅速下降，随后以0.023 K/GPa回升至69.7 GPa下的4.31 K。Bc2(0)呈穹顶状（dome-shaped）压力依赖，在5 GPa处达到最大值，约常压值的两倍，且在整个压力范围内超过弱耦合泡利顺磁极限（Pauli paramagnetic limit）Bp。未观察到结构相变，体模量（bulk modulus）为192 GPa。第一性原理计算表明，非单调Tc与Ti4Co2O压缩过程中态密度演化密切相关。

Conclusion: 在弱自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的Ti4Co2O中，超导性对外部刺激（如压力）高度敏感；识别出两个不同的超导区：低压相具有增强的Bc2(0)值和费米液体（Fermi-liquid）电输运（指数n=2），高压相具有单调增加的Tc及增强的声子散射（指数n=4）。

Abstract: We report on the pressure dependence of superconducting transition temperature Tc and upper critical field Bc2(0) through electrical transport of the Ti4Co2O superconductor (eg.,the superconducting transition temperature Tc = 2.5 K and the Bc2(0)=7.2T=2.9Tc). We find that the Tc exhibits non-monotonic pressure dependence:it rises monotonically at first with a pressure coefficient of dTc/dP=0.034 K/GPa, but rapidly decreases around 10-20 GPa, and then increases with the dTc/dP = 0.023 K/GPa, up to= 4.31 K at 69.7 GPa. Concurrently, the Bc2(0)exhibits a dome shaped pressure dependence, with its maximum at 5 GPa of almost twice the value at ambient pressure, exceeding the weak-coupling Pauli paramagnetic limit Bp throughout the whole pressure range. By comparing the normal-state and superconducting properties, we identify two distinct superconducting regimes, with a low-pressure superconducting phase characterized by an enhanced Bc2(0)values and Fermi-liquid normal-state electrical transport (the exponent n = 2), and a high-pressure superconducting phase with a monotonically increased Tc and an enhancement in phonon scatterings (the exponent n = 4). Room-temperature synchrotron X-ray diffraction indicates that there is no structural transition up to 55.8 GPa, which gives a relatively large bulk modulus of 192 GPa in comparison with other alloy superconductors. First-principles calculations suggest that the nonmonotonic Tc maybe closely related to the evolution of the density of states of Ti4Co2O upon compression, which is different from those of isostructural superconductors Ti4Ir2O and Nb4Rh2C. Our results show that even in the Ti4Co2O with weak spin-orbit coupling, superconductivity remains highly sensitive to the external stimuli such as pressure.

</details>


### [257] [Spin-polarized Josephson current induced by inhomogeneous altermagnetic interlayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02140)
*Wenjun Zhao,Yuri Fukaya,Pablo Burset,Jorge Cayao,Yukio Tanaka,Bo Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用非均匀交变磁（altermagnetic）中间层实现无磁场约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）的方案，通过调控Néel矢量的取向角，可大幅增强超导临界电流并消除0-π跃迁，同时产生自旋极化的约瑟夫森电流（spin-polarized Josephson current），为无耗散自旋电子学器件提供高度可调的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现无耗散的自旋超流（dissipationless spin supercurrents）是超导自旋电子学（superconducting spintronics）的核心目标。现有方案通常需要外加磁场或复杂结构，缺乏无磁场、高度可调的实现途径。

Method: 提出一种场-free的约瑟夫森结结构，中间层采用非均匀交变磁（altermagnetic）材料，其Néel矢量位于面内（in-plane）且具有空间不均匀性。通过改变两侧交变磁层的Néel矢量之间的错向角（misorientation angle）来调控超导配对行为。

Result: 当Néel矢量错向角为π且两层厚度相等时，由质心动量（center-of-mass momentum）驱动的超导配对振幅（pair amplitude）的空间振荡相互抵消，抑制了单层的对破缺效应（pair-breaking），显著增强临界电流并消除0-π跃迁。此外，非共线排列的Néel矢量可产生净自旋极化的约瑟夫森电流，该自旋电流是自旋三重态配对关联（spin-triplet pair correlations）的明确标志。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种高度可调、无需外加磁场的平台，可用于实现无耗散自旋电子学器件，为超导自旋电子学提供新的设计思路。

Abstract: The pursuit of dissipationless spin supercurrents is a central theme in superconducting spintronics. We propose a field-free Josephson junction using an inhomogeneous altermagnetic interlayer with in-plane Néel vectors. We show that the current-phase relation and critical Josephson current is highly sensitive to the misorientation angle between the altermagnetic layers' Néel vectors. Specifically, at a $π$ misorientation with equal layer thicknesses the spatial oscillations of the superconducting pair amplitude, governed by the center-of-mass momentum, undergo mutual cancellation. This compensation suppresses individual layer pair-breaking, significantly enhancing the critical current and eliminating $0$-$π$ transitions. Furthermore, the non-collinear alignment of the Néel vectors facilitates the emergence of a net spin-polarized Josephson current. This spin current serves as a distinct signature of spin-triplet pair correlations, generated by the spin-dependent momentum shifts inherent to the altermagnetic exchange field. Our results establish a highly tunable, field-free platform for the realization of dissipationless spintronic devices.

</details>


### [258] [Revisiting the surface density of states of midgap Andreev edge states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02423)
*Gota Sato,Yasushi Nagato,Seiji Higashitani*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了粗糙表面对 p-波和 d-波超导体中带隙内安德烈夫边缘态（MAES）的影响，发现 d-波态中平带包含两种不同的 MAES 模式，其间的漫散射导致表面态密度峰展宽并形成 V 形结构，而 p-波态因仅含单一 MAES 模式而对粗糙表面保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清 p-波和 d-波超导体中表面粗糙度对带隙内安德烈夫边缘态（midgap Andreev edge states, MAES）影响差异显著的物理起源，从而深入理解 MAES 对粗糙表面的响应机制。

Method: 通过分析两种超导态中平带（flat band）的 MAES 模式构成，分别考察 p-波态（单一模式）和 d-波态（两种不同模式）在漫散射（diffuse scattering）下表面态密度（SDOS）的变化，并对比两者行为差异。

Result: d-波态中平带由两种不同 MAES 模式构成，模式间的漫散射导致带隙峰（midgap peak）显著展宽，并在费米能级（Fermi energy）附近形成 V 形结构；p-波态由于平带仅包含单一 MAES 模式，带隙峰对漫散射保持鲁棒（robust）。

Conclusion: 表面粗糙度对 MAES 的影响取决于平带中 MAES 模式的数目与类型：多模式体系（d-波）中间模式散射主导响应行为，而单模式体系（p-波）则表现出更强的抗粗糙表面干扰能力，这一发现为理解 MAES 表面敏感性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We revisit the effect of surface roughness on midgap Andreev edge states (MAES) in p- and d- wave superconductors. For a perfectly specular surface, MAES form a flat band at the Fermi energy, which manifests as a sharp midgap peak in the surface density of states (SDOS). Previous theoretical studies have shown that MAES in p- and d-wave superconductors respond markedly differently to surface roughness. In the d-wave state, diffuse surface scattering significantly broadens the midgap peak in the SDOS, accompanied by the emergence of a V-shaped structure centered at the Fermi energy. In contrast, the midgap peak in the p-wave state remains robust against diffuse scattering. In this work, we clarify the physical origin of this contrasting behavior. A key aspect of our analysis is that the flat band in the d-wave state consists of two distinct types of MAES modes. We show that inter-mode diffuse scattering leads to substantial broadening of the midgap peak and to the formation of the V-shaped structure. By contrast, the robustness of MAES in the p-wave state arises from the presence of a single MAES mode in the flat band. These results provide new insight into the response of MAES to surface roughness.

</details>


### [259] [Interfacial charge-induced adsorption mode for electron pairing in high-temperature superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02619)
*Jiu Hui Wu,Hua Tian,Kejiang Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文揭示了高温超导体中由界面电荷诱导吸附模式（interfacial charge-induced adsorption mode）驱动的电子配对机制。针对YBCO超导体，论文详细推导了有效相互作用势、电子-吸附模式耦合强度（吸附耦合常数高达43.4），并基于一维Ginzburg-Landau方程和能隙方程分别计算了相干长度和超导能隙，其结果与文献和扫描隧道显微镜/光谱学（STM/STS）实验测量值（17 meV）高度吻合，验证了所提出的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高温超导体的电子配对机制长期未明，现有理论难以定量解释实验观测。本文旨在揭示界面电荷诱导吸附模式如何实现电子配对，并建立可定量验证的理论框架。

Method: 通过分析YBCO超导体中电子与氧离子价柔性态（valence-flexible state）的耦合，建立由吸附势（adsorption potential）调控的界面电荷层模型。利用一维Ginzburg-Landau方程（无磁场条件）推导相干长度表达式，并建立能隙方程计算超导能隙。

Result: 吸附耦合常数达43.4；d波对称性来源于界面吸附力的各向异性；计算的相干长度与文献结果非常接近；计算得到的超导能隙与STM/STS测量值17 meV高度吻合。

Conclusion: 定量预测与已知实验及文献结果的一致性验证了所提出理论框架的正确性，表明界面电荷诱导吸附模式是高温超导体电子配对的关键机制。

Abstract: The electron pairing mechanism by the interfacial charge-induced adsorption mode of high-temperature superconductors is revealed. For the YBCO superconductors, the coupling of electrons and valence-flexible state of oxygen ions forms a charge-regulated interfacial layer induced by the adsorption potential, and electrons are paired by sharing the optimized interfacial structure and exchanging the adsorption mode, generating strong attraction to form Cooper pairs. Then the effective interaction potential between electrons is exactly derived in details, as well as the electron-adsorption-mode coupling strength, in which the adsorption coupling constant is up to 43.4. Furthermore, we verify that d-wave come from the anisotropy of interfacial adsorption forces, and explain the pseudo-energy gap behavior. By using the one-dimensional Ginzburg-Landau equation in the absence of a magnetic field, we obtain the coherence length expression, and the coherence length calculated is very close to the literature results. By establishing the energy gap equation, we obtain the superconducting gap , which is very close to the measured result of 17meV by Scanning Tunneling Microscopy/Spectroscopy. These quantitative predictions close to the known results could verify our theoretical framework.

</details>


### [260] [Vortex Transport in Ni/Bi Bilayer Superconductor with Strong Spin-Orbit and Exchange Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02677)
*Laxmipriya Nanda,Sohini Guin,Yasen Hou,Rajib Sarkar,Naresh Shyaga,Souvik Banerjee,A. Sundaresan,N. S. Vidhyadhiraja,Jagadeesh S. Moodera,Dhavala Suri*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过磁输运实验揭示了Ni/Bi双层薄膜中涡旋动力学（vortex dynamics）主导的输运行为，证实其超导态符合常规s波序参量（s-wave order parameter），且超导性遍及整个双层结构而非仅局限于界面，任何非常规超导贡献均微乎其微。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ni/Bi双层体系因铁磁镍与强自旋轨道耦合金属铋的结合，为探索非常规超导（unconventional superconductivity）提供了理想平台，但其配对机制与磁环境中的输运特性尚未明确。

Method: 对Ni/Bi双层薄膜近超导转变温度（Tc）区域开展磁输运测量（magneto transport measurements），并结合铁磁绝缘体对照实验，分析涡旋动力学与交换邻近效应（exchange proximity effects）的行为。

Result: 发现孤立涡旋对面外磁场（out-of-plane fields）敏感，产生反对称横向电阻峰（antisymmetric transverse resistance peaks），归因于Magnus力与粘滞力（viscous forces）的竞争；对照实验证实超导性遍及整个双层而非仅局限于界面。

Conclusion: 涡旋动力学主导的输运统一图景表明，Ni/Bi双层中的超导可用常规s波序参量描述，任何可能的非常规贡献均十分微小。

Abstract: Nickel/bismuth (Ni/Bi) bilayers are a promising platform for exploring unconventional superconductivity. Ferromagnetic Ni is coupled to Bi, a strong spin orbit metal that only becomes superconducting below approx 10 mK, forming a bilayer exhibits superconductivity at a much higher temperatures, a Tc of 3 to 4 K. Such a bilayer thus makes an ideal system to probe Cooper pairing in strong spin orbit coupled magnetic environments. Magneto transport studies near Tc reveal the behavior of vortex dynamics and exchange proximity effects. It is seen that isolated vortices of the bilayers respond sensitively to out of plane fields, producing antisymmetric transverse resistance peaks attributable to competing Magnus and viscous forces. Control experiments using a ferromagnetic insulator confirm that superconductivity extends throughout the bilayer, not just confined at the interface. Overall, the results provide a unified picture of transport dominated by vortex dynamics and show that a conventional s wave order parameter accounts for the observations, with any likely unconventional contributions being only subtle.

</details>

# cs.AI [[Back]](#toc)

### [261] [Accelerating battery research with an AI interface between FINALES and Kadi4Mat](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00909)
*Giovanna Tosato,Leon Merker,Monika Vogler,Michael Selzer,Arnd Koeppe*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出一个跨平台互操作框架（结合FINALES与Kadi RDM生态系统），通过多目标贝叶斯优化（multi-objective Bayesian optimization）高效探索钠离子扣式电池化成协议（formation protocol）中化成时间与寿命末期性能之间的权衡，逼近帕累托前沿（Pareto front），以最少实验次数实现快速、高性能的电池化成流程优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钠离子扣式电池（sodium-ion coin cells）的化成过程耗时过长，严重影响电池寿命和性能。本研究旨在优化化成协议，在减少实验次数以节省资源的同时，兼顾化成时间最小化与寿命末期（End of Life, EOL）性能最大化这两个潜在冲突的目标。

Method: 构建一个跨平台的互操作性（interoperability）框架，整合FINALES与Kadi RDM两大生态系统：FINALES负责在POLiS MAP平台上编排实验计划与执行，Kadi4Mat中实现的主动学习（active-learning）代理则采用多目标批量贝叶斯优化（multi-objective batched Bayesian optimization）来指导实验选择，从而高效探索参数空间。

Result: 通过该框架迭代探索化成时间与EOL性能之间的权衡关系，识别出逼近帕累托前沿（Pareto front）的候选解决方案，证明了可互操作基础设施在电池研究数据驱动优化中的可行性。

Conclusion: 该工作流展示了跨系统、跨研究中心的协同分布式协作能力，建立了一个可迁移至多种材料科学与工程优化任务的通用框架。

Abstract: The time-consuming formation process critically impacts the longevity of sodium-ion coin cells and End Of Life (EOL) performance. This study aims to optimize formation protocols for duration efficiency, targeting high-performance outcomes while minimizing the number of experiments to reduce resource consumption and accelerate discovery. Specifically, we consider two potentially competing objectives: minimizing formation time and maximizing EOL performance. Beyond this application focus, we also present a methodological contribution: a framework designed to enable interoperability between the FINALES and Kadi RDM ecosystems, which we employ to tackle our optimization problem. In this setup, the FINALES framework orchestrates experiment planning and execution on the POLiS MAP, while an active-learning agent implemented within Kadi4Mat guides experiment selection, using multi-objective batched Bayesian optimization to efficiently explore the parameter space. This interoperability enhancement enables coordinated, distributed collaboration across automated systems and human-operated workflows, bridging multiple research centers. Using this approach, we iteratively explore the trade-off between formation time and EOL performance and identify candidate solutions approximating the Pareto front. The resulting workflow demonstrates the capability of interoperable infrastructures to facilitate data-driven optimization in battery research, and establishes a transferable framework applicable to diverse materials science and engineering optimization tasks.

</details>
